 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet dvaipāyanoṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śivaṃ ca yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati vācyamānaṃ kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalair abhiṣecanena śuklāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ śaśivarṇaṃ caturbhujam prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa kṛtodakaṃ tu rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥc puraskṛtya mahābāhur uttatārākulendriyaḥa uttīrya ca mahīpālo bāṣpavyākulalocanaḥc papāta tīre gaṅgāyā vyādhaviddha iva dvipaḥa taṃ sīdamānaṃ jagrāha bhīmaḥ kṛṣṇena coditaḥc maivam ity abravīc cainaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ parabalārdanaḥa tam ārtaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau niśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥc dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍavā rājan dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhirama taṃ dṛṣṭvā dīnamanasaṃ gatasattvaṃ janeśvaramc bhūyaḥ śokasamāviṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samupāviśana rājā ca dhṛtarāṣṭras tam upāsīno mahābhujaḥc vākyam āha mahāprājño mahāśokaprapīḍitama uttiṣṭha kuruśārdūla kuru kāryam anantaramc kṣatradharmeṇa kauravya jiteyam avanis tvayāa tāṃ bhuṅkṣva bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ suhṛdbhiś ca janeśvarac na śocitavyaṃ paśyāmi tvayā dharmabhṛtāṃ varaa śocitavyaṃ mayā caiva gāndhāryā ca viśāṃ patec putrair vihīno rājyena svapnalabdhadhano yathāa aśrutvā hitakāmasya vidurasya mahātmanaḥc vākyāni sumahārthāni paritapyāmi durmatiḥa uktavān eṣa māṃ pūrvaṃ dharmātmā divyadarśanaḥc duryodhanāparādhena kulaṃ te vinaśiṣyatia svasti ced icchase rājan kulasyātmana eva cac vadhyatām eṣa duṣṭātmā mando rājā suyodhanaḥa karṇaś ca śakuniś caiva mainaṃ paśyatu karhi citc dyūtasaṃpātam apy eṣām apramatto nivārayaa abhiṣecaya rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc sa pālayiṣyati vaśī dharmeṇa pṛthivīm imāma atha necchasi rājānaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramb vināśam upayāsyanti tava putrā na saṃśayaḥc meḍhībhūtaḥ svayaṃ rājyaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva pārthivaa samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu vartamānaṃ narādhipac anujīvantu sarve tvāṃ jñātayo jñātivardhanaa evaṃ bruvati kaunteya vidure dīrghadarśinic duryodhanam ahaṃ pāpam anvavartaṃ vṛthāmatiḥa aśrutvā hy asya vīrasya vākyāni madhurāṇy ahamc phalaṃ prāpya mahad duḥkhaṃ nimagnaḥ śokasāgarea vṛddhau hi te svaḥ pitarau paśyāvāṃ duḥkhitau nṛpac na śocitavyaṃ bhavatā paśyāmīha janādhipa vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktas tu rājñā sa dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dhīmatāc tūṣṇīṃ babhūva medhāvī tam uvācātha keśavaḥa atīva manasā śokaḥ kriyamāṇo janādhipac saṃtāpayati vaitasya pūrvapretān pitāmahāna yajasva vividhair yajñair bahubhiḥ svāptadakṣiṇaiḥc devāṃs tarpaya somena svadhayā ca pitṝn apid atithīn annapānena kāmair anyair akiṃcanāna tvadvidhasya mahābuddhe naitad adyopapadyatec viditaṃ veditavyaṃ te kartavyam api te kṛtama śrutāś ca rājadharmās te bhīṣmād bhāgīrathīsutātc kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāc caiva nāradād vidurāt tathāa nemām arhasi mūḍhānāṃ vṛttiṃ tvam anuvartitumc pitṛpaitāmahīṃ vṛttim āsthāya dhuram udvahaa yuktaṃ hi yaśasā kṣatraṃ svargaṃ prāptum asaṃśayamc na hi kaś cana śūrāṇāṃ nihato tra parāṅmukhaḥa tyaja śokaṃ mahārāja bhavitavyaṃ hi tat tathāc na śakyās te punar draṣṭuṃ tvayā hy asmin raṇe hatāḥa etāvad uktvā govindo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc virarāma mahātejās tam uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥa govinda mayi yā prītis tava sā viditā mamac sauhṛdena tathā premṇā sadā mām anukampasea priyaṃ tu me syāt sumahat kṛtaṃ cakragadādharac śrīman prītena manasā sarvaṃ yāvadanandanaa yadi mām anujānīyād bhavān gantuṃ tapovanamb kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyāmi iti me niścitā matiḥc na hi śāntiṃ prapaśyāmi ghātayitvā pitāmahame karṇaṃ ca puruṣavyāghraṃ saṃgrāmeṣv apalāyinama karmaṇā yena mucyeyam asmāt krūrād ariṃdamac karmaṇas tad vidhatsveha yena śudhyati me manaḥa tam evaṃvādinaṃ vyāsas tataḥ provāca dharmavitc sāntvayan sumahātejāḥ śubhaṃ vacanam arthavata akṛtā te matis tāta punar bālyena muhyasec kim ākāśe vayaṃ sarve pralapāma muhur muhuḥa viditāḥ kṣatradharmās te yeṣāṃ yuddhena jīvikāc yathā pravṛtto nṛpatir nādhibandhena yujyatea mokṣadharmāś ca nikhilā yāthātathyena te śrutāḥb yathā vai kāmajāṃ māyāṃ parityaktuṃ tvam arhasic asakṛc caiva saṃdehāś chinnās te kāmajā mayāa aśraddadhāno durmedhā luptasmṛtir asi dhruvamc maivaṃ bhava na te yuktam idam ajñānam īdṛśama prāyaścittāni sarvāṇi viditāni ca te naghac yuddhadharmāś ca te sarve dānadharmāś ca te śrutāḥa sa kathaṃ sarvadharmajñaḥ sarvāgamaviśāradaḥc parimuhyasi bhūyas tvam ajñānād iva bhārata vyāsa uvācaa yudhiṣṭhira tava prajñā na samyag iti me matiḥc na hi kaś cit svayaṃ martyaḥ svavaśaḥ kurute kriyāḥa īśvareṇa niyukto yaṃ sādhv asādhu ca mānavaḥc karoti puruṣaḥ karma tatra kā paridevanāa ātmānaṃ manyase cātha pāpakarmāṇam antataḥc śṛṇu tatra yathā pāpam apakṛṣyeta bhārataa tapobhiḥ kratubhiś caiva dānena ca yudhiṣṭhirab pūyante tu narā rājaṃs tasmād yajñāḥ parāyaṇamc taranti nityaṃ puruṣā ye sma pāpāni kurvatea yajñena tapasā caiva dānena ca narādhipac pūyante rājaśārdūla narā duṣkṛtakarmiṇaḥa asurāś ca surāś caiva puṇyahetor makhakriyāmc prayatante mahātmānas tasmād yajñāḥ parāyaṇama yajñair eva mahātmāno babhūvur adhikāḥ surāḥc tato devāḥ kriyāvanto dānavān abhyadharṣayana rājasūyāśvamedhau ca sarvamedhaṃ ca bhāratac naramedhaṃ ca nṛpate tvam āhara yudhiṣṭhiraa yajasva vājimedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatāc bahukāmānnavittena rāmo dāśarathir yathāa yathā ca bharato rājā dauḥṣantiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥc śākuntalo mahāvīryas tava pūrvapitāmahaḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa asaṃśayaṃ vājimedhaḥ pāvayet pṛthivīm apic abhiprāyas tu me kaś cit taṃ tvaṃ śrotum ihārhasia imaṃ jñātivadhaṃ kṛtvā sumahāntaṃ dvijottamac dānam alpaṃ na śakyāmi dātuṃ vittaṃ ca nāsti mea na ca bālān imān dīnān utsahe vasu yācitumc tathaivārdravraṇān kṛcchre vartamānān nṛpātmajāna svayaṃ vināśya pṛthivīṃ yajñārthe dvijasattamac karam āhārayiṣyāmi kathaṃ śokaparāyaṇāna duryodhanāparādhena vasudhā vasudhādhipāḥc pranaṣṭā yojayitvāsmān akīrtyā munisattamaa duryodhanena pṛthivī kṣayitā vittakāraṇātc kośaś cāpi viśīrṇo sau dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥa pṛthivī dakṣiṇā cātra vidhiḥ prathamakalpikaḥc vidvadbhiḥ paridṛṣṭo yaṃ śiṣṭo vidhiviparyayaḥa na ca pratinidhiṃ kartuṃ cikīrṣāmi tapodhanac atra me bhagavan samyak sācivyaṃ kartum arhasi vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktas tu pārthena kṛṣṇadvaipāyanas tadāc muhūrtam anusaṃcintya dharmarājānam abravītd kośaś cāpi viśīrṇo yaṃ paripūrṇo bhaviṣyatia vidyate draviṇaṃ pārtha girau himavati sthitamc utsṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇair yajñe maruttasya mahīpateḥe tad ānayasva kaunteya paryāptaṃ tad bhaviṣyati yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa kathaṃ yajñe maruttasya draviṇaṃ tat samācitamc kasmiṃś ca kāle sa nṛpo babhūva vadatāṃ vara vyāsa uvācaa yadi śuśrūṣase pārtha śṛṇu kāraṃdhamaṃ nṛpamc yasmin kāle mahāvīryaḥ sa rājāsīn mahādhanaḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa śuśrūṣe tasya dharmajña rājarṣeḥ parikīrtanamc dvaipāyana maruttasya kathāṃ prabrūhi me nagha vyāsa uvācaa āsīt kṛtayuge pūrvaṃ manur daṇḍadharaḥ prabhuḥc tasya putro maheṣvāsaḥ prajātir iti viśrutaḥa prajāter abhavat putraḥ kṣupa ity abhiviśrutaḥc kṣupasya putras tv ikṣvākur mahīpālo bhavat prabhuḥa tasya putraśataṃ rājann āsīt paramadhārmikamc tāṃs tu sarvān mahīpālān ikṣvākur akarot prabhuḥa teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhas tu viṃśo bhūt pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatāmc viṃśasya putraḥ kalyāṇo viviṃśo nāma bhārataa viviṃśasya sutā rājan babhūvur daśa pañca cac sarve dhanuṣi vikrāntā brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥa dānadharmaratāḥ santaḥ satataṃ priyavādinaḥc teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ khanīnetraḥ sa tān sarvān apīḍayata khanīnetras tu vikrānto jitvā rājyam akaṇṭakamc nāśaknod rakṣituṃ rājyaṃ nānvarajyanta taṃ prajāḥa tam apāsya ca tad rāṣṭraṃ tasya putraṃ suvarcasamc abhyaṣiñcata rājendra muditaṃ cābhavat tadāa sa pitur vikriyāṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyān nirasanaṃ tathāc niyato vartayām āsa prajāhitacikīrṣayāa brahmaṇyaḥ satyavādī ca śuciḥ śamadamānvitaḥc prajās taṃ cānvarajyanta dharmanityaṃ manasvinama tasya dharmapravṛttasya vyaśīryat kośavāhanamc taṃ kṣīṇakośaṃ sāmantāḥ samantāt paryapīḍayana sa pīḍyamāno bahubhiḥ kṣīṇakośas tv avāhanaḥc ārtim ārchat parāṃ rājā saha bhṛtyaiḥ pureṇa caa na cainaṃ parihartuṃ te śaknuvan parisaṃkṣayec samyagvṛtto hi rājā sa dharmanityo yudhiṣṭhiraa yadā tu paramām ārtiṃ gato sau sapuro nṛpaḥc tataḥ pradadhmau sa karaṃ prādurāsīt tato balama tatas tān ajayat sarvān prātisīmān narādhipānc etasmāt kāraṇād rājan viśrutaḥ sa karaṃdhamaḥa tasya kāraṃdhamaḥ putras tretāyugamukhe bhavatb putras tretāyugamukhe bhavad āvikṣasaṃjñakaḥb kāraṃdhama iti khyāto babhūva jagatīpatiḥc indrād anavaraḥ śrīmān devair api sudurjayaḥa tasya sarve mahīpālā vartante sma vaśe tadāc sa hi samrāḍ abhūt teṣāṃ vṛttena ca balena caa avikṣin nāma dharmātmā śauryeṇendrasamo bhavatc yajñaśīlaḥ karmaratir dhṛtimān saṃyatendriyaḥa tejasādityasadṛśaḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥc bṛhaspatisamo buddhyā himavān iva susthiraḥa karmaṇā manasā vācā damena praśamena cac manāṃsy ārādhayām āsa prajānāṃ sa mahīpatiḥa ya īje hayamedhānāṃ śatena vidhivat prabhuḥc yājayām āsa yaṃ vidvān svayam evāṅgirāḥ prabhuḥa tasya putro ticakrāma pitaraṃ guṇavattayāc marutto nāma dharmajñaś cakravartī mahāyaśāḥa nāgāyutasamaprāṇaḥ sākṣād viṣṇur ivāparaḥc sa yakṣyamāṇo dharmātmā śātakumbhamayāny utae kārayām āsa śubhrāṇi bhājanāni sahasraśaḥa meruṃ parvatam āsādya himavatpārśva uttarec kāñcanaḥ sumahān pādas tatra karma cakāra saḥa tataḥ kuṇḍāni pātrīś ca piṭharāṇy āsanāni cac cakruḥ suvarṇakartāro yeṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyatea tasyaiva ca samīpe sa yajñavāṭo babhūva hac īje tatra sa dharmātmā vidhivat pṛthivīpatiḥe maruttaḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ prajāpālair narādhipaḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa kathaṃvīryaḥ samabhavat sa rājā vadatāṃ varaḥc kathaṃ ca jātarūpeṇa samayujyata sa dvijaa kva ca tat sāṃprataṃ dravyaṃ bhagavann avatiṣṭhatec kathaṃ ca śakyam asmābhis tad avāptuṃ tapodhana vyāsa uvācaa asurāś caiva devāś ca dakṣasyāsan prajāpateḥc apatyaṃ bahulaṃ tāta te spardhanta parasparama tathaivāṅgirasaḥ putrau vratatulyau babhūvatuḥc bṛhaspatir bṛhattejāḥ saṃvartaś ca tapodhanaḥa tāv api spardhinau rājan pṛthag āstāṃ parasparamc bṛhaspatiś ca saṃvartaṃ bādhate sma punaḥ punaḥa sa bādhyamānaḥ satataṃ bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena bhāratac arthān utsṛjya digvāsā vanavāsam arocayata vāsavo py asurān sarvān nirjitya ca nihatya cac indratvaṃ prāpya lokeṣu tato vavre purohitame putram aṅgiraso jyeṣṭhaṃ vipraśreṣṭhaṃ bṛhaspatima yājyas tv aṅgirasaḥ pūrvam āsīd rājā karaṃdhamaḥc vīryeṇāpratimo loke vṛttena ca balena cae śatakratur ivaujasvī dharmātmā saṃśitavrataḥa vāhanaṃ yasya yodhāś ca dravyāṇi vividhāni cab śayanāni ca mukhyāni mahārhāṇi ca sarvaśaḥc dhyānād evābhavad rājan mukhavātena sarvaśaḥa sa guṇaiḥ pārthivān sarvān vaśe cakre narādhipaḥc saṃjīvya kālam iṣṭaṃ ca saśarīro divaṃ gataḥa babhūva tasya putras tu yayātir iva dharmavitc avikṣin nāma śatrukṣit sa vaśe kṛtavān mahīme vikrameṇa guṇaiś caiva pitevāsīt sa pārthivaḥa tasya vāsavatulyo bhūn marutto nāma vīryavānc putras tam anuraktābhūt pṛthivī sāgarāmbarāa spardhate satataṃ sa sma devarājena pārthivaḥc vāsavo pi maruttena spardhate pāṇḍunandanaa śuciḥ sa guṇavān āsīn maruttaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥc yatamāno pi yaṃ śakro na viśeṣayati sma haa so śaknuvan viśeṣāya samāhūya bṛhaspatimc uvācedaṃ vaco devaiḥ sahito harivāhanaḥa bṛhaspate maruttasya mā sma kārṣīḥ kathaṃ canac daivaṃ karmātha vā pitryaṃ kartāsi mama cet priyama ahaṃ hi triṣu lokeṣu surāṇāṃ ca bṛhaspatec indratvaṃ prāptavān eko maruttas tu mahīpatiḥa kathaṃ hy amartyaṃ brahmaṃs tvaṃ yājayitvā surādhipamc yājayer mṛtyusaṃyuktaṃ maruttam aviśaṅkayāa māṃ vā vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te maruttaṃ vā mahīpatimc parityajya maruttaṃ vā yathājoṣaṃ bhajasva māma evam uktaḥ sa kauravya devarājñā bṛhaspatiḥc muhūrtam iva saṃcintya devarājānam abravīta tvaṃ bhūtānām adhipatis tvayi lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥc namucer viśvarūpasya nihantā tvaṃ balasya caa tvam ājahartha devānām eko vīra śriyaṃ parāmc tvaṃ bibharṣi bhuvaṃ dyāṃ ca sadaiva balasūdanaa paurohityaṃ kathaṃ kṛtvā tava devagaṇeśvarac yājayeyam ahaṃ martyaṃ maruttaṃ pākaśāsanaa samāśvasihi deveśa nāhaṃ martyāya karhi citc grahīṣyāmi sruvaṃ yajñe śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mamaa hiraṇyaretaso mbhaḥ syāt parivarteta medinīc bhāsaṃ ca na raviḥ kuryān matsatyaṃ vicaled yadia bṛhaspativacaḥ śrutvā śakro vigatamatsaraḥc praśasyainaṃ viveśātha svam eva bhavanaṃ tadā vyāsa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc bṛhaspateś ca saṃvādaṃ maruttasya ca bhārataa devarājasya samayaṃ kṛtam āṅgirasena hac śrutvā marutto nṛpatir manyum āhārayat tadāa saṃkalpya manasā yajñaṃ karaṃdhamasutātmajaḥc bṛhaspatim upāgamya vāgmī vacanam abravīta bhagavan yan mayā pūrvam abhigamya tapodhanac kṛto bhisaṃdhir yajñāya bhavato vacanād guroa tam ahaṃ yaṣṭum icchāmi saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhṛtāś ca mec yājyo smi bhavataḥ sādho tat prāpnuhi vidhatsva ca bṛhaspatir uvācaa na kāmaye yājayituṃ tvām ahaṃ pṛthivīpatec vṛto smi devarājena pratijñātaṃ ca tasya me marutta uvācaa pitryam asmi tava kṣetraṃ bahu manye ca te bhṛśamc na cāsmy ayājyatāṃ prāpto bhajamānaṃ bhajasva mām bṛhaspatir uvācaa amartyaṃ yājayitvāhaṃ yājayiṣye na mānuṣamc marutta gaccha vā mā vā nivṛtto smy adya yājanāta na tvāṃ yājayitāsmy adya vṛṇu tvaṃ yam ihecchasic upādhyāyaṃ mahābāho yas te yajñaṃ kariṣyati vyāsa uvācaa evam uktas tu nṛpatir marutto vrīḍito bhavatc pratyāgacchac ca saṃvigno dadarśa pathi nāradama devarṣiṇā samāgamya nāradena sa pārthivaḥc vidhivat prāñjalis tasthāv athainaṃ nārado bravīta rājarṣe nātihṛṣṭo si kaccit kṣemaṃ tavānaghac kva gato si kuto vedam aprītisthānam āgatama śrotavyaṃ cen mayā rājan brūhi me pārthivarṣabhac vyapaneṣyāmi te manyuṃ sarvayatnair narādhipaa evam ukto maruttas tu nāradena maharṣiṇāc vipralambham upādhyāyāt sarvam eva nyavedayata gato smy aṅgirasaḥ putraṃ devācāryaṃ bṛhaspatimc yajñārtham ṛtvijaṃ draṣṭuṃ sa ca māṃ nābhyanandataa pratyākhyātaś ca tenāhaṃ jīvituṃ nādya kāmayec parityaktaś ca guruṇā dūṣitaś cāsmi nāradaa evam uktas tu rājñā sa nāradaḥ pratyuvāca hac āvikṣitaṃ mahārāja vācā saṃjīvayann ivaa rājann aṅgirasaḥ putraḥ saṃvarto nāma dhārmikaḥc caṅkramīti diśaḥ sarvā digvāsā mohayan prajāḥa taṃ gaccha yadi yājyaṃ tvāṃ na vāñchati bṛhaspatiḥc prasannas tvāṃ mahārāja saṃvarto yājayiṣyati marutta uvācaa saṃjīvito haṃ bhavatā vākyenānena nāradac paśyeyaṃ kva nu saṃvartaṃ śaṃsa me vadatāṃ varaa kathaṃ ca tasmai varteyaṃ kathaṃ māṃ na parityajetc pratyākhyātaś ca tenāpi nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe nārada uvācaa unmattaveṣaṃ bibhrat sa caṅkramīti yathāsukhamc vārāṇasīṃ tu nagarīm abhīkṣṇam upasevated yatra sākṣān mahādevo dehānte parameśvaraḥd vyācaṣṭe tārakajñānaṃ jantūnām apavargadama tasyā dvāraṃ samāsādya nyasethāḥ kuṇapaṃ kva citc taṃ dṛṣṭvā yo nivarteta sa saṃvarto mahīpatea taṃ pṛṣṭhato nugacchethā yatra gacchet sa vīryavānc tam ekānte samāsādya prāñjaliḥ śaraṇaṃ vrajeḥa pṛcchet tvāṃ yadi kenāhaṃ tavākhyāta iti sma hac brūyās tvaṃ nāradeneti saṃtapta iva śatruhana sa cet tvām anuyuñjīta mamābhigamanepsayāc śaṃsethā vahnim ārūḍhaṃ mām api tvam aśaṅkayā vyāsa uvācaa sa tatheti pratiśrutya pūjayitvā ca nāradamc abhyanujñāya rājarṣir yayau vārāṇasīṃ purīma tatra gatvā yathoktaṃ sa puryā dvāre mahāyaśāḥc kuṇapaṃ sthāpayām āsa nāradasya vacaḥ smarana yaugapadyena vipraś ca sa purīdvāram āviśatc tataḥ sa kuṇapaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā sa nyavartataa sa taṃ nivṛttam ālakṣya prāñjaliḥ pṛṣṭhato nvagātc āvikṣito mahīpālaḥ saṃvartam upaśikṣituma sa enaṃ vijane dṛṣṭvā pāṃsubhiḥ kardamena cac śleṣmaṇā cāpi rājānaṃ ṣṭhīvanaiś ca samākirata sa tathā bādhyamāno pi saṃvartena mahīpatiḥc anvagād eva tam ṛṣiṃ prāñjaliḥ saṃprasādayana tato nivṛtya saṃvartaḥ pariśrānta upāviśatc śītalacchāyam āsādya nyagrodhaṃ bahuśākhinam saṃvarta uvācaa katham asmi tvayā jñātaḥ kena vā kathito smi tec etad ācakṣva me tattvam icchase cet priyaṃ mamaa satyaṃ te bruvataḥ sarve saṃpatsyante manorathāḥc mithyā tu bruvato mūrdhā saptadhā te phaliṣyati marutta uvācaa nāradena bhavān mahyam ākhyāto hy aṭatā pathic guruputro mameti tvaṃ tato me prītir uttamā saṃvarta uvācaa satyam etad bhavān āha sa māṃ jānāti satriṇamc kathayasvaitad ekaṃ me kva nu saṃprati nāradaḥ marutta uvācaa bhavantaṃ kathayitvā tu mama devarṣisattamaḥc tato mām abhyanujñāya praviṣṭo havyavāhanamd yojanīyo ham adhunā bhavatā munisattama vyāsa uvācaa śrutvā tu pārthivasyaitat saṃvartaḥ parayā mudāc etāvad aham apy enaṃ kuryām iti tadābravīta tato maruttam unmatto vācā nirbhartsayann ivac rūkṣayā brāhmaṇo rājan punaḥ punar athābravīta vātapradhānena mayā svacittavaśavartināc evaṃ vikṛtarūpeṇa kathaṃ yājitum icchasia bhrātā mama samarthaś ca vāsavena ca satkṛtaḥc vartate yājane caiva tena karmāṇi kārayaa gṛhaṃ svaṃ caiva yājyāś ca sarvā gṛhyāś ca devatāḥc pūrvajena mamākṣiptaṃ śarīraṃ varjitaṃ tv idama nāhaṃ tenānanujñātas tvām āvikṣita karhi citc yājayeyaṃ kathaṃ cid vai sa hi pūjyatamo mamaa sa tvaṃ bṛhaspatiṃ gaccha tam anujñāpya cāvrajac tato haṃ yājayiṣye tvāṃ yadi yaṣṭum ihecchasi marutta uvācaa bṛhaspatiṃ gataḥ pūrvam ahaṃ saṃvarta tac chṛṇuc na māṃ kāmayate yājyam asau vāsavavāritaḥa amaraṃ yājyam āsādya mām ṛṣe mā sma mānuṣamc yājayethā maruttaṃ tvaṃ martyadharmāṇam āturamd śakreṇa pratiṣiddho haṃ maruttaṃ mā sma yājayeḥd na māṃ rocayate rājyam ayājyaṃ mām amānuṣama spardhate ca mayā vipra sadā vai sa hi pārthivaḥc evam astv iti cāpy ukto bhrātrā te balavṛtrahāa sa mām abhigataṃ premṇā yājyavan na bubhūṣatic devarājam upāśritya tad viddhi munipuṃgavaa so ham icchāmi bhavatā sarvasvenāpi yājitumc kāmaye samatikrāntuṃ vāsavaṃ tvatkṛtair guṇaiḥa na hi me vartate buddhir gantuṃ brahman bṛhaspatimc pratyākhyāto hi tenāsmi tathānapakṛte sati saṃvarta uvācaa cikīrṣasi yathākāmaṃ sarvam etat tvayi dhruvamc yadi sarvān abhiprāyān kartāsi mama pārthivaa yājyamānaṃ mayā hi tvāṃ bṛhaspatipuraṃdarauc dviṣetāṃ samabhikruddhāv etad ekaṃ samarthayaa sthairyam atra kathaṃ te syāt sa tvaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ kuruc kupitas tvāṃ na hīdānīṃ bhasma kuryāṃ sabāndhavam marutta uvācaa yāvat tapet sahasrāṃśus tiṣṭheraṃś cāpi parvatāḥc tāval lokān na labheyaṃ tyajeyaṃ saṃgataṃ yadia mā cāpi śubhabuddhitvaṃ labheyam iha karhi citc samyag jñāne vaiṣaye vā tyajeyaṃ saṃgataṃ yadi saṃvarta uvācaa āvikṣita śubhā buddhir dhīyatāṃ tava karmasuc yājanaṃ hi mamāpy evaṃ vartate tvayi pārthivaa saṃvidhāsye ca te rājann akṣayaṃ dravyam uttamamc yena devān sagandharvāñ śakraṃ cābhibhaviṣyasia na tu me vartate buddhir dhane yājyeṣu vā punaḥc vipriyaṃ tu cikīrṣāmi bhrātuś cendrasya cobhayoḥa gamayiṣyāmi cendreṇa samatām api te dhruvamc priyaṃ ca te kariṣyāmi satyam etad bravīmi te saṃvarta uvācaa girer himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe muñjavān nāma parvataḥc tapyate yatra bhagavāṃs tapo nityam umāpatiḥa vanaspatīnāṃ mūleṣu ṭaṅkeṣu śikhareṣu cac guhāsu śailarājasya yathākāmaṃ yathāsukhama umāsahāyo bhagavān yatra nityaṃ maheśvaraḥc āste śūlī mahātejā nānābhūtagaṇāvṛtaḥa tatra rudrāś ca sādhyāś ca viśve tha vasavas tathāc yamaś ca varuṇaś caiva kuberaś ca sahānugaḥa bhūtāni ca piśācāś ca nāsatyāv aśvināv apic gandharvāpsarasaś caiva yakṣā devarṣayas tathāa ādityā marutaś caiva yātudhānāś ca sarvaśaḥb brahmādayaś ca maruto munayo dhyātmacintakāḥc upāsante mahātmānaṃ bahurūpam umāpatima ramate bhagavāṃs tatra kuberānucaraiḥ sahac vikṛtair vikṛtākāraiḥ krīḍadbhiḥ pṛthivīpatee śriyā jvalan dṛśyate vai bālādityasamadyutiḥa na rūpaṃ dṛśyate tasya saṃsthānaṃ vā kathaṃ canac nirdeṣṭuṃ prāṇibhiḥ kaiś cit prākṛtair māṃsalocanaiḥa noṣṇaṃ na śiśiraṃ tatra na vāyur na ca bhāskaraḥc na jarā kṣutpipāse vā na mṛtyur na bhayaṃ nṛpaa tasya śailasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu jayatāṃ varac dhātavo jātarūpasya raśmayaḥ savitur yathāa rakṣyante te kuberasya sahāyair udyatāyudhaiḥc cikīrṣadbhiḥ priyaṃ rājan kuberasya mahātmanaḥd tatra gatvā tvam anvāsya mahāyogeśvaraṃ śivamd kuru praṇāmaṃ rājarṣe bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥa tasmai bhagavate kṛtvā namaḥ śarvāya vedhaseb ebhis tvaṃ nāmabhir devaṃ sarvavidyādhipaṃ stuhic rudrāya śitikaṇṭhāya surūpāya suvarcasea kapardine karālāya haryakṣṇe varadāya cac tryakṣṇe pūṣṇo dantabhide vāmanāya śivāya caa yāmyāyāvyaktakeśāya sadvṛtte śaṃkarāya cac kṣemyāya harinetrāya sthāṇave puruṣāya caa harikeśāya muṇḍāya kṛśāyottāraṇāya cac bhāskarāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhased bahurūpāya śarvāya priyāya priyavāsasea uṣṇīṣiṇe suvaktrāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣec giriśāya praśāntāya yataye cīravāsasea bilvadaṇḍāya siddhāya sarvadaṇḍadharāya cac mṛgavyādhāya mahate dhanvine tha bhavāya caa varāya saumyavaktrāya paśuhastāya varṣiṇec hiraṇyabāhave rājann ugrāya pataye diśāmd lelihānāya gotrāya siddhamantrāya vṛṣṇayea paśūnāṃ pataye caiva bhūtānāṃ pataye tathāc vṛṣāya mātṛbhaktāya senānye madhyamāya caa sruvahastāya pataye dhanvine bhārgavāya cac ajāya kṛṣṇanetrāya virūpākṣāya caiva haa tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāya tīkṣṇāya vaiśvānaramukhāya cac mahādyutaye naṅgāya sarvāṅgāya prajāvated vilohitāya dīptāya dīptākṣāya mahaujasea tathā śukrādhipataye pṛthave kṛttivāsasec kapālamāline nityaṃ suvarṇamukuṭāya caa mahādevāya kṛṣṇāya tryambakāyānaghāya cac krodhanāya nṛśaṃsāya mṛdave bāhuśālinea daṇḍine taptatapase tathaiva krūrakarmaṇec sahasraśirase caiva sahasracaraṇāya cae namaḥ svadhāsvarūpāya bahurūpāya daṃṣṭriṇea pinākinaṃ mahādevaṃ mahāyoginam avyayamc triśūlapāṇiṃ varadaṃ tryambakaṃ bhuvaneśvarama tripuraghnaṃ trinayanaṃ trilokeśaṃ mahaujasamc prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ dharaṇīdharama īśānaṃ śaṃkaraṃ sarvaṃ śivaṃ viśveśvaraṃ bhavamc umāpatiṃ paśupatiṃ viśvarūpaṃ maheśvarama virūpākṣaṃ daśabhujaṃ tiṣyagovṛṣabhadhvajamb anantaṃ śāśvataṃ devaṃ triśṛṅgaṃ vṛṣabhekṣaṇamc ugraṃ sthāṇuṃ śivaṃ ghoraṃ śarvaṃ gaurīśam īśvarama śitikaṇṭham ajaṃ śukraṃ pṛthuṃ pṛthuharaṃ haramc viśvarūpaṃ virūpākṣaṃ bahurūpam umāpatima praṇamya śirasā devam anaṅgāṅgaharaṃ haramc śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāhi mahādevaṃ caturmukhamd virocamānaṃ vapuṣā divyābharaṇabhūṣitamd anādyantam ajaṃ śaṃbhuṃ sarvavyāpinam īśvaramd nistraiguṇyaṃ nirudvegaṃ nirmalaṃ nidhim ojasāmd praṇamya prāñjaliḥ śarvaṃ prayāmi śaraṇaṃ haramd sāmānyaṃ niścalaṃ nityam akāraṇam alepanamd adhyātmavedam āsādya prayāmi śaraṇaṃ muhuḥd yasya nityaṃ viduḥ sthānaṃ mokṣam adhyātmacintakāḥd yoginas tattvamārgasthāḥ kaivalyaṃ padam akṣaramd yaṃ viduḥ saṅganirmuktāḥ sāmānyaṃ samadarśinaḥd taṃ prapadye jagadyonim ayoniṃ nirguṇātmakamd asṛjad yas tu bhūtādīn sapta lokān sanātanānd sthitaḥ satyopari sthāṇus taṃ prapadye sanātanamd bhaktānāṃ sulabhaṃ taṃ hi durlabhaṃ dūrapātināmd adūrastham ajaṃ devaṃ prakṛteḥ parataḥ sthitamd namāmi sarvalokasthaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ śivama evaṃ kṛtvā namas tasmai mahādevāya raṃhasec mahātmane kṣitipate tat suvarṇam avāpsyasid labhante gāṇapatyaṃ ca tadekāgrā hi mānavāḥd kiṃ punaḥ svarṇabhāṇḍāni tasmāt tvaṃ gaccha mā ciramd mahattaraṃ hi te lābhaṃ hastyaśvoṣṭrādibhiḥ sahae suvarṇam āhariṣyantas tatra gacchantu te narāḥ vyāsa uvācaa ity uktaḥ sa vacas tasya cakre kāraṃdhamātmajaḥb gaṅgādharaṃ namaskṛtya labdhavān dhanam uttamamb kubera iva tat prāpya mahādevaprasādataḥc tato timānuṣaṃ sarvaṃ cakre yajñasya saṃvidhime sauvarṇāni ca bhāṇḍāni saṃcakrus tatra śilpinaḥf śālāś ca sarvasaṃbhārān kratoḥ saṃvartaśāsanāta bṛhaspatis tu tāṃ śrutvā maruttasya mahīpateḥc samṛddhim ati devebhyaḥ saṃtāpam akarod bhṛśama sa tapyamāno vaivarṇyaṃ kṛśatvaṃ cāgamat paramc bhaviṣyati hi me śatruḥ saṃvarto vasumān itia taṃ śrutvā bhṛśasaṃtaptaṃ devarājo bṛhaspatimc abhigamyāmaravṛtaḥ provācedaṃ vacas tadā indra uvācaa kaccit sukhaṃ svapiṣi tvaṃ bṛhaspatekaccin manojñāḥ paricārakās tec kaccid devānāṃ sukhakāmo si viprakaccid devās tvāṃ paripālayanti bṛhaspatir uvācaa sukhaṃ śaye haṃ śayane mahendratathā manojñāḥ paricārakā mec tathā devānāṃ sukhakāmo smi śakradevāś ca māṃ subhṛśaṃ pālayanti indra uvācaa kuto duḥkhaṃ mānasaṃ dehajaṃ vāpāṇḍur vivarṇaś ca kutas tvam adyac ācakṣva me tad dvija yāvad etānnihanmi sarvāṃs tava duḥkhakartṝn bṛhaspatir uvācaa maruttam āhur maghavan yakṣyamāṇaṃmahāyajñenottamadakṣiṇenac taṃ saṃvarto yājayiteti me śrutaṃtad icchāmi na sa taṃ yājayeta indra uvācaa sarvān kāmān anujāto si viprayas tvaṃ devānāṃ mantrayase purodhāḥc ubhau ca te janmamṛtyū vyatītaukiṃ saṃvartas tava kartādya vipra bṛhaspatir uvācaa devaiḥ saha tvam asurān saṃpraṇudyajighāṃsase dyāpy uta sānubandhānc yaṃ yaṃ samṛddhaṃ paśyasi tatra tatraduḥkhaṃ sapatneṣu samṛddhabhāvaḥa ato smi devendra vivarṇarūpaḥsapatno me vardhate tan niśamyac sarvopāyair maghavan saṃniyacchasaṃvartaṃ vā pārthivaṃ vā maruttam indra uvācaa ehi gaccha prahito jātavedobṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec ayaṃ vai tvā yājayitā bṛhaspatistathāmaraṃ caiva kariṣyatīti agnir uvācaa ayaṃ gacchāmi tava śakrādya dūtobṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec vācaṃ satyāṃ puruhūtasya kartuṃbṛhaspateś cāpacitiṃ cikīrṣuḥ vyāsa uvācaa tataḥ prāyād dhūmaketur mahātmāvanaspatīn vīrudhaś cāvamṛdnanc kāmād dhimānte parivartamānaḥkāṣṭhātigo mātariśveva nardan marutta uvācaa āścaryam adya paśyāmi rūpiṇaṃ vahnim āgatamc āsanaṃ salilaṃ pādyaṃ gāṃ copānaya vai mune agnir uvācaa āsanaṃ salilaṃ pādyaṃ pratinandāmi te naghac indreṇa tu samādiṣṭaṃ viddhi māṃ dūtam āgatam marutta uvācaa kaccic chrīmān devarājaḥ sukhī cakaccic cāsmān prīyate dhūmaketoc kaccid devāś cāsya vaśe yathāvattad brūhi tvaṃ mama kārtsnyena deva agnir uvācaa śakro bhṛśaṃ susukhī pārthivendraprītiṃ cecchaty ajarāṃ vai tvayā saḥc devāś ca sarve vaśagās tasya rājansaṃdeśaṃ tvaṃ śṛṇu me devarājñaḥa yadarthaṃ māṃ prāhiṇot tvatsakāśaṃbṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec ayaṃ gurur yājayitā nṛpa tvāṃmartyaṃ santam amaraṃ tvāṃ karotu marutta uvācaa saṃvarto yaṃ yājayitā dvijo mebṛhaspater añjalir eṣa tasyac nāsau devaṃ yājayitvā mahendraṃmartyaṃ santaṃ yājayann adya śobhet agnir uvācaa ye vai lokā devaloke mahāntaḥsaṃprāpsyase tān devarājaprasādātc tvāṃ ced asau yājayed vai bṛhaspatirnūnaṃ svargaṃ tvaṃ jayeḥ kīrtiyuktaḥa tathā lokā mānuṣā ye ca divyāḥprajāpateś cāpi ye vai mahāntaḥc te te jitā devarājyaṃ ca kṛtsnaṃbṛhaspatiś ced yājayet tvāṃ narendra saṃvarta uvācaa māsmān evaṃ tvaṃ punar āgāḥ kathaṃ cidbṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec mā tvāṃ dhakṣye cakṣuṣā dāruṇenasaṃkruddho haṃ pāvaka tan nibodha vyāsa uvācaa tato devān agamad dhūmaketurdāhād bhīto vyathito śvatthaparṇavatc taṃ vai dṛṣṭvā prāha śakro mahātmābṛhaspateḥ saṃnidhau havyavāhama yat tvaṃ gataḥ prahito jātavedobṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec tat kiṃ prāha sa nṛpo yakṣyamāṇaḥkaccid vacaḥ pratigṛhṇāti tac ca agnir uvācaa na te vācaṃ rocayate maruttobṛhaspater añjaliṃ prāhiṇot saḥc saṃvarto māṃ yājayitety abhīkṣṇaṃpunaḥ punaḥ sa mayā procyamānaḥa uvācedaṃ mānuṣā ye ca divyāḥprajāpater ye ca lokā mahāntaḥc tāṃś cel labheyaṃ saṃvidaṃ tena kṛtvātathāpi neccheyam iti pratītaḥ indra uvācaa punar bhavān pārthivaṃ taṃ sametyavākyaṃ madīyaṃ prāpaya svārthayuktamc punar yady ukto na kariṣyate vacastato vajraṃ saṃprahartāsmi tasmai agnir uvācaa gandharvarāḍ yātv ayaṃ tatra dūtobibhemy ahaṃ vāsava tatra gantumc saṃrabdho mām abravīt tīkṣṇaroṣaḥsaṃvarto vākyaṃ caritabrahmacaryaḥa yady āgaccheḥ punar evaṃ kathaṃ cidbṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ maruttec daheyaṃ tvāṃ cakṣuṣā dāruṇenasaṃkruddha ity etad avaihi śakra indra uvācaa tvam evānyān dahase jātavedona hi tvad anyo vidyate bhasmakartāc tvatsaṃsparśāt sarvaloko bibhetyaśraddheyaṃ vadase havyavāha agnir uvācaa divaṃ devendra pṛthivīṃ caiva sarvāṃsaṃveṣṭayes tvaṃ svabalenaiva śakrac evaṃvidhasyeha satas tavāsaukathaṃ vṛtras tridivaṃ prāg jahāra indra uvācaa na caṇḍikā jaṅgamā no kareṇurna vārisomaṃ prapibāmi vahnec na durbale vai visṛjāmi vajraṃko me sukhāya praharen manuṣyaḥa pravrājayeyaṃ kālakeyān pṛthivyāmapākarṣaṃ dānavān antarikṣātc divaḥ prahrādam avasānam ānayaṃko me sukhāya prahareta martyaḥ agnir uvācaa yatra śaryātiṃ cyavano yājayiṣyansahāśvibhyāṃ somam agṛhṇad ekaḥc taṃ tvaṃ kruddhaḥ pratyaṣedhīḥ purastāccharyātiyajñaṃ smara taṃ mahendraa vajraṃ gṛhītvā ca puraṃdara tvaṃsaṃprāhārṣīś cyavanasyātighoramc sa te vipraḥ saha vajreṇa bāhumapāgṛhṇāt tapasā jātamanyuḥa tato roṣāt sarvato ghorarūpaṃsapatnaṃ te janayām āsa bhūyaḥc madaṃ nāmāsuraṃ viśvarūpaṃyaṃ tvaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakṣuṣī saṃnyamīlaḥa hanur ekā jagatīsthā tathaikādivaṃ gatā mahato dānavasyac sahasraṃ dantānāṃ śatayojanānāṃsutīkṣṇānāṃ ghorarūpaṃ babhūvaa vṛttāḥ sthūlā rajatastambhavarṇādaṃṣṭrāś catasro dve śate yojanānāmc sa tvāṃ dantān vidaśann abhyadhāvajjighāṃsayā śūlam udyamya ghorama apaśyas tvaṃ taṃ tadā ghorarūpaṃsarve tv anye dadṛśur darśanīyamc yasmād bhītaḥ prāñjalis tvaṃ maharṣimāgacchethāḥ śaraṇaṃ dānavaghnaa kṣatrād evaṃ brahmabalaṃ garīyona brahmataḥ kiṃ cid anyad garīyaḥc so haṃ jānan brahmatejo yathāvanna saṃvartaṃ gantum icchāmi śakra indra uvācaa evam etad brahmabalaṃ garīyona brahmataḥ kiṃ cid anyad garīyaḥc āvikṣitasya tu balaṃ na mṛṣyevajram asmai prahariṣyāmi ghorama dhṛtarāṣṭra prahito gaccha maruttaṃsaṃvartena sahitaṃ taṃ vadasvac bṛhaspatiṃ tvam upaśikṣasva rājanvajraṃ vā te prahariṣyāmi ghoram vyāsa uvācaa tato gatvā dhṛtarāṣṭro narendraṃprovācedaṃ vacanaṃ vāsavasyac gandharvaṃ māṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ nibodhatvām āgataṃ vaktukāmaṃ narendraa aindraṃ vākyaṃ śṛṇu me rājasiṃhayat prāha lokādhipatir mahātmāc bṛhaspatiṃ yājakaṃ tvaṃ vṛṇīṣvavajraṃ vā te prahariṣyāmi ghorame vacaś ced etan na kariṣyase meprāhaitad etāvad acintyakarmāf bṛhaspatiṃ yājayituṃ na cecchedf vajraṃ tasmai prahariṣyāmi ghoram marutta uvācaa tvaṃ caivaitad vettha puraṃdaraś caviśvedevā vasavaś cāśvinau cac mitradrohe niṣkṛtir vai yathaivanāstīti lokeṣu sadaiva vādaḥa bṛhaspatir yājayitā mahendraṃdevaśreṣṭhaṃ vajrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhamc saṃvarto māṃ yājayitādya rājanna te vākyaṃ tasya vā rocayāmi gandharva uvācaa ghoro nādaḥ śrūyate vāsavasyanabhastale garjato rājasiṃhac vyaktaṃ vajraṃ mokṣyate te mahendraḥkṣemaṃ rājaṃś cintyatām eṣa kālaḥ vyāsa uvācaa ity evam ukto dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājāśrutvā nādaṃ nadato vāsavasyac taponityaṃ dharmavidāṃ variṣṭhaṃsaṃvartaṃ taṃ jñāpayām āsa kāryam marutta uvācaa imam aśmānaṃ plavamānam ārādadhvā dūraṃ tena na dṛśyate dyac prapadye haṃ śarma viprendra tvattaḥprayaccha tasmād abhayaṃ vipramukhyaa ayam āyāti vai vajrī diśo vidyotayan daśac amānuṣeṇa ghoreṇa sadasyās trāsitā hi naḥ saṃvarta uvācaa bhayaṃ śakrād vyetu te rājasiṃhapraṇotsye haṃ bhayam etat sughoramc saṃstambhinyā vidyayā kṣipram evamā bhais tvam asmād bhava cāpi pratītaḥa ahaṃ saṃstambhayiṣyāmi mā bhais tvaṃ śakrato nṛpac sarveṣām eva devānāṃ kṣapitāny āyudhāni mea diśo vajraṃ vrajatāṃ vāyur etuvarṣaṃ bhūtvā nipatatu kānaneṣuc āpaḥ plavantv antarikṣe vṛthā casaudāminī dṛśyatāṃ mā bibhas tvama atho vahnis trātu vā sarvatas tekāmaṃ varṣaṃ varṣatu vāsavo vāc vajraṃ tathā sthāpayatāṃ ca vāyurmahāghoraṃ plavamānaṃ jalaughaiḥ marutta uvācaa ghoraḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate vai mahāsvanovajrasyaiṣa sahito mārutenac ātmā hi me pravyathate muhur muhurna me svāsthyaṃ jāyate cādya vipra saṃvarta uvācaa vajrād ugrād vyetu bhayaṃ tavādyavāto bhūtvā hanmi narendra vajramc bhayaṃ tyaktvā varam anyaṃ vṛṇīṣvakaṃ te kāmaṃ tapasā sādhayāmi marutta uvācaa indraḥ sākṣāt sahasābhyetu viprahavir yajñe pratigṛhṇātu caivac svaṃ svaṃ dhiṣṇyaṃ caiva juṣantu devāḥsutaṃ somaṃ pratigṛhṇantu caiva saṃvarta uvācaa ayam indro haribhir āyāti rājandevaiḥ sarvaiḥ sahitaḥ somapīthīc mantrāhūto yajñam imaṃ mayādyapaśyasvainaṃ mantravisrastakāyam vyāsa uvācaa tato devaiḥ sahito devarājorathe yuktvā tān harīn vājimukhyānc āyād yajñam adhi rājñaḥ pipāsurāvikṣitasyāprameyasya somama tam āyāntaṃ sahitaṃ devasaṃghaiḥpratyudyayau sapurodhā maruttaḥc cakre pūjāṃ devarājāya cāgryāṃyathāśāstraṃ vidhivat prīyamāṇaḥ saṃvarta uvācaa svāgataṃ te puruhūteha vidvanyajño dyāyaṃ saṃnihite tvayīndrac śośubhyate balavṛtraghna bhūyaḥpibasva somaṃ sutam udyataṃ mayā marutta uvācaa śivena māṃ paśya namaś ca te stuprāpto yajñaḥ saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mec ayaṃ yajñaṃ kurute me surendrabṛhaspater avaro janmanā yaḥ indra uvācaa jānāmi te gurum enaṃ tapodhanaṃbṛhaspater anujaṃ tigmatejasamc yasyāhvānād āgato haṃ narendraprītir me dya tvayi manuḥ pranaṣṭaḥ saṃvarta uvācaa yadi prītas tvam asi vai devarājatasmāt svayaṃ śādhi yajñe vidhānamc svayaṃ sarvān kuru mārgān surendrajānātv ayaṃ sarvalokaś ca deva vyāsa uvācaa evam uktas tv āṅgirasena śakraḥsamādideśa svayam eva devānc sabhāḥ kriyantām āvasathāś ca mukhyāḥsahasraśaś citrabhaumāḥ samṛddhāḥa kḷptasthūṇāḥ kurutārohaṇānigandharvāṇām apsarasāṃ ca śīghramc yeṣu nṛtyerann apsarasaḥ sahasraśaḥsvargoddeśaḥ kriyatāṃ yajñavāṭaḥa ity uktās te cakrur āśu pratītādivaukasaḥ śakravākyān narendrac tato vākyaṃ prāha rājānam indraḥprīto rājan pūjayāno maruttama eṣa tvayāham iha rājan sametyaye cāpy anye tava pūrve narendrāḥc sarvāś cānyā devatāḥ prīyamāṇāhavis tubhyaṃ pratigṛhṇantu rājana āgneyaṃ vai lohitam ālabhantāṃvaiśvadevaṃ bahurūpaṃ virājanc nīlaṃ cokṣāṇaṃ medhyam abhyālabhantāṃcalac chiśnaṃ matpradiṣṭaṃ dvijendrāḥa tato yajño vavṛdhe tasya rājñoyatra devāḥ svayam annāni jahruḥc yasmiñ śakro brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjyamānaḥsadasyo bhūd dharimān devarājaḥa tataḥ saṃvartaś cityagato mahātmāyathā vahniḥ prajvalito dvitīyaḥc havīṃṣy uccair āhvayan devasaṃghāñjuhāvāgnau mantravat supratītaḥa tataḥ pītvā balabhit somam agryaṃye cāpy anye somapā vai divaukasaḥc sarve nujñātāḥ prayayuḥ pārthivenayathājoṣaṃ tarpitāḥ prītimantaḥa tato rājā jātarūpasya rāśīnpade pade kārayām āsa hṛṣṭaḥc dvijātibhyo visṛjan bhūri vittaṃrarāja vitteśa ivārihantāa tato vittaṃ vividhaṃ saṃnidhāyayathotsāhaṃ kārayitvā ca kośamc anujñāto guruṇā saṃnivṛtyaśaśāsa gām akhilāṃ sāgarāntāma evaṃguṇaḥ saṃbabhūveha rājāyasya kratau tat suvarṇaṃ prabhūtamc tat tvaṃ samādāya narendra vittaṃyajasva devāṃs tarpayāno vidhānaiḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tato rājā pāṇḍavo hṛṣṭarūpaḥśrutvā vākyaṃ satyavatyāḥ sutasyac manaś cakre tena vittena yaṣṭuṃtato mātyair mantrayām āsa bhūyaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity ukte nṛpatau tasmin vyāsenādbhutakarmaṇāc vāsudevo mahātejās tato vacanam ādadea taṃ nṛpaṃ dīnamanasaṃ nihatajñātibāndhavamc upaplutam ivādityaṃ sadhūmam iva pāvakama nirviṇṇamanasaṃ pārthaṃ jñātvā vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥc āśvāsayan dharmasutaṃ pravaktum upacakrame vāsudeva uvācaa sarvaṃ jihmaṃ mṛtyupadam ārjavaṃ brahmaṇaḥ padamc etāvāñ jñānaviṣayaḥ kiṃ pralāpaḥ kariṣyatia naiva te niṣṭhitaṃ karma naiva te śatravo jitāḥc kathaṃ śatruṃ śarīrastham ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyasea atra te vartayiṣyāmi yathādharmaṃ yathāśrutamc indrasya saha vṛtreṇa yathā yuddham avartataa vṛtreṇa pṛthivī vyāptā purā kila narādhipac dṛṣṭvā sa pṛthivīṃ vyāptāṃ gandhasya viṣaye hṛtee dharāharaṇadurgandho viṣayaḥ samapadyataa śatakratuś cukopātha gandhasya viṣaye hṛtec vṛtrasya sa tataḥ kruddho vajraṃ ghoram avāsṛjata sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa pṛthivyāṃ bhūritejasāc viveśa sahasaivāpo jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥa vyāptāsv athāpsu vṛtreṇa rase ca viṣaye hṛtec śatakratur abhikruddhas tāsu vajram avāsṛjata sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa salile bhūritejasāc viveśa sahasā jyotir jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥa vyāpte jyotiṣi vṛtreṇa rūpe tha viṣaye hṛtec śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjata sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa subhṛśaṃ bhūritejasāc viveśa sahasā vāyuṃ jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥa vyāpte vāyau tu vṛtreṇa sparśe tha viṣaye hṛtec śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjata sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa tasminn amitatejasāc ākāśam abhidudrāva jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥa ākāśe vṛtrabhūte ca śabde ca viṣaye hṛtec śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjata sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa tasminn amitatejasāc viveśa sahasā śakraṃ jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥa tasya vṛtragṛhītasya mohaḥ samabhavan mahānc rathaṃtareṇa taṃ tāta vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyabodhayata tato vṛtraṃ śarīrasthaṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabhac śatakratur adṛśyena vajreṇetīha naḥ śrutama idaṃ dharmarahasyaṃ ca śakreṇoktaṃ maharṣiṣuc ṛṣibhiś ca mama proktaṃ tan nibodha narādhipa vāsudeva uvācaa dvividho jāyate vyādhiḥ śārīro mānasas tathāc parasparaṃ tayor janma nirdvaṃdvaṃ nopalabhyatea śarīre jāyate vyādhiḥ śārīro nātra saṃśayaḥc mānaso jāyate vyādhir manasy eveti niścayaḥa śītoṣṇe caiva vāyuś ca guṇā rājañ śarīrajāḥc teṣāṃ guṇānāṃ sāmyaṃ cet tad āhuḥ svasthalakṣaṇame uṣṇena bādhyate śītaṃ śītenoṣṇaṃ ca bādhyatef ubhābhyāṃ badhyate vāyur vidhānam idam ucyatea sattvaṃ rajas tamaś ceti trayas tv ātmaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥc teṣāṃ guṇānāṃ sāmyaṃ cet tad āhuḥ svasthalakṣaṇame teṣām anyatamotseke vidhānam upadiśyatea harṣeṇa bādhyate śoko harṣaḥ śokena bādhyateb ubhābhyāṃ vadhyate moho vidhānam idam ucyatec kaś cid duḥkhe vartamānaḥ sukhasya smartum icchatie kaś cit sukhe vartamāno duḥkhasya smartum icchatia sa tvaṃ na duḥkhī duḥkhasya na sukhī susukhasya vāc smartum icchasi kaunteya diṣṭaṃ hi balavattarama atha vā te svabhāvo yaṃ yena pārthāvakṛṣyasec dṛṣṭvā sabhāgatāṃ kṛṣṇām ekavastrāṃ rajasvalāme miṣatāṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ na tat saṃsmartum icchasia pravrājanaṃ ca nagarād ajinaiś ca vivāsanamc mahāraṇyanivāsaś ca na tasya smartum icchasia jaṭāsurāt parikleśaś citrasenena cāhavaḥc saindhavāc ca parikleśo na tasya smartum icchasia punar ajñātacaryāyāṃ kīcakena padā vadhaḥc yājñasenyās tadā pārtha na tasya smartum icchasia yac ca te droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ yuddham āsīd ariṃdamac manasaikena yoddhavyaṃ tat te yuddham upasthitame tasmād abhyupagantavyaṃ yuddhāya bharatarṣabhaa param avyaktarūpasya paraṃ muktvā svakarmabhiḥc yatra naiva śaraiḥ kāryaṃ na bhṛtyair na ca bandhubhiḥe ātmanaikena yoddhavyaṃ tat te yuddham upasthitama tasminn anirjite yuddhe kām avasthāṃ gamiṣyasic etaj jñātvā tu kaunteya kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasia etāṃ buddhiṃ viniścitya bhūtānām āgatiṃ gatimc pitṛpaitāmahe vṛtte śādhi rājyaṃ yathocitam vāsudeva uvācaa na bāhyaṃ dravyam utsṛjya siddhir bhavati bhāratac śārīraṃ dravyam utsṛjya siddhir bhavati vā na vāa bāhyadravyavimuktasya śārīreṣu ca gṛdhyataḥc yo dharmo yat sukhaṃ caiva dviṣatām astu tat tathāa dvyakṣaras tu bhaven mṛtyus tryakṣaraṃ brahma śāśvatamc mameti dvyakṣaro mṛtyur na mameti ca śāśvatama brahma mṛtyuś ca tau rājann ātmany eva vyavasthitauc adṛśyamānau bhūtāni yodhayetām asaṃśayama avināśo sya sattvasya niyato yadi bhāratac bhittvā śarīraṃ bhūtānām ahiṃsāṃ pratipadyatea labdhvāpi pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sahasthāvarajaṅgamāmc mamatvaṃ yasya naiva syāt kiṃ tayā sa kariṣyatia atha vā vasataḥ pārtha vane vanyena jīvataḥc mamatā yasya dravyeṣu mṛtyor āsye sa vartatea bāhyāntarāṇāṃ śatrūṇāṃ svabhāvaṃ paśya bhāratac yan na paśyati tad bhūtaṃ mucyate sa mahābhayāta kāmātmānaṃ na praśaṃsanti lokena cākāmāt kā cid asti pravṛttiḥb sarve kāmā manaso ṅgāt prasūtāb yān paṇḍitaḥ saṃharate vicintyab bhūyo bhūyo janmano bhyāsayogādb yogī yogaṃ sāramārgaṃ vicintyac dānaṃ hi vedādhyayanaṃ tapaś cakāmena karmāṇi ca vaidikānia vrataṃ yajñān niyamān dhyānayogānkāmena yo nārabhate viditvāc yad yad dhy ayaṃ kāmayate sa dharmona yo dharmo niyamas tasya mūlama atra gāthāḥ kāmagītāḥ kīrtayanti purāvidaḥc śṛṇu saṃkīrtyamānās tā nikhilena yudhiṣṭhiraa nāhaṃ śakyo nupāyena hantuṃ bhūtena kena citc yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ jñātvā praharaṇe balame tasya tasmin praharaṇe punaḥ prādurbhavāmy ahama yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥc jaṅgameṣv iva karmātmā punaḥ prādurbhavāmy ahama yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ vedair vedāntasādhanaiḥc sthāvareṣv iva śāntātmā tasya prādurbhavāmy ahama yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ dhṛtyā satyaparākramaḥc bhāvo bhavāmi tasyāhaṃ sa ca māṃ nāvabudhyatea yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ tapasā saṃśitavrataḥc tatas tapasi tasyātha punaḥ prādurbhavāmy ahama yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ mokṣam āsthāya paṇḍitaḥc tasya mokṣaratisthasya nṛtyāmi ca hasāmi cae avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānām aham ekaḥ sanātanaḥa tasmāt tvam api taṃ kāmaṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥc dharmaṃ kuru mahārāja tatra te sa bhaviṣyatia yajasva vājimedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatāc anyaiś ca vividhair yajñaiḥ samṛddhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥa mā te vyathāstu nihatān bandhūn vīkṣya punaḥ punaḥc na śakyās te punar draṣṭuṃ ye hatāsmin raṇājirea sa tvam iṣṭvā mahāyajñaiḥ samṛddhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥc loke kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya gatim agryāṃ gamiṣyasi vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evaṃ bahuvidhair vākyair munibhis tais tapodhanaiḥc samāśvasyata rājarṣir hatabandhur yudhiṣṭhiraḥa so nunīto bhagavatā viṣṭaraśravasā svayamc dvaipāyanena kṛṣṇena devasthānena cābhibhūḥa nāradenātha bhīmena nakulena ca pārthivaḥc kṛṣṇayā sahadevena vijayena ca dhīmatāa anyaiś ca puruṣavyāghrair brāhmaṇaiḥ śāstradṛṣṭibhiḥc vyajahāc chokajaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṃtāpaṃ caiva mānasama arcayām āsa devāṃś ca brāhmaṇāṃś ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥc kṛtvātha pretakāryāṇi bandhūnāṃ sa punar nṛpaḥe anvaśāsata dharmātmā pṛthivīṃ sāgarāmbarāma praśāntacetāḥ kauravyaḥ svarājyaṃ prāpya kevalamc vyāsaṃ ca nāradaṃ caiva tāṃś cānyān abravīn nṛpaḥa āśvāsito haṃ prāg vṛddhair bhavadbhir munipuṃgavaiḥc na sūkṣmam api me kiṃ cid vyalīkam iha vidyatea arthaś ca sumahān prāpto yena yakṣyāmi devatāḥc puraskṛtyeha bhavataḥ samāneṣyāmahe makhama himavantaṃ tvayā guptā gamiṣyāmaḥ pitāmahab tathā vidhatsva viprarṣe tvayyāyattaḥ sa me kratuḥc bahvāścaryo hi deśaḥ sa śrūyate dvijasattamaa tathā bhagavatā citraṃ kalyāṇaṃ bahu bhāṣitamc devarṣiṇā nāradena devasthānena caiva haa nābhāgadheyaḥ puruṣaḥ kaś cid evaṃvidhān gurūnc labhate vyasanaṃ prāpya suhṛdaḥ sādhusaṃmatāna evam uktās tu te rājñā sarva eva maharṣayaḥc abhyanujñāpya rājānaṃ tathobhau kṛṣṇaphalgunaue paśyatām eva sarveṣāṃ tatraivādarśanaṃ yayuḥa tato dharmasuto rājā tatraivopāviśat prabhuḥc evaṃ nātimahān kālaḥ sa teṣām abhyavartataa kurvatāṃ śaucakarmāṇi bhīṣmasya nidhane tadāc mahādānāni viprebhyo dadatām aurdhvadaihikama bhīṣmakarṇapurogāṇāṃ kurūṇāṃ kurunandanac sahito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa pradadāv aurdhvadaihikama tato dattvā bahu dhanaṃ viprebhyaḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥc dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya viveśa gajasāhvayama sa samāśvāsya pitaraṃ prajñācakṣuṣam īśvaramc anvaśād vai sa dharmātmā pṛthivīṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahad yathā manur mahārāja rāmo dāśarathir yathād tathā bharatasiṃho pi pālayām āsa medinīmd nādharmyam abhavat tatra sarvo dharmarucir janaḥd babhūva naraśārdūla yathā kṛtayugaṃ yugamd kalim āsannam āviṣṭaṃ nivārya nṛpanandanaḥd bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito dhīmān babhau dharmabaloddhṛtaḥd vavarṣa bhagavān devaḥ kāle deśe yathepsitamd nirāmayaṃ jagad abhūt kṣutpipāse na kiṃ canad ādhir nāsti manuṣyāṇāṃ vyasane nābhavan matiḥd brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇās te svadharmottarāḥ śivāḥd dharmaḥ satyapradhānaś ca satyaṃ sadviṣayānvitamd dharmāsanasthaḥ sadbhiḥ sa strībālāturavṛddhakānd varṇakramāt pūrvakṛtān nākālo rakṣaṇodyataḥd suvṛttivṛttidānādyair yajñārthair dāpitair apid āmuṣmikaṃ bhayaṃ nāsti aihikaṃ kṛtam eva tud svargalokopamo lokas tadā tasmin praśāsatid babhūva sukham evātra tad viśiṣṭataraṃ paramd nāryaḥ pativratāḥ sarvā rūpavatyaḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥd yathoktavṛttāḥ svaguṇair babhūvuḥ prītihetavaḥd pumāṃsaḥ puṇyaśīlāḍhyāḥ svaṃ svaṃ dharmam anuvratāḥd sukhinaḥ sūkṣmam apy eno nākurvanta kadā canad sarve narāś ca nāryaś ca satataṃ priyavādinaḥd ajihmamanasaḥ śuklā babhūvuḥ śramavarjitāḥd bhūṣitāḥ kuṇḍalair hāraiḥ kaṭakaiḥ kaṭisūtrakaiḥd suvāsasaḥ sugandhāḍhyāḥ prāyaśaḥ pṛthivītaled sarve brahmavidaḥ śāntāḥ sarvatra pariniṣṭhitāḥd valīpalitahīnās tu sukhino dīrghadarśinaḥd icchā na jāyate nyatra varṇeṣu ca na saṃkaraḥd manuṣyāṇāṃ mahārāja maryādāsu vyavasthitāḥd tasmiñ śāsati rājendra mṛgavyālasarīsṛpāḥd anyonyam api cānyeṣu na bādhante vayāṃsi cad gāvaś ca guṇabhūyiṣṭhāḥ suvāladhimukhodarāḥd apīḍitāḥ karṣaṇādyair hṛtavyādhitavatsarāḥd avadhyakālā manujāḥ puruṣārtheṣu ca kramātd viṣayeṣv aniṣiddheṣu vedaśāstreṣu codyatāḥd suvṛttā vṛṣabhāḥ puṣṭā bhārasāhāḥ sukhodayāḥd atīva madhuraḥ śabdaḥ sparśaś cātisukho rasaḥd rūpaṃ dṛṣṭikṣamaṃ ramyaṃ manojñaṃ gandham udbabhaud dharmārthakāmasaṃyuktaṃ mokṣābhyudayasādhanamd prahlādajananaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃbabhūvātha mānasamd sthāvarā bahupuṣpāḍhyāḥ phalacchāyāvahās tathād susparśā viṣahīnāś ca supatratvakprarohiṇaḥd manonukūlāḥ sarveṣāṃ ceṣṭā bhūtvāpavarjitāḥd tathāvidho pi rājarṣis tad vṛttam abhavad bhuvid sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ pāṇḍavā dharmacāriṇaḥd jyeṣṭhānuvartinaḥ sarve babhūvuḥ priyadarśanāḥd siṃhoraskā jitakrodhās tejobalasamanvitāḥd ājānubāhavaḥ sarve dānaśīlā jitendriyāḥd teṣu śāsatsu pṛthivīm ṛtavaḥ svaguṇair babhuḥd sukhodayāya vartante grahās tārāgaṇaiḥ sahad mahī sasyaprabahulā sarvaratnaguṇodayād kāmadhug dhenuvad bhogān phalati sma sahasradhād manvādibhiḥ kṛtāḥ pūrvaṃ maryādā mānaveṣu yāḥd anatikramya tāḥ sarvāḥ kuleṣu samayāni cad anvaśāsanta te nityaṃ dharmaputrapriyaṃkarāḥd mahākulāni dharmiṣṭhā vardhayanto viśeṣataḥd manupraṇītayā vṛttyā te nvaśāsan vasuṃdharāmd rājavṛttir hi sā śaśvad dharmiṣṭhābhūn mahītaled prāyo lokamatis tāta rājavṛttānugāminīd evaṃ bhāratavarṣaṃ svaṃ rājā svargaṃ surendravatd śaśāsa viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ gupto gāṇḍīvadhanvanā janamejaya uvācaa vijite pāṇḍaveyais tu praśānte ca dvijottamac rāṣṭre kiṃ cakratur vīrau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa vijite pāṇḍaveyais tu praśānte ca viśāṃ patec rāṣṭre babhūvatur hṛṣṭau vāsudevadhanaṃjayaua vijahrāte mudā yuktau divi deveśvarāv ivac tau vaneṣu vicitreṣu parvatānāṃ ca sānuṣua śaileṣu ramaṇīyeṣu palvaleṣu nadīṣu cac caṅkramyamāṇau saṃhṛṣṭāv aśvināv iva nandanea indraprasthe mahātmānau remāte kṛṣṇapāṇḍavauc praviśya tāṃ sabhāṃ ramyāṃ vijahrāte ca bhārataa tatra yuddhakathāś citrāḥ parikleśāṃś ca pārthivac kathāyoge kathāyoge kathayām āsatus tadād kathayām āsa yogena kathayām anupūrvaśaḥ sica ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca vaṃśāṃs tāv āhatus tadāc prīyamāṇau mahātmānau purāṇāv ṛṣisattamaua madhurās tu kathāś citrāś citrārthapadaniścayāḥc niścayajñaḥ sa pārthāya kathayām āsa keśavaḥa putraśokābhisaṃtaptaṃ jñātīnāṃ ca sahasraśaḥc kathābhiḥ śamayām āsa pārthaṃ śaurir janārdanaḥa sa tam āśvāsya vidhivad vidhānajño mahātapāḥc apahṛtyātmano bhāraṃ viśaśrāmeva sātvataḥa tataḥ kathānte govindo guḍākeśam uvāca hac sāntvayañ ślakṣṇayā vācā hetuyuktam idaṃ vacaḥa vijiteyaṃ dharā kṛtsnā savyasācin paraṃtapac tvadbāhubalam āśritya rājñā dharmasutena haa asapatnāṃ mahīṃ bhuṅkte dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhīmasenaprabhāvena yamayoś ca narottamaa dharmeṇa rājñā dharmajña prāptaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakamc dharmeṇa nihataḥ saṃkhye sa ca rājā suyodhanaḥa adharmarucayo lubdhāḥ sadā cāpriyavādinaḥc dhārtarāṣṭrā durātmānaḥ sānubandhā nipātitāḥa praśāntām akhilāṃ pārtha pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpatiḥc bhuṅkte dharmasuto rājā tvayā guptaḥ kurūdvahaa rame cāhaṃ tvayā sārdham araṇyeṣv api pāṇḍavac kim u yatra jano yaṃ vai pṛthā cāmitrakarśanaa yatra dharmasuto rājā yatra bhīmo mahābalaḥc yatra mādravatīputrau ratis tatra parā mamaa tathaiva svargakalpeṣu sabhoddeśeṣu bhāratac ramaṇīyeṣu puṇyeṣu sahitasya tvayānaghaa kālo mahāṃs tv atīto me śūraputram apaśyataḥc baladevaṃ ca kauravya tathānyān vṛṣṇipuṃgavāna so haṃ gantum abhīpsāmi purīṃ dvāravatīṃ pratic rocatāṃ gamanaṃ mahyaṃ tavāpi puruṣarṣabhaa ukto bahuvidhaṃ rājā tatra tatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥc sa ha bhīṣmeṇa yady uktam asmābhiḥ śokakāritea śiṣṭo yudhiṣṭhiro smābhiḥ śāstā sann api pāṇḍavaḥc tena tac ca vacaḥ samyag gṛhītaṃ sumahātmanāa dharmaputre hi dharmajñe kṛtajñe satyavādinic satyaṃ dharmo matiś cāgryā sthitiś ca satataṃ sthirāa tad gatvā taṃ mahātmānaṃ yadi te rocate rjunac asmadgamanasaṃyuktaṃ vaco brūhi janādhipama na hi tasyāpriyaṃ kuryāṃ prāṇatyāge py upasthitec kuto gantuṃ mahābāho purīṃ dvāravatīṃ pratia sarvaṃ tv idam ahaṃ pārtha tvatprītihitakāmyayāc bravīmi satyaṃ kauravya na mithyaitat kathaṃ canaa prayojanaṃ ca nirvṛttam iha vāse mamārjunac dhārtarāṣṭro hato rājā sabalaḥ sapadānugaḥa pṛthivī ca vaśe tāta dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥc sthitā samudravasanā saśailavanakānanāe citā ratnair bahuvidhaiḥ kururājasya pāṇḍavaa dharmeṇa rājā dharmajñaḥ pātu sarvāṃ vasuṃdharāmc upāsyamāno bahubhiḥ siddhaiś cāpi mahātmabhiḥe stūyamānaś ca satataṃ bandibhir bharatarṣabhaa tan mayā saha gatvādya rājānaṃ kuruvardhanamc āpṛccha kuruśārdūla gamanaṃ dvārakāṃ pratia idaṃ śarīraṃ vasu yac ca me gṛheniveditaṃ pārtha sadā yudhiṣṭhirec priyaś ca mānyaś ca hi me yudhiṣṭhiraḥsadā kurūṇām adhipo mahāmatiḥa prayojanaṃ cāpi nivāsakāraṇena vidyate me tvad ṛte mahābhujac sthitā hi pṛthvī tava pārtha śāsaneguroḥ suvṛttasya yudhiṣṭhirasya haa itīdam uktaṃ sa tadā mahātmanājanārdanenāmitavikramo rjunaḥc tatheti kṛcchrād iva vācam īrayajjanārdanaṃ saṃpratipūjya pārthiva janamejaya uvācaa sabhāyāṃ vasatos tasyāṃ nihatyārīn mahātmanoḥc keśavārjunayoḥ kā nu kathā samabhavad dvija vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pārthaḥ svarājyaṃ prāpya kevalamc tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ ramyāyāṃ vijahāra mudā yutaḥa tataḥ kaṃ cit sabhoddeśaṃ svargoddeśasamaṃ nṛpac yadṛcchayā tau muditau jagmatuḥ svajanāvṛtaua tataḥ pratītaḥ kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pāṇḍavo rjunaḥc nirīkṣya tāṃ sabhāṃ ramyām idaṃ vacanam abravīta viditaṃ te mahābāho saṃgrāme samupasthitec māhātmyaṃ devakīmātas tac ca te rūpam aiśvarama yat tu tad bhavatā proktaṃ tadā keśava sauhṛdātc tat sarvaṃ puruṣavyāghra naṣṭaṃ me naṣṭacetasaḥa mama kautūhalaṃ tv asti teṣv artheṣu punaḥ prabhoc bhavāṃś ca dvārakāṃ gantā nacirād iva mādhavaa evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ phalgunaṃ pratyabhāṣatac pariṣvajya mahātejā vacanaṃ vadatāṃ varaḥa śrāvitas tvaṃ mayā guhyaṃ jñāpitaś ca sanātanamc dharmaṃ svarūpiṇaṃ pārtha sarvalokāṃś ca śāśvatāna abuddhvā yan na gṛhṇīthās tan me sumahad apriyamb na ca sādya punar bhūyaḥ smṛtir me saṃbhaviṣyatic nūnam aśraddadhāno si durmedhāś cāsi pāṇḍavad na ca śakyaḥ punar vaktum aśeṣeṇa dhanaṃjayaa sa hi dharmaḥ suparyāpto brahmaṇaḥ padavedanec na śakyaṃ tan mayā bhūyas tathā vaktum aśeṣataḥa paraṃ hi brahma kathitaṃ yogayuktena tan mayāc itihāsaṃ tu vakṣyāmi tasminn arthe purātanama yathā tāṃ buddhim āsthāya gatim agryāṃ gamiṣyasic śṛṇu dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha gadataḥ sarvam eva mea āgacchad brāhmaṇaḥ kaś cit svargalokād ariṃdamac brahmalokāc ca durdharṣaḥ so smābhiḥ pūjito bhavatd paripṛṣṭaś ca sa tadā yad āha dvijasattamaḥa asmābhiḥ paripṛṣṭaś ca yad āha bharatarṣabhac divyena vidhinā pārtha tac chṛṇuṣvāvicārayan brāhmaṇa uvācaa mokṣadharmaṃ samāśritya kṛṣṇa yan mānupṛcchasic bhūtānām anukampārthaṃ yan mohacchedanaṃ prabhoa tat te haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvan madhusūdanac śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā gadato mama mādhavaa kaś cid vipras tapoyuktaḥ kāśyapo dharmavittamaḥc āsasāda dvijaṃ kaṃ cid dharmāṇām āgatāgamama gatāgate subahuśo jñānavijñānapāragamc lokatattvārthakuśalaṃ jñātāraṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥa jātīmaraṇatattvajñaṃ kovidaṃ puṇyapāpayoḥc draṣṭāram uccanīcānāṃ karmabhir dehināṃ gatima carantaṃ muktavat siddhaṃ praśāntaṃ saṃyatendriyamc dīpyamānaṃ śriyā brāhmyā kramamāṇaṃ ca sarvaśaḥa antardhānagatijñaṃ ca śrutvā tattvena kāśyapaḥc tathaivāntarhitaiḥ siddhair yāntaṃ cakradharaiḥ sahaa saṃbhāṣamāṇam ekānte samāsīnaṃ ca taiḥ sahac yadṛcchayā ca gacchantam asaktaṃ pavanaṃ yathāa taṃ samāsādya medhāvī sa tadā dvijasattamaḥc caraṇau dharmakāmo vai tapasvī susamāhitaḥe pratipede yathānyāyaṃ bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥa vismitaś cādbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā kāśyapas taṃ dvijottamamc paricāreṇa mahatā guruṃ vaidyam atoṣayata prītātmā copapannaś ca śrutacāritrasaṃyutaḥc bhāvena toṣayac cainaṃ guruvṛttyā paraṃtapaḥa tasmai tuṣṭaḥ sa śiṣyāya prasanno thābravīd guruḥc siddhiṃ parām abhiprekṣya śṛṇu tan me janārdanaa vividhaiḥ karmabhis tāta puṇyayogaiś ca kevalaiḥc gacchantīha gatiṃ martyā devaloke pi ca sthitima na kva cit sukham atyantaṃ na kva cic chāśvatī sthitiḥc sthānāc ca mahato bhraṃśo duḥkhalabdhāt punaḥ punaḥa aśubhā gatayaḥ prāptāḥ kaṣṭā me pāpasevanātc kāmamanyuparītena tṛṣṇayā mohitena caa punaḥ punaś ca maraṇaṃ janma caiva punaḥ punaḥc āhārā vividhā bhuktāḥ pītā nānāvidhāḥ stanāḥa mātaro vividhā dṛṣṭāḥ pitaraś ca pṛthagvidhāḥc sukhāni ca vicitrāṇi duḥkhāni ca mayānaghaa priyair vivāso bahuśaḥ saṃvāsaś cāpriyaiḥ sahac dhananāśaś ca saṃprāpto labdhvā duḥkhena tad dhanama avamānāḥ sukaṣṭāś ca parataḥ svajanāt tathāc śārīrā mānasāś cāpi vedanā bhṛśadāruṇāḥa prāptā vimānanāś cogrā vadhabandhāś ca dāruṇāḥc patanaṃ niraye caiva yātanāś ca yamakṣayea jarā rogāś ca satataṃ vāsanāni ca bhūriśaḥc loke sminn anubhūtāni dvaṃdvajāni bhṛśaṃ mayāa tataḥ kadā cin nirvedān nikārān nikṛtena cac lokatantraṃ parityaktaṃ duḥkhārtena bhṛśaṃ mayād loke sminn anubhūyāham imaṃ mārgam anuṣṭhitaḥe tataḥ siddhir iyaṃ prāptā prasādād ātmano mayāa nāhaṃ punar ihāgantā lokān ālokayāmy ahamc ā siddher ā prajāsargād ātmano me gatiḥ śubhāa upalabdhā dvijaśreṣṭha tatheyaṃ siddhir uttamāc itaḥ paraṃ gamiṣyāmi tataḥ parataraṃ punaḥe brahmaṇaḥ padam avyagraṃ mā te bhūd atra saṃśayaḥa nāhaṃ punar ihāgantā martyalokaṃ paraṃtapac prīto smi te mahāprājña brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi tea yadīpsur upapannas tvaṃ tasya kālo yam āgataḥc abhijāne ca tad ahaṃ yadarthaṃ mā tvam āgataḥe acirāt tu gamiṣyāmi yenāhaṃ tvām acūcudama bhṛśaṃ prīto smi bhavataś cāritreṇa vicakṣaṇac paripṛccha yāvad bhavate bhāṣeyaṃ yat tavepsitama bahu manye ca te buddhiṃ bhṛśaṃ saṃpūjayāmi cac yenāhaṃ bhavatā buddho medhāvī hy asi kāśyapa vāsudeva uvācaa tatas tasyopasaṃgṛhya pādau praśnān sudurvacānc papraccha tāṃś ca sarvān sa prāha dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ kāśyapa uvācaa kathaṃ śarīraṃ cyavate kathaṃ caivopapadyatec kathaṃ kaṣṭāc ca saṃsārāt saṃsaran parimucyatea ātmānaṃ vā kathaṃ yuktvā tac charīraṃ vimuñcatic śarīrataś ca nirmuktaḥ katham anyat prapadyatea kathaṃ śubhāśubhe cāyaṃ karmaṇī svakṛte naraḥc upabhuṅkte kva vā karma videhasyopatiṣṭhati brāhmaṇa uvācaa evaṃ saṃcoditaḥ siddhaḥ praśnāṃs tān pratyabhāṣatac ānupūrvyeṇa vārṣṇeya yathā tan me vacaḥ śṛṇud siddhaḥd asminn evāśubhaphalā āyuṣyās tu kriyāḥ smṛtāḥ siddha uvācaa āyuḥkīrtikarāṇīha yāni karmāṇi sevatec śarīragrahaṇe nyasmiṃs teṣu kṣīṇeṣu sarvaśaḥa āyuḥkṣayaparītātmā viparītāni sevatec buddhir vyāvartate cāsya vināśe pratyupasthitea sattvaṃ balaṃ ca kālaṃ cāpy aviditvātmanas tathāc ativelam upāśnāti tair viruddhāny anātmavāna yadāyam atikaṣṭāni sarvāṇy upaniṣevatec atyartham api vā bhuṅkte na vā bhuṅkte kadā canaa duṣṭānnaṃ viṣamānnaṃ ca so nyonyena virodhi cac guru vāpi samaṃ bhuṅkte nātijīrṇe pi vā punaḥa vyāyāmam atimātraṃ vā vyavāyaṃ copasevatec satataṃ karmalobhād vā prāptaṃ vegavidhāraṇama rasātiyuktam annaṃ vā divāsvapnaṃ niṣevatec apakvānāgate kāle svayaṃ doṣān prakopayana svadoṣakopanād rogaṃ labhate maraṇāntikamc atha codbandhanādīni parītāni vyavasyatia tasya taiḥ kāraṇair jantoḥ śarīrāc cyavate yathāc jīvitaṃ procyamānaṃ tad yathāvad upadhārayaa ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥc śarīram anuparyeti sarvān prāṇān ruṇaddhi vaia atyarthaṃ balavān ūṣmā śarīre parikopitaḥc bhinatti jīvasthānāni tāni marmāṇi viddhi caa tataḥ savedanaḥ sadyo jīvaḥ pracyavate kṣaranc śarīraṃ tyajate jantuś chidyamāneṣu marmasue vedanābhiḥ parītātmā tad viddhi dvijasattamaa jātīmaraṇasaṃvignāḥ satataṃ sarvajantavaḥc dṛśyante saṃtyajantaś ca śarīrāṇi dvijarṣabhaa garbhasaṃkramaṇe cāpi marmaṇām atisarpaṇec tādṛśīm eva labhate vedanāṃ mānavaḥ punaḥa bhinnasaṃdhir atha kledam adbhiḥ sa labhate naraḥc yathā pañcasu bhūteṣu saṃśritatvaṃ nigacchatie śaityāt prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥa yaḥ sa pañcasu bhūteṣu prāṇāpāne vyavasthitaḥc sa gacchaty ūrdhvago vāyuḥ kṛcchrān muktvā śarīriṇama śarīraṃ ca jahāty eva nirucchvāsaś ca dṛśyatec nirūṣmā sa nirucchvāso niḥśrīko gatacetanaḥa brahmaṇā saṃparityakto mṛta ity ucyate naraḥc srotobhir yair vijānāti indriyārthāñ śarīrabhṛte tair eva na vijānāti prāṇam āhārasaṃbhavama tatraiva kurute kāye yaḥ sa jīvaḥ sanātanaḥc teṣāṃ yad yad bhaved yuktaṃ saṃnipāte kva cit kva cite tat tan marma vijānīhi śāstradṛṣṭaṃ hi tat tathāa teṣu marmasu bhinneṣu tataḥ sa samudīrayanc āviśya hṛdayaṃ jantoḥ sattvaṃ cāśu ruṇaddhi vaie tataḥ sa cetano jantur nābhijānāti kiṃ canaa tamasā saṃvṛtajñānaḥ saṃvṛteṣv atha marmasuc sa jīvo niradhiṣṭhānaś cāvyate mātariśvanāa tataḥ sa taṃ mahocchvāsaṃ bhṛśam ucchvasya dāruṇamc niṣkrāman kampayaty āśu tac charīram acetanama sa jīvaḥ pracyutaḥ kāyāt karmabhiḥ svaiḥ samāvṛtaḥc aṅkitaḥ svaiḥ śubhaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pāpair vāpy upapadyatea brāhmaṇā jñānasaṃpannā yathāvac chrutaniścayāḥc itaraṃ kṛtapuṇyaṃ vā taṃ vijānanti lakṣaṇaiḥa yathāndhakāre khadyotaṃ līyamānaṃ tatas tataḥc cakṣuṣmantaḥ prapaśyanti tathā taṃ jñānacakṣuṣaḥa paśyanty evaṃvidhāḥ siddhā jīvaṃ divyena cakṣuṣāc cyavantaṃ jāyamānaṃ ca yoniṃ cānupraveśitama tasya sthānāni dṛṣṭāni trividhānīha śāstrataḥc karmabhūmir iyaṃ bhūmir yatra tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥa tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ kṛtvā labhante sarvadehinaḥc ihaivoccāvacān bhogān prāpnuvanti svakarmabhiḥa ihaivāśubhakarmā tu karmabhir nirayaṃ gataḥc avāk sa niraye pāpo mānavaḥ pacyate bhṛśamd arvāg gatir iyaṃ kaṣṭā yatra pacyanti mānavāḥe tasmāt sudurlabho mokṣa ātmā rakṣyo bhṛśaṃ tataḥa ūrdhvaṃ tu jantavo gatvā yeṣu sthāneṣv avasthitāḥc kīrtyamānāni tānīha tattvataḥ saṃnibodha mee tac chrutvā naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhiṃ budhyethāḥ karmaniścayāta tārārūpāṇi sarvāṇi yac caitac candramaṇḍalamc yac ca vibhrājate loke svabhāsā sūryamaṇḍalame sthānāny etāni jānīhi narāṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇāma karmakṣayāc ca te sarve cyavante vai punaḥ punaḥc tatrāpi ca viśeṣo sti divi nīcoccamadhyamaḥa na tatrāpy asti saṃtoṣo dṛṣṭvā dīptatarāṃ śriyamc ity etā gatayaḥ sarvāḥ pṛthaktve samudīritāḥa upapattiṃ tu garbhasya vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ paramc yathāvat tāṃ nigadataḥ śṛṇuṣvāvahito dvija brāhmaṇa uvācaa śubhānām aśubhānāṃ ca neha nāśo sti karmaṇāmc prāpya prāpya tu pacyante kṣetraṃ kṣetraṃ tathā tathāa yathā prasūyamānas tu phalī dadyāt phalaṃ bahuc tathā syād vipulaṃ puṇyaṃ śuddhena manasā kṛtama pāpaṃ cāpi tathaiva syāt pāpena manasā kṛtamc purodhāya mano hīha karmaṇy ātmā pravartatea yathā karmasamādiṣṭaṃ kāmamanyusamāvṛtaḥc naro garbhaṃ praviśati tac cāpi śṛṇu cottarama śukraṃ śoṇitasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ striyā garbhāśayaṃ gatamc kṣetraṃ karmajam āpnoti śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubhama saukṣmyād avyaktabhāvāc ca na sa kva cana sajjatec saṃprāpya brahmaṇaḥ kāyaṃ tasmāt tad brahma śāśvatame tad bījaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tena jīvanti jantavaḥa sa jīvaḥ sarvagātrāṇi garbhasyāviśya bhāgaśaḥc dadhāti cetasā sadyaḥ prāṇasthāneṣv avasthitaḥe tataḥ spandayate ṅgāni sa garbhaś cetanānvitaḥa yathā hi lohaniṣyando niṣikto bimbavigrahamc upaiti tadvaj jānīhi garbhe jīvapraveśanama lohapiṇḍaṃ yathā vahniḥ praviśaty abhitāpayanc tathā tvam api jānīhi garbhe jīvopapādanama yathā ca dīpaḥ śaraṇaṃ dīpyamānaḥ prakāśayetc evam eva śarīrāṇi prakāśayati cetanāa yad yac ca kurute karma śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubhamc pūrvadehakṛtaṃ sarvam avaśyam upabhujyatea tatas tat kṣīyate caiva punaś cānyat pracīyatec yāvat tan mokṣayogasthaṃ dharmaṃ naivāvabudhyatea tatra dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi sukhī bhavati yena vaic āvartamāno jātīṣu tathānyonyāsu sattamad śubhapradāni yāny āhus tāni kuryāc ca buddhimāna dānaṃ vrataṃ brahmacaryaṃ yathoktavratadhāraṇamc damaḥ praśāntatā caiva bhūtānāṃ cānukampanama saṃyamaś cānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca parasvādānavarjanamc vyalīkānām akaraṇaṃ bhūtānāṃ yatra sā bhuvia mātāpitroś ca śuśrūṣā devatātithipūjanamc gurupūjā ghṛṇā śaucaṃ nityam indriyasaṃyamaḥa pravartanaṃ śubhānāṃ ca tat satāṃ vṛttam ucyateb sadbhir ācarito dharmaḥ sadācāre pratiṣṭhitaḥb ubhayārtho bhavaty eva svargārtho mokṣadas tathāc tato dharmaḥ prabhavati yaḥ prajāḥ pāti śāśvatīḥa evaṃ satsu sadā paśyet tatra hy eṣā dhruvā sthitiḥc ācāro dharmam ācaṣṭe yasmin santo vyavasthitāḥa teṣu tad dharmanikṣiptaṃ yaḥ sa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥc yas taṃ samabhipadyeta na sa durgatim āpnuyāta ato niyamyate lokaḥ pramuhya dharmavartmasuc yas tu yogī ca muktaś ca sa etebhyo viśiṣyatea vartamānasya dharmeṇa puruṣasya yathā tathāc saṃsāratāraṇaṃ hy asya kālena mahatā bhaveta evaṃ pūrvakṛtaṃ karma sarvo jantur niṣevatec sarvaṃ tat kāraṇaṃ yena nikṛto yam ihāgataḥa śarīragrahaṇaṃ cāsya kena pūrvaṃ prakalpitamc ity evaṃ saṃśayo loke tac ca vakṣyāmy ataḥ parama śarīram ātmanaḥ kṛtvā sarvabhūtapitāmahaḥc trailokyam asṛjad brahmā kṛtsnaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamama tataḥ pradhānam asṛjac cetanā sā śarīriṇāmc yayā sarvam idaṃ vyāptaṃ yāṃ loke paramāṃ viduḥa iha tat kṣaram ity uktaṃ paraṃ tv amṛtam akṣaramc trayāṇāṃ mithunaṃ sarvam ekaikasya pṛthak pṛthaka asṛjat sarvabhūtāni pūrvasṛṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥc sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni ity eṣā paurvikī śrutiḥa tasya kālaparīmāṇam akarot sa pitāmahaḥc bhūteṣu parivṛttiṃ ca punarāvṛttim eva caa yathātra kaś cin medhāvī dṛṣṭātmā pūrvajanmanic yat pravakṣyāmi tat sarvaṃ yathāvad upapadyatea sukhaduḥkhe sadā samyag anitye yaḥ prapaśyatic kāyaṃ cāmedhyasaṃghātaṃ vināśaṃ karmasaṃhitama yac ca kiṃ cit sukhaṃ tac ca sarvaṃ duḥkham iti smaranc saṃsārasāgaraṃ ghoraṃ tariṣyati sudustarama jātīmaraṇarogaiś ca samāviṣṭaḥ pradhānavitc cetanāvatsu caitanyaṃ samaṃ bhūteṣu paśyatia nirvidyate tataḥ kṛtsnaṃ mārgamāṇaḥ paraṃ padamc tasyopadeśaṃ vakṣyāmi yāthātathyena sattamaa śāśvatasyāvyayasyātha padasya jñānam uttamamc procyamānaṃ mayā vipra nibodhedam aśeṣataḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa yaḥ syād ekāyane līnas tūṣṇīṃ kiṃ cid acintayanc pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ parityajya sa nirārambhako bhaveta sarvamitraḥ sarvasahaḥ samarakto jitendriyaḥc vyapetabhayamanyuś ca kāmahā mucyate naraḥa ātmavat sarvabhūteṣu yaś caren niyataḥ śuciḥb nityam eva yathānyāyaṃ yaś caren niyatendriyaḥc amānī nirabhīmānaḥ sarvato mukta eva saḥa jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ cobhe sukhaduḥkhe tathaiva cac lābhālābhe priyadveṣye yaḥ samaḥ sa ca mucyatea na kasya cit spṛhayate nāvajānāti kiṃ canac nirdvaṃdvo vītarāgātmā sarvato mukta eva saḥa anamitro tha nirbandhur anapatyaś ca yaḥ kva citc tyaktadharmārthakāmaś ca nirākāṅkṣī sa mucyatea naiva dharmī na cādharmī pūrvopacitahā ca yaḥc dhātukṣayapraśāntātmā nirdvaṃdvaḥ sa vimucyatea akarmā cāvikāṅkṣaś ca paśyañ jagad aśāśvatamc asvastham avaśaṃ nityaṃ janmasaṃsāramohitama vairāgyabuddhiḥ satataṃ tāpadoṣavyapekṣakaḥc ātmabandhavinirmokṣaṃ sa karoty acirād ivaa agandharasam asparśam aśabdam aparigrahamc arūpam anabhijñeyaṃ dṛṣṭvātmānaṃ vimucyatea pañcabhūtaguṇair hīnam amūrtimad alepakamc aguṇaṃ guṇabhoktāraṃ yaḥ paśyati sa mucyatea vihāya sarvasaṃkalpān buddhyā śārīramānasānc śanair nirvāṇam āpnoti ātmania indriyāṇi tu saṃhṛtya mana ātmani dhārayetc tīvraṃ taptvā tapaḥ pūrvaṃ tato yoktum upakrameta tapasvī tyaktasaṃkalpo dambhāhaṃkāravarjitaḥc manīṣī manasā vipraḥ paśyaty ātmānam ātmania sa cec chaknoty ayaṃ sādhur yoktum ātmānam ātmanic tata ekāntaśīlaḥ sa paśyaty ātmānam ātmania saṃyataḥ satataṃ yukta ātmavān vijitendriyaḥc tathāyam ātmanātmānaṃ sādhu yuktaḥ prapaśyatia yathā hi puruṣaḥ ālokayati manasā prahasann ivad tad evam āśrayaṃ kṛtvā mokṣaṃ yāti tato mayia idaṃ sarvarahasyaṃ te mayoktaṃ dvijasattamac āpṛcche sādhayiṣyāmi gaccha śiṣya yathāsukhama ity uktaḥ sa tadā kṛṣṇa mayā pārtha śrutam ekāgracetasāc tadāpi hi rathasthas tvaṃ śrutavān etad eva hia naitat pārtha suvijñeyaṃ vyāmiśreṇeti me matiḥc nareṇākṛtasaṃjñena vidagdhenākṛtātmanāa surahasyam idaṃ proktaṃ devānāṃ bharatarṣabhac kaccin nedaṃ śrutaṃ pārtha martyenānyena kena cita na hy etac chrotum arho nyo manuṣyas tvām ṛte naghac naitad adya suvijñeyaṃ vyāmiśreṇāntarātmanāa kriyāvadbhir hi kaunteya devalokaḥ samāvṛtaḥc na caitad iṣṭaṃ devānāṃ martyai rūpanivartanama parā hi sā gatiḥ pārtha yat tad brahma sanātanamc yatrāmṛtatvaṃ prāpnoti tyaktvā duḥkhaṃ sadā sukhīa evaṃ hi dharmam āsthāya ye pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥc striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te pi yānti parāṃ gatima kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ pārtha kṣatriyā vā bahuśrutāḥc svadharmaratayo nityaṃ brahmalokaparāyaṇāḥa hetumac caitad uddiṣṭam upāyāś cāsya
