praviśanty agnijaṃ mukhamc antarvāsam uṣitvā ca jāyante svāsu yoniṣue tatraiva ca nirudhyante pralaye bhūtabhāvanea tataḥ saṃjāyate gandhas tataḥ saṃjāyate rasaḥc tataḥ saṃjāyate rūpaṃ tataḥ sparśo bhijāyatea tataḥ saṃjāyate śabdaḥ saṃśayas tatra jāyatec tataḥ saṃjāyate niṣṭhā janmaitat saptadhā viduḥa anenaiva prakāreṇa pragṛhītaṃ purātanaiḥc pūrṇāhutibhir āpūrṇās te bhipūryanti tejasā brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamb indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃvādaṃ manasaś caiva bhāminic nibodha daśahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśamd śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caraṇau karaud upasthaḥ pāyur etāni hotṝṇi daśa bhāminid śabdasparśau rūparasau gandho vākyaṃ kriyā gatiḥd retomūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ tyāgo daśa havīṃṣi cad diśo vāyū raviś candraḥ pṛthvyagnī viṣṇur eva cad indraḥ prajāpatir mitram agnayo daśa bhāminid daśendriyāṇi hotṝṇi havīṃṣi daśa bhāminid viṣayā nāma samidho hūyante tu daśāgniṣud cittaṃ sruvaṃ ca vittaṃ ca pavitraṃ jñānam uttamamd suvibhaktam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagad āsīd iti śrutamd tato viviktā cintāsīt sā cittaṃ paryavekṣated śrutvā cittaṃ srug ity eva manaś cittaṃ tad ucyated tayor viviktā nāgāsīd acalā śabdalakṣaṇād nagneva yoṣā savrīḍā sā vāsaḥ paryavekṣated tasmāt saṃjajñire varṇāḥ svarā mantrās tathaiva cad etac ca naḥ sarasvatyāḥ prajāpatir athābravīta sarvam evātra vijñeyaṃ cittaṃ jñānam avekṣatec retaḥ śarīrabhṛtkāye vijñātā tu śarīrabhṛta śarīrabhṛd gārhapatyas tasmād anyaḥ praṇīyatec tataś cāhavanīyas tu tasmin saṃkṣipyate haviḥa tato vācaspatir jajñe samānaḥ paryavekṣatec rūpaṃ bhavati vai vyaktaṃ tad anudravate manaḥ brāhmaṇy uvācaa kasmād vāg abhavat pūrvaṃ kasmāt paścān mano bhavatc manasā cintitaṃ vākyaṃ yadā samabhipadyatea kena vijñānayogena matiś cittaṃ samāsthitāc samunnītā nādhyagacchat ko vaināṃ pratiṣedhati brāhmaṇa uvācaa tām apānaḥ patir bhūtvā tasmāt preṣyaty apānatāmc tāṃ matiṃ manasaḥ prāhur manas tasmād avekṣatea praśnaṃ tu vāṅmanasor māṃ yasmāt tvam anupṛcchasic tasmāt te vartayiṣyāmi tayor eva samāhvayama ubhe vāṅmanasī gatvā bhūtātmānam apṛcchatāmc āvayoḥ śreṣṭham ācakṣva chindhi nau saṃśayaṃ vibhoa mana ity eva bhagavāṃs tadā prāha sarasvatīmc ahaṃ vai kāmadhuk tubhyam iti taṃ prāha vāg athaa sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva viddhy ubhe manasī mamac sthāvaraṃ matsakāśe vai jaṅgamaṃ viṣaye tavaa yas tu te viṣayaṃ gacchen mantro varṇaḥ svaro pi vāc tan mano jaṅgamaṃ nāma tasmād asi garīyasīa yasmād asi ca mā vocaḥ svayam abhyetya śobhanec tasmād ucchvāsam āsādya na vakṣyasi sarasvatia prāṇāpānāntare devī vāg vai nityaṃ sma tiṣṭhatic preryamāṇā mahābhāge vinā prāṇam apānatīe prajāpatim upādhāvat prasīda bhagavann itia tataḥ prāṇaḥ prādurabhūd vācam āpyāyayan punaḥc tasmād ucchvāsam āsādya na vāg vadati karhi cita ghoṣiṇī jātanirghoṣā nityam eva pravartatec tayor api ca ghoṣiṇyor nirghoṣaiva garīyasīa gaur iva prasravaty eṣā rasam uttamaśālinīc satataṃ syandate hy eṣā śāśvataṃ brahmavādinīa divyādivyaprabhāvena bhāratī gauḥ śucismitec etayor antaraṃ paśya sūkṣmayoḥ syandamānayoḥa anutpanneṣu vākyeṣu codyamānā sisṛkṣayāc kiṃ nu pūrvaṃ tato devī vyājahāra sarasvatīa prāṇena yā saṃbhavate śarīreprāṇād apānaṃ pratipadyate cac udānabhūtā ca visṛjya dehaṃvyānena sarvaṃ divam āvṛṇotia tataḥ samāne pratitiṣṭhatīhaity eva pūrvaṃ prajajalpa cāpic tasmān manaḥ sthāvaratvād viśiṣṭaṃtathā devī jaṅgamatvād viśiṣṭā brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc subhage saptahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśama ghrāṇaṃ cakṣuś ca jihvā ca tvak śrotraṃ caiva pañcamamc mano buddhiś ca saptaite hotāraḥ pṛthag āśritāḥa sūkṣme vakāśe santas te na paśyantītaretaramc etān vai saptahotṝṃs tvaṃ svabhāvād viddhi śobhane brāhmaṇy uvācaa sūkṣme vakāśe santas te kathaṃ nānyonyadarśinaḥc kathaṃsvabhāvā bhagavann etad ācakṣva me vibho brāhmaṇa uvācaa guṇājñānam avijñānaṃ guṇijñānam abhijñatāc parasparaguṇān ete na vijānanti karhi cita jihvā cakṣus tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva cac na gandhān adhigacchanti ghrāṇas tān adhigacchatia ghrāṇaṃ cakṣus tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva cac na rasān adhigacchanti jihvā tān adhigacchatia ghrāṇaṃ jihvā tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva cac na rūpāṇy adhigacchanti cakṣus tāny adhigacchatia ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ buddhir manas tathāc na sparśān adhigacchanti tvak ca tān adhigacchatia ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvaṅ mano buddhir eva cac na śabdān adhigacchanti śrotraṃ tān adhigacchatid ghrāṇaṃ cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca tvag jihvā buddhir eva caa ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak śrotraṃ buddhir eva cac saṃśayān nādhigacchanti manas tān adhigacchatia ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak śrotraṃ mana eva cac na niṣṭhām adhigacchanti buddhis tām adhigacchatia atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃvādaṃ manasaś caiva bhāmini mana uvācaa na ghrāti mām ṛte ghrāṇaṃ rasaṃ jihvā na budhyatec rūpaṃ cakṣur na gṛhṇāti tvak sparśaṃ nāvabudhyatea na śrotraṃ budhyate śabdaṃ mayā hīnaṃ kathaṃ canac pravaraṃ sarvabhūtānām aham asmi sanātanama agārāṇīva śūnyāni śāntārciṣa ivāgnayaḥc indriyāṇi na bhāsante mayā hīnāni nityaśaḥa kāṣṭhānīvārdraśuṣkāṇi yatamānair apīndriyaiḥc guṇārthān nādhigacchanti mām ṛte sarvajantavaḥ indriyāṇy ūcuḥa evam etad bhavet satyaṃ yathaitan manyate bhavānc ṛte smān asmadarthāṃs tu bhogān bhuṅkte bhavān yadia yady asmāsu pralīneṣu tarpaṇaṃ prāṇadhāraṇamc bhogān bhuṅkṣe rasān bhuṅkṣe yathaitan manyate tathāa atha vāsmāsu līneṣu tiṣṭhatsu viṣayeṣu cac yadi saṃkalpamātreṇa bhuṅkte bhogān yathārthavata atha cen manyase siddhim asmadartheṣu nityadāc ghrāṇena rūpam ādatsva rasam ādatsva cakṣuṣāa śrotreṇa gandham ādatsva niṣṭhām ādatsva jihvayāc tvacā ca śabdam ādatsva buddhyā sparśam athāpi caa balavanto hy aniyamā niyamā durbalīyasāmc bhogān apūrvān ādatsva nocchiṣṭaṃ bhoktum arhasia yathā hi śiṣyaḥ śāstāraṃ śrutyartham abhidhāvatic tataḥ śrutam upādāya śrutārtham upatiṣṭhatia viṣayān evam asmābhir darśitān abhimanyasec anāgatān atītāṃś ca svapne jāgaraṇe tathāa vaimanasyaṃ gatānāṃ ca jantūnām alpacetasāmc asmadarthe kṛte kārye dṛśyate prāṇadhāraṇama bahūn api hi saṃkalpān matvā svapnān upāsya cac bubhukṣayā pīḍyamāno viṣayān eva dhāvasia agāram advāram iva praviśyasaṃkalpabhogo viṣayān avindanc prāṇakṣaye śāntim upaiti nityaṃdārukṣaye gnir jvalito yathaivaa kāmaṃ tu naḥ sveṣu guṇeṣu saṅgaḥkāmaṃ ca nānyonyaguṇopalabdhiḥc asmān ṛte nāsti tavopalabdhistvām apy ṛte smān na bhajeta harṣaḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc subhage pañcahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśama prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samāno vyāna eva cac pañcahotṝn athaitān vai paraṃ bhāvaṃ vidur budhāḥ brāhmaṇy uvācaa svabhāvāt sapta hotāra iti te pūrvikā matiḥc yathā vai pañca hotāraḥ paro bhāvas tathocyatām brāhmaṇa uvācaa prāṇena saṃbhṛto vāyur apāno jāyate tataḥc apāne saṃbhṛto vāyus tato vyānaḥ pravartatea vyānena saṃbhṛto vāyus tatodānaḥ pravartatec udāne saṃbhṛto vāyuḥ samānaḥ saṃpravartatea te pṛcchanta purā gatvā pūrvajātaṃ prajāpatimc yo no jyeṣṭhas tam ācakṣva sa naḥ śreṣṭho bhaviṣyati brahmovācaa yasmin pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec yasmin pracīrṇe ca punaś carantisa vai śreṣṭho gacchata yatra kāmaḥ prāṇa uvācaa mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś carantiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam brāhmaṇa uvācaa prāṇaḥ pralīyata tataḥ punaś ca pracacāra hac samānaś cāpy udānaś ca vaco brūtāṃ tataḥ śubhea na tvaṃ sarvam idaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhasīha yathā vayamc na tvaṃ śreṣṭho si naḥ prāṇa apāno hi vaśe tavae pracacāra punaḥ prāṇas tam apāno bhyabhāṣataa mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś carantiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnamd śreṣṭho ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunāa vyānaś ca tam udānaś ca bhāṣamāṇam athocatuḥc apāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho si prāṇo hi vaśagas tavaa apānaḥ pracacārātha vyānas taṃ punar abravītc śreṣṭho ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunāa mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś carantiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnama prālīyata tato vyānaḥ punaś ca pracacāra hac prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samānaś ca tam abruvane na tvaṃ śreṣṭho si no vyāna samāno hi vaśe tavaa pracacāra punar vyānaḥ samānaḥ punar abravītc śreṣṭho ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunāa mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś carantiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnama tataḥ samānaḥ prālilye punaś ca pracacāra hab tato vyānaḥ samānaṃ tu prāṇāpānau tathocatuḥc prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca vyānaś caiva tam abruvane samāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho si vyāna eva vaśe tavaf śreṣṭho ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ kena hetunāf tatodānaḥ pralīyāśu samānaḥ punar abravīta samānaḥ pracacārātha udānas tam uvāca hac śreṣṭho ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunāa mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajantisarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīrec mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś carantiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnama tataḥ prālīyatodānaḥ punaś ca pracacāra hac prāṇāpānau samānaś ca vyānaś caiva tam abruvane udāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho si vyāna eva vaśe tavaa tatas tān abravīd brahmā samavetān prajāpatiḥc sarve śreṣṭhā na vā śreṣṭhāḥ sarve cānyonyadharmiṇaḥe sarve svaviṣaye śreṣṭhāḥ sarve cānyonyarakṣiṇaḥa ekaḥ sthiraś cāsthiraś ca viśeṣāt pañca vāyavaḥc eka eva mamaivātmā bahudhāpy upacīyatea parasparasya suhṛdo bhāvayantaḥ parasparamc svasti vrajata bhadraṃ vo dhārayadhvaṃ parasparam brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc nāradasya ca saṃvādam ṛṣer devamatasya ca devamata uvācaa jantoḥ saṃjāyamānasya kiṃ nu pūrvaṃ pravartatec prāṇo pānaḥ samāno vā vyāno vodāna eva ca nārada uvācaa yenāyaṃ sṛjyate jantus tato nyaḥ pūrvam eti tamc prāṇadvaṃdvaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ tiryagaṃ cordhvagaṃ ca yat devamata uvācaa kenāyaṃ sṛjyate jantuḥ kaś cānyaḥ pūrvam eti tamc prāṇadvaṃdvaṃ ca me brūhi tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca niścayāt nārada uvācaa saṃkalpāj jāyate harṣaḥ śabdād api ca jāyatec rasāt saṃjāyate cāpi rūpād api ca jāyatea sparśāt saṃjāyate cāpi gandhād api ca jāyatec etad rūpam udānasya harṣo mithunasaṃbhavaḥa kāmāt saṃjāyate śukraṃ kāmāt saṃjāyate rasaḥc samānavyānajanite sāmānye śukraśoṇitea śukrāc choṇitasaṃsṛṣṭāt pūrvaṃ prāṇaḥ pravartatec prāṇena vikṛte śukre tato pānaḥ pravartatea prāṇāpānāv idaṃ dvaṃdvam avāk cordhvaṃ ca gacchataḥc vyānaḥ samānaś caivobhau tiryag dvaṃdvatvam ucyatea agnir vai devatāḥ sarvā iti vedasya śāsanamc saṃjāyate brāhmaṇeṣu jñānaṃ buddhisamanvitama tasya dhūmas tamorūpaṃ rajo bhasma suretasaḥc sattvaṃ saṃjāyate tasya yatra prakṣipyate haviḥa āghārau samāno vyānaś ca iti yajñavido viduḥc prāṇāpānāv ājyabhāgau tayor madhye hutāśanaḥe etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa nirdvaṃdvam iti yat tv etat tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇua ahorātram idaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa ubhe caivāyane dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa ubhe satyānṛte dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa ubhe śubhāśubhe dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa sac cāsac caiva tad dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥa prathamaṃ samāno vyāno vyasyate karma tena tatc tṛtīyaṃ tu samānena punar eva vyavasyatea śāntyarthaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca śāntir brahma sanātanamc etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥd yāvad dravyaguṇas tāvat pradīpaḥ saṃprakāśayetd kṣīṇe dravyaguṇe jyotir antardhānāya gacchatid vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇe hy eṣa puruṣo vyaktir īśated etad vipra vijānīṣva hanta bhūyo bravīmi ted sahasreṇāpi durmedhā buddhimān sukham edhated evaṃ dharmasya vijñeyaṃ saṃsādhanam upāyataḥd upāyajño hi medhāvī sukham atyantam aśnuted yathādhvānam apātheyaḥ prapanno mānavaḥ kva citd kleśena yāti mahatā vinaśyaty antarāpi vād tathā karmasu vijñeyaṃ phalaṃ bhavati mānavad puruṣasyātmaniḥśreyaḥ śubhāśubhanidarśanaḥd yathā ca dīrgham adhvānaṃ padbhyām eva prapadyated adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ sahasā tattvadarśanavakritaḥd prāpnuvanto yathādhvānaṃ rathenehāśugāminād yāyād aśvaprayuktena tathā buddhimatāṃ gatiḥd uccaparvatam āruhya nanv avekṣeta bhūgatamd rathena rathinaṃ paśyec caitanyena ca cetanamd yāvad rathapathas tāvad rathe samupagacchatid kṣīṇe rathapathe prājño ratham utsṛjya gacchatid evaṃ gacchati medhāvī tattvayogavidhānavitd samājñāya mahābuddher uttarād uttarottaramd yathā mahārṇavaṃ ghoram udbhavaḥ saṃpragāhated bāhubhyām eva saṃmohād vadhaṃ gacchaty asaṃśayamd nāvayā ca yathā prājño vinā prajñātaritrayād akrāntasalilaṃ gāhe kḷptaṃ saṃtarati svayamd tīrṇo gacchet paraṃ pāraṃ nāvam utsṛjya nirmamaḥd vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena yathā rathapadātināmd mohāt saṃmoham āpanno mā vināśaṃ yathā tathād mamatvenābhibhūtasya tatraiva paridevaned nāvaṃ na śakyam āruhya sthale pi paribhāvitumd tathaiva sthalam āruhya nāpsu yātuṃ vidhīyated evaṃ karma kṛtaṃ cittaṃ viṣamasthaṃ pṛthak pṛthakd yathā karma kṛtaṃ loke tathā tad upapadyated yatraiva gandho na raso na rūpasparśaśabdavatd manyate tha mano buddhyā tat pradhānaṃ pracakṣated yat tat pradhānam avyaktam avyaktasya guṇo mahānd mahataḥ pradhānabhūtasya guṇāḥ     smṛtāḥd bījadharmi yathā vyaktaṃ tathaiva prasavātmakamd bījadharmā mahān ātmā vasavaś ceti naḥ śrutamd bījadharmāt tv ahaṃkāraḥ prasavatve punaḥ punaḥd bījaprasavadharmāṇi mahābhūtāni pañca vaid bījadharmiṇam ity āhuḥ prasavaṃ naiva kurvated viśeṣāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaṃ viśeṣaṇamd etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc cāturhotravidhānasya vidhānam iha yādṛśama tasya sarvasya vidhivad vidhānam upadekṣyatec śṛṇu me gadato bhadre rahasyam idam uttamama karaṇaṃ karma kartā ca mokṣa ity eva bhāminic catvāra ete hotāro yair idaṃ jagad āvṛtama hotṝṇāṃ sādhanaṃ caiva śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣataḥc ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak ca śrotraṃ ca pañcamame mano buddhiś ca saptaite vijñeyā guṇahetavaḥa gandho rasaś ca rūpaṃ ca śabdaḥ sparśaś ca pañcamaḥc mantavyam atha boddhavyaṃ saptaite karmahetavaḥa ghrātā bhakṣayitā draṣṭā spraṣṭā śrotā ca pañcamaḥc mantā boddhā ca saptaite vijñeyāḥ kartṛhetavaḥa svaguṇaṃ bhakṣayanty ete guṇavantaḥ śubhāśubhamc ahaṃ ca nirguṇo treti saptaite mokṣahetavaḥa viduṣāṃ budhyamānānāṃ svaṃ svaṃ sthānaṃ yathāvidhic guṇās te devatābhūtāḥ satataṃ bhuñjate haviḥa adan hy avidvān annāni mamatvenopapadyatec ātmārthaṃ pācayan nityaṃ mamatvenopahanyatea abhakṣyabhakṣaṇaṃ caiva madyapānaṃ ca hanti tamc sa cānnaṃ hanti tac cānnaṃ sa hatvā hanyate budhaḥa attā hy annam idaṃ vidvān punar janayatīśvaraḥc sa cānnāj jāyate tasmin sūkṣmo nāma vyatikramaḥa manasā gamyate yac ca yac ca vācā nirudyatec śrotreṇa śrūyate yac ca cakṣuṣā yac ca dṛśyatea sparśena spṛśyate yac ca ghrāṇena ghrāyate ca yatc manaḥṣaṣṭhāni saṃyamya havīṃṣy etāni sarvaśaḥa guṇavatpāvako mahyaṃ dīpyate havyavāhanaḥc yogayajñaḥ pravṛtto me jñānabrahmamanodbhavaḥe prāṇastotro pānaśastraḥ sarvatyāgasudakṣiṇaḥa karmānumantā brahmā me kartādhvaryuḥ kṛtastutiḥc kṛtapraśāstā tac chāstram apavargo sya dakṣiṇāa ṛcaś cāpy atra śaṃsanti nārāyaṇavido janāḥc nārāyaṇāya devāya yad abadhnan paśūn purāa tatra sāmāni gāyanti tāni cāhur nidarśanamc devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ bhīru sarvātmānaṃ nibodha me brāhmaṇa uvācaa ekaḥ śāstā na dvitīyo sti śāstāyathā niyukto smi tathā carāmia yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmic hṛdy eṣa tiṣṭhan puruṣaḥ śāsti śāstātenaiva yuktaḥ pravaṇād ivodakama eko gurur nāsti tato dvitīyoyo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmic tenānuśiṣṭā guruṇā sadaivaparābhūtā dānavāḥ sarva evaa eko bandhur nāsti tato dvitīyoyo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmic tenānuśiṣṭā bāndhavā bandhumantaḥsaptarṣayaḥ sapta divi prabhāntia ekaḥ śrotā nāsti tato dvitīyoyo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmic tasmin gurau guruvāsaṃ niruṣyaśakro gataḥ sarvalokāmaratvama eko dveṣṭā nāsti tato dvitīyoyo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmic tenānuśiṣṭā guruṇā sadaivalokadviṣṭāḥ pannagāḥ sarva evaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc prajāpatau pannagānāṃ devarṣīṇāṃ ca saṃvidama devarṣayaś ca nāgāś ca asurāś ca prajāpatimc paryapṛcchann upāsīnāḥ śreyo naḥ procyatām itia teṣāṃ provāca bhagavāñ śreyaḥ samanupṛcchatāmc om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma te śrutvā prādravan diśaḥa teṣāṃ prādravamāṇānām upadeśārtham ātmanaḥc sarpāṇāṃ daśane bhāvaḥ pravṛttaḥ pūrvam eva tua asurāṇāṃ pravṛttas tu dambhabhāvaḥ svabhāvajaḥc dānaṃ devā vyavasitā damam eva maharṣayaḥa ekaṃ śāstāram āsādya śabdenaikena saṃskṛtāḥc nānā vyavasitāḥ sarve sarpadevarṣidānavāḥa śṛṇoty ayaṃ procyamānaṃ gṛhṇāti ca yathātathamc pṛcchatas tāvato bhūyo gurur anyo numanyatea tasya cānumate karma tataḥ paścāt pravartatec gurur boddhā ca śatruś ca dveṣṭā ca hṛdi saṃśritaḥa pāpena vicaraṃl loke pāpacārī bhavaty ayamc śubhena vicaraṃl loke śubhacārī bhavaty utaa kāmacārī tu kāmena ya indriyasukhe rataḥc vratavārī sadaivaiṣa ya indriyajaye rataḥa apetavratakarmā tu kevalaṃ brahmaṇi śritaḥc brahmabhūtaś caraṃl loke brahmacārī bhavaty ayama brahmaiva samidhas tasya brahmāgnir brahmasaṃstaraḥc āpo brahma gurur brahma sa brahmaṇi samāhitaḥa etad etādṛśaṃ sūkṣmaṃ brahmacaryaṃ vidur budhāḥc viditvā cānvapadyanta kṣetrajñenānudarśinaḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa saṃkalpadaṃśamaśakaṃ śokaharṣahimātapamc mohāndhakāratimiraṃ lobhavyālasarīsṛpama viṣayaikātyayādhvānaṃ kāmakrodhavirodhakamc tad atītya mahādurgaṃ praviṣṭo smi mahad vanam brāhmaṇy uvācaa kva tad vanaṃ mahāprājña ke vṛkṣāḥ saritaś ca kāḥc girayaḥ parvatāś caiva kiyaty adhvani tad vanam brāhmaṇa uvācaa na tad asti pṛthagbhāve kiṃ cid anyat tataḥ samamc na tad asty apṛthagbhāve kiṃ cid dūrataraṃ tataḥa tasmād dhrasvataraṃ nāsti na tato sti bṛhattaramc nāsti tasmād duḥkhataraṃ nāsty anyat tatsamaṃ sukhama na tat praviśya śocanti na prahṛṣyanti ca dvijāḥc na ca bibhyati keṣāṃ cit tebhyo bibhyati ke ca naa tasmin vane sapta mahādrumāś caphalāni saptātithayaś ca saptac saptāśramāḥ sapta samādhayaś cadīkṣāś ca saptaitad araṇyarūpama pañcavarṇāni divyāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama suvarṇāni dvivarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama caturvarṇāni divyāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama śaṃkarāṇi trivarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama surabhīṇy ekavarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama bahūny avyaktavarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cac visṛjantau mahāvṛkṣau tad vanaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhataḥd visṛjanto mahāvṛkṣā vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanama eko hy agniḥ sumanā brāhmaṇo trapañcendriyāṇi samidhaś cātra santic tebhyo mokṣāḥ sapta bhavanti dīkṣāguṇāḥ phalāny atithayaḥ phalāśāḥa ātithyaṃ pratigṛhṇanti tatra sapta maharṣayaḥc arciteṣu pralīneṣu teṣv anyad rocate vanama pratijñāvṛkṣam aphalaṃ śānticchāyāsamanvitamc jñānāśrayaṃ tṛptitoyam antaḥkṣetrajñabhāskarama ye dhigacchanti tat santas teṣāṃ nāsti bhayaṃ punaḥc ūrdhvaṃ cāvāk ca tiryak ca tasya nānto dhigamyatea sapta striyas tatra vasanti sadyoavāṅmukhā bhānumatyo janitryaḥc ūrdhvaṃ rasānāṃ dadate prajābhyaḥsarvān yathā sarvam anityatāṃ caa tatraiva pratitiṣṭhanti punas tatrodayanti cac sapta saptarṣayaḥ siddhā vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sahaa yaśo varco bhagaś caiva vijayaḥ siddhitejasīc evam evānuvartante sapta jyotīṃṣi bhāskarama girayaḥ parvatāś caiva santi tatra samāsataḥc nadyaś ca sarito vāri vahantyo brahmasaṃbhavama nadīnāṃ saṃgamas tatra vaitānaḥ samupahvarec svātmatṛptā yato yānti sākṣād dāntāḥ pitāmahama kṛśāśāḥ suvratāśāś ca tapasā dagdhakilbiṣāḥc ātmany ātmānam āveśya brahmāṇaṃ samupāsatea ṛcam apy atra śaṃsanti vidyāraṇyavido janāḥc tad araṇyam abhipretya yathādhīram ajāyataa etad etādṛśaṃ divyam araṇyaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥc viditvā cānvatiṣṭhanta kṣetrajñenānudarśitam brāhmaṇa uvācaa gandhān na jighrāmi rasān na vedmirūpaṃ na paśyāmi na ca spṛśāmic na cāpi śabdān vividhāñ śṛṇomina cāpi saṃkalpam upaimi kiṃ cita arthān iṣṭān kāmayate svabhāvaḥsarvān dveṣyān pradviṣate svabhāvaḥc kāmadveṣāv udbhavataḥ svabhāvātprāṇāpānau jantudehān niveśyaa tebhyaś cānyāṃs teṣv anityāṃś ca bhāvānbhūtātmānaṃ lakṣayeyaṃ śarīrec tasmiṃs tiṣṭhan nāsmi śakyaḥ kathaṃ citkāmakrodhābhyāṃ jarayā mṛtyunā caa akāmayānasya ca sarvakāmānavidviṣāṇasya ca sarvadoṣānc na me svabhāveṣu bhavanti lepāstoyasya bindor iva puṣkareṣuc naujaṃ tu dehāni tathā sametya sica nityasya caitasya bhavanti nityānirīkṣamāṇasya bahūn svabhāvānc na sajjate karmasu bhogajālaṃdivīva sūryasya mayūkhajālama atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc adhvaryuyatisaṃvādaṃ taṃ nibodha yaśasvinia prokṣyamāṇaṃ paśuṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñakarmaṇy athābravītc yatir adhvaryum āsīno hiṃseyam iti kutsayana tam adhvaryuḥ pratyuvāca nāyaṃ chāgo vinaśyatic śreyasā yokṣyate jantur yadi śrutir iyaṃ tathāa yo hy asya pārthivo bhāgaḥ pṛthivīṃ sa gamiṣyatic yad asya vārijaṃ kiṃ cid apas tat pratipadyatea sūryaṃ cakṣur diśaḥ śrotre prāṇo sya divam eva cac āgame vartamānasya na me doṣo sti kaś cana yatir uvācaa prāṇair viyoge chāgasya yadi śreyaḥ prapaśyasic chāgārthe vartate yajño bhavataḥ kiṃ prayojanama anu tvā manyatāṃ mātā pitā bhrātā sakhāpi cac mantrayasvainam unnīya paravantaṃ viśeṣataḥa ya evam anumanyeraṃs tān bhavān praṣṭum arhatic teṣām anumataṃ śrutvā śakyā kartuṃ vicāraṇāa prāṇā apy asya chāgasya prāpitās te svayoniṣuc śarīraṃ kevalaṃ śiṣṭaṃ niśceṣṭam iti me matiḥa indhanasya tu tulyena śarīreṇa vicetasāc hiṃsā nirveṣṭukāmānām indhanaṃ paśusaṃjñitama ahiṃsā sarvadharmāṇām iti vṛddhānuśāsanamc yad ahiṃsraṃ bhavet karma tat kāryam iti vidmahea ahiṃseti pratijñeyaṃ yadi vakṣyāmy ataḥ paramc śakyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vaktuṃ bhavataḥ kāryadūṣaṇama ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ nityam asmāsu rocatec pratyakṣataḥ sādhayāmo na parokṣam upāsmahe adhvaryur uvācaa bhūmer gandhaguṇān bhuṅkṣe pibasy āpomayān rasānc jyotiṣāṃ paśyase rūpaṃ spṛśasy anilajān guṇāna śṛṇoṣy ākāśajaṃ śabdaṃ manasā manyase matimc sarvāṇy etāni bhūtāni prāṇā iti ca manyasea prāṇādāne ca nityo si hiṃsāyāṃ vartate bhavānc nāsti ceṣṭā vinā hiṃsāṃ kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase dvija yatir uvācaa akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva dvaidhībhāvo yam ātmanaḥc akṣaraṃ tatra sadbhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṣara ucyatea prāṇo jihvā manaḥ sattvaṃ svabhāvo rajasā sahac bhāvair etair vimuktasya nirdvaṃdvasya nirāśiṣaḥa samasya sarvabhūteṣu nirmamasya jitātmanaḥc samantāt parimuktasya na bhayaṃ vidyate kva cit adhvaryur uvācaa sadbhir eveha saṃvāsaḥ kāryo matimatāṃ varac bhavato hi mataṃ śrutvā pratibhāti matir mamaa bhagavan bhagavadbuddhyā pratibuddho bravīmy ahamc mataṃ mantuṃ kratuṃ kartuṃ nāparādho sti me dvija brāhmaṇa uvācaa upapattyā yatis tūṣṇīṃ vartamānas tataḥ paramc adhvaryur api nirmohaḥ pracacāra mahāmakhea evam etādṛśaṃ mokṣaṃ susūkṣmaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥc viditvā cānutiṣṭhanti kṣetrajñenānudarśinā brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc kārtavīryasya saṃvādaṃ samudrasya ca bhāminia kārtavīryārjuno nāma rājā bāhusahasravānc yena sāgaraparyantā dhanuṣā nirjitā mahīa sa kadā cit samudrānte vicaran baladarpitaḥc avākirac charaśataiḥ samudram iti naḥ śrutama taṃ samudro namaskṛtya kṛtāñjalir uvāca hac mā muñca vīra nārācān brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi tea madāśrayāṇi bhūtāni tvadvisṛṣṭair maheṣubhiḥc vadhyante rājaśārdūla tebhyo dehy abhayaṃ vibho arjuna uvācaa matsamo yadi saṃgrāme śarāsanadharaḥ kva citc vidyate taṃ mamācakṣva yaḥ samāsīta māṃ mṛdhe samudra uvācaa maharṣir jamadagnis te yadi rājan pariśrutaḥc tasya putras tavātithyaṃ yathāvat kartum arhatia tataḥ sa rājā prayayau krodhena mahatā vṛtaḥc sa tam āśramam āgamya rāmam evānvapadyataa sa rāmapratikūlāni cakāra saha bandhubhiḥc āyāsaṃ janayām āsa rāmasya ca mahātmanaḥa tatas tejaḥ prajajvāla rāmasyāmitatejasaḥc pradahad ripusainyāni tadā kamalalocanea tataḥ paraśum ādāya sa taṃ bāhusahasriṇamc ciccheda sahasā rāmo bāhuśākham iva drumama taṃ hataṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sametāḥ sarvabāndhavāḥc asīn ādāya śaktīś ca bhārgavaṃ paryavārayana rāmo pi dhanur ādāya ratham āruhya satvaraḥc visṛjañ śaravarṣāṇi vyadhamat pārthivaṃ balama tatas tu kṣatriyāḥ ke cij jamadagniṃ nihatya cac viviśur giridurgāṇi mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā ivaa teṣāṃ svavihitaṃ karma tadbhayān nānutiṣṭhatāmc prajā vṛṣalatāṃ prāptā brāhmaṇānām adarśanāta ta ete dramiḍāḥ kāśāḥ puṇḍrāś ca śabaraiḥ sahac vṛṣalatvaṃ parigatā vyutthānāt kṣatradharmataḥa tatas tu hatavīrāsu kṣatriyāsu punaḥ punaḥc dvijair utpāditaṃ kṣatraṃ jāmadagnyo nyakṛntataa ekaviṃśatimedhānte rāmaṃ vāg aśarīriṇīc divyā provāca madhurā sarvalokapariśrutāa rāma rāma nivartasva kaṃ guṇaṃ tāta paśyasic kṣatrabandhūn imān prāṇair viprayojya punaḥ punaḥa tathaiva taṃ mahātmānam ṛcīkapramukhās tadāc pitāmahā mahābhāga nivartasvety athābruvana pitur vadham amṛṣyaṃs tu rāmaḥ provāca tān ṛṣīnc nārhantīha bhavanto māṃ nivārayitum ity uta pitara ūcuḥa nārhase kṣatrabandhūṃs tvaṃ nihantuṃ jayatāṃ varac na hi yuktaṃ tvayā hantuṃ brāhmaṇena satā nṛpān pitara ūcuḥa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc śrutvā ca tat tathā kāryaṃ bhavatā dvijasattamaa alarko nāma rājarṣir abhavat sumahātapāḥc dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca mahātmā sumahāvrataḥa sa sāgarāntāṃ dhanuṣā vinirjitya mahīm imāmc kṛtvā suduṣkaraṃ karma manaḥ sūkṣme samādadhea sthitasya vṛkṣamūle tha tasya cintā babhūva hac utsṛjya sumahad rājyaṃ sūkṣmaṃ prati mahāmate alarka uvācaa manaso me balaṃ jātaṃ mano jitvā dhruvo jayaḥc anyatra bāṇān asyāmi śatrubhiḥ parivāritaḥa yad idaṃ cāpalān mūrteḥ sarvam etac cikīrṣatic manaḥ prati sutīkṣṇāgrān ahaṃ mokṣyāmi sāyakān mana uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasia anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravītd indriyārtheṣu sarveṣu buddhis teṣv iha gṛdhyatid tasmād buddhiṃ prati śarān atimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān alarka uvācaa āghrāya subahūn gandhāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyatic tasmād ghrāṇaṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān ghrāṇa uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasia anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt alarka uvācaa iyaṃ svādūn rasān bhuktvā tān eva pratigṛdhyatic tasmāj jihvāṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān jihvovācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasia anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt alarka uvācaa spṛṣṭvā tvag vividhān sparśāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyatic tasmāt tvacaṃ pāṭayiṣye vividhaiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ tvag uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasia anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt alarka uvācaa śrutvā vai vividhāñ śabdāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyatic tasmāc chrotraṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān śrotra uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti tato hāsyasi jīvitama anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt alarka uvācaa dṛṣṭvā vai vividhān bhāvāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyatic tasmāc cakṣuḥ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān cakṣur uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasia anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasic tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt alarka uvācaa iyaṃ niṣṭhā bahuvidhā prajñayā tv adhyavasyatic tasmād buddhiṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān buddhir uvācaa neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ canac tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasid anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi pitara ūcuḥa tato larkas tapo ghoram āsthāyātha suduṣkaramc nādhyagacchat paraṃ śaktyā bāṇam eteṣu saptasue susamāhitacetās tu tato cintayata prabhuḥa sa vicintya ciraṃ kālam alarko dvijasattamac nādhyagacchat paraṃ śreyo yogān matimatāṃ varaḥa sa ekāgraṃ manaḥ kṛtvā niścalo yogam āsthitaḥc indriyāṇi jaghānāśu bāṇenaikena vīryavāne yogenātmānam āviśya saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ yayaua vismitaś cāpi rājarṣir imāṃ gāthāṃ jagāda hac aho kaṣṭaṃ yad asmābhiḥ pūrvaṃ rājyam anuṣṭhitamd bhogatṛṣṇāsamāyuktaiḥ pūrvaṃ rājyam upāsitame iti paścān mayā jñātaṃ yogān nāsti paraṃ sukhama iti tvam api jānīhi rāma mā kṣatriyāñ jahic tapo ghoram upātiṣṭha tataḥ śreyo bhipatsyase brāhmaṇa uvācaa ity uktaḥ sa tapo ghoraṃ jāmadagnyaḥ pitāmahaiḥc āsthitaḥ sumahābhāgo yayau siddhiṃ ca durgamāmd ity uktaḥ pitṛbhiḥ so tha tapo ghoraṃ samāsthitaḥd jāmadagnyo mahābhāgaḥ siddhiṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa trayo vai ripavo loke nava vai guṇataḥ smṛtāḥc harṣaḥ stambho bhimānaś ca trayas te sāttvikā guṇāḥa śokaḥ krodho tisaṃrambho rājasās te guṇāḥ smṛtāḥc svapnas tandrī ca mohaś ca trayas te tāmasā guṇāḥa etān nikṛtya dhṛtimān bāṇasaṃghair atandritaḥc jetuṃ parān utsahate praśāntātmā jitendriyaḥa atra gāthāḥ kīrtayanti purākalpavido janāḥc ambarīṣeṇa yā gītā rājñā rājyaṃ praśāsatāa samudīrṇeṣu doṣeṣu vadhyamāneṣu sādhuṣuc jagrāha tarasā rājyam ambarīṣa iti śrutiḥa sa nigṛhya mahādoṣān sādhūn samabhipūjya cac jagāma mahatīṃ siddhiṃ gāthāṃ cemāṃ jagāda haa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ me jitā doṣā nihatāḥ sarvaśatravaḥc eko doṣo vaśiṣṭas tu vadhyaḥ sa na hato mayāa yena yukto jantur ayaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ nādhigacchatic tṛṣṇārta iva nimnāni dhāvamāno na budhyatea akāryam api yeneha prayuktaḥ sevate naraḥc taṃ lobham asibhis tīkṣṇair nikṛntantaṃ nikṛntataa lobhād dhi jāyate tṛṣṇā tataś cintā prasajyatec sa lipsamāno labhate bhūyiṣṭhaṃ rājasān guṇānd tad avāptau tu labhate bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tāmasān guṇānd etair doṣaiḥ punar dehī badhyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥd bhuktvā vai rājasān bhogāñ jāyate karma cehatea sa tair guṇaiḥ saṃhatadehabandhanaḥpunaḥ punar jāyati karma cehatec janmakṣaye bhinnavikīrṇadehaḥpunar mṛtyuṃ gacchati janmani svea tasmād enaṃ samyag avekṣya lobhaṃnigṛhya dhṛtyātmani rājyam icchetc etad rājyaṃ nānyad astīti vidyādyas tv atra rājā vijito mamaikaḥa iti rājñāmbarīṣeṇa gāthā gītā yaśasvināc ādhirājyaṃ puraskṛtya lobham ekaṃ nikṛntatā brāhmaṇa uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc brāhmaṇasya ca saṃvādaṃ janakasya ca bhāminia brāhmaṇaṃ janako rājā sannaṃ kasmiṃś cid āgamec viṣaye me na vastavyam iti śiṣṭyartham abravīta ity uktaḥ pratyuvācātha brāhmaṇo rājasattamamc ācakṣva viṣayaṃ rājan yāvāṃs tava vaśe sthitaḥa so nyasya viṣaye rājño vastum icchāmy ahaṃ vibhoc vacas te kartum icchāmi yathāśāstraṃ mahīpatea ity uktaḥ sa tadā rājā brāhmaṇena yaśasvināc muhur uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya na sa taṃ pratyabhāṣataa tam āsīnaṃ dhyāyamānaṃ rājānam amitaujasamc kaśmalaṃ sahasāgacchad bhānumantam iva grahaḥa samāśvāsya tato rājā vyapete kaśmale tadāc tato muhūrtād iva taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vākyam abravīta pitṛpaitāmahe rājye vaśye janapade satic viṣayaṃ nādhigacchāmi vicinvan pṛthivīm imāma nādhyagacchaṃ yadā pṛthvyāṃ mithilā mārgitā mayāc nādhyagacchaṃ yadā tasyāṃ svaprajā mārgitā mayāa nādhyagacchaṃ yadā tāsu tadā me kaśmalo bhavatc tato me kaśmalasyānte matiḥ punar upasthitāa tayā na viṣayaṃ manye sarvo vā viṣayo mamac ātmāpi cāyaṃ na mama sarvā vā pṛthivī mamad yathā mama tathānyeṣām iti manye dvijottamae uṣyatāṃ yāvad utsāho bhujyatāṃ yāvad iṣyatea pitṛpaitāmahe rājye vaśye janapade satic brūhi kāṃ buddhim āsthāya mamatvaṃ varjitaṃ tvayāa kāṃ vā buddhiṃ viniścitya sarvo vai viṣayas tavac nāvaiṣi viṣayaṃ yena sarvo vā viṣayas tava janaka uvācaa antavanta ihārambhā viditāḥ sarvakarmasuc nādhyagaccham ahaṃ yasmān mamedam iti yad bhaveta kasyedam iti kasya svam iti vedavacas tathāc nādhyagaccham ahaṃ buddhyā mamedam iti yad bhaveta etāṃ buddhiṃ viniścitya mamatvaṃ varjitaṃ mayāc śṛṇu buddhiṃ tu yāṃ jñātvā sarvatra viṣayo mamaa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi gandhān ghrāṇagatān apic tasmān me nirjitā bhūmir vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadāa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi rasān āsye pi vartataḥc āpo me nirjitās tasmād vaśe tiṣṭhanti nityadāa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi rūpaṃ jyotiś ca cakṣuṣāc tasmān me nirjitaṃ jyotir vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadāa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi sparśāṃs tvaci gatāś ca yec tasmān me nirjito vāyur vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadāa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi śabdāñ śrotragatān apic tasmān me nirjitāḥ śabdā vaśe tiṣṭhanti nityadāa nāham ātmārtham icchāmi mano nityaṃ manontarec mano me nirjitaṃ tasmād vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadāa devebhyaś ca pitṛbhyaś ca bhūtebhyo tithibhiḥ sahac ityarthaṃ sarva eveme samārambhā bhavanti vaia tataḥ prahasya janakaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ punar abravītc tvajjijñāsārtham adyeha viddhi māṃ dharmam āgatama tvam asya brahmanābhasya buddhyārasyānivartinaḥc sattvaneminiruddhasya cakrasyaikaḥ pravartakaḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaa nāhaṃ tathā bhīru carāmi loketathā tvaṃ māṃ tarkayase svabuddhyāc vipro smi mukto smi vanecaro smigṛhasthadharmā brahmacārī tathāsmia nāham asmi yathā māṃ tvaṃ paśyase cakṣuṣā śubhec mayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ yat kiṃ cij jagatīgatama ye ke cij jantavo loke jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāś ca hac teṣāṃ mām antakaṃ viddhi dārūṇām iva pāvakama rājyaṃ pṛthivyāṃ sarvasyām atha vāpi triviṣṭapec tathā buddhir iyaṃ vetti buddhir eva dhanaṃ mamaa ekaḥ panthā brāhmaṇānāṃ yena gacchanti tadvidaḥc gṛheṣu vanavāseṣu guruvāseṣu bhikṣuṣue liṅgair bahubhir avyagrair ekā buddhir upāsyatea nānāliṅgāśramasthānāṃ yeṣāṃ buddhiḥ śamātmikāc te bhāvam ekam āyānti saritaḥ sāgaraṃ yathāa buddhyāyaṃ gamyate mārgaḥ śarīreṇa na gamyatec ādyantavanti karmāṇi śarīraṃ karmabandhanama tasmāt te subhage nāsti paralokakṛtaṃ bhayamc madbhāvabhāvaniratā mamaivātmānam eṣyasi brāhmaṇy uvācaa nedam alpātmanā śakyaṃ vedituṃ nākṛtātmanāc bahu cālpaṃ ca saṃkṣiptaṃ viplutaṃ ca mataṃ mamaa upāyaṃ tu mama brūhi yenaiṣā labhyate matiḥc tan manye kāraṇatamaṃ yata eṣā pravartate brāhmaṇa uvācaa araṇīṃ brāhmaṇīṃ viddhi gurur asyottarāraṇiḥc tapaḥśrute bhimathnīto jñānāgnir jāyate tataḥ brāhmaṇy uvācaa yad idaṃ brahmaṇo liṅgaṃ kṣetrajñam iti saṃjñitamc grahītuṃ yena tac chakyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya tat kva nu brāhmaṇa uvācaa aliṅgo nirguṇaś caiva kāraṇaṃ nāsya vidyatec upāyam eva vakṣyāmi yena gṛhyeta vā na vāa samyag apy upadiṣṭaś ca bhramarair iva lakṣyatec karmabuddhir abuddhitvāj jñānaliṅgair ivāśritama idaṃ kāryam idaṃ neti na mokṣeṣūpadiśyatec paśyataḥ śṛṇvato buddhir ātmano yeṣu jāyatea yāvanta iha śakyeraṃs tāvato ṃśān prakalpayetc vyaktān avyaktarūpāṃś ca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa sarvān nānātvayuktāṃś ca sarvān pratyakṣahetukānc yataḥ paraṃ na vidyeta tato bhyāse bhaviṣyati vāsudeva uvācaa tatas tu tasyā brāhmaṇyā matiḥ kṣetrajñasaṃkṣayec kṣetrajñād eva parataḥ kṣetrajño nyaḥ pravartate arjuna uvācaa kva nu sā brāhmaṇī kṛṣṇa kva cāsau brāhmaṇarṣabhaḥc yābhyāṃ siddhir iyaṃ prāptā tāv ubhau vada me cyuta vāsudeva uvācaa mano me brāhmaṇaṃ viddhi buddhiṃ me viddhi brāhmaṇīmc kṣetrajña iti yaś coktaḥ so ham eva dhanaṃjaya arjuna uvācaa brahma yat paramaṃ vedyaṃ tan me vyākhyātum arhasic bhavato hi prasādena sūkṣme me ramate matiḥ vāsudeva uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc saṃvādaṃ mokṣasaṃyuktaṃ śiṣyasya guruṇā sahaa kaś cid brāhmaṇam āsīnam ācāryaṃ saṃśitavratamc śiṣyaḥ papraccha medhāvī kiṃ svic chreyaḥ paraṃtapaa bhagavantaṃ prapanno haṃ niḥśreyasaparāyaṇaḥc yāce tvāṃ śirasā vipra yad brūyāṃ tad vicakṣva mea tam evaṃvādinaṃ pārtha śiṣyaṃ gurur uvāca hac kathayasva pravakṣyāmi yatra te saṃśayo dvijaa ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭha guruṇā guruvatsalaḥc prāñjaliḥ paripapraccha yat tac chṛṇu mahāmate śiṣya uvācaa kutaś cāhaṃ kutaś ca tvaṃ tat satyaṃ brūhi yat paramc kuto jātāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi caa kena jīvanti bhūtāni teṣām āyuḥ kim ātmakamc kiṃ satyaṃ kiṃ tapo vipra ke guṇāḥ sadbhir īritāḥe ke panthānaḥ śivāḥ santi kiṃ sukhaṃ kiṃ ca duṣkṛtama etān me bhagavan praśnān yāthātathyena sattamac vaktum arhasi viprarṣe yathāvad iha tattvataḥd tvad anyaḥ kaś ca na praśnān etān vaktum ihārhatid brūhi dharmavidāṃ śreṣṭha paraṃ kautūhalaṃ mamad mokṣadharmārthakuśalo bhavāṃl lokeṣu gīyated sarvasaṃśayasaṃchettā tvad anyo na ca vidyated saṃsārabhīravaś caiva mokṣakāmās tathā vayam vāsudeva uvācaa tasmai saṃpratipannāya yathāvat paripṛcchatec śiṣyāya guṇayuktāya śāntāya guruvartinee chāyābhūtāya dāntāya yataye brahmacāriṇee kulīnāya suśīlāya bhaktāya brahmavādinea tān praśnān abravīt pārtha medhāvī sa dhṛtavrataḥc guruḥ kurukulaśreṣṭha samyak sarvān ariṃdamaa brahmaproktam idaṃ dharmam ṛṣipravarasevitamc vedavidyāsamāvāpyaṃ tattvabhūtārthabhāvanamd jñānaṃ tv eva paraṃ vidmaḥ saṃnyāsaṃ tapa uttamamd yas tu veda nirābādhaṃ jñānatattvaṃ viniścayātd sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sa sarvagatir iṣyated yo vidvān sahavāsaṃ ca vivāsaṃ caiva paśyatid tathaivaikatvanānātve sa duḥkhāt parimucyated yo na kāmayate kiṃ cin na kiṃ cid abhimanyated ihalokastha evaiṣa brahmabhūyāya kalpated pradhānaguṇatattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtavidhānavitd nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥd avyaktabījaprabhavo buddhiskandhamayo mahānd mahāhaṃkāraviṭapa indriyāṅkurakoṭaraḥd mahābhūtaviśeṣaś ca viśeṣapratiśākhavānd sadāparṇaḥ sadāpuṣpaḥ sadāśubhaphalodayaḥd ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmabījaḥ sanātanaḥd etaj jñātvā ca tattvena jñānena parāmāsinād chittvā cāmaratāṃ prāpya jahāti mṛtyujanmanīa bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyādidharmakāmārthaniścayamc siddhasaṃghaparijñātaṃ purākalpaṃ sanātanama pravakṣye haṃ mahāprājña padam uttamam adya tec buddhvā yad iha saṃsiddhā bhavantīha manīṣiṇaḥa upagamyarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ jijñāsantaḥ parasparamc bṛhaspatibharadvājau gautamo bhārgavas tathāa vasiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapaś caiva viśvāmitro trir eva cac mārgān sarvān parikramya pariśrāntāḥ svakarmabhiḥa ṛṣim āṅgirasaṃ vṛddhaṃ puraskṛtya tu te dvijāḥc dadṛśur brahmabhavane brahmāṇaṃ vītakalmaṣama taṃ praṇamya mahātmānaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ maharṣayaḥc papracchur vinayopetā niḥśreyasam idaṃ parama kathaṃ karma kriyāt sādhu kathaṃ mucyeta kilbiṣātc ke no mārgāḥ śivāś ca syuḥ kiṃ satyaṃ kiṃ ca duṣkṛtama kenobhau karmapanthānau mahattvaṃ kena vindatic pralayaṃ cāpavargaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayaua ity uktaḥ sa muniśreṣṭhair yad āha prapitāmahaḥc tat te haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇu śiṣya yathāgamam brahmovācaa satyād bhūtāni jātāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi cac tapasā tāni jīvanti iti tad vitta suvratāḥa svāṃ yoniṃ punar āgamya vartante svena karmaṇāc satyaṃ hi guṇasaṃyuktaṃ niyataṃ pañcalakṣaṇama brahma satyaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ caiva prajāpatiḥc satyād bhūtāni jātāni bhūtaṃ satyamayaṃ mahata tasmāt satyāśrayā viprā nityaṃ yogaparāyaṇāḥc atītakrodhasaṃtāpā niyatā dharmasetavaḥa anyonyaniyatān vaidyān dharmasetupravartakānc tān ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śāśvatān lokabhāvanāna cāturvidyaṃ tathā varṇāṃś caturaś cāśramān pṛthakc dharmam ekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ nityam āhur manīṣiṇaḥa panthānaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śivaṃ kṣemakaraṃ dvijāḥc niyataṃ brahmabhāvāya yātaṃ pūrvaṃ manīṣibhiḥa gadatas taṃ mamādyeha panthānaṃ durvidaṃ paramc nibodhata mahābhāgā nikhilena paraṃ padama brahmacārikam evāhur āśramaṃ prathamaṃ padamc gārhasthyaṃ tu dvitīyaṃ syād vānaprastham ataḥ parame tataḥ paraṃ tu vijñeyam adhyātmaṃ paramaṃ padama jyotir ākāśam ādityo vāyur indraḥ prajāpatiḥc nopaiti yāvad adhyātmaṃ tāvad etān na paśyatie tasyopāyaṃ pravakṣyāmi purastāt taṃ nibodhataa phalamūlānilabhujāṃ munīnāṃ vasatāṃ vanec vānaprasthaṃ dvijātīnāṃ trayāṇām upadiśyatea sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ gārhasthyaṃ tad vidhīyatec śraddhālakṣaṇam ity evaṃ dharmaṃ dhīrāḥ pracakṣated naiṣṭhiko tha yatir vāpi vibhakto brahmacāriṇaḥa ity ete devayānā vaḥ panthānaḥ parikīrtitāḥc sadbhir adhyāsitā dhīraiḥ karmabhir dharmasetavaḥa eteṣāṃ pṛthag adhyāste yo dharmaṃ saṃśitavrataḥc kālāt paśyati bhūtānāṃ sadaiva prabhavāpyayaua atas tattvāni vakṣyāmi yāthātathyena hetunāc viṣayasthāni sarvāṇi vartamānāni bhāgaśaḥa mahān ātmā tathāvyaktam ahaṃkāras tathaiva cac indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca mahābhūtāni pañca caa viśeṣāḥ pañcabhūtānām ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥc caturviṃśatir eṣā vas tattvānāṃ saṃprakīrtitāa tattvānām atha yo veda sarveṣāṃ prabhavāpyayauc sa dhīraḥ sarvabhūteṣu na moham adhigacchatia tattvāni yo vedayate yathātathaṃguṇāṃś ca sarvān akhilāś ca devatāḥc vidhūtapāpmā pravimucya bandhanaṃsa sarvalokān amalān samaśnute brahmovācaa tad avyaktam anudriktaṃ sarvavyāpi dhruvaṃ sthiramc navadvāraṃ puraṃ vidyāt triguṇaṃ pañcadhātukama ekādaśaparikṣepaṃ mano vyākaraṇātmakamc buddhisvāmikam ity etat param ekādaśaṃ bhaveta trīṇi srotāṃsi yāny asminn āpyāyante punaḥ punaḥc praṇāḍyas tisra evaitāḥ pravartante guṇātmikāḥa tamo rajas tathā sattvaṃ guṇān etān pracakṣatec anyonyamithunāḥ sarve tathānyonyānujīvinaḥa anyonyāpāśrayāś caiva tathānyonyānuvartinaḥc anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca triguṇāḥ pañca dhātavaḥa tamaso mithunaṃ sattvaṃ sattvasya mithunaṃ rajaḥc rajasaś cāpi sattvaṃ syāt sattvasya mithunaṃ tamaḥa niyamyate tamo yatra rajas tatra pravartatec niyamyate rajo yatra sattvaṃ tatra pravartatea naiśātmakaṃ tamo vidyāt triguṇaṃ mohasaṃjñitamc adharmalakṣaṇaṃ caiva niyataṃ pāpakarmasud tāmasaṃ rūpam etat tu dṛśyate cāpi saṃgatama pravṛttyātmakam evāhū rajaḥ paryāyakārakamc pravṛttaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dṛśyatotpattilakṣaṇama prakāśaṃ sarvabhūteṣu lāghavaṃ śraddadhānatāc sāttvikaṃ rūpam evaṃ tu lāghavaṃ sādhusaṃmitama eteṣāṃ guṇatattvaṃ hi vakṣyate hetvahetubhiḥc samāsavyāsayuktāni tattvatas tāni vitta mea saṃmoho jñānam atyāgaḥ karmaṇām avinirṇayaḥc svapnaḥ stambho bhayaṃ lobhaḥ śokaḥ sukṛtadūṣaṇama asmṛtiś cāvipākaś ca nāstikyaṃ bhinnavṛttitāc nirviśeṣatvam andhatvaṃ jaghanyaguṇavṛttitāa akṛte kṛtamānitvam ajñāne jñānamānitāc amaitrī vikṛto bhāvo aśraddhā mūḍhabhāvanāa anārjavam asaṃjñatvaṃ karma pāpam acetanāc gurutvaṃ sannabhāvatvam asitatvam avāg gatiḥa sarva ete guṇā viprās tāmasāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥc ye cānye niyatā bhāvā loke smin mohasaṃjñitāḥa tatra tatra niyamyante sarve te tāmasā guṇāḥc parivādakathā nityaṃ devabrāhmaṇavaidikāḥa atyāgaś cābhimānaś ca moho manyus tathākṣamāc matsaraś caiva bhūteṣu tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyatea vṛthārambhāś ca ye ke cid vṛthādānāni yāni cac vṛthābhakṣaṇam ity etat tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyatea ativādo titikṣā ca mātsaryam atimānitāc aśraddadhānatā caiva tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyatea evaṃvidhās tu ye ke cil loke smin pāpakarmiṇaḥc manuṣyā bhinnamaryādāḥ sarve te tāmasā janāḥa teṣāṃ yoniṃ pravakṣyāmi niyatāṃ pāpakarmaṇāmc avāṅnirayabhāvāya tiryaṅnirayagāminaḥa sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni paśavo vāhanāni cac kravyādā dandaśūkāś ca kṛmikīṭavihaṃgamāḥa aṇḍajā jantavo ye ca sarve cāpi catuṣpadāḥc unmattā badhirā mūkā ye cānye pāparogiṇaḥa magnās tamasi durvṛttāḥ svakarmakṛtalakṣaṇāḥc avāksrotasa ity ete magnās tamasi tāmasāḥa teṣām utkarṣam udrekaṃ vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ paramc yathā te sukṛtāṃl lokāṃl labhante puṇyakarmiṇaḥa anyathā pratipannās tu vivṛddhā ye ca karmasuc svakarmaniratānāṃ ca brāhmaṇānāṃ śubhaiṣiṇāma saṃskāreṇordhvam āyānti yatamānāḥ salokatāmc svargaṃ gacchanti devānām ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥa anyathā pratipannās tu vivṛddhāḥ sveṣu karmasuc punarāvṛttidharmāṇas te bhavantīha mānuṣāḥa pāpayoniṃ samāpannāś caṇḍālā mūkacūcukāḥc varṇān paryāyaśaś cāpi prāpnuvanty uttarottarama śūdrayonim atikramya ye cānye tāmasā guṇāḥc srotomadhye samāgamya vartante tāmase guṇea abhiṣaṅgas tu kāmeṣu mahāmoha iti smṛtaḥc ṛṣayo munayo devā muhyanty atra sukhepsavaḥa tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisraḥ krodhasaṃjñitaḥc maraṇaṃ tv andhatāmisraṃ tāmisraṃ krodha ucyatea bhāvato guṇataś caiva yonitaś caiva tattvataḥc sarvam etat tamo viprāḥ kīrtitaṃ vo yathāvidhia ko nv etad budhyate sādhu ko nv etat sādhu paśyatic atattve tattvadarśī yas tamasas tattvalakṣaṇama tamoguṇā vo bahudhā prakīrtitāyathāvad uktaṃ ca tamaḥ parāvaramc naro hi yo veda guṇān imān sadāsa tāmasaiḥ sarvaguṇaiḥ pramucyate brahmovācaa rajo haṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi yāthātathyena sattamāḥc nibodhata mahābhāgā guṇavṛttaṃ ca sarvaśaḥa saṃghāto rūpam āyāsaḥ sukhaduḥkhe himātapauc aiśvaryaṃ vigrahaḥ saṃdhir hetuvādo ratiḥ kṣamāa balaṃ śauryaṃ mado roṣo vyāyāmakalahāv apic īrṣyepsā paiśunaṃ yuddhaṃ mamatvaṃ paripālanama vadhabandhaparikleśāḥ krayo vikraya eva cac nikṛnta chindhi bhindhīti paramarmāvakartanama ugraṃ dāruṇam ākrośaḥ paravittānuśāsanamc lokacintā vicintā ca matsaraḥ paribhāṣaṇama mṛṣāvādo mṛṣādānaṃ vikalpaḥ paribhāṣaṇamc nindā stutiḥ praśaṃsā ca pratāpaḥ paritarpaṇama paricaryā ca śuśrūṣā sevā tṛṣṇā vyapāśrayaḥc vyūho nayaḥ pramādaś ca paritāpaḥ parigrahaḥa saṃskārā ye ca loke smin pravartante pṛthak pṛthakc nṛṣu nārīṣu bhūteṣu dravyeṣu śaraṇeṣu caa saṃtāpo pratyayaś caiva vratāni niyamāś ca yec pradānam āśīryuktaṃ ca satataṃ me bhavatv itid āśīryuktāni karmāṇi paurtāni vividhāni caa svadhākāro namaskāraḥ svāhākāro vaṣaṭkriyāc yājanādhyāpane cobhe tathaivāhuḥ parigrahamd dānaṃ pratigrahaś caiva prāyaścittāni maṅgalama idaṃ me syād idaṃ me syāt sneho guṇasamudbhavaḥc abhidrohas tathā māyā nikṛtir māna eva caa stainyaṃ hiṃsā parīvādaḥ paritāpaḥ prajāgaraḥc stambho dambho tha rāgaś ca bhaktiḥ prītiḥ pramodanama dyūtaṃ ca janavādaś ca saṃbandhāḥ strīkṛtāś ca yec nṛttavāditragītāni prasaṅgā ye ca ke canae sarva ete guṇā viprā rājasāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥa bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ bhuvi bhāvanāḥc trivarganiratā nityaṃ dharmo rthaḥ kāma ity apia kāmavṛttāḥ pramodante sarvakāmasamṛddhibhiḥc arvāksrotasa ity ete taijasā rajasāvṛtāḥa asmiṃl loke pramodante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥc pretyabhāvikam īhanta iha laukikam eva cad pretyabhāvakarīṃ siddhim īhante rājasā janāḥe dadati pratigṛhṇanti japanty atha ca juhvatia rajoguṇā vo bahudhānukīrtitāyathāvad uktaṃ guṇavṛttam eva cac naro hi yo veda guṇān imān sadāsa rājasaiḥ sarvaguṇair vimucyate brahmovācaa ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tṛtīyaṃ guṇam uttamamc sarvabhūtahitaṃ loke satāṃ dharmam aninditama ānandaḥ prītir udrekaḥ prākāśyaṃ sukham eva cac akārpaṇyam asaṃrambhaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ śraddadhānatāa kṣamā dhṛtir ahiṃsā ca samatā satyam ārjavamc akrodhaś cānasūyā ca śaucaṃ dākṣyaṃ parākramaḥa mudhā jñānaṃ mudhā vṛttaṃ mudhā sevā mudhā śramaḥc evaṃ yo yuktadharmaḥ syāt so mutrānantyam aśnutea nirmamo nirahaṃkāro nirāśīḥ sarvataḥ samaḥc akāmahata ity eṣa satāṃ dharmaḥ sanātanaḥa viśrambho hrīs titikṣā ca tyāgaḥ śaucam atandritāc ānṛśaṃsyam asaṃmoho dayā bhūteṣv apaiśunama harṣas tuṣṭir vismayaś ca vinayaḥ sādhuvṛttatāc śāntikarma viśuddhiś ca śubhā buddhir vimocanama upekṣā brahmacaryaṃ ca parityāgaś ca sarvaśaḥc nirmamatvam anāśīstvam aparikrītadharmatāa mudhā dānaṃ mudhā yajño mudhādhītaṃ mudhā vratamc mudhā pratigrahaś caiva mudhā dharmo mudhā tapaḥa evaṃvṛttās tu ye ke cil loke smin sattvasaṃśrayāḥc brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthās te dhīrāḥ sādhudarśinaḥa hitvā sarvāṇi pāpāni niḥśokā hy ajarāmarāḥc divaṃ prāpya tu te dhīrāḥ kurvate vai tatas tataḥa īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca laghutvaṃ manasaś ca tec vikurvate mahātmāno devās tridivagā ivaa ūrdhvasrotasa ity ete devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥc vikurvate prakṛtyā vai divaṃ prāptās tatas tataḥe yad yad icchanti tat sarvaṃ bhajante vibhajanti caa ity etat sāttvikaṃ vṛttaṃ kathitaṃ vo dvijarṣabhāḥc etad vijñāya vidhival labhate yad yad icchatia prakīrtitāḥ sattvaguṇā viśeṣatoyathāvad uktaṃ guṇavṛttam eva cac naras tu yo veda guṇān imān sadāguṇān sa bhuṅkte na guṇaiḥ sa bhujyate brahmovācaa naiva śakyā guṇā vaktuṃ pṛthaktveneha sarvaśaḥc avicchinnāni dṛśyante rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamas tathāa anyonyam anuṣajjante anyonyaṃ cānujīvinaḥc anyonyāpāśrayāḥ sarve tathānyonyānuvartinaḥa yāvat sattvaṃ tamas tāvad vartate nātra saṃśayaḥc yāvat tamaś ca sattvaṃ ca rajas tāvad ihocyatea saṃhatya kurvate yātrāṃ sahitāḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥc saṃghātavṛttayo hy ete vartante hetvahetubhiḥa udrekavyatirekāṇāṃ teṣām anyonyavartināmc vartate tad yathānyūnaṃ vyatiriktaṃ ca sarvaśaḥa vyatiriktaṃ tamo yatra tiryagbhāvagataṃ bhavetc alpaṃ tatra rajo jñeyaṃ sattvaṃ cālpataraṃ tataḥa udriktaṃ ca rajo yatra madhyasrotogataṃ bhavetc alpaṃ tatra tamo jñeyaṃ sattvaṃ cālpataraṃ tataḥa udriktaṃ ca yadā sattvam ūrdhvasrotogataṃ bhavetc alpaṃ tatra rajo jñeyaṃ tamaś cālpataraṃ tataḥa sattvaṃ vaikārikaṃ yonir indriyāṇāṃ prakāśikāc na hi sattvāt paro bhāvaḥ kaś cid anyo vidhīyatea ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti sattvasthā madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥc jaghanyaguṇasaṃyuktā yānty adhas tāmasā janāḥa tamaḥ śūdre rajaḥ kṣatre brāhmaṇe sattvam uttamamc ity evaṃ triṣu varṇeṣu vivartante guṇās trayaḥa dūrād api hi dṛśyante sahitāḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥc tamaḥ sattvaṃ rajaś caiva pṛthaktvaṃ nānuśuśrumaa dṛṣṭvā cādityam udyantaṃ kucorāṇāṃ bhayaṃ bhavetc adhvagāḥ paritapyeraṃs tṛṣṇārtā duḥkhabhāginaḥa ādityaḥ sattvam uddiṣṭaṃ kucorās tu yathā tamaḥc paritāpo dhvagānāṃ ca rājaso guṇa ucyatea prākāśyaṃ sattvam āditye saṃtāpo rājaso guṇaḥc upaplavas tu vijñeyas tāmasas tasya parvasua evaṃ jyotiḥṣu sarveṣu vivartante guṇās trayaḥc paryāyeṇa ca vartante tatra tatra tathā tathāa sthāvareṣu ca bhūteṣu tiryagbhāvagataṃ tamaḥc rājasās tu vivartante snehabhāvas tu sāttvikaḥa ahas tridhā tu vijñeyaṃ tridhā rātrir vidhīyatec māsārdhamāsavarṣāṇi ṛtavaḥ saṃdhayas tathāa tridhā dānāni dīyante tridhā yajñaḥ pravartatec tridhā lokās tridhā vedās tridhā vidyās tridhā gatiḥa bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca dharmo rthaḥ kāma ity apic prāṇāpānāv udānaś cāpy eta eva trayo guṇāḥa yat kiṃ cid iha vai loke sarvam eṣv eva tat triṣuc trayo guṇāḥ pravartante avyaktā nityam eva tue sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva guṇasargaḥ sanātanaḥa tamo vyaktaṃ śivaṃ nityam ajaṃ yoniḥ sanātanaḥc prakṛtir vikāraḥ pralayaḥ pradhānaṃ prabhavāpyayaua anudriktam anūnaṃ ca hy akampam acalaṃ dhruvamc sad asac caiva tat sarvam avyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ smṛtame jñeyāni nāmadheyāni narair adhyātmacintakaiḥa avyaktanāmāni guṇāṃś ca tattvatoyo veda sarvāṇi gatīś ca kevalāḥc vimuktadehaḥ pravibhāgatattvavitsa mucyate sarvaguṇair nirāmayaḥ brahmovācaa avyaktāt pūrvam utpanno mahān ātmā mahāmatiḥc ādir guṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prathamaḥ sarga ucyatea mahān ātmā matir viṣṇur viśvaḥ śaṃbhuś ca vīryavānc buddhiḥ prajñopalabdhiś ca tathā khyātir dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥa paryāyavācakaiḥ śabdair mahān ātmā vibhāvyatec taṃ jānan brāhmaṇo vidvān na pramohaṃ nigacchatia sarvataḥpāṇipādaś ca sarvatokṣiśiromukhaḥc sarvataḥśrutimāṃl loke sarvaṃ vyāpya sa tiṣṭhatia mahāprabhārciḥ puruṣaḥ sarvasya hṛdi niśritaḥc aṇimā laghimā prāptir īśāno jyotir avyayaḥa tatra buddhimatāṃ lokāḥ saṃnyāsaniratāś ca yec dhyānino nityayogāś ca satyasaṃdhā jitendriyāḥa jñānavantaś ca ye ke cid alubdhā jitamanyavaḥc prasannamanaso dhīrā nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥe vimuktāḥ sarva evaite mahattvam upayānti vaia ātmano mahato veda yaḥ puṇyāṃ gatim uttamāmc sa dhīraḥ sarvalokeṣu na moham adhigacchatie viṣṇur evādisargeṣu svayaṃbhūr bhavati prabhuḥa evaṃ hi yo veda guhāśayaṃ prabhuṃnaraḥ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ viśvarūpamc hiraṇmayaṃ buddhimatāṃ parāṃ gatiṃsa buddhimān buddhim atītya tiṣṭhati brahmovācaa ya utpanno mahān pūrvam ahaṃkāraḥ sa ucyatec aham ity eva saṃbhūto dvitīyaḥ sarga ucyatea ahaṃkāraś ca bhūtādir vaikārika iti smṛtaḥc tejasaś cetanā dhātuḥ prajāsargaḥ prajāpatiḥa devānāṃ prabhavo devo manasaś ca trilokakṛtc aham ity eva tat sarvam abhimantā sa ucyatea adhyātmajñānanityānāṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanāmc svādhyāyakratusiddhānām eṣa lokaḥ sanātanaḥa ahaṃkāreṇāharato guṇān imānbhūtādir evaṃ sṛjate sa bhūtakṛtc vaikārikaḥ sarvam idaṃ viceṣṭatesvatejasā rañjayate jagat tathā brahmovācaa ahaṃkārāt prasūtāni mahābhūtāni pañca vaic pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotiś ca pañcamama teṣu bhūtāni muhyante mahābhūteṣu pañcasuc śabdasparśanarūpeṣu rasagandhakriyāsu caa mahābhūtavināśānte pralaye pratyupasthitec sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ dhīrā mahad utpadyate bhayama yady asmāj jāyate bhūtaṃ tatra tat pravilīyatec līyante pratilomāni jāyante cottarottarama tataḥ pralīne sarvasmin bhūte sthāvarajaṅgamec smṛtimantas tadā dhīrā na līyante kadā canaa śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥc kriyākāraṇayuktāḥ syur anityā mohasaṃjñitāḥa lobhaprajanasaṃyuktā nirviśeṣā hy akiṃcanāḥc māṃsaśoṇitasaṃghātā anyonyasyopajīvinaḥa bahir ātmāna ity ete dīnāḥ kṛpaṇavṛttayaḥc prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samāno vyāna eva caa antarātmeti cāpy ete niyatāḥ pañca vāyavaḥc vāṅmanobuddhir ity ebhiḥ sārdham aṣṭātmakaṃ jagata tvagghrāṇaśrotracakṣūṃṣi rasanaṃ vāk ca saṃyatāc viśuddhaṃ ca mano yasya buddhiś cāvyabhicāriṇīa aṣṭau yasyāgnayo hy ete na dahante manaḥ sadāc sa tad brahma śubhaṃ yāti yasmād bhūyo na vidyatea ekādaśa ca yāny āhur indriyāṇi viśeṣataḥc ahaṃkāraprasūtāni tāni vakṣyāmy ahaṃ dvijāḥa śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamīc pādau pāyur upasthaṃ ca hastau vāg daśamī bhaveta indriyagrāma ity eṣa mana ekādaśaṃ bhavetc etaṃ grāmaṃ jayet pūrvaṃ tato brahma prakāśatea buddhīndriyāṇi pañcāhuḥ pañca karmendriyāṇi cac śrotrādīny api pañcāhur buddhiyuktāni tattvataḥa aviśeṣāṇi cānyāni karmayuktāni tāni tuc ubhayatra mano jñeyaṃ buddhir dvādaśamī bhaveta ity uktānīndriyāṇīmāny ekādaśa mayā kramātc manyante kṛtam ity eva viditvaitāni paṇḍitāḥd ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvaṃ vividham indriyama trīṇi sthānāni bhūtānāṃ caturthaṃ nopapadyatec sthalam āpas tathākāśaṃ janma cāpi caturvidhama aṇḍajodbhijjasaṃsvedajarāyujam athāpi cac caturdhā janma ity etad bhūtagrāmasya lakṣyatea acarāṇy api bhūtāni khecarāṇi tathaiva cac aṇḍajāni vijānīyāt sarvāṃś caiva sarīsṛpāna saṃsvedāḥ kṛmayaḥ proktā jantavaś ca tathāvidhāḥc janma dvitīyam ity etaj jaghanyataram ucyatea bhittvā tu pṛthivīṃ yāni jāyante kālaparyayātc udbhijjānīti tāny āhur bhūtāni dvijasattamāḥa dvipādabahupādāni tiryaggatimatīni cac jarāyujāni bhūtāni vitta tāny api sattamāḥa dvividhāpīha vijñeyā brahmayoniḥ sanātanāc tapaḥ karma ca yat puṇyam ity eṣa viduṣāṃ nayaḥa dvividhaṃ karma vijñeyam ijyā dānaṃ ca yan makhec jātasyādhyayanaṃ puṇyam iti vṛddhānuśāsanama etad yo veda vidhivat sa muktaḥ syād dvijarṣabhāḥc vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhya iti caiva nibodhataa ākāśaṃ prathamaṃ bhūtaṃ śrotram adhyātmam ucyatec adhibhūtaṃ tathā śabdo diśas tatrādhidaivatama dvitīyaṃ māruto bhūtaṃ tvag adhyātmaṃ ca viśrutamc spraṣṭavyam adhibhūtaṃ ca vidyut tatrādhidaivatama tṛtīyaṃ jyotir ity āhuś cakṣur adhyātmam ucyatec adhibhūtaṃ tato rūpaṃ sūryas tatrādhidaivatama caturtham āpo vijñeyaṃ jihvā cādhyātmam iṣyateb raso dhibhūtaṃ vijñeyam āpas tatrādhidaivatamc adhibhūtaṃ rasaś cātra somas tatrādhidaivatama pṛthivī pañcamaṃ bhūtaṃ ghrāṇaś cādhyātmam iṣyatec adhibhūtaṃ tathā gandho vāyus tatrādhidaivatama eṣa pañcasu bhūteṣu catuṣṭayavidhiḥ smṛtaḥc ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvaṃ trividham indriyama pādāv adhyātmam ity āhur brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥc adhibhūtaṃ tu gantavyaṃ viṣṇus tatrādhidaivatama avāggatir apānaś ca pāyur adhyātmam iṣyatec adhibhūtaṃ visargaś ca mitras tatrādhidaivatama prajanaḥ sarvabhūtānām upastho dhyātmam ucyatec adhibhūtaṃ tathā śukraṃ daivataṃ ca prajāpatiḥa hastāv adhyātmam ity āhur adhyātmaviduṣo janāḥc adhibhūtaṃ tu karmāṇi śakras tatrādhidaivatama vaiśvadevī manaḥpūrvā vāg adhyātmam ihocyatec vaktavyam adhibhūtaṃ ca vahnis tatrādhidaivatama adhyātmaṃ mana ity āhuḥ pañcabhūtānucārakamc adhibhūtaṃ ca mantavyaṃ candramāś cādhidaivatamd ahaṃkāras tathādhyātmaṃ sarvasaṃsārakārakamd abhimāno dhibhūtaṃ ca rudras tatrādhidaivatama adhyātmaṃ buddhir ity āhuḥ ṣaḍindriyavicāriṇīc adhibhūtaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ brahmā tatrādhidaivatama yathāvad adhyātmavidhir eṣa vaḥ kīrtito mayāc jñānam asya hi dharmajñāḥ prāptaṃ buddhimatām ihaa indriyāṇīndriyārthāś ca mahābhūtāni pañca cac sarvāṇy etāni saṃdhāya manasā saṃpradhārayeta kṣīṇe manasi sarvasmin na janmasukham iṣyatec jñānasaṃpannasattvānāṃ tat sukhaṃ viduṣāṃ matama ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sūkṣmabhāvakarīṃ śivāmc nivṛttiṃ sarvabhūteṣu mṛdunā dāruṇena vāa guṇāguṇam anāsaṅgam ekacaryam anantaramc etad brāhmaṇato vṛttam āhur ekapadaṃ sukhama vidvān kūrma ivāṅgāni kāmān saṃhṛtya sarvaśaḥc virajāḥ sarvato mukto yo naraḥ sa sukhī sadāa kāmān ātmani saṃyamya kṣīṇatṛṣṇaḥ samāhitaḥc sarvabhūtasuhṛn maitro brahmabhūyaṃ sa gacchatia indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena sarveṣāṃ viṣayaiṣiṇāmc muner janapadatyāgād adhyātmāgniḥ samidhyatea yathāgnir indhanair iddho mahājyotiḥ prakāśatec tathendriyanirodhena mahān ātmā prakāśatea yadā paśyati bhūtāni prasannātmātmano hṛdib etad eva hi loke smin mano hṛdi samāśritamc svayaṃyonis tadā sūkṣmāt sūkṣmam āpnoty anuttamama agnī rūpaṃ payaḥ sroto vāyuḥ sparśanam eva cac mahī paṅkadharaṃ ghoram ākāśaṃ śravaṇaṃ tathād dṛśyam ādityam evāhur adhyātmaviduṣo janāḥa rāgaśokasamāviṣṭaṃ pañcasrotaḥsamāvṛtamc pañcabhūtasamāyuktaṃ navadvāraṃ dvidaivatama rajasvalam athādṛśyaṃ triguṇaṃ ca tridhātukamc saṃsargābhirataṃ mūḍhaṃ śarīram iti dhāraṇāa duścaraṃ jīvaloke smin sattvaṃ prati samāśritamc etad eva hi loke smin kālacakraṃ pravartatea etan mahārṇavaṃ ghoram agādhaṃ mohasaṃjñitamc visṛjet saṃkṣipec caiva bodhayet sāmaraṃ jagata kāmakrodhau bhayaṃ moham abhidroham athānṛtamc indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena sa tāṃs tyajati dustyajāna yasyaite nirjitā loke triguṇāḥ pañca dhātavaḥc vyomni tasya paraṃ sthānam anantam atha lakṣyatea kāmakūlām apārāntāṃ manaḥsrotobhayāvahāmb pañcendriyamahākūlāṃ manovegamahodakāmc nadīṃ durgahradāṃ tīrṇaḥ kāmakrodhāv ubhau jayeta sa sarvadoṣanirmuktas tataḥ paśyati yat paramc mano manasi saṃdhāya paśyaty ātmānam ātmania sarvavit sarvabhūteṣu vīkṣaty ātmānam ātmanic ekadhā bahudhā caiva vikurvāṇas tatas tataḥa dhruvaṃ paśyati rūpāṇi dīpād dīpaśataṃ yathāc sa vai viṣṇuś ca mitraś ca varuṇo gniḥ prajāpatiḥa sa hi dhātā vidhātā ca sa prabhuḥ sarvatomukhaḥc hṛdayaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ mahān ātmā prakāśatea taṃ viprasaṃghāś ca surāsurāś cayakṣāḥ piśācāḥ pitaro vayāṃsic rakṣogaṇā bhūtagaṇāś ca sarvemaharṣayaś caiva sadā stuvanti brahmovācaa manuṣyāṇāṃ tu rājanyaḥ kṣatriyo madhyamo guṇaḥc kuñjaro vāhanānāṃ ca siṃhaś cāraṇyavāsināma aviḥ paśūnāṃ sarveṣām ākhuś ca bilavāsināmc gavāṃ govṛṣabhaś caiva strīṇāṃ puruṣa eva caa nyagrodho jambuvṛkṣaś ca pippalaḥ śālmalis tathāc śiṃśapā meṣaśṛṅgaś ca tathā kīcakaveṇavaḥe ete drumāṇāṃ rājāno loke smin nātra saṃśayaḥa himavān pāriyātraś ca sahyo vindhyas trikūṭavānc śveto nīlaś ca bhāsaś ca kāṣṭhavāṃś caiva parvataḥa śubhaskandho mahendraś ca mālyavān parvatas tathāc ete parvatarājāno gaṇānāṃ marutas tathāa sūryo grahāṇām adhipo nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥc yamaḥ pitṝṇām adhipaḥ saritām atha sāgaraḥa ambhasāṃ varuṇo rājā sattvānāṃ mitra ucyatec arko dhipatir uṣṇānāṃ jyotiṣām indur ucyatea agnir bhūtapatir nityaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ bṛhaspatiḥc oṣadhīnāṃ patiḥ somo viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥa tvaṣṭādhirājo rūpāṇāṃ paśūnām īśvaraḥ śivaḥc dakṣiṇānāṃ tathā yajño vedānām ṛṣayas tathāa diśām udīcī viprāṇāṃ somo rājā pratāpavānc kuberaḥ sarvayakṣāṇāṃ devatānāṃ puraṃdaraḥe eṣa bhūtādikaḥ sargaḥ prajānāṃ ca prajāpatiḥa sarveṣām eva bhūtānām ahaṃ brahmamayo mahānc bhūtaṃ parataraṃ matto viṣṇor vāpi na vidyatea rājādhirājaḥ sarvāsāṃ viṣṇur brahmamayo mahānc īśvaraṃ taṃ vijānīmaḥ sa vibhuḥ sa prajāpatiḥa narakiṃnarayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasāmc devadānavanāgānāṃ sarveṣām īśvaro hi saḥa bhagadevānuyātānāṃ sarvāsāṃ vāmalocanāc māheśvarī mahādevī procyate pārvatīti yāa umāṃ devīṃ vijānīta nārīṇām uttamāṃ śubhāmc ratīnāṃ vasumatyas tu strīṇām apsarasas tathāa dharmakāmāś ca rājāno brāhmaṇā dharmalakṣaṇāḥc tasmād rājā dvijātīnāṃ prayateteha rakṣaṇea rājñāṃ hi viṣaye yeṣām avasīdanti sādhavaḥc hīnās te svaguṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ pretyāvāṅmārgagāminaḥa rājñāṃ tu viṣaye yeṣāṃ sādhavaḥ parirakṣitāḥc te smiṃl loke pramodante pretya cānantyam eva cae prāpnuvanti mahātmāna iti vitta dvijarṣabhāḥa ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi niyataṃ dharmalakṣaṇamc ahiṃsālakṣaṇo dharmo hiṃsā cādharmalakṣaṇāa prakāśalakṣaṇā devā manuṣyāḥ karmalakṣaṇāḥc śabdalakṣaṇam ākāśaṃ vāyus tu sparśalakṣaṇaḥa jyotiṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ rūpam āpaś ca rasalakṣaṇāḥc dharaṇī sarvabhūtānāṃ pṛthivī gandhalakṣaṇāa svaravyañjanasaṃskārā bhāratī satyalakṣaṇāc manaso lakṣaṇaṃ cintā tathoktā buddhir anvayāta manasā cintayāno rthān buddhyā caiva vyavasyatic buddhir hi vyavasāyena lakṣyate nātra saṃśayaḥa lakṣaṇaṃ mahato dhyānam avyaktaṃ sādhulakṣaṇamc pravṛttilakṣaṇo yogo jñānaṃ saṃnyāsalakṣaṇama tasmāj jñānaṃ puraskṛtya saṃnyased iha buddhimānc saṃnyāsī jñānasaṃyuktaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatime atīto dvaṃdvam abhyeti tamomṛtyujarātigama dharmalakṣaṇasaṃyuktam uktaṃ vo vidhivan mayāc guṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ samyag vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ parama pārthivo yas tu gandho vai ghrāṇeneha sa gṛhyatec ghrāṇasthaś ca tathā vāyur gandhajñāne vidhīyatea apāṃ dhāturaso nityaṃ jihvayā sa tu gṛhyatec jihvāsthaś ca tathā somo rasajñāne vidhīyatea jyotiṣaś ca guṇo rūpaṃ cakṣuṣā tac ca gṛhyatec cakṣuḥsthaś ca tathādityo rūpajñāne vidhīyatea vāyavyas tu tathā sparśas tvacā prajñāyate ca saḥc tvaksthaś caiva tathā vāyuḥ sparśajñāne vidhīyatea ākāśasya guṇo ghoṣaḥ śrotreṇa sa tu gṛhyatec śrotrasthāś ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ śabdajñāne prakīrtitāḥa manasas tu guṇaś cintā prajñayā sa tu gṛhyatec hṛdisthacetanādhātur manojñāne vidhīyatea buddhir adhyavasāyena dhyānena ca mahāṃs tathāc niścitya grahaṇaṃ nityam avyaktaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥa aliṅgagrahaṇo nityaḥ kṣetrajño nirguṇātmakaḥc tasmād aliṅgaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kevalaṃ jñānalakṣaṇaḥa avyaktaṃ kṣetram uddiṣṭaṃ guṇānāṃ prabhavāpyayamc sadā paśyāmy ahaṃ līnaṃ vijānāmi śṛṇomi caa puruṣas tad vijānīte tasmāt kṣetrajña ucyatec guṇavṛttaṃ tathā kṛtsnaṃ kṣetrajñaḥ paripaśyatia ādimadhyāvasānāntaṃ sṛjyamānam acetanamc na guṇā vidur ātmānaṃ sṛjyamānaṃ punaḥ punaḥa na satyaṃ veda vai kaś cit kṣetrajñas tv eva vindatic guṇānāṃ guṇabhūtānāṃ yat paraṃ parato mahata tasmād guṇāṃś ca tattvaṃ ca parityajyeha tattvavitc kṣīṇadoṣo guṇān hitvā kṣetrajñaṃ praviśaty athaa nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvadhākāra eva cac acalaś cāniketaś ca kṣetrajñaḥ sa paro vibhuḥ brahmovācaa yad ādimadhyaparyantaṃ grahaṇopāyam eva cac nāmalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaṃ vakṣyāmi tattvataḥa ahaḥ pūrvaṃ tato rātrir māsāḥ śuklādayaḥ smṛtāḥc śraviṣṭhādīni ṛkṣāṇi ṛtavaḥ śiśirādayaḥa bhūmir ādis tu gandhānāṃ rasānām āpa eva cac rūpāṇāṃ jyotir ādis tu sparśādir vāyur ucyatee śabdasyādis tathākāśam eṣa bhūtakṛto guṇaḥa ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūtānām ādim uttamamc ādityo jyotiṣām ādir agnir bhūtādir iṣyatea sāvitrī sarvavidyānāṃ devatānāṃ prajāpatiḥc oṃkāraḥ sarvavedānāṃ vacasāṃ prāṇa eva cae yady asmin niyataṃ loke sarvaṃ sāvitram ucyatea gāyatrī chandasām ādiḥ paśūnām aja ucyatec gāvaś catuṣpadām ādir manuṣyāṇāṃ dvijātayaḥa śyenaḥ patatriṇām ādir yajñānāṃ hutam uttamamc parisarpiṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ sarpo dvijottamāḥa kṛtam ādir yugānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥc hiraṇyaṃ sarvaratnānām oṣadhīnāṃ yavās tathāa sarveṣāṃ bhakṣyabhojyānām annaṃ paramam ucyatec dravāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ peyānām āpa uttamāḥa sthāvarāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ sarveṣām aviśeṣataḥc brahmakṣetraṃ sadā puṇyaṃ plakṣaḥ prathamajaḥ smṛtaḥa ahaṃ prajāpatīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥc mama viṣṇur acintyātmā svayaṃbhūr iti sa smṛtaḥa parvatānāṃ mahāmeruḥ sarveṣām agrajaḥ smṛtaḥc diśāṃ ca pradiśāṃ cordhvā digjātā prathamaṃ tathāa tathā tripathagā gaṅgā nadīnām agrajā smṛtāc tathā sarodapānānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sāgaro grajaḥa devadānavabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasāmc narakiṃnarayakṣāṇāṃ sarveṣām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥa ādir viśvasya jagato viṣṇur brahmamayo mahānc bhūtaṃ parataraṃ tasmāt trailokye neha vidyatea āśramāṇāṃ ca gārhasthyaṃ sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥc lokānām ādir avyaktaṃ sarvasyāntas tad eva caa ahāny astamayāntāni udayāntā ca śarvarīc sukhasyāntaḥ sadā duḥkhaṃ duḥkhasyāntaḥ sadā sukhama sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥc saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitama sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ vināśāntaṃ jātasya maraṇaṃ dhruvamc aśāśvataṃ hi loke smin sarvaṃ śiṣṭācārasamāhitaḥc vaiṇavīṃ dhārayed yaṣṭiṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalumd trīṇi dhārayate nityaṃ kamaṇḍalum atandritaḥd ekam ācamanārthāya ekaṃ vai pādadhāvanamd ekaṃ śaucavidhānārtham ity etat tritayaṃ tathāa adhītyādhyāpanaṃ kuryāt tathā yajanayājanec dānaṃ pratigrahaṃ caiva ṣaḍguṇāṃ vṛttim ācareta trīṇi karmāṇi yānīha brāhmaṇānāṃ tu jīvikāc yājanādhyāpane cobhe śuddhāc cāpi pratigrahaḥa avaśeṣāṇi yajñopavītī svādhyāyī aluptaniyatavrataḥa pūtābhiś ca tathaivādbhiḥ sadā daivatatarpaṇamc bhāvena niyataḥ kurvan brahmacārī praśasyatea evaṃ yukto jayet svargam ūrdhvaretāḥ samāhitaḥc na saṃsarati na grāmaṃ praviśet punaḥa arcayann atithīn kāle dadyāc cāpi pratiśrayamc phalapatrāvarair mūlaiḥ śyāmākena ca vartayana pravṛttam udakaṃ vāyuṃ sarvaṃ vāneyam ā tṛṇātc prāśnīyād ānupūrvyeṇa yathādīkṣam atandritaḥa āmūlaphalabhikṣābhir arced atithim āgatamc yadbhakṣaḥ syāt tato dadyād bhikṣāṃ nityam atandritaḥa devatātithipūrvaṃ ca sadā bhuñjīta vāgyataḥc askanditamanāś caiva laghvāśī devatāśrayaḥa dānto maitraḥ kṣamāyuktaḥ keśaśmaśru ca dhārayanc juhvan svādhyāyaśīlaś ca satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥa tyaktadehaḥ sadā dakṣo vananityaḥ samāhitaḥc evaṃ yukto jayet svargaṃ vānaprastho jitendriyaḥa gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho tha vā punaḥc ya icchen mokṣam āsthātum uttamāṃ vṛttim āśrayeta abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dattvā naiṣkarmyam ācaretc sarvabhūtahito maitraḥ sarvendriyayato muniḥa ayācitam asaṃkḷptam upapannaṃ yadṛcchayāc joṣayeta sadā bhojyaṃ grāsam āgatam aspṛhaḥa yātrāmātraṃ ca bhuñjīta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikamc dharmalabdhaṃ tathāśnīyān na kāmam anuvartayeta grāsād ācchādanāc cānyan na gṛhṇīyāt kathaṃ canac yāvad āhārayet tāvat pratigṛhṇīta nānyathāa parebhyo na pratigrāhyaṃ na ca deyaṃ kadā canac dainyabhāvāc ca bhūtānāṃ saṃvibhajya sadā budhaḥa nādadīta parasvāni na gṛhṇīyād ayācitamc na kiṃ cid viṣayaṃ bhuktvā spṛhayet tasya vai punaḥa mṛdam āpas tathāśmānaṃ patrapuṣpaphalāni cac asaṃvṛtāni gṛhṇīyāt pravṛttānīha kāryavāna na śilpajīvikāṃ jīved dvirannaṃ nota kāmayetc na dveṣṭā nopadeṣṭā ca bhaveta nirupaskṛtaḥe śraddhāpūtāni bhuñjīta nimittāni vivarjayeta mudhāvṛttir asaktaś ca sarvabhūtair asaṃvidamc kṛtvā vahniṃ cared bhaikṣyaṃ vidhūme bhuktavajjanea vṛtte śarāvasaṃpāte bhaikṣyaṃ lipseta mokṣavitc lābhe na ca prahṛṣyeta nālābhe vimanā bhavetd na cātibhikṣāṃ bhikṣeta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikaḥa mātrāśī kālam ākāṅkṣaṃś cared bhaikṣyaṃ samāhitaḥc lābhaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ necchen na bhuñjītābhipūjitaḥe abhipūjitalābhād dhi vijugupseta bhikṣukaḥa śuktāny amlāni tiktāni kaṣāyakaṭukāni cac nāsvādayīta bhuñjāno rasāṃś ca madhurāṃs tathāe yātrāmātraṃ ca bhuñjīta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikama asaṃrodhena bhūtānāṃ vṛttiṃ lipseta mokṣavitc na cānyam anubhikṣeta bhikṣamāṇaḥ kathaṃ canaa na saṃnikāśayed dharmaṃ vivikte virajāś caretc śūnyāgāram araṇyaṃ vā vṛkṣamūlaṃ nadīṃ tathāe pratiśrayārthaṃ seveta pārvatīṃ vā punar guhāma grāmaikarātriko grīṣme varṣāsv ekatra vā vasetc adhvā sūryeṇa nirdiṣṭaḥ kīṭavac ca caren mahīma dayārthaṃ caiva bhūtānāṃ samīkṣya pṛthivīṃ caretc saṃcayāṃś ca na kurvīta snehavāsaṃ ca varjayeta pūtena cāmbhasā nityaṃ kāryaṃ kurvīta mokṣavitc upaspṛśed uddhṛtābhir adbhiś ca puruṣaḥ sadāa ahiṃsā brahmacaryaṃ ca satyam ārjavam eva cac akrodhaś cānasūyā ca damo nityam apaiśunama aṣṭāsv eteṣu yuktaḥ syād vrateṣu niyatendriyaḥc apāpam aśaṭhaṃ vṛttam ajihmaṃ nityam ācareta āśīryuktāni karmāṇi hiṃsāyuktāni yāni cac lokasaṃgrahadharmaṃ ca naiva kuryān na kārayeta sarvabhāvān atikramya laghumātraḥ parivrajetc samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu caa paraṃ nodvejayet kaṃ cin na ca kasya cid udvijetc viśvāsyaḥ sarvabhūtānām agryo mokṣavid ucyatea anāgataṃ ca na dhyāyen nātītam anucintayetc vartamānam upekṣeta kālākāṅkṣī samāhitaḥa na cakṣuṣā na manasā na vācā dūṣayet kva citc na pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā kiṃ cid duṣṭaṃ samācareta indriyāṇy upasaṃhṛtya kūrmo ṅgānīva sarvaśaḥc kṣīṇendriyamanobuddhir nirīkṣeta nirindriyaḥa nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvāhākāra eva cac nirmamo nirahaṃkāro niryogakṣema eva caa nirāśīḥ sarvabhūteṣu nirāsaṅgo nirāśrayaḥc sarvajñaḥ sarvato mukto mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥa apāṇipādapṛṣṭhaṃ tam aśiraskam anūdaramc prahīṇaguṇakarmāṇaṃ kevalaṃ vimalaṃ sthirama agandharasam asparśam arūpāśabdam eva cac atvagasthy atha vāmajjam amāṃsam api caiva haa niścintam avyayaṃ nityaṃ hṛdistham api nityadāc sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ ye paśyanti na te mṛtāḥa na tatra kramate buddhir nendriyāṇi na devatāḥc vedā yajñāś ca lokāś ca na tapo na parākramaḥe yatra jñānavatāṃ prāptir aliṅgagrahaṇā smṛtāa tasmād aliṅgo dharmajño dharmavratam anuvrataḥc gūḍhadharmāśrito vidvān ajñātacaritaṃ careta amūḍho mūḍharūpeṇa cared dharmam adūṣayanc yathainam avamanyeran pare satatam eva hia tathāvṛttaś cared dharmaṃ satāṃ vartmāvidūṣayanc yo hy evaṃ vṛttasaṃpannaḥ sa muniḥ śreṣṭha ucyatea indriyāṇīndriyārthāṃś ca mahābhūtāni pañca cac manobuddhir athātmānam avyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ tathāa sarvam etat prasaṃkhyāya samyak saṃtyajya nirmalaḥc tataḥ svargam avāpnoti vimuktaḥ sarvabandhanaiḥa etad evāntavelāyāṃ parisaṃkhyāya tattvavitc dhyāyed ekāntam āsthāya mucyate tha nirāśrayaḥa nirmuktaḥ sarvasaṅgebhyo vāyur ākāśago yathāc kṣīṇakośo nirātaṅkaḥ prāpnoti paramaṃ padam brahmovācaa saṃnyāsaṃ tapa ity āhur vṛddhā niścitadarśinaḥc brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthā jñānaṃ brahma paraṃ viduḥa avidūrāt paraṃ brahma vedavidyāvyapāśrayamc nirdvaṃdvaṃ nirguṇaṃ nityam acintyaṃ guhyam uttamama jñānena tapasā caiva dhīrāḥ paśyanti tat padamc nirṇiktatamasaḥ pūtā vyutkrāntarajaso malāḥa tapasā kṣemam adhvānaṃ gacchanti paramaiṣiṇaḥc saṃnyāsaniratā nityaṃ ye brahmaviduṣo janāḥa tapaḥ pradīpa ity āhur ācāro dharmasādhakaḥc jñānaṃ tv eva paraṃ vidma saṃnyāsas tapa uttamama yas tu veda nirābādhaṃ jñānaṃ tattvaviniścayātc sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sa sarvagatir iṣyatea yo vidvān sahavāsaṃ ca vivāsaṃ caiva paśyatic tathaivaikatvanānātve sa duḥkhāt parimucyatea yo na kāmayate kiṃ cin na kiṃ cid avamanyatec ihalokastha evaiṣa brahmabhūyāya kalpatea pradhānaguṇatattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtavidhānavitc nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥa nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvadhākāra eva cac nirguṇaṃ nityam advaṃdvaṃ praśamenaiva gacchatia hitvā guṇamayaṃ sarvaṃ karma jantuḥ śubhāśubhamc ubhe satyānṛte hitvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥa avyaktabījaprabhavo buddhiskandhamayo mahānc mahāhaṃkāraviṭapa indriyāntarakoṭaraḥa mahābhūtaviśākhaś ca viśeṣapratiśākhavānc sadāparṇaḥ sadāpuṣpaḥ śubhāśubhaphalodayaḥe ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥa etac chittvā ca bhittvā ca jñānena paramāsināc hitvā cāmaratāṃ prāpya jahyād vai mṛtyujanmanīd   tattvajñānāsinā budhaḥd hitvā saṅgamayān pāśān mṛtyujanmajarodayāne nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥa dvāv etau pakṣiṇau nityau sakhāyau cāpy acetanauc etābhyāṃ tu paro yasya cetanāvān iti smṛtaḥa acetanaḥ sattvasaṃghātayuktaḥsattvāt paraṃ cetayate ntarātmāc sa kṣetrajñaḥ sattvasaṃghātabuddhirguṇātigo mucyate mṛtyupāśāt brahmovācaa ke cid brahmamayaṃ vṛkṣaṃ ke cid brahmamayaṃ mahatc ke cit puruṣam avyaktaṃ ke cit param anāmayame manyante sarvam apy etad avyaktaprabhavāvyayama ucchvāsamātram api ced yo ntakāle samo bhavetc ātmānam upasaṃgamya so mṛtatvāya kalpatea nimeṣamātram api cet saṃyamyātmānam ātmanic gacchaty ātmaprasādena viduṣāṃ prāptim avyayāma prāṇāyāmair atha prāṇān saṃyamya sa punaḥ punaḥc daśadvādaśabhir vāpi caturviṃśāt paraṃ tataḥa evaṃ pūrvaṃ prasannātmā labhate yad yad icchatic avyaktāt sattvam udriktam amṛtatvāya kalpatea sattvāt parataraṃ nānyat praśaṃsantīha tadvidaḥc anumānād vijānīmaḥ puruṣaṃ sattvasaṃśrayame na śakyam anyathā gantuṃ puruṣaṃ tam atho dvijāḥa kṣamā dhṛtir ahiṃsā ca samatā satyam ārjavamc jñānaṃ tyāgo tha saṃnyāsaḥ sāttvikaṃ vṛttam iṣyatea etenaivānumānena manyante tha manīṣiṇaḥc sattvaṃ ca puruṣaś caikas tatra nāsti vicāraṇāa āhur eke ca vidvāṃso ye jñāne supratiṣṭhitāḥc kṣetrajñasattvayor aikyam ity etan nopapadyatea pṛthagbhūtas tato nityam ity etad avicāritamc pṛthagbhāvaś ca vijñeyaḥ sahajaś cāpi tattvataḥa tathaivaikatvanānātvam iṣyate viduṣāṃ nayaḥc maśakodumbare tv aikyaṃ pṛthaktvam api dṛśyatea matsyo yathānyaḥ syād apsu saṃprayogas tathānayoḥc saṃbandhas toyabindūnāṃ parṇe kokanadasya ca gurur uvācaa ity uktavantaṃ te viprās tadā lokapitāmahamc punaḥ saṃśayam āpannāḥ papracchur dvijasattamāḥ ṛṣaya ūcuḥa kiṃ svid eveha dharmāṇām anuṣṭheyatamaṃ smṛtamc vyāhatām iva paśyāmo dharmasya vividhāṃ gatima ūrdhvaṃ dehād vadanty eke naitad astīti cāparec ke cit saṃśayitaṃ sarvaṃ niḥsaṃśayam athāparea anityaṃ nityam ity eke nāsty astīty api cāparec ekarūpaṃ dvidhety eke vyāmiśram iti cāparee ekam eke pṛthak cānye bahutvam iti cāparea manyante brāhmaṇā evaṃ prājñās tattvārthadarśinaḥc jaṭājinadharāś cānye muṇḍāḥ ke cid asaṃvṛtāḥa asnānaṃ ke cid icchanti snānam ity api cāparec āhāraṃ ke cid icchanti ke cic cānaśane ratāḥa karma ke cit praśaṃsanti praśāntim api cāparec deśakālāv ubhau ke cin naitad astīti cāparee ke cin mokṣaṃ praśaṃsanti ke cid bhogān pṛthagvidhāna dhanāni ke cid icchanti nirdhanatvaṃ tathāparec upāsyasādhanaṃ tv eke naitad astīti cāparea ahiṃsāniratāś cānye ke cid dhiṃsāparāyaṇāḥc puṇyena yaśasety eke naitad astīti cāparea sadbhāvaniratāś cānye ke cit saṃśayite sthitāḥc duḥkhād anye sukhād anye dhyānam ity apare sthitāḥa yajñam ity apare dhīrāḥ pradānam iti cāparec sarvam eke praśaṃsanti na sarvam iti cāparea tapas tv anye praśaṃsanti svādhyāyam apare janāḥc jñānaṃ saṃnyāsam ity eke svabhāvaṃ bhūtacintakāḥa evaṃ vyutthāpite dharme bahudhā vipradhāvatic niścayaṃ nādhigacchāmaḥ saṃmūḍhāḥ surasattamaa idaṃ śreya idaṃ śreya ity evaṃ prasthito janaḥc yo hi yasmin rato dharme sa taṃ pūjayate sadāa tatra no vihatā prajñā manaś ca bahulīkṛtamc etad ākhyātum icchāmaḥ śreyaḥ kim iti sattamaa ataḥ paraṃ ca yad guhyaṃ tad bhavān vaktum arhatic sattvakṣetrajñayoś caiva saṃbandhaḥ kena hetunāa evam uktaḥ sa tair viprair bhagavāṃl lokabhāvanaḥc tebhyaḥ śaśaṃsa dharmātmā yāthātathyena buddhimān brahmovācaa hanta vaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yan māṃ pṛcchatha sattamāḥb guruṇā śiṣyam āsādya yad uktaṃ tan nibodhatac samastam iha tac chrutvā samyag evāvadhāryatāma ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānām etat kṛtyatamaṃ matamc etat padam anudvignaṃ variṣṭhaṃ dharmalakṣaṇama jñānaṃ niḥśreya ity āhur vṛddhā niścayadarśinaḥc tasmāj jñānena śuddhena mucyate sarvapātakaiḥa hiṃsāparāś ca ye loke ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥc lobhamohasamāyuktās te vai nirayagāminaḥa āśīryuktāni karmāṇi kurvate ye tv atandritāḥc te smiṃl loke pramodante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥa kurvate ye tu karmāṇi śraddadhānā vipaścitaḥc anāśīryogasaṃyuktās te dhīrāḥ sādhudarśinaḥa ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sattvakṣetrajñayor yathāc saṃyogo viprayogaś ca tan nibodhata sattamāḥa viṣayo viṣayitvaṃ ca saṃbandho yam ihocyatec viṣayī puruṣo nityaṃ sattvaṃ ca viṣayaḥ smṛtaḥa vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena maśakodumbaraṃ yathāc bhujyamānaṃ na jānīte nityaṃ sattvam acetaname yas tv eva tu vijānīte yo bhuṅkte yaś ca bhujyatea anityaṃ dvaṃdvasaṃyuktaṃ sattvam āhur guṇātmakamc nirdvaṃdvo niṣkalo nityaḥ kṣetrajño nirguṇātmakaḥa samaḥ saṃjñāgatas tv evaṃ yadā sarvatra dṛśyatec upabhuṅkte sadā sattvam āpaḥ puṣkaraparṇavata sarvair api guṇair vidvān vyatiṣakto na lipyatec jalabindur yathā lolaḥ padminīpatrasaṃsthitaḥe evam evāpy asaṃsaktaḥ puruṣaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥa dravyamātram abhūt sattvaṃ puruṣasyeti niścayaḥc yathā dravyaṃ ca kartā ca saṃyogo py anayos tathāa yathā pradīpam ādāya kaś cit tamasi gacchatic tathā sattvapradīpena gacchanti paramaiṣiṇaḥa yāvad dravyaguṇas tāvat pradīpaḥ saṃprakāśatec kṣīṇadravyaguṇaṃ jyotir antardhānāya gacchatia vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇas tv evaṃ puruṣo vyakta iṣyatec etad viprā vijānīta hanta bhūyo bravīmi vaḥa sahasreṇāpi durmedhā na vṛddhim adhigacchatib tat padaṃ samanuprāptaṃ yatra gatvā na śocatib tvam apy etan mahābhāga yathoktaṃ brahmavarcasāb vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇas tv evaṃ buddhimān sukham edhatec caturthenāpy athāṃśena buddhimān sukham edhatea evaṃ dharmasya vijñeyaṃ saṃsādhanam upāyataḥc upāyajño hi medhāvī sukham atyantam aśnutea yathādhvānam apātheyaḥ prapanno mānavaḥ kva citc kleśena yāti mahatā vinaśyaty antarāpi vāa tathā karmasu vijñeyaṃ phalaṃ bhavati vā na vāc puruṣasyātmaniḥśreyaḥ śubhāśubhanidarśanama yathā ca dīrgham adhvānaṃ padbhyām eva prapadyatec adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ sahasā tattvadarśanavarjitaḥa tam eva ca yathādhvānaṃ rathenehāśugāmināc yāyād aśvaprayuktena tathā buddhimatāṃ gatiḥa uccaṃ parvatam āruhya nānvavekṣeta bhūgatamc rathena rathinaṃ paśyet kliśyamānam acetanama yāvad rathapathas tāvad rathena sa tu gacchatic kṣīṇe rathapathe prājño ratham utsṛjya gacchatia evaṃ gacchati medhāvī tattvayogavidhānavitc samājñāya mahābuddhir uttarād uttarottarama yathā mahārṇavaṃ ghoram aplavaḥ saṃpragāhatec bāhubhyām eva saṃmohād vadhaṃ carcchaty asaṃśayama nāvā cāpi yathā prājño vibhāgajñas taritrayāc aklāntaḥ salilaṃ gāhet kṣipraṃ saṃtarati dhruvama tīrṇo gacchet paraṃ pāraṃ nāvam utsṛjya nirmamaḥc vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena yathā rathipadātinaua snehāt saṃmoham āpanno nāvi dāśo yathā tathāc mamatvenābhibhūtaḥ sa tatraiva parivartatea nāvaṃ na śakyam āruhya sthale viparivartitumc tathaiva ratham āruhya nāpsu caryā vidhīyatea evaṃ karma kṛtaṃ citraṃ viṣayasthaṃ pṛthak pṛthakc yathā karma kṛtaṃ loke tathā tad upapadyatea yan naiva gandhino rasyaṃ na rūpasparśaśabdavatc manyante munayo buddhyā tat pradhānaṃ pracakṣatec rasanaṃ rūpasaṃsparśaṃ śabdavan manyate manaḥc yat paraś ca tato buddhyāa tatra pradhānam avyaktam avyaktasya guṇo mahānc mahataḥ pradhānabhūtasya guṇo haṃkāra eva caa ahaṃkārapradhānasya mahābhūtakṛto guṇaḥc pṛthaktvena hi bhūtānāṃ viṣayā vai guṇāḥ smṛtāḥa bījadharmaṃ yathāvyaktaṃ tathaiva prasavātmakamc bījadharmā mahān ātmā prasavaś ceti naḥ śrutama bījadharmā tv ahaṃkāraḥ prasavaś ca punaḥ punaḥc bījaprasavadharmāṇi mahābhūtāni pañca vaia bījadharmiṇa ity āhuḥ prasavaṃ ca na kurvatec viśeṣāḥ pañcabhūtānāṃ teṣāṃ vittaṃ viśeṣaṇama tatraikaguṇam ākāśaṃ dviguṇo vāyur ucyatec triguṇaṃ jyotir ity āhur āpaś cāpi caturguṇāḥa pṛthvī pañcaguṇā jñeyā trasasthāvarasaṃkulāc sarvabhūtakarī devī śubhāśubhanidarśanāa śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥc ete pañca guṇā bhūmer vijñeyā dvijasattamāḥa pārthivaś ca sadā gandho gandhaś ca bahudhā smṛtaḥc tasya gandhasya vakṣyāmi vistareṇa bahūn guṇāna iṣṭaś cāniṣṭagandhaś ca madhuro mlaḥ kaṭus tathāc nirhārī saṃhataḥ snigdho rūkṣo viśada eva cae evaṃ daśavidho jñeyaḥ pārthivo gandha ity utaa śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ rasaś cāpāṃ guṇāḥ smṛtāḥc rasajñānaṃ tu vakṣyāmi rasas tu bahudhā smṛtaḥa madhuro mlaḥ kaṭus tiktaḥ kaṣāyo lavaṇas tathāc evaṃ ṣaḍvidhavistāro raso vārimayaḥ smṛtaḥa śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ triguṇaṃ jyotir ucyatec jyotiṣaś ca guṇo rūpaṃ rūpaṃ ca bahudhā smṛtama śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā raktaṃ nīlaṃ pītāruṇaṃ tathāc hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tathā sthūlaṃ caturasrāṇu vṛttakama evaṃ dvādaśavistāraṃ tejaso rūpam ucyatec vijñeyaṃ brāhmaṇair nityaṃ dharmajñaiḥ satyavādibhiḥa śabdasparśau ca vijñeyau dviguṇo vāyur ucyatec vāyoś cāpi guṇaḥ sparśaḥ sparśaś ca bahudhā smṛtaḥa uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ sukho duḥkhaḥ snigdho viśada eva cac kaṭhinaś cikkaṇaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ picchilo dāruṇo mṛduḥa evaṃ dvādaśavistāro vāyavyo guṇa ucyatec vidhivad brahmaṇaiḥ siddhair dharmajñais tattvadarśibhiḥa tatraikaguṇam ākāśaṃ śabda ity eva ca smṛtaḥc tasya śabdasya vakṣyāmi vistareṇa bahūn guṇāna ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca gāndhāro madhyamaḥ pañcamas tathāc ataḥ paraṃ tu vijñeyo niṣādo dhaivatas tathāa iṣṭo niṣṭaś ca śabdas tu saṃhataḥ pravibhāgavānc evaṃ bahuvidho jñeyaḥ śabda ākāśasaṃbhavaḥa ākāśam uttamaṃ bhūtam ahaṃkāras tataḥ paramc ahaṃkārāt parā buddhir buddher ātmā tataḥ paraḥa tasmāt tu param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥc parāvarajño bhūtānāṃ yaṃ prāpyānantyam pāṇḍavāḥ śiṣṭā hatamitrā hatātmajāḥc dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca nihatāḥ sarve sasutabāndhavāḥa ity uktavacane kṛṣṇe bhṛśaṃ krodhasamanvitaḥc uttaṅkaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ roṣād utphālya locanea yasmāc chaktena te kṛṣṇa na trātāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc saṃbandhinaḥ priyās tasmāc chapsye haṃ tvām asaṃśayama na ca te prasabhaṃ yasmāt te nigṛhya nivartitāḥc tasmān manyuparītas tvāṃ śapsyāmi madhusūdanaa tvayā hi śaktena satā mithyācāreṇa mādhavac upacīrṇāḥ kuruśreṣṭhā yas tv etān samupekṣathāḥ vāsudeva uvācaa śṛṇu me vistareṇedaṃ yad vakṣye bhṛgunandanac gṛhāṇānunayaṃ cāpi tapasvī hy asi bhārgavaa śrutvā tvam etad adhyātmaṃ muñcethāḥ śāpam adya vaic na ca māṃ tapasālpena śakto bhibhavituṃ pumāna na ca te tapaso nāśam icchāmi japatāṃ varac tapas te sumahad dīptaṃ guravaś cāpi toṣitāḥa kaumāraṃ brahmacaryaṃ te jānāmi dvijasattamac duḥkhārjitasya tapasas tasmān necchāmi te vyayam uttaṅka uvācaa brūhi keśava tattvena tvam adhyātmam aninditamc śrutvā śreyo bhidhāsyāmi śāpaṃ vā te janārdana vāsudeva uvācaa tamo rajaś ca sattvaṃ ca viddhi bhāvān madāśrayānb sthitisṛṣṭilayādhyakṣo viṣṇubrahmeśasaṃjñitaḥb kadā cit tamasā rudro viṣṇuḥ sattvaguṇe sthitaḥb rajasy api tathā brahmā guṇād anyaguṇānugaub praṇavātmā ca śabdādīṃs triguṇātmā carācaramc tathā rudrān vasūṃś cāpi viddhi matprabhavān dvijaa mayi sarvāṇi bhūtāni sarvabhūteṣu cāpy ahamc sthita ity abhijānīhi mā te bhūd atra saṃśayaḥa tathā daityagaṇān sarvān yakṣarākṣasapannagānc gandharvāpsarasaś caiva viddhi matprabhavān dvijac   yakṣagandharvarākṣasānc nāgān apsarasaś caivaa sad asac caiva yat prāhur avyaktaṃ vyaktam eva cac akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva sarvam etan madātmakama ye cāśrameṣu vai dharmāś caturṣu vihitā munec daivāni caiva karmāṇi viddhi sarvaṃ madātmakama asac ca sadasac caiva yad viśvaṃ sadasataḥ paramc tataḥ paraṃ nāsti caiva devadevāt sanātanāta oṃkāraprabhavān vedān viddhi māṃ tvaṃ bhṛgūdvahac yūpaṃ somaṃ tathaiveha tridaśāpyāyanaṃ makhea hotāram api havyaṃ ca viddhi māṃ bhṛgunandanac adhvaryuḥ kalpakaś cāpi haviḥ paramasaṃskṛtama udgātā cāpi māṃ stauti gītaghoṣair mahādhvarec prāyaścitteṣu māṃ brahmañ śāntimaṅgalavācakāḥe stuvanti viśvakarmāṇaṃ satataṃ dvijasattamāḥa viddhi mahyaṃ sutaṃ dharmam agrajaṃ dvijasattamac mānasaṃ dayitaṃ vipra sarvabhūtadayātmakama tatrāhaṃ vartamānaiś ca nivṛttaiś caiva mānavaiḥc bahvīḥ saṃsaramāṇo vai yonīr hi dvijasattamaa dharmasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya dharmasaṃsthāpanāya cac tais tair veṣaiś ca rūpaiś ca triṣu lokeṣu bhārgavaa ahaṃ viṣṇur ahaṃ brahmā śakro tha prabhavāpyayaḥc bhūtagrāmasya sarvasya sraṣṭā saṃhāra eva caa adharme vartamānānāṃ sarveṣām aham apy utac dharmasya setuṃ badhnāmi calite calite yugee tās tā yonīḥ praviśyāhaṃ prajānāṃ hitakāmyayāa yadā tv ahaṃ devayonau vartāmi bhṛgunandanac tadāhaṃ devavat sarvam ācarāmi na saṃśayaḥa yadā gandharvayonau
