prabhuḥc suptotthita ivottasthau mṛṣṭalohitalocanaḥa tam utthitaṃ mahātmānaṃ labdhasaṃjñaṃ manasvinamc samīkṣya pitaraṃ svasthaṃ vavande babhruvāhanaḥa utthite puruṣavyāghre punar lakṣmīvati prabhoc divyāḥ sumanasaḥ puṇyā vavṛṣe pākaśāsanaḥa anāhatā dundubhayaḥ praṇedur meghanisvanāḥc sādhu sādhv iti cākāśe babhūva sumahān svanaḥa utthāya tu mahābāhuḥ paryāśvasto dhanaṃjayaḥc babhruvāhanam āliṅgya samājighrata mūrdhania dadarśa cāvidūre sya mātaraṃ śokakarśitāmc ulūpyā saha tiṣṭhantīṃ tato pṛcchad dhanaṃjayaḥa kim idaṃ lakṣyate sarvaṃ śokavismayaharṣavatc raṇājiram amitraghna yadi jānāsi śaṃsa mea jananī ca kimarthaṃ te raṇabhūmim upāgatāc nāgendraduhitā ceyam ulūpī kim ihāgatāa jānāmy aham idaṃ yuddhaṃ tvayā madvacanāt kṛtamc strīṇām āgamane hetum aham icchāmi vedituma tam uvāca tataḥ pṛṣṭo maṇipūrapatis tadāc prasādya śirasā vidvān ulūpī pṛcchyatām iti arjuna uvācaa kim āgamanakṛtyaṃ te kauravyakulanandinic maṇipūrapater mātus tathaiva ca raṇājirea kaccit kuśalakāmāsi rājño sya bhujagātmajec mama vā cañcalāpāṅge kaccit tvaṃ śubham icchasia kaccit te pṛthulaśroṇi nāpriyaṃ śubhadarśanec akārṣam aham ajñānād ayaṃ vā babhruvāhanaḥa kaccic ca rājaputrī te sapatnī caitravāhinīc citrāṅgadā varārohā nāparādhyati kiṃ canaa tam uvācoragapater duhitā prahasanty athac na me tvam aparāddho si na nṛpo babhruvāhanaḥe na janitrī tathāsyeyaṃ mama yā preṣyavat sthitāa śrūyatāṃ yad yathā cedaṃ mayā sarvaṃ viceṣṭitamc na me kopas tvayā kāryaḥ śirasā tvāṃ prasādayea tvatprītyarthaṃ hi kauravya kṛtam etan mayānaghac yat tac chṛṇu mahābāho nikhilena dhanaṃjayaa mahābhāratayuddhe yat tvayā śāṃtanavo nṛpaḥc adharmeṇa hataḥ pārtha tasyaiṣā niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtāa na hi bhīṣmas tvayā vīra yudhyamāno nipātitaḥc śikhaṇḍinā tu saṃsaktas tam āśritya hatas tvayāa tasya śāntim akṛtvā tu tyajes tvaṃ yadi jīvitamc karmaṇā tena pāpena patethā niraye dhruvama eṣā tu vihitā śāntiḥ putrād yāṃ prāptavān asic vasubhir vasudhāpāla gaṅgayā ca mahāmatea purā hi śrutam etad vai vasubhiḥ kathitaṃ mayāc gaṅgāyās tīram āgamya hate śāṃtanave nṛpea āplutya devā vasavaḥ sametya ca mahānadīmc idam ūcur vaco ghoraṃ bhāgīrathyā mate tadāa eṣa śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo nihataḥ savyasācināc ayudhyamānaḥ saṃgrāme saṃsakto nyena bhāminia tad anenābhiṣaṅgeṇa vayam apy arjunaṃ śubhec śāpena yojayāmeti tathāstv iti ca sābravīta tad ahaṃ pitur āvedya bhṛśaṃ pravyathitendriyāc abhavaṃ sa ca tac chrutvā viṣādam agamat parama pitā tu me vasūn gatvā tvadarthaṃ samayācatac punaḥ punaḥ prasādyaināṃs ta enam idam abruvana punas tasya mahābhāga maṇipūreśvaro yuvāc sa enaṃ raṇamadhyasthaṃ śaraiḥ pātayitā bhuvia evaṃ kṛte sa nāgendra muktaśāpo bhaviṣyatic gaccheti vasubhiś cokto mama cedaṃ śaśaṃsa saḥa tac chrutvā tvaṃ mayā tasmāc chāpād asi vimokṣitaḥc na hi tvāṃ devarājo pi samareṣu parājayeta ātmā putraḥ smṛtas tasmāt tenehāsi parājitaḥc nātra doṣo mama mataḥ kathaṃ vā manyase vibhoa ity evam ukto vijayaḥ prasannātmābravīd idamc sarvaṃ me supriyaṃ devi yad etat kṛtavaty asia ity uktvāthābravīt putraṃ maṇipūreśvaraṃ jayaḥc citrāṅgadāyāḥ śṛṇvantyāḥ kauravyaduhitus tathāa yudhiṣṭhirasyāśvamedhaḥ parāṃ caitrīṃ bhaviṣyatic tatrāgaccheḥ sahāmātyo mātṛbhyāṃ sahito nṛpaa ity evam uktaḥ pārthena sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥc uvāca pitaraṃ dhīmān idam asrāvilekṣaṇaḥa upayāsyāmi dharmajña bhavataḥ śāsanād ahamc aśvamedhe mahāyajñe dvijātipariveṣakaḥa mama tv anugrahārthāya praviśasva puraṃ svakamc bhāryābhyāṃ saha śatrughna mā bhūt te tra vicāraṇāa uṣitveha viśalyas tvaṃ sukhaṃ sve veśmani prabhoc punar aśvānugamanaṃ kartāsi jayatāṃ varaa ity uktaḥ sa tu putreṇa tadā vānaraketanaḥc smayan provāca kaunteyas tadā citrāṅgadāsutama viditaṃ te mahābāho yathā dīkṣāṃ carāmy ahamc na sa tāvat pravekṣyāmi puraṃ te pṛthulocanaa yathākāmaṃ prayāty eṣa yajñiyaś ca turaṃgamaḥc svasti te stu gamiṣyāmi na sthānaṃ vidyate mamaa sa tatra vidhivat tena pūjitaḥ pākaśāsaniḥc bhāryābhyām abhyanujñātaḥ prāyād bharatasattamaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa tu vājī samudrāntāṃ paryetya pṛthivīm imāmc nivṛtto bhimukho rājan yena nāgāhvayaṃ purama anugacchaṃś ca tejasvī nivṛtto tha kirīṭabhṛtc yadṛcchayā samāpede puraṃ rājagṛhaṃ tadāa tam abhyāśagataṃ rājā jarāsaṃdhātmajātmajaḥc kṣatradharme sthito vīraḥ samarāyājuhāva haa tataḥ purāt sa niṣkramya rathī dhanvī śarī talīc meghasaṃdhiḥ padātiṃ taṃ dhanaṃjayam upādravata āsādya ca mahātejā meghasaṃdhir dhanaṃjayamc bālabhāvān mahārāja provācedaṃ na kauśalāta kim ayaṃ cāryate vājī strīmadhya iva bhāratac hayam enaṃ hariṣyāmi prayatasva vimokṣaṇea adattānunayo yuddhe yadi tvaṃ pitṛbhir mamab ārto nanu purā yuddheb   śilpa ity api pāragaḥc kariṣyāmi tavātithyaṃ prahara praharāmi vāa ity uktaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ pāṇḍavaḥ prahasann ivac vighnakartā mayā vārya iti me vratam āhitama bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena nṛpate tavāpi viditaṃ dhruvamc praharasva yathāśakti na manyur vidyate mamaa ity uktaḥ prāharat pūrvaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ magadheśvaraḥc kirañ śarasahasrāṇi varṣāṇīva sahasradṛka tato gāṇḍīvabhṛc chūro gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥc cakāra moghāṃs tān bāṇān ayatnād bharatarṣabhaa sa moghaṃ tasya bāṇaughaṃ kṛtvā vānaraketanaḥc śarān mumoca jvalitān dīptāsyān iva pannagāna dhvaje patākādaṇḍeṣu rathayantre hayeṣu cac anyeṣu ca rathāṅgeṣu na śarīre na sārathaua saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena śarīre phalgunasya hac manyamānaḥ svavīryaṃ tan māgadhaḥ prāhiṇoc charāna tato gāṇḍīvabhṛc chūro māgadhena samāhataḥc babhau vāsantika iva palāśaḥ puṣpito mahāna avadhyamānaḥ so bhyaghnan māgadhaḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhamc tena tasthau sa kauravya lokavīrasya darśanea savyasācī tu saṃkruddho vikṛṣya balavad dhanuḥc hayāṃś cakāra nirdehān sāratheś ca śiro harata dhanuś cāsya mahac citraṃ kṣureṇa pracakarta hac hastāvāpaṃ patākāṃ ca dhvajaṃ cāsya nyapātayata sa rājā vyathito vyaśvo vidhanur hatasārathiḥc gadām ādāya kaunteyam abhidudrāva vegavāna tasyāpatata evāśu gadāṃ hemapariṣkṛtāmc śaraiś cakarta bahudhā bahubhir gṛdhravājitaiḥa sā gadā śakalībhūtā viśīrṇamaṇibandhanāc vyālī nirmucyamāneva papātāsya sahasradhāa virathaṃ taṃ vidhanvānaṃ gadayā parivarjitamc naicchat tāḍayituṃ dhīmān arjunaḥ samarāgraṇīḥa tata enaṃ vimanasaṃ kṣatradharme samāsthitamc sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vākyam abravīt kapiketanaḥa paryāptaḥ kṣatradharmo yaṃ darśitaḥ putra gamyatāmc bahv etat samare karma tava bālasya pārthivaa yudhiṣṭhirasya saṃdeśo na hantavyā nṛpā itic tena jīvasi rājaṃs tvam aparāddho pi me raṇea iti matvā sa cātmānaṃ pratyādiṣṭaṃ sma māgadhaḥc tathyam ity avagamyainaṃ prāñjaliḥ pratyapūjayatd parājito smi bhadraṃ te nāhaṃ yoddhum ihotsahed yac ca kṛtyaṃ mayā te dya tad brūhi kṛtam eva tua tam arjunaḥ samāśvāsya punar evedam abravītc āgantavyaṃ parāṃ caitrīm aśvamedhe nṛpasya naḥa ity uktaḥ sa tathety uktvā pūjayām āsa taṃ hayamc phalgunaṃ ca yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vidhivat sahadevajaḥa tato yatheṣṭam agamat punar eva sa kesarīc tataḥ samudratīreṇa vaṅgān puṇḍrān sakeralāna tatra tatra ca bhūrīṇi mlecchasainyāny anekaśaḥc vijigye dhanuṣā rājan gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa māgadhenārcito rājan pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥc dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āsthāya cārayām āsa taṃ hayama tataḥ sa punar āvṛtya hayaḥ kāmacaro balīc āsasāda purīṃ ramyāṃ cedīnāṃ śuktisāhvayāma śarabheṇārcitas tatra śiśupālātmajena saḥc yuddhapūrveṇa mānena pūjayā ca mahābalaḥa tatrārcito yayau rājaṃs tadā sa turagottamaḥc kāśīn andhrān kosalāṃś ca kirātān atha taṅgaṇāna tatra pūjāṃ yathānyāyaṃ pratigṛhya sa pāṇḍavaḥc punar āvṛtya kaunteyo daśārṇān agamat tadāa tatra citrāṅgado nāma balavān vasudhādhipaḥc tena yuddham abhūt tasya vijayasyātibhairavama taṃ cāpi vaśam ānīya kirīṭī puruṣarṣabhaḥc niṣādarājño viṣayam ekalavyasya jagmivāna ekalavyasutaś cainaṃ yuddhena jagṛhe tadāc tataś cakre niṣādaiḥ sa saṃgrāmaṃ romaharṣaṇama tatas tam api kaunteyaḥ samareṣv aparājitaḥc jigāya samare vīro yajñavighnārtham udyatama sa taṃ jitvā mahārāja naiṣādiṃ pākaśāsaniḥc arcitaḥ prayayau bhūyo dakṣiṇaṃ salilārṇavama tatrāpi draviḍair andhrai raudrair māhiṣakair apic tathā kollagireyaiś ca yuddham āsīt kirīṭinaḥd tāṃś cāpi vijayo jitvā nātitīvreṇa karmaṇāa turagasya vaśenātha surāṣṭrān abhito yayauc gokarṇam api cāsādya prabhāsam api jagmivāna tato dvāravatīṃ ramyāṃ vṛṣṇivīrābhirakṣitāmc āsasāda hayaḥ śrīmān kururājasya yajñiyaḥa tam unmathya hayaśreṣṭhaṃ yādavānāṃ kumārakāḥc prayayus tāṃs tadā rājann ugraseno nyavārayata tataḥ puryā viniṣkramya vṛṣṇyandhakapatis tadāc sahito vasudevena mātulena kirīṭinaḥa tau sametya kuruśreṣṭhaṃ vidhivat prītipūrvakamc parayā bharataśreṣṭhaṃ pūjayā samavasthitaue tatas tābhyām anujñāto yayau yena hayo gataḥa tataḥ sa paścimaṃ deśaṃ samudrasya tadā hayaḥc krameṇa vyacarat sphītaṃ tataḥ pañcanadaṃ yayaua tasmād api sa kauravya gāndhāraviṣayaṃ hayaḥc vicacāra yathākāmaṃ kaunteyānugatas tadāa tatra gāndhārarājena yuddham āsīn mahātmanaḥc ghoraṃ śakuniputreṇa pūrvavairānusāriṇā vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa śakunes tu suto vīro gāndhārāṇāṃ mahārathaḥc pratyudyayau guḍākeśaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥe hastyaśvarathapūrṇena patākādhvajamālināa amṛṣyamāṇās te yodhā nṛpateḥ śakuner vadhamc abhyayuḥ sahitāḥ pārthaṃ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥa tān uvāca sa dharmātmā bībhatsur aparājitaḥc yudhiṣṭhirasya vacanaṃ na ca te jagṛhur hitama vāryamāṇās tu pārthena sāntvapūrvam amarṣitāḥc parivārya hayaṃ jagmus tataś cukrodha pāṇḍavaḥa tataḥ śirāṃsi dīptāgrais teṣāṃ ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥc kṣurair gāṇḍīvanirmuktair nātiyatnād ivārjunaḥa te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena hayam utsṛjya saṃbhramātc nyavartanta mahārāja śaravarṣārditā bhṛśama vitudyamānas taiś cāpi gāndhāraiḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥc ādiśyādiśya tejasvī śirāṃsy eṣāṃ nyapātayata vadhyamāneṣu teṣv ājau gāndhāreṣu samantataḥc sa rājā śakuneḥ putraḥ pāṇḍavaṃ pratyavārayata taṃ yudhyamānaṃ rājānaṃ kṣatradharme vyavasthitamc pārtho bravīn na me vadhyā rājāno rājaśāsanāte alaṃ yuddhena te vīra na te sty adya parājayaḥa ity uktas tad anādṛtya vākyam ajñānamohitaḥc sa śakrasamakarmāṇam avākirata sāyakaiḥa tasya pārthaḥ śirastrāṇam ardhacandreṇa patriṇāc apāharad asaṃbhrānto jayadrathaśiro yathāa tad dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ jagmur gāndhārāḥ sarva eva tec icchatā tena na hato rājety api ca te viduḥa gāndhārarājaputras tu palāyanakṛtakṣaṇaḥc babhau tair eva sahitas trastaiḥ kṣudramṛgair ivaa teṣāṃ tu tarasā pārthas tatraiva paridhāvatāmc vijahārottamāṅgāni bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa ucchritāṃs tu bhujān ke cin nābudhyanta śarair hṛtānc śarair gāṇḍīvanirmuktaiḥ pṛthubhiḥ pārthacoditaiḥa saṃbhrāntanaranāgāśvam atha tad vidrutaṃ balamc hatavidhvastabhūyiṣṭham āvartata muhur muhuḥa na hy adṛśyanta vīrasya ke cid agre gryakarmaṇaḥc ripavaḥ pātyamānā vai ye saheyur mahāśarāna tato gāndhārarājasya mantrivṛddhapuraḥsarāc jananī niryayau bhītā puraskṛtyārghyam uttamama sā nyavārayad avyagrā taṃ putraṃ yuddhadurmadamc prasādayām āsa ca taṃ jiṣṇum akliṣṭakāriṇama tāṃ pūjayitvā kaunteyaḥ prasādam akarot tadāc śakuneś cāpi tanayaṃ sāntvayann idam abravīta na me priyaṃ mahābāho yat te buddhir iyaṃ kṛtāc pratiyoddhum amitraghna bhrātaiva tvaṃ mamānaghaa gāndhārīṃ mātaraṃ smṛtvā dhṛtarāṣṭrakṛtena cac tena jīvasi rājaṃs tvaṃ nihatās tv anugās tavaa maivaṃ bhūḥ śāmyatāṃ vairaṃ mā te bhūd buddhir īdṛśīc āgantavyaṃ parāṃ caitrīm aśvamedhe nṛpasya naḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity uktvānuyayau pārtho hayaṃ taṃ kāmacāriṇamb te nyavartanta gāndhārā hataśiṣṭāḥ svakaṃ puramc nyavartata tato vājī yena nāgāhvayaṃ purama taṃ nivṛttaṃ tu śuśrāva cāreṇaiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥc śrutvārjunaṃ kuśalinaṃ sa ca hṛṣṭamanābhavata vijayasya ca tat karma gāndhāraviṣaye tadāc śrutvānyeṣu ca deśeṣu sa suprīto bhavan nṛpaḥa etasminn eva kāle tu dvādaśīṃ māghapākṣikīmc iṣṭaṃ gṛhītvā nakṣatraṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa samānāyya mahātejāḥ sarvān bhrātṝn mahāmanāḥc bhīmaṃ ca nakulaṃ caiva sahadevaṃ ca kauravaḥa provācedaṃ vacaḥ kāle tadā dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥc āmantrya vadatāṃ śreṣṭho bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramama āyāti bhīmasenāsau sahāśvena tavānujaḥc yathā me puruṣāḥ prāhur ye dhanaṃjayasāriṇaḥa upasthitaś ca kālo yam abhito vartate hayaḥc māghī ca paurṇamāsīyaṃ māsaḥ śeṣo vṛkodaraa tat prasthāpyantu vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥc vājimedhārthasiddhyarthaṃ deśaṃ paśyantu yajñiyama ity uktaḥ sa tu tac cakre bhīmo nṛpatiśāsanamc hṛṣṭaḥ śrutvā narapater āyāntaṃ savyasācinama tato yayau bhīmasenaḥ prājñaiḥ sthapatibhiḥ sahac brāhmaṇān agrataḥ kṛtvā kuśalān yajñakarmasud yajñaślāghyaṃ tadā sthānaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutama taṃ saśālacayagrāmaṃ saṃpratolīviṭaṅkinamc māpayām āsa kauravyo yajñavāṭaṃ yathāvidhid prāsādaśatasaṃbādhaṃ maṇipravarakuṭṭikama sadaḥ sapatnīsadanaṃ sāgnīdhram api cottaramc kārayām āsa vidhivan maṇihemavibhūṣitama stambhān kanakacitrāṃś ca toraṇāni bṛhanti cac yajñāyatanadeśeṣu dattvā śuddhaṃ ca kāñcanama antaḥpurāṇi rājñāṃ ca nānādeśanivāsināmc kārayām āsa dharmātmā tatra tatra yathāvidhia brāhmaṇānāṃ ca veśmāni nānādeśasameyuṣāmc kārayām āsa bhīmaḥ sa vividhāni hy anekaśaḥa tathā saṃpreṣayām āsa dūtān nṛpatiśāsanātc bhīmaseno mahārāja rājñām akliṣṭakarmaṇāma te priyārthaṃ kurupater āyayur nṛpasattamāḥc ratnāny anekāny ādāya striyo śvān āyudhāni caa teṣāṃ niviśatāṃ teṣu śibireṣu sahasraśaḥc nardataḥ sāgarasyeva śabdo divam ivāspṛśatd pratyudgamya namaskṛtya brāhmaṇāṃś ca nyavedayata teṣām abhyāgatānāṃ sa rājā rājīvalocanaḥc vyādideśānnapānāni śayyāś cāpy atimānuṣāḥa vāhanānāṃ ca vividhāḥ śālāḥ śālīkṣugorasaiḥc upetāḥ puruṣavyāghra vyādideśa sa dharmarāṭd varṇāḥ pṛthak saṃniviṣṭā hy uttarottarapūjitāḥa tathā tasmin mahāyajñe dharmarājasya dhīmataḥc samājagmur munigaṇā bahavo brahmavādinaḥa ye ca dvijātipravarās tatrāsan pṛthivīpatec samājagmuḥ saśiṣyāṃs tān pratijagrāha kauravaḥa sarvāṃś ca tān anuyayau yāvad āvasathād itic svayam eva mahātejā dambhaṃ tyaktvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥa tataḥ kṛtvā sthapatayaḥ śilpino nye ca ye tadāc kṛtsnaṃ yajñavidhiṃ rājan dharmarājñe nyavedayana tac chrutvā dharmarājaḥ sa kṛtaṃ sarvam aninditamc hṛṣṭarūpo bhavad rājā saha bhrātṛbhir acyutaḥc śrīmannāmā ca bhavatu janānāṃ puṇyadaḥ prabhuḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasmin yajñe pravṛtte tu vāgmino hetuvādinaḥc hetuvādān bahūn prāhuḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥa dadṛśus taṃ nṛpatayo yajñasya vidhim uttamamc devendrasyeva vihitaṃ bhīmena kurunandanaa dadṛśus toraṇāny atra śātakumbhamayāni tec śayyāsanavihārāṃś ca subahūn ratnabhūṣitāna ghaṭān pātrīḥ kaṭāhāni kalaśān vardhamānakānc na hi kiṃ cid asauvarṇam apaśyaṃs tatra pārthivāḥa yūpāṃś ca śāstrapaṭhitān dāravān hemabhūṣitānc upakḷptān yathākālaṃ vidhivad bhūrivarcasaḥa sthalajā jalajā ye ca paśavaḥ ke cana prabhoc sarvān eva samānītāṃs tān apaśyanta te nṛpāḥa gāś caiva mahiṣīś caiva tathā vṛddhāḥ striyo pi cac audakāni ca sattvāni śvāpadāni vayāṃsi caa jarāyujāny aṇḍajāni svedajāny udbhidāni cac parvatānūpavanyāni bhūtāni dadṛśuś ca ted sarve rājan yathānyāyam ānītā nṛpaśāsanāta evaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ paśugodhanadhānyataḥc yajñavāṭaṃ nṛpā dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayam āgamand aniśaṃ dīyate ca sma tatra bhojyaṃ pṛthagvidhame brāhmaṇānāṃ viśāṃ caiva bahumṛṣṭānnam ṛddhimata pūrṇe śatasahasre tu viprāṇāṃ tatra bhuñjatāmc dundubhir meghanirghoṣo muhur muhur atāḍyataa vinanādāsakṛt so tha divase divase tadāc evaṃ sa vavṛte yajño dharmarājasya dhīmataḥa annasya bahavo rājann utsargāḥ parvatopamāḥc dadhikulyāś ca dadṛśuḥ sarpiṣaś ca hradāñjanāḥa jambūdvīpo hi sakalo nānājanapadāyutaḥc rājann adṛśyataikastho rājñas tasmin mahākrataua tatra jātisahasrāṇi puruṣāṇāṃ tatas tataḥc gṛhītvā dhanam ājagmur bahūni bharatarṣabhaa rājānaḥ sragviṇaś cāpi sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalāḥc paryaveṣan dvijāgryāṃs tāñ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa vividhāny annapānāni puruṣā ye nuyāyinaḥc teṣāṃ nṛpopabhojyāni brāhmaṇebhyo daduḥ sma te vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa samāgatān vedavido rājñaś ca pṛthivīśvarānc dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmasenam athābravīta upayātā naravyāghrā ya ime jagadīśvarāḥc eteṣāṃ kriyatāṃ pūjā pūjārhā hi nareśvarāḥa ity uktaḥ sa tathā cakre narendreṇa yaśasvināc bhīmaseno mahātejā yamābhyāṃ saha bhārataa athābhyagacchad govindo vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha dharmajamb yajñeśo yajñapuruṣaḥ sarvavedāntaveditaḥb devāś ca munayo viprā manasā vandya keśavamb pratyutthitās tatas tatra praviveśa sa mādhavaḥc baladevaṃ puraskṛtya sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ varaḥa yuyudhānena sahitaḥ pradyumnena gadena cac niśaṭhenātha sāmbena tathaiva kṛtavarmaṇāa teṣām api parāṃ pūjāṃ cakre bhīmo mahābhujaḥc viviśus te ca veśmāni ratnavanti nararṣabhāḥa yudhiṣṭhirasamīpe tu kathānte madhusūdanaḥc arjunaṃ kathayām āsa bahusaṃgrāmakarśitama sa taṃ papraccha kaunteyaḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamamc dharmarāḍ bhrātaraṃ jiṣṇuṃ samācaṣṭa jagatpatiḥa āgamad dvārakāvāsī mamāptaḥ puruṣo nṛpac yo drākṣīt pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaṃ bahusaṃgrāmakarśitama samīpe ca mahābāhum ācaṣṭa ca mama prabhoc kuru kāryāṇi kaunteya hayamedhārthasiddhayea ity uktaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc diṣṭyā sa kuśalī jiṣṇur upayāti ca mādhavaa tava yat saṃdideśāsau pāṇḍavānāṃ balāgraṇīḥc tad ākhyātum ihecchāmi bhavatā yadunandanaa ity ukte rājaśārdūla vṛṣṇyandhakapatis tadāc provācedaṃ vaco vāgmī dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhirama idam āha mahārāja pārthavākyaṃ naraḥ sa māmc vācyo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kṛṣṇa kāle vākyam idaṃ mamaa āgamiṣyanti rājānaḥ sarvataḥ kauravān pratic teṣām ekaikaśaḥ pūjā kāryety etat kṣamaṃ hi naḥa ity etad vacanād rājā vijñāpyo mama mānadac na tad ātyayikaṃ hi syād yad arghyānayane bhaveta kartum arhati tad rājā bhavāṃś cāpy anumanyatāmc rājadveṣād vinaśyeyur nemā rājan prajāḥ punaḥa idam anyac ca kaunteya vacaḥ sa puruṣo bravītc dhanaṃjayasya nṛpate tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇua upayāsyati yajñaṃ no maṇipūrapatir nṛpaḥc putro mama mahātejā dayito babhruvāhanaḥa taṃ bhavān madapekṣārthaṃ vidhivat pratipūjayetc sa hi bhakto nuraktaś ca mama nityam iti prabhoa ity etad vacanaṃ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc abhinandyāsya tad vākyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa śrutaṃ priyam idaṃ kṛṣṇa yat tvam arhasi bhāṣitumc tan me mṛtarasaprakhyaṃ mano hlādayate vibhoa bahūni kila yuddhāni vijayasya narādhipaiḥc punar āsan hṛṣīkeśa tatra tatreti me śrutama mannimittaṃ hi sa sadā pārthaḥ sukhavivarjitaḥc atīva vijayo dhīmān iti me dūyate manaḥa saṃcintayāmi vārṣṇeya sadā kuntīsutaṃ rahaḥb atīva duḥkhabhāgī sa satataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥc kiṃ nu tasya śarīre sti sarvalakṣaṇapūjitee aniṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇa yena duḥkhāny upāśnutea atīva duḥkhabhāgī sa satataṃ kuntinandanaḥc na ca paśyāmi bībhatsor nindyaṃ gātreṣu kiṃ canae śrotavyaṃ cen mayaitad vai tan me vyākhyātum arhasia ity uktaḥ sa hṛṣīkeśo dhyātvā sumahad antaramc rājānaṃ bhojarājanyavardhano viṣṇur abravīta na hy asya nṛpate kiṃ cid aniṣṭam upalakṣayec ṛte puruṣasiṃhasya piṇḍike syātikāyataḥa tābhyāṃ sa puruṣavyāghro nityam adhvasu yujyatec na hy anyad anupaśyāmi yenāsau duḥkhabhāg jayaḥa ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭhas tathyaṃ kṛṣṇena dhīmatāc provāca vṛṣṇiśārdūlam evam etad iti prabhoa kṛṣṇā tu draupadī kṛṣṇaṃ tiryak sāsūyam aikṣatac pratijagrāha tasyās taṃ praṇayaṃ cāpi keśihāe sakhyuḥ sakhā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sākṣād iva dhanaṃjayaḥa tatra bhīmādayas te tu kuravo yādavās tathāc remuḥ śrutvā vicitrārthā dhanaṃjayakathā vibhoa tathā kathayatām eva teṣām arjunasaṃkathāḥc upāyād vacanān martyo vijayasya mahātmanaḥa so bhigamya kuruśreṣṭhaṃ namaskṛtya ca buddhimānc upāyātaṃ naravyāghram arjunaṃ pratyavedayata tac chrutvā nṛpatis tasya harṣabāṣpākulekṣaṇaḥc priyākhyānanimittaṃ vai dadau bahu dhanaṃ tadāa tato dvitīye divase mahāñ śabdo vyavardhatac āyāti puruṣavyāghre pāṇḍavānāṃ dhuraṃdharea tato reṇuḥ samudbhūto vibabhau tasya vājinaḥc abhito vartamānasya yathoccaiḥśravasas tathāa tatra harṣakalā vāco narāṇāṃ śuśruve rjunaḥc diṣṭyāsi pārtha kuśalī dhanyo rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥa ko nyo hi pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnām avajitya sapārthivāmc cārayitvā hayaśreṣṭham upāyāyād ṛte rjunama ye vyatītā mahātmāno rājānaḥ sagarādayaḥc teṣām apīdṛśaṃ karma na kiṃ cid anuśuśrumaa naitad anye kariṣyanti bhaviṣyāḥ pṛthivīkṣitaḥc yat tvaṃ kurukulaśreṣṭha duṣkaraṃ kṛtavān ihaa ity evaṃ vadatāṃ teṣāṃ nṝṇāṃ śrutisukhā giraḥc śṛṇvan viveśa dharmātmā phalguno yajñasaṃstarama tato rājā sahāmātyaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca yadunandanaḥc dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya te taṃ pratyudyayus tadāa so bhivādya pituḥ pādau dharmarājasya dhīmataḥc bhīmādīṃś cāpi saṃpūjya paryaṣvajata keśavamd saumyātmany amṛtādhāre pariṣvakte sukhaṃ yayaua taiḥ sametyārcitas tān sa pratyarcya ca yathāvidhic viśaśrāmātha dharmātmā tīraṃ labdhveva pāragaḥa etasminn eva kāle tu sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥc mātṛbhyāṃ sahito dhīmān kurūn abhyājagāma had tatra vṛddhān yathā vatsa kurūn anyāṃś ca pārthivāna sa sametya kurūn sarvān sarvais tair abhinanditaḥb abhivādya mahābāhus taiś cāpi pratinanditaḥc praviveśa pitāmahyāḥ kuntyā bhavanam uttamam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa praviśya yathānyāyaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ niveśanama   mātṛbhyāṃ sahito vaśīa praśrayāvanataḥ kuntyā gāndhāryāś ca yathāvidhia vavande caraṇau tatrac pitāmahīm abhyavadat sāmnā paramavalgunāa tathā citrāṅgadā devī kauravyasyātmajāpi cac pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ ca sahite vinayenābhijagmatuḥe subhadrāṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ yāś cānyāḥ kuruyoṣitaḥa dadau kuntī tatas tābhyāṃ ratnāni vividhāni cac draupadī ca subhadrā ca yāś cāpy anyā daduḥ striyaḥa ūṣatus tatra te devyau mahārhaśayanāsanec supūjite svayaṃ kuntyā pārthasya priyakāmyayāa sa ca rājā mahāvīryaḥ pūjito babhruvāhanaḥc dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahīpālam upatasthe yathāvidhia yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca rājānaṃ bhīmādīṃś cāpi pāṇḍavānc upagamya mahātejā vinayenābhyavādayata sa taiḥ premṇā pariṣvaktaḥ pūjitaś ca yathāvidhic dhanaṃ cāsmai dadur bhūri prīyamāṇā mahārathāḥa tathaiva sa mahīpālaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ cakragadādharamc pradyumna iva govindaṃ vinayenopatasthivāna tasmai kṛṣṇo dadau rājñe mahārham abhipūjitamc rathaṃ hemapariṣkāraṃ divyāśvayujam uttamama dharmarājaś ca bhīmaś ca yamajau phalgunas tathāc pṛthak pṛthag atīvainaṃ mānārhaṃ samapūjayana tatas tṛtīye divase satyavatyāḥ suto muniḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samabhyetya vāgmī vacanam abravīta adya prabhṛti kaunteya yajasva samayo hi tec muhūrto yajñiyaḥ prāptaś codayanti ca yājakāḥa ahīno nāma rājendra kratus te yaṃ vikalpavānc bahutvāt kāñcanasyāsya khyāto bahusuvarṇakaḥa evam eva mahārāja dakṣiṇāṃ triguṇāṃ kuruc tritvaṃ vrajatu te rājan brāhmaṇā hy atra kāraṇama trīn aśvamedhān atra tvaṃ saṃprāpya bahudakṣiṇānc jñātivadhyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prahāsyasi narādhipaa pavitraṃ paramaṃ hy etat pāvanānāṃ ca pāvanamc yad aśvamedhāvabhṛthaṃ prāpsyase kurunandanaa ity uktaḥ sa tu tejasvī vyāsenāmitatejasāc dīkṣāṃ viveśa dharmātmā vājimedhāptaye tadāe narādhipaḥ prāyajata vājimedhaṃ mahākratumf bahvannadakṣiṇaṃ rājā sarvakāmaguṇānvitama tatra vedavido rājaṃś cakruḥ karmāṇi yājakāḥc parikramantaḥ śāstrajñā vidhivat sādhuśikṣitāḥa na teṣāṃ skhalitaṃ tatra nāsīd apahutaṃ tathāc kramayuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca cakrus tatra dvijarṣabhāḥa kṛtvā pravargyaṃ dharmajñā yathāvad dvijasattamāḥc cakrus te vidhivad rājaṃs tathaivābhiṣavaṃ dvijāḥa abhiṣūya tato rājan somaṃ somapasattamāḥc savanāny ānupūrvyeṇa cakruḥ śāstrānusāriṇaḥa na tatra kṛpaṇaḥ kaś cin na daridro babhūva hac kṣudhito duḥkhito vāpi prākṛto vāpi mānavaḥa bhojanaṃ bhojanārthibhyo dāpayām āsa nityadāc bhīmaseno mahātejāḥ satataṃ rājaśāsanāta saṃstare kuśalāś cāpi sarvakarmāṇi yājakāḥc divase divase cakrur yathāśāstrārthacakṣuṣaḥa nāṣaḍaṅgavid atrāsīt sadasyas tasya dhīmataḥc nāvrato nānupādhyāyo na ca vādākṣamo dvijaḥa tato yūpocchraye prāpte ṣaḍ bailvān bharatarṣabhac khādirān bilvasamitāṃs tāvataḥ sarvavarṇinaḥa devadārumayau dvau tu yūpau kurupateḥ kratauc śleṣmātakamayaṃ caikaṃ yājakāḥ samakārayand sarvān etān yathāśāstraṃ yājakāḥ samayojayana śobhārthaṃ cāparān yūpān kāñcanān puruṣarṣabhac sa bhīmaḥ kārayām āsa dharmarājasya śāsanāta te vyarājanta rājarṣe vāsobhir upaśobhitāḥc narendrābhigatā devān yathā saptarṣayo divia iṣṭakāḥ kāñcanīś cātra cayanārthaṃ kṛtābhavanc śuśubhe cayanaṃ tatra dakṣasyeva prajāpateḥa catuścityaḥ sa tasyāsīd aṣṭādaśakarātmakaḥc sa rukmapakṣo nicitas triguṇo garuḍākṛtiḥa tato niyuktāḥ paśavo yathāśāstraṃ manīṣibhiḥc taṃ taṃ devaṃ samuddiśya pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaś ca yea ṛṣabhāḥ śāstrapaṭhitās tathā jalacarāś ca yec sarvāṃs tān abhyayuñjaṃs te tatrāgnicayakarmaṇia yūpeṣu niyataṃ cāsīt paśūnāṃ triśataṃ tathāc aśvaratnottaraṃ rājñaḥ kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥa sa yajñaḥ śuśubhe tasya sākṣād devarṣisaṃkulaḥc gandharvagaṇasaṃkīrṇaḥ śobhito psarasāṃ gaṇaiḥa sa kiṃpuruṣagītaiś ca kiṃnarair upaśobhitaḥc siddhavipranivāsaiś ca samantād abhisaṃvṛtaḥa tasmin sadasi nityās tu vyāsaśiṣyā dvijottamāḥc sarvaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ kuśalā yajñakarmasua nāradaś ca babhūvātra tumburuś ca mahādyutiḥc viśvāvasuś citrasenas tathānye gītakovidāḥa gandharvā gītakuśalā nṛtteṣu ca viśāradāḥc ramayanti sma tān viprān yajñakarmāntareṣv atha vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa śamayitvā paśūn anyān vidhivad dvijasattamāḥc turagaṃ taṃ yathāśāstram ālabhanta dvijātayaḥa tataḥ saṃjñāpya turagaṃ vidhivad yājakarṣabhāḥc upasaṃveśayan rājaṃs tatas tāṃ drupadātmajāmd sarvaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ kuśalā yajñakarmasue kalābhis tisṛbhī rājan yathāvidhi manasvinīma uddhṛtya tu vapāṃ tasya yathāśāstraṃ dvijarṣabhāḥc śrapayām āsur avyagrāḥ śāstravad bharatarṣabhaa taṃ vapādhūmagandhaṃ tu dharmarājaḥ sahānujaḥc upājighrad yathānyāyaṃ sarvapāpmāpahaṃ tadāa śiṣṭāny aṅgāni yāny āsaṃs tasyāśvasya narādhipac tāny agnau juhuvur dhīrāḥ samastāḥ ṣoḍaśartvijaḥa saṃsthāpyaivaṃ tasya rājñas taṃ kratuṃ śakratejasaḥc vyāsaḥ saśiṣyo bhagavān vardhayām āsa taṃ nṛpama tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prādāt sadasyebhyo yathāvidhic koṭīsahasraṃ niṣkāṇāṃ vyāsāya tu vasuṃdharāma pratigṛhya dharāṃ rājan vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥc abravīd bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhirama pṛthivī bhavatas tv eṣā saṃnyastā rājasattamac niṣkrayo dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ brāhmaṇā hi dhanārthinaḥa yudhiṣṭhiras tu tān viprān pratyuvāca mahāmanāḥc bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito dhīmān madhye rājñāṃ mahātmanāma aśvamedhe mahāyajñe pṛthivī dakṣiṇā smṛtāc arjunena jitā seyam ṛtvigbhyaḥ prāpitā mayāa vanaṃ pravekṣye viprendrā vibhajadhvaṃ mahīm imāmc caturdhā pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā cāturhotrapramāṇataḥa nāham ādātum icchāmi brahmasvaṃ munisattamāḥc idaṃ hi me mataṃ nityaṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca mamānaghāḥa ity uktavati tasmiṃs te bhrātaro draupadī ca sāc evam etad iti prāhus tad abhūd romaharṣaṇama tato ntarikṣe vāg āsīt sādhu sādhv iti bhāratac tathaiva dvijasaṃghānāṃ śaṃsatāṃ vibabhau svanaḥa dvaipāyanas tathoktas tu punar eva yudhiṣṭhiramc uvāca madhye viprāṇām idaṃ saṃpūjayan muniḥa dattaiṣā bhavatā mahyaṃ tāṃ te pratidadāmy ahamc hiraṇyaṃ dīyatām ebhyo dvijātibhyo dharās tu tea tato bravīd vāsudevo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc yathāha bhagavān vyāsas tathā tat kartum arhasia ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭhaḥ prītātmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahac koṭikoṭikṛtāṃ prādād dakṣiṇāṃ triguṇāṃ kratoḥa na kariṣyati tal loke kaś cid anyo narādhipaḥc yat kṛtaṃ kurusiṃhena maruttasyānukurvatāa pratigṛhya tu tad dravyaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥc ṛtvigbhyaḥ pradadau vidvāṃś caturdhā vyabhajaṃś ca tea pṛthivyā niṣkrayaṃ dattvā tad dhiraṇyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥc dhūtapāpmā jitasvargo mumude bhrātṛbhiḥ sahaa ṛtvijas tam aparyantaṃ suvarṇanicayaṃ tadāc vyabhajanta dvijātibhyo yathotsāhaṃ yathābalama yajñavāṭe tu yat kiṃ cid dhiraṇyam api bhūṣaṇamc toraṇāni ca yūpāṃś ca ghaṭāḥ pātrīs tatheṣṭakāḥe yudhiṣṭhirābhyanujñātāḥ sarvaṃ tad vyabhajan dvijāḥa anantaraṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ kṣatriyā jahrire vasuc tathā viṭśūdrasaṃghāś ca tathānye mlecchajātayaḥe kālena mahatā jahrus tat suvarṇaṃ tatas tataḥa tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve muditā jagmur ālayānc tarpitā vasunā tena dharmarājñā mahātmanāa svam aṃśaṃ bhagavān vyāsaḥ kuntyai pādābhivādanātc pradadau tasya mahato hiraṇyasya mahādyutiḥa śvaśurāt prītidāyaṃ taṃ prāpya sā prītamānasāc cakāra puṇyaṃ loke tu sumahāntaṃ pṛthā tadāa gatvā tv avabhṛthaṃ rājā vipāpmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahac sabhājyamānaḥ śuśubhe mahendro daivatair ivaa pāṇḍavāś ca mahīpālaiḥ sametaiḥ saṃvṛtās tadāc aśobhanta mahārāja grahās tārāgaṇair ivaa rājabhyo pi tataḥ prādād ratnāni vividhāni cac gajān aśvān alaṃkārān striyo vastrāṇi kāñcanama tad dhanaugham aparyantaṃ pārthaḥ pārthivamaṇḍalec visṛjañ śuśubhe rājā yathā vaiśravaṇas tathāa ānāyya ca tathā vīraṃ rājānaṃ babhruvāhanamc pradāya vipulaṃ vittaṃ gṛhān prāsthāpayat tadāa duḥśalāyāś ca taṃ pautraṃ bālakaṃ pārthivarṣabhac svarājye pitṛbhir gupte prītyā samabhiṣecayata rājñaś caivāpi tān sarvān suvibhaktān supūjitānc prasthāpayām āsa vaśī kururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥd govindaṃ ca mahātmānaṃ baladevaṃ mahābalamd tathānyān vṛṣṇivīrāṃś ca pradyumnādīn sahasraśaḥd pūjayitvā mahārāja yathāvidhi mahādyutiḥd bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājā prāsthāpayad ariṃdamaḥa evaṃ babhūva yajñaḥ sa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥc bahvannadhanaratnaughaḥ surāmaireyasāgaraḥa sarpiḥpaṅkā hradā yatra bahavaś cānnaparvatāḥc rasālākardamāḥ kulyā babhūvur bharatarṣabhaa bhakṣyaṣāṇḍavarāgāṇāṃ kriyatāṃ bhujyatām itic paśūnāṃ vadhyatāṃ cāpi nāntas tatra sma dṛśyatea mattonmattapramuditaṃ pragītayuvatījanamc mṛdaṅgaśaṅkhaśabdaiś ca manoramam abhūt tadāa dīyatāṃ bhujyatāṃ ceti divārātram avāritama   tatra śabdo mahān abhūta pīyatāṃ dīyatāṃ cetic taṃ mahotsavasaṃkāśam atihṛṣṭajanākulame kathayanti sma puruṣā nānādeśanivāsinaḥa varṣitvā dhanadhārābhiḥ kāmai ratnair dhanais tathāc vipāpmā bharataśreṣṭhaḥ kṛtārthaḥ prāviśat puram janamejaya uvācaa pitāmahasya me yajñe dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥc yad āścaryam abhūt kiṃ cit tad bhavān vaktum arhati vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa śrūyatāṃ rājaśārdūla mahad āścaryam uttamamc aśvamedhe mahāyajñe nivṛtte yad abhūd vibhoa tarpiteṣu dvijāgryeṣu jñātisaṃbandhibandhuṣuc dīnāndhakṛpaṇe cāpi tadā bharatasattamaa ghuṣyamāṇe mahādāne dikṣu sarvāsu bhāratac patatsu puṣpavarṣeṣu dharmarājasya mūrdhania bilān niṣkramya nakulo rukmapārśvas tadānaghac vajrāśanisamaṃ nādam amuñcata viśāṃ patea sakṛd utsṛjya taṃ nādaṃ trāsayāno mṛgadvijānc mānuṣaṃ vacanaṃ prāha dhṛṣṭo bilaśayo mahāna saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo narādhipāḥc uñchavṛtter vadānyasya kurukṣetranivāsinaḥa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā nakulasya viśāṃ patec vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ sarve te brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥa tataḥ sametya nakulaṃ paryapṛcchanta te dvijāḥc kutas tvaṃ samanuprāpto yajñaṃ sādhusamāgamama kiṃ balaṃ paramaṃ tubhyaṃ kiṃ śrutaṃ kiṃ parāyaṇamc kathaṃ bhavantaṃ vidyāma yo no yajñaṃ vigarhasea avilupyāgamaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vidhijñair yājakaiḥ kṛtamc yathāgamaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kartavyaṃ ca yathākṛtama pūjārhāḥ pūjitāś cātra vidhivac chāstracakṣuṣāc mantrapūtaṃ hutaś cāgnir dattaṃ deyam amatsarama tuṣṭā dvijarṣabhāś cātra dānair bahuvidhair apic kṣatriyāś ca suyuddhena śrāddhair api pitāmahāḥa pālanena viśas tuṣṭāḥ kāmais tuṣṭā varastriyaḥc anukrośais tathā śūdrā dānaśeṣaiḥ pṛthagjanāḥa jñātisaṃbandhinas tuṣṭāḥ śaucena ca nṛpasya naḥc devā havirbhiḥ puṇyaiś ca rakṣaṇaiḥ śaraṇāgatāḥa yad atra tathyaṃ tad brūhi satyasaṃdha dvijātiṣuc yathāśrutaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ pṛṣṭo brāhmaṇakāmyayāa śraddheyavākyaḥ prājñas tvaṃ divyaṃ rūpaṃ bibharṣi cac samāgataś ca viprais tvaṃ tattvato vaktum arhasia iti pṛṣṭo dvijais taiḥ sa prahasya nakulo bravītc naiṣānṛtā mayā vāṇī proktā darpeṇa vā dvijāḥa yan mayoktam idaṃ kiṃ cid yuṣmābhiś cāpy upaśrutamc saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo narādhipāḥe uñchavṛtter vadānyasya kurukṣetranivāsinaḥa ity avaśyaṃ mayaitad vo vaktavyaṃ dvijapuṃgavāḥc śṛṇutāvyagramanasaḥ śaṃsato me dvijarṣabhāḥa anubhūtaṃ ca dṛṣṭaṃ ca yan mayādbhutam uttamamc uñchavṛtter yathāvṛttaṃ kurukṣetranivāsinaḥa svargaṃ yena dvijaḥ prāptaḥ sabhāryaḥ sasutasnuṣaḥc yathā cārdhaṃ śarīrasya mamedaṃ kāñcanīkṛtam nakula uvācaa hanta vo vartayiṣyāmi dānasya paramaṃ phalamc nyāyalabdhasya sūkṣmasya vipradattasya yad dvijāḥa dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre dharmajñair bahubhir vṛtec uñchavṛttir dvijaḥ kaś cit kāpotir abhavat purāa sabhāryaḥ saha putreṇa sasnuṣas tapasi sthitaḥc vadhūcaturtho vṛddhaḥ sa dharmātmā niyatendriyaḥa ṣaṣṭhe kāle tadā vipro bhuṅkte taiḥ saha suvrataḥc ṣaṣṭhe kāle kadā cic ca tasyāhāro na vidyatee bhuṅkte nyasmin kadā cit sa ṣaṣṭhe kāle dvijottamaḥa kapotadharmiṇas tasya durbhikṣe sati dāruṇec nāvidyata tadā viprāḥ saṃcayas tān nibodhatae kṣīṇauṣadhisamāvāyo dravyahīno bhavat tadāa kāle kāle sya saṃprāpte naiva vidyeta bhojanamc kṣudhāparigatāḥ sarve prātiṣṭhanta tadā tu tea uñchaṃs tadā śuklapakṣe madhyaṃ tapati bhāskarec uṣṇārtaś ca kṣudhārtaś ca sa vipras tapasi sthitaḥe uñcham aprāptavān eva sārdhaṃ parijanena haa sa tathaiva kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ spṛṣṭvā toyaṃ yathāvidhic kṣapayām āsa taṃ kālaṃ kṛcchraprāṇo dvijottamaḥa atha ṣaṣṭhe gate kāle yavaprastham upārjayatc yavaprasthaṃ ca te saktūn akurvanta tapasvinaḥa kṛtajapyāhvikās te tu hutvā vahniṃ yathāvidhic kuḍavaṃ kuḍavaṃ sarve vyabhajanta tapasvinaḥa athāgacchad dvijaḥ kaś cid atithir bhuñjatāṃ tadāc te taṃ dṛṣṭvātithiṃ tatra prahṛṣṭamanaso bhavana te bhivādya sukhapraśnaṃ pṛṣṭvā tam atithiṃ tadāc viśuddhamanaso dāntāḥ śraddhādamasamanvitāḥa anasūyavo gatakrodhāḥ sādhavo gatamatsarāḥc tyaktamānā jitakrodhā dharmajñā dvijasattamāḥa sabrahmacaryaṃ svaṃ gotraṃ samākhyāya parasparamc kuṭīṃ praveśayām āsuḥ kṣudhārtam atithiṃ tadāa idam arghyaṃ ca pādyaṃ ca bṛsī ceyaṃ tavānaghac śucayaḥ saktavaś ceme niyamopārjitāḥ prabhoe pratigṛhṇīṣva bhadraṃ te mayā dattā dvijottamaa ity uktaḥ pratigṛhyātha saktūnāṃ kuḍavaṃ dvijaḥc bhakṣayām āsa rājendra na ca tuṣṭiṃ jagāma saḥa sa uñchavṛttiḥ taṃ prekṣya kṣudhāparigataṃ dvijamc āhāraṃ cintayām āsa kathaṃ tuṣṭo bhaved itia tasya bhāryābravīd rājan madbhāgo dīyatām itic gacchatv eṣa yathākāmaṃ saṃtuṣṭo dvijasattamaḥa iti bruvantīṃ tāṃ sādhvīṃ dharmātmā sa dvijarṣabhaḥc kṣudhāparigatāṃ jñātvā saktūṃs tān nābhyanandatad ātmānumānato vidvān sa tu viprarṣabhas tadāa jānan vṛddhāṃ kṣudhārtāṃ ca śrāntāṃ glānāṃ tapasvinīmc tvagasthibhūtāṃ vepantīṃ tato bhāryām uvāca tāma api kīṭapataṃgānāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ caiva śobhanec striyo rakṣyāś ca poṣyāś ca naivaṃ tvaṃ vaktum arhasia anukampito naro nāryā puṣṭo rakṣita eva cac prapated yaśaso dīptān na ca lokān avāpnuyātd dharmakāmārthakāryāṇi śuśrūṣā kulasaṃtatiḥd dāreṣv adhīno dharmaś ca pitṝṇām ātmanas tathād na vetti karmato bhāryārakṣaṇe yo kṣamaḥ pumānd ayaśo mahad āpnoti narakāṃś caiva gacchatia ity uktā sā tataḥ prāha dharmārthau nau samau dvijac saktuprasthacaturbhāgaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ prasīda mea satyaṃ ratiś ca dharmaś ca svargaś ca guṇanirjitaḥc strīṇāṃ patisamādhīnaṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ ca dvijottamaa ṛtur mātuḥ pitur bījaṃ daivataṃ paramaṃ patiḥc bhartuḥ prasādāt strīṇāṃ vai ratiḥ putraphalaṃ tathāa pālanād dhi patis tvaṃ me bhartāsi bharaṇān mamac putrapradānād varadas tasmāt saktūn gṛhāṇa mea jarāparigato vṛddhaḥ kṣudhārto durbalo bhṛśamc upavāsapariśrānto yadā tvam api karśitaḥa ity uktaḥ sa tayā saktūn pragṛhyedaṃ vaco bravītc dvija saktūn imān bhūyaḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva sattamaa sa tān pragṛhya bhuktvā ca na tuṣṭim agamad dvijaḥc tam uñchavṛttir ālakṣya tataś cintāparo bhavatd tam uvāca tataḥ putraḥ pitaraṃ dīnamānasamd praśrayāvanato bhūtvā hetuyuktam idaṃ vacaḥ putra uvācaa saktūn imān pragṛhya tvaṃ dehi viprāya sattamac ity evaṃ sukṛtaṃ manye tasmād etat karomy ahama bhavān hi paripālyo me sarvayatnair dvijottamac sādhūnāṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ hy etat pitur vṛddhasya poṣaṇama putrārtho vihito hy eṣa sthāvirye paripālanamc śrutir eṣā hi viprarṣe triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāa prāṇadhāraṇamātreṇa śakyaṃ kartuṃ tapas tvayāc prāṇo hi paramo dharmaḥ sthito deheṣu dehinām pitovācaa api varṣasahasrī tvaṃ bāla eva mato mamac utpādya putraṃ hi pitā kṛtakṛtyo bhavaty utaa bālānāṃ kṣud balavatī jānāmy etad ahaṃ vibhoc vṛddho haṃ dhārayiṣyāmi tvaṃ balī bhava putrakaa jīrṇena vayasā putra na mā kṣud bādhate pi cac dīrghakālaṃ tapas taptaṃ na me maraṇato bhayam putra uvācaa apatyam asmi te putras trāṇāt putro hi viśrutaḥc ātmā putraḥ smṛtas tasmāt trāhy ātmānam ihātmanād putro haṃ tava viprarṣe tvayā pālyo smi sarvadād idānīṃ tu imān saktūn dīyatāṃ kṣudhitāya ca pitovācaa rūpeṇa sadṛśas tvaṃ me śīlena ca damena cac parīkṣitaś ca bahudhā saktūn ādadmi te tataḥd praśrayeṇa tathā buddhyā vṛttyā kṣāntyā tathaiva caa ity uktvādāya tān saktūn prītātmā dvijasattamaḥc prahasann iva viprāya sa tasmai pradadau tadāa bhuktvā tān api saktūn sa naiva tuṣṭo babhūva hac uñchavṛttis tu savrīḍo babhūva dvijasattamaḥa taṃ vai vadhūḥ sthitā sādhvī brāhmaṇapriyakāmyayāc saktūn ādāya saṃhṛṣṭā guruṃ taṃ vākyam abravīta saṃtānāt tava saṃtānaṃ mama vipra bhaviṣyatic saktūn imān atithaye gṛhītvā tvaṃ prayaccha mea tava prasavanirvṛtyā mama lokāḥ kilākṣayāḥc pautreṇa tān avāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocatia dharmādyā hi yathā tretā vahnitretā tathaiva cac tathaiva putrapautrāṇāṃ svarge tretā kilākṣayāa pitṝṃs trāṇāt tārayati putra ity anuśuśrumac putrapautraiś ca niyataṃ sādhulokān upāśnute śvaśura uvācaa vātātapaviśīrṇāṅgīṃ tvāṃ vivarṇāṃ nirīkṣya vaic karśitāṃ suvratācāre kṣudhāvihvalacetasama kathaṃ saktūn grahīṣyāmi bhūtvā dharmopaghātakaḥc kalyāṇavṛtte kalyāṇi naivaṃ tvaṃ vaktum arhasia ṣaṣṭhe kāle vratavatīṃ śīlaśaucasamanvitāmc kṛcchravṛttiṃ nirāhārāṃ drakṣyāmi tvāṃ kathaṃ nv ahama bālā kṣudhārtā nārī ca rakṣyā tvaṃ satataṃ mayāc upavāsapariśrāntā tvaṃ hi bāndhavanandinī snuṣovācaa guror mama gurus tvaṃ vai yato daivatadaivatamc devātidevas tasmāt tvaṃ saktūn ādatsva me vibhoa dehaḥ prāṇaś ca dharmaś ca śuśrūṣārtham idaṃ guroḥc tava vipra prasādena lokān prāpsyāmy abhīpsitāna avekṣyā iti kṛtvā tvaṃ dṛḍhabhaktyeti vā dvijac cintyā mameyam iti vā saktūn ādātum arhasi śvaśura uvācaa anena nityaṃ sādhvī tvaṃ śīlavṛttena śobhasec yā tvaṃ dharmavratopetā guruvṛttim avekṣasea tasmāt saktūn grahīṣyāmi vadhūr nārhasi vañcanāmc gaṇayitvā mahābhāge tvaṃ hi dharmabhṛtāṃ varāa ity uktvā tān upādāya saktūn prādād dvijātayec tatas tuṣṭo bhavad vipras tasya sādhor mahātmanaḥa prītātmā sa tu taṃ vākyam idam āha dvijarṣabhamc vāgmī tadā dvijaśreṣṭho dharmaḥ puruṣavigrahaḥa śuddhena tava dānena nyāyopāttena yatnataḥc yathāśakti vimuktena prīto smi dvijasattamaa aho dānaṃ ghuṣyate te svarge svarganivāsibhiḥc gaganāt puṣpavarṣaṃ ca paśyasva patitaṃ bhuvid gantāśu devavarṣāṇi anantāni mahāmatea surarṣidevagandharvā ye ca devapuraḥsarāḥc stuvanto devadūtāś ca sthitā dānena vismitāḥa brahmarṣayo vimānasthā brahmalokagatāś ca yec kāṅkṣante darśanaṃ tubhyaṃ divaṃ gaccha dvijarṣabhaa pitṛlokagatāḥ sarve tāritāḥ pitaras tvayāc anāgatāś ca bahavaḥ subahūni yugāni caa brahmacaryeṇa yajñena dānena tapasā tathāc agahvareṇa dharmeṇa tasmād gaccha divaṃ dvijaa śraddhayā parayā yas tvaṃ tapaś carasi suvratac tasmād devās tavānena prītā dvijavarottamac prītātmā devatāḥ sarve yate na tapasā tathāa sarvasvam etad yasmāt te tyaktaṃ śuddhena cetasāc kṛcchrakāle tataḥ svargo jito yaṃ tava karmaṇāa kṣudhā nirṇudati prajñāṃ dharmyāṃ buddhiṃ vyapohatic kṣudhāparigatajñāno dhṛtiṃ tyajati caiva haa bubhukṣāṃ jayate yas tu sa svargaṃ jayate dhruvamc yadā dānarucir bhavati tadā dharmo na sīdatia anavekṣya sutasnehaṃ kalatrasneham eva cac dharmam eva guruṃ jñātvā tṛṣṇā na gaṇitā tvayāa dravyāgamo nṛṇāṃ sūkṣmaḥ pātre dānaṃ tataḥ paramc kālaḥ parataro dānāc chraddhā cāpi tataḥ parāa svargadvāraṃ susūkṣmaṃ hi narair mohān na dṛśyatec svargārgalaṃ lobhabījaṃ rāgaguptaṃ durāsadama tat tu paśyanti puruṣā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥc brāhmaṇās tapasā yuktā yathāśaktipradāyinaḥa sahasraśaktiś ca śataṃ śataśaktir daśāpi cac dadyād apaś ca yaḥ śaktyā sarve tulyaphalāḥ smṛtāḥa rantidevo hi nṛpatir apaḥ prādād akiṃcanaḥc śuddhena manasā vipra nākapṛṣṭhaṃ tato gataḥa na dharmaḥ prīyate tāta dānair dattair mahāphalaiḥc nyāyalabdhair yathā sūkṣmaiḥ śraddhāpūtaiḥ sa tuṣyatia gopradānasahasrāṇi dvijebhyo dān nṛgo nṛpaḥc ekāṃ dattvā sa pārakyāṃ narakaṃ samavāptavāna ātmamāṃsapradānena śibir auśīnaro nṛpaḥc prāpya puṇyakṛtāṃl lokān modate divi suvrataḥa vibhave na nṛṇāṃ puṇyaṃ svaśaktyā svarjitaṃ satāmb nṛṇāṃ puṇyaṃ sa śaktyā ca varjitaṃ garjanaṃ tadāc na yajñair vividhair vipra yathānyāyena saṃcitaiḥa krodho dānaphalaṃ hanti lobhāt svargaṃ na gacchatic nyāyavṛttir hi tapasā dānavit svargam aśnutea na rājasūyair bahubhir iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥc na cāśvamedhair bahubhiḥ phalaṃ samam idaṃ tavaa saktuprasthena hi jito brahmalokas tvayānaghac virajo brahmabhavanaṃ gaccha vipra yathecchakama sarveṣāṃ vo dvijaśreṣṭha divyaṃ yānam upasthitamc ārohata yathākāmaṃ dharmo smi dvija paśya māma pāvito hi tvayā deho loke kīrtiḥ sthirā ca tec sabhāryaḥ sahaputraś ca sasnuṣaś ca divaṃ vrajaa ity uktavākyo dharmeṇa yānam āruhya sa dvijaḥc sabhāryaḥ sasutaś cāpi sasnuṣaś ca divaṃ yayaua tasmin vipre gate svargaṃ sasute sasnuṣe tadāc bhāryācaturthe dharmajñe tato haṃ niḥsṛto bilāta tatas tu saktugandhena kledena salilasya cac divyapuṣpāvamardāc ca sādhor dānalavaiś ca taiḥe viprasya tapasā tasya śiro me kāñcanīkṛtama tasya satyābhisaṃdhasya sūkṣmadānena caiva hac śarīrārdhaṃ ca me viprāḥ śātakumbhamayaṃ kṛtame paśyatedaṃ suvipulaṃ tapasā tasya dhīmataḥa katham evaṃvidhaṃ me syād anyat pārśvam iti dvijāḥc tapovanāni yajñāṃś ca hṛṣṭo bhyemi punaḥ punaḥa yajñaṃ tv aham imaṃ śrutvā kururājasya dhīmataḥc āśayā parayā prāpto na cāhaṃ kāñcanīkṛtaḥa tato mayoktaṃ tad vākyaṃ prahasya dvijasattamāḥc saktuprasthena yajño yaṃ saṃmito neti sarvathāa saktuprasthalavais tair hi tadāhaṃ kāñcanīkṛtaḥc na hi yajño mahān eṣa sadṛśas tair mato mamad saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo matir mama vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity uktvā nakulaḥ sarvān yajñe dvijavarāṃs tadāc jagāmādarśanaṃ rājan viprās te ca yayur gṛhāna etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ mayā parapuraṃjayac yad āścaryam abhūt tasmin vājimedhe mahākrataua na vismayas te nṛpate yajñe kāryaḥ kathaṃ canac ṛṣikoṭisahasrāṇi tapobhir ye divaṃ gatāḥa adrohaḥ sarvabhūteṣu saṃtoṣaḥ śīlam ārjavamc tapo damaś ca satyaṃ ca dānaṃ ceti samaṃ matam janamejaya uvācaa yajñe saktā nṛpatayas tapaḥsaktā maharṣayaḥc śāntivyavasitā viprāḥ śamo dama iti prabhoa tasmād yajñaphalais tulyaṃ na kiṃ cid iha vidyatec iti me vartate buddhis tathā caitad asaṃśayama yajñair iṣṭvā hi bahavo rājāno dvijasattamac iha kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya pretya svargam ito gatāḥa devarājaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥc devarājyaṃ mahātejāḥ prāptavān akhilaṃ vibhuḥd yajñais tapobhir vipulai rājāno dvijasattamāḥd iha loke parāṃ kīrtiṃ vimucya divi saṃsthitāḥa yathā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmārjunapuraḥsaraḥc sadṛśo devarājena samṛddhyā vikrameṇa caa atha kasmāt sa nakulo garhayām āsa taṃ kratumc aśvamedhaṃ mahāyajñaṃ rājñas tasya mahātmanaḥd iti hetor mahārāja nakulo garhayac ca tatd karma rājño mahābuddhe dharmaḥ sūkṣmo mahīpate vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa yajñasya vidhim agryaṃ vai phalaṃ caiva nararṣabhac gadataḥ śṛṇu me rājan yathāvad iha bhārataa purā śakrasya yajataḥ sarva ūcur maharṣayaḥc ṛtvikṣu karmavyagreṣu vitate yajñakarmaṇia hūyamāne tathā vahnau hotre bahuguṇānvitec deveṣv āhūyamāneṣu sthiteṣu paramarṣiṣua supratītais tadā vipraiḥ svāgamaiḥ susvanair nṛpac aśrāntaiś cāpi laghubhir adhvaryuvṛṣabhais tathāa ālambhasamaye tasmin gṛhīteṣu paśuṣv athac maharṣayo mahārāja saṃbabhūvuḥ kṛpānvitāḥa tato dīnān paśūn dṛṣṭvā ṛṣayas te tapodhanāḥc ūcuḥ śakraṃ samāgamya nāyaṃ yajñavidhiḥ śubhaḥa apavijñānam etat te mahāntaṃ dharmam icchataḥc na hi yajñe paśugaṇā vidhidṛṣṭāḥ puraṃdaraa dharmopaghātakas tv eṣa samārambhas tava prabhoc nāyaṃ dharmakṛto dharmo na hiṃsā dharma ucyatea āgamenaiva te yajñaṃ kurvantu yadi hecchasic vidhidṛṣṭena yajñena dharmas te sumahān bhaveta yaja bījaiḥ sahasrākṣa trivarṣaparamoṣitaiḥc eṣa dharmo mahāñ śakra cintyamāno dhigamyatea śatakratus tu tad vākyam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥc uktaṃ na pratijagrāha mānamohavaśānugaḥa teṣāṃ vivādaḥ sumahāñ jajñe śakramaharṣiṇāmc jaṅgamaiḥ sthāvarair vāpi yaṣṭavyam iti bhārataa te tu khinnā vivādena ṛṣayas tattvadarśinaḥc tataḥ saṃdhāya śakreṇa papracchur nṛpatiṃ vasumd dharmasaṃśayam āpannān satyaṃ brūhi mahāmatea mahābhāga kathaṃ yajñeṣv āgamo nṛpate smṛtaḥc yaṣṭavyaṃ paśubhir medhyair atho bījair ajair apia tac chrutvā tu vacas teṣām avicārya balābalamc yathopanītair yaṣṭavyam iti provāca pārthivaḥa evam uktvā sa nṛpatiḥ praviveśa rasātalamc uktveha vitathaṃ rājaṃś cedīnām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥd tasmān na vācyaṃ hy ekena bahujñenāpi saṃśayed prajāpatim apāhāya svayaṃbhuvam ṛte prabhuma anyāyopagataṃ dravyam atītaṃ yo hy apaṇḍitaḥc dharmābhikāṅkṣī yajate na dharmaphalam aśnutea dharmavaitaṃsiko yas tu pāpātmā puruṣas tathāc dadāti dānaṃ viprebhyo lokaviśvāsakārakama pāpena karmaṇā vipro dhanaṃ labdhvā niraṅkuśaḥc rāgamohānvitaḥ so nte kaluṣāṃ gatim āpnutea tena dattāni dānāni pāpena hatabuddhināc tāni sattvam anāsādya naśyanti vipulāny apia tasyādharmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥc dāne na kīrtir bhavati pretya ceha ca durmateḥa api saṃcayabuddhir hi lobhamohavaśaṃgataḥc udvejayati bhūtāni hiṃsayā pāpacetanaḥa evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ lobhād yajate yo dadāti cac sa kṛtvā karmaṇā tena na sidhyati durāgamātd   yo hi dadyād yajeta vād na tasya sa phalaṃ pretya bhuṅkte pāpadhanāgamāta uñchaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ śākam udapātraṃ tapodhanāḥc dānaṃ vibhavato dattvā narāḥ svar yānti dharmiṇaḥa eṣa dharmo mahāṃs tyāgo dānaṃ bhūtadayā tathāc brahmacaryaṃ tathā satyam anukrośo dhṛtiḥ kṣamāe sanātanasya dharmasya mūlam etat sanātanama śrūyante hi purā viprā viśvāmitrādayo nṛpāḥc viśvāmitro sitaś caiva janakaś ca mahīpatiḥe kakṣasenārṣṭiṣeṇau ca sindhudvīpaś ca pārthivaḥa ete cānye ca bahavaḥ siddhiṃ paramikāṃ gatāḥc nṛpāḥ satyaiś ca dānaiś ca nyāyalabdhais tapodhanāḥa brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā ye cāśritās tapaḥc dānadharmāgninā śuddhās te svargaṃ yānti bhārata janamejaya uvācaa dharmāgatena tyāgena bhagavan sarvam asti cetc etan me sarvam ācakṣva kuśalo hy asi bhāṣituma tatoñchavṛtter yad vṛttaṃ saktudāne phalaṃ mahatc kathitaṃ me mahad brahmaṃs tathyam etad asaṃśayama kathaṃ hi sarvayajñeṣu niścayaḥ paramo bhavetc etad arhasi me vaktuṃ nikhilena dvijarṣabha vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc agastyasya mahāyajñe purāvṛttam ariṃdamaa purāgastyo mahātejā dīkṣāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīmc praviveśa mahārāja sarvabhūtahite rataḥa tatrāgnikalpā hotāra āsan satre mahātmanaḥc mūlāhārā nirāhārāḥ sāśmakuṭṭā marīcipāḥa parighṛṣṭikā vaighasikāḥ saṃprakṣālās tathaiva cac yatayo bhikṣavaś cātra babhūvuḥ paryavasthitāḥa sarve pratyakṣadharmāṇo jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥc dame sthitāś ca te sarve dambhamohavivarjitāḥa vṛtte śuddhe sthitā nityam indriyaiś cāpy avāhitāḥc upāsate sma taṃ yajñaṃ bhuñjānās te maharṣayaḥa yathāśaktyā bhagavatā tad annaṃ samupārjitamc tasmin satre tu yat kiṃ cid ayogyaṃ tatra nābhavate tathā hy anekair munibhir mahāntaḥ kratavaḥ kṛtāḥa evaṃvidhes tv agastyasya vartamāne mahādhvarec na vavarṣa sahasrākṣas tadā bharatasattamaa tataḥ karmāntare rājann agastyasya mahātmanaḥc katheyam abhinirvṛttā munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanāma agastyo yajamāno sau dadāty annaṃ vimatsaraḥc na ca varṣati parjanyaḥ katham annaṃ bhaviṣyatia satraṃ cedaṃ mahad viprā muner dvādaśavārṣikamc na varṣiṣyati devaś ca varṣāṇy etāni dvādaśaa etad bhavantaḥ saṃcintya maharṣer asya dhīmataḥc agastyasyātitapasaḥ kartum arhanty anugrahama ity evam ukte vacane tato gastyaḥ pratāpavānc provācedaṃ vaco vāgmī prasādya śirasā munīna yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥc cintāyajñaṃ kariṣyāmi vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥa yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥb sparśayajñaṃ kariṣyāmi vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥb yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥc vyāyāmenāhariṣyāmi yajñān anyān ativratānd dhyeyātmanā hariṣyāmi yajñān etān yatavrataḥa bījayajño mayāyaṃ vai bahuvarṣasamācitaḥc bījaiḥ kṛtaiḥ kariṣye ca nātra vighno bhaviṣyatia nedaṃ śakyaṃ vṛthā kartuṃ mama satraṃ kathaṃ canac varṣiṣyatīha vā devo na vā devo bhaviṣyatia atha vābhyarthanām indraḥ kuryān na tv iha kāmataḥc svayam indro bhaviṣyāmi jīvayiṣyāmi ca prajāḥa yo yad āhārajātaś ca sa tathaiva bhaviṣyatic viśeṣaṃ caiva kartāsmi punaḥ punar atīva hia adyeha svarṇam abhyetu yac cānyad vasu durlabhamc triṣu lokeṣu yac cāsti tad ihāgacchatāṃ svayama divyāś cāpsarasāṃ saṃghāḥ sagandharvāḥ sakiṃnarāḥc viśvāvasuś ca ye cānye te py upāsantu vaḥ sadāa uttarebhyaḥ kurubhyaś ca yat kiṃ cid vasu vidyatec sarvaṃ tad iha yajñe me svayam evopatiṣṭhatue svargaṃ svargasadaś caiva dharmaś ca svayam eva tua ity ukte sarvam evaitad abhavat tasya dhīmataḥb tasya dīptāgnimahasas tv agastyasyātitejasaḥc tatas te munayo dṛṣṭvā munes tasya tapobalame vismitā vacanaṃ prāhur idaṃ sarve mahārthavata prītāḥ sma tava vākyena na tv icchāmas tapovyayamc svair eva yajñais tuṣṭāḥ smo nyāyenecchāmahe vayama yajñān dīkṣās tathā homān yac cānyan mṛgayāmahec tan no stu svakṛtair yajñair nānyato mṛgayāmahea nyāyenopārjitāhārāḥ svakarmaniratā vayamc vedāṃś ca brahmacaryeṇa nyāyataḥ prārthayāmahea nyāyenottarakālaṃ ca gṛhebhyo niḥsṛtā vayamc dharmadṛṣṭair vidhidvārais tapas tapsyāmahe vayama bhavataḥ samyag eṣā hi buddhir hiṃsāvivarjitāc etām ahiṃsāṃ yajñeṣu brūyās tvaṃ satataṃ prabhoa prītās tato bhaviṣyāmo vayaṃ dvijavarottamac visarjitāḥ samāptau ca satrād asmād vrajāmahe vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tathā kathayatām eva devarājaḥ puraṃdaraḥc vavarṣa sumahātejā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapobalama asamāptau ca yajñasya tasyāmitaparākramaḥc nikāmavarṣī devendro babhūva janamejayaa prasādayām āsa ca tam agastyaṃ tridaśeśvaraḥc svayam abhyetya rājarṣe puraskṛtya bṛhaspatima tato yajñasamāptau tān visasarja mahāmunīnb vipine tatra nakulo nakulo ntarhitas tadāc agastyaḥ paramaprītaḥ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi janamejaya uvācaa ko sau nakularūpeṇa śirasā kāñcanena vaic prāha mānuṣavad vācam etat pṛṣṭo vadasva me vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa etat pūrvaṃ na pṛṣṭo haṃ na cāsmābhiḥ prabhāṣitamc śrūyatāṃ nakulo yo sau yathā vāg asya mānuṣīa śrāddhaṃ saṃkalpayām āsa jamadagniḥ purā kilac homadhenus tam āgāc ca svayaṃ cāpi dudoha tāma tat kṣīraṃ sthāpayām āsa nave bhāṇḍe dṛḍhe śucauc tac ca krodhaḥ svarūpeṇa piṭharaṃ paryavartayata jijñāsus tam ṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ kiṃ kuryād vipriye kṛtec iti saṃcintya durmedhā dharṣayām āsa tat payaḥa tam ājñāya muniḥ krodhaṃ naivāsya cukupe tataḥc sa tu krodhas tam āhedaṃ prāñjalir mūrtimān sthitaḥd jite tasmin bhṛguśreṣṭham abhyabhāṣad amarṣaṇaḥa jito smīti bhṛguśreṣṭha bhṛgavo hy atiroṣaṇāḥc loke mithyāpravādo yaṃ yat tvayāsmi parājitaḥa so haṃ tvayi sthito hy adya kṣamāvati mahātmanic bibhemi tapasaḥ sādho prasādaṃ kuru me vibho janamejaya uvācaa sākṣād dṛṣṭo si me krodha gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥc na mamāpakṛtaṃ te dya na manyur vidyate mamaa yān uddiśya tu saṃkalpaḥ payaso sya kṛto mayāc pitaras te mahābhāgās tebhyo budhyasva gamyatāma ity ukto jātasaṃtrāsaḥ sa tatrāntaradhīyatac pitṝṇām abhiṣaṅgāt tu nakulatvam upāgataḥa sa tān prasādayām āsa śāpasyānto bhaved itib tenāpy ukto mahārāja dharmarājasya vai tadāb aśvamedhe tadāgantā śāpān mukto bhaviṣyatic taiś cāpy ukto yadā dharmaṃ kṣepsyase mokṣyase tadāa taiś cokto yajñiyān deśān dharmāraṇyāni caiva hac jugupsan paridhāvan sa yajñaṃ taṃ samupāsadata dharmaputram athākṣipya saktuprasthena tena saḥc muktaḥ śāpāt tataḥ krodho dharmo hy āsīd yudhiṣṭhiraḥa evam etat tadā vṛttaṃ tasya yajñe mahātmanaḥc paśyatāṃ cāpi nas tatra nakulo ntarhitas tadād sa cāpi bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥd yajñiyo yajñanāthaś ca puṇḍarīko janārdanaḥd vāsudevo harir viṣṇur ananto bhaktavatsalaḥd ā samāpter jagannātho yajñaṃ rakṣitavān hariḥd rakṣitvā sa mahābāhur jagāma dvārakāṃ purīmd etat puṇyaṃ mahārāja śṛṇvatāṃ bhuktimuktidamd śrotā ca śrāvako yaś ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatimd janamejayaḥd aśvamedhe purā vṛtte keśavaṃ keśisūdanamd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd dharmasaṃśayam uddiśya kim apṛcchat pitāmahaḥd paścimenāśvamedhena yadā snāto yudhiṣṭhiraḥd tadā rājan namaskṛtya keśavaṃ punar abravītd bhagavan vaiṣṇavā dharmāḥ kiṃphalāḥ kiṃparāyaṇāḥd kiṃ dharmam adhikṛtyātha bhavatotpāditāḥ purād yadi te ham anugrāhyaḥ priyo smi madhusūdanad śrotavyā yadi me kṛṣṇa tan me kathaya suvratad pavitrāḥ kila te dharmāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥd sarvadharmottamāḥ puṇyā bhagavaṃs tvanmukhodgatāḥd yāñ śrutvā brahmahā goghno mātṛhā gurutalpagaḥd pākabhedī kṛtaghnaś ca surāpo brahmavikrayīd mitraviśvāsaghātī ca vīrahā bhrūṇahā tathād tapovikrayiṇaś caiva dānavikrayiṇas tathād ātmavikrayiṇo mūḍhā jīved yaś ca vikarmabhiḥd pāpāḥ śaṭhā naikṛtikā ḍāmbhikā dūṣakās tathād rasabhedakarā ye ca ye ca syur brahmaghātakāḥd śūdrapreṣyakarāś corā viprā ye ca purohitāḥd nikṣepahāriṇaḥ strīghnās tathā ye pāradārikāḥd ete cānye ca pāpās te mucyante te pi kilbiṣātd tān ācakṣva suraśreṣṭha tvadbhaktasya mamācyutad ity evaṃ kathite deve dharmaputreṇa saṃsadid vasiṣṭhādyās tapoyuktā munayas tattvadarśinaḥd śrotukāmāḥ paraṃ guhyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmam uttamamd yudhiṣṭhiraḥd tathā bhāgavatāś caiva tatas taṃ paryavārayand tattvatas tu bhavān eva pādamūlam upāgatamd yadi jānāsi māṃ bhaktaṃ snigdhaṃ vā bhaktavatsalad dharmaguhyāni sarvāṇi vettum icchāmi tattvataḥd dharmān kathaya deveśa yady anugrahabhāg ahamd śrutā me mānavā dharmā vāsiṣṭhāḥ kāśyapās tathād gārgīyā gautamīyāś ca tathā gopālakasya cad parāśarakṛtāḥ pūrvaṃ maitreyasya ca dhīmataḥd aumā māheśvarāś caiva nandidharmāś ca pāvanāḥd brahmaṇā kathitā ye ca kaumārāś ca śrutā mayād dhūmrāyaṇakṛtā dharmāḥ kāṇḍavaiśvānarā apid bhārgavyā yājñavalkyāś ca mārkaṇḍeyakṛtās tathād bhāradvājakṛtā ye ca bṛhaspatikṛtāś ca yed kuṇeś ca kuṇibāhoś ca viśvāmitrakṛtāś ca yed sumantujaiminikṛtāḥ śākuneyās tathaiva cad pulastyapulahodgītāḥ pāvakīyās tathaiva cad agastyagītā maudgalyāḥ śāṇḍilyāś caiva pāvanāḥd vālakhilyakṛtā ye ca ye ca saptarṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥd āpastambakṛtā dharmāḥ śaṅkhasya likhitasya cad prājāpatyās tathā yāmyā māhendrāś ca śrutā mayād vaiyyāghrā vyāsagītāś ca vibhāṇḍakakṛtāś ca yed nāradīyāḥ śrutā dharmāḥ kāpotāś ca śrutā mayād tathā viduravākyāni bhṛgor aṅgirasas tathād krauñcā mṛdaṅgagītāś ca sauryā hārītakāś ca yed ye piśaṅgakṛtāś cāpi kautupā haṃsapālakāḥd uddālakakṛtā dharmā auśanasyās tathaiva cad vaiśaṃpāyanagītāś ca ye cānye py evamādayaḥd etebhyaḥ sarvadharmebhyo deva tvanmukhaniḥsṛtāḥd pāvanatvāt pavitratvād viśiṣṭā iti me matiḥd tasmād dhi tvāṃ prapannasya tvadbhaktasya ca bhāvataḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd yuṣmadīyān varān dharmān puṇyān kathaya me cyutad evaṃ pṛṣṭas tu dharmajño dharmaputreṇa keśavaḥd uvāca dharmān sūkṣmārthān dharmaputrasya harṣitaḥd evaṃ te yasya kaunteya yatno dharmeṣu suvratad tvatsamo durlabho loke na kaś cid iha vidyated dharmaḥ śruto vā dṛṣṭo vā kathito vā kṛto pi vād anumodito vā rājendra punātīha naraṃ sadād dharmaḥ pitā ca mātā ca dharmo nāthaḥ suhṛt tathād dharmo bhrātā sakhā caiva dharmaḥ svāmī paraṃtapad dharmād arthaś ca kāmaś ca dharmād bhogāḥ sukhāni cad dharmād aiśvaryam evāgryaṃ dharmāt svargagatiḥ parād dharmo yaḥ sevitaḥ śuddhas trāyate mahato bhayātd dharmād dvijatvaṃ devatvaṃ dharmaḥ prāpayate naramd yadā ca kṣīyate pāpaṃ kālena puruṣasya tud tadā saṃjāyate buddhir dharmaṃ kartuṃ yudhiṣṭhirad janmāntarasahasrais tu manuṣyatvaṃ hi durlabhamd tad gatvāpīha yo dharmaṃ na karoti sa vañcitaḥd kutsitā ye daridrāś ca virūpā vyādhitās tathād parapreṣyāś ca mūrkhāś ca na tair dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ purād ye ca dīrghāyuṣaḥ śūrāḥ paṇḍitā bhoginas tathād nīrogā rūpasaṃpannās tair dharmaḥ sukṛtaḥ purād evaṃ dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ śuddho nayate gatim uttamāmd adharmaṃ sevamānas tu tiryag yonyāṃ pataty asaud idaṃ rahasyaṃ kaunteya śṛṇu dharmam anuttamamd kathayiṣye paraṃ dharmaṃ mama bhaktasya pāṇḍavad iṣṭas tvam asi me tyarthaṃ prapannaś cāpi māṃ sadād paramārtham api brūmaḥ kiṃ punar dharmasaṃhitāmd idaṃ me mānuṣaṃ janma kṛtam ātmani māyayād dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya duṣṭānāṃ śāsanāya cad mānuṣyaṃ bhāvam āpannaṃ ye māṃ gṛhṇanty avajñayād saṃsarantīha te mūḍhās tiryag yoniṣv anekaśaḥd ye ca māṃ sarvabhūtasthaṃ paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣād madbhaktāṃs tān sadā yuktān matsamīpaṃ nayāmy ahamd madbhaktā na vinaśyanti madbhaktā vītakalmaṣāḥd madbhaktānāṃ tu mānuṣye saphalaṃ janma pāṇḍavad api pāpeṣv abhiratā madbhaktāḥ pāṇḍunandanad mucyante pāpakaiḥ sarvaiḥ padmapatram ivāmbhasād janmāntarasahasreṣu tapasā bhāvitātmanāmd bhaktir utpadyate tāta manuṣyāṇāṃ na saṃśayaḥd yac ca rūpaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvamd na dṛśyate tathā devair madbhaktair dṛśyate yathād aparaṃ yac ca me rūpaṃ prādurbhāveṣu dṛśyated tad arcayanti sarvārthaiḥ sarvabhūtāni pāṇḍavad kalpakoṭisahasreṣu vyatīteṣv āgateṣu cad darśayāmīha tad rūpaṃ tat prapaśyanti me surāḥd sthityutpattivyayakaraṃ yo māṃ jñātvā prapadyated anugṛhṇāmy ahaṃ taṃ vai saṃsārān mocayāmi cad aham ādir hi devānāṃ sṛṣṭā brahmādayo mayād prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya jagat sarvaṃ sṛjāmy ahamd tamomūlo ham avyakto rajo madhye pratiṣṭhitaḥd ūrdhvaṃ sattvaviśālo haṃ brahmādistambasaṃjñitaḥd mūrdhānaṃ me divaṃ viddhi candrādityau ca locaned devāgnir brāhmaṇā vaktraṃ mārutaḥ śvasanaś ca med diśo me bāhavaś cāṣṭau nakṣatrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇamd antarikṣam uro viddhi sarvabhūtāvakāśakamd mārgo meghānilābhyāṃ tu yan mamodaram avyayamd pṛthivīmaṇḍalaṃ yad vai dvīpārṇavanagair yutamd sarvasaṃdhāraṇopetaṃ pādau mama yudhiṣṭhirad sthito hy ekaguṇaḥ khe haṃ dviguṇaś cāsmi māruted triguṇo gnau sthito haṃ vai salile tu caturguṇaḥd śabdādyā ye guṇāḥ pañca mahābhūteṣu pañcasud tanmātrasaṃsthitaḥ so haṃ pṛthivyāṃ pañcadhā sthitaḥd ahaṃ sahasraśīrṣas tu sahasravadanekṣaṇaḥd sahasrabāhūdaradṛk sahasroruḥ sahasrapātd dhṛtvorvīṃ sarvataḥ samyag atyatiṣṭhad daśāṅgulamd sarvabhūtātmabhūtasthaḥ sarvavyāpī tato hy ahamd acintyo ham ananto ham ajaro ham ajo hy ahamd anadyo ham avadhyo ham aprameyo ham avyayaḥd nirguṇo ham agūḍhātmā nirdvandvo nirmamo nṛpad niṣkalo nirvikāro haṃ nidānam amṛtasya tud sudhā cāhaṃ svadhā cāhaṃ svāhā cāhaṃ narādhipad tejasā tapasā cāhaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidhamd snehapāśaguṇair baddhvā dhārayāmy ātmamāyayād caturāśramadharmo haṃ cāturhotraphalāśanaḥd caturmūrtiś caturvyūhaś caturāśramabhāvanaḥd saṃhṛtyāhaṃ jagat sarvaṃ kṛtvā vai garbham ātmanaḥd śayāmi divyayogena pralayeṣu yudhiṣṭhirad sahasrayugaparyantāṃ brāhmīṃ rātriṃ mahārṇaved sthitvā sṛjāmi bhūtāni jaṅgamāni sthirāṇi cad kalpe kalpe ca bhūtāni saṃharāmi sṛjāmi cad na ca māṃ tāni jānanti māyayā mohitāni med mama caivāndhakārasya mārgitavyasya nityaśaḥd praśāntasyeva dīpasya gatir naivopalabhyated na tad asti kva cid rājan yatrāhaṃ na pratiṣṭhitaḥd na ca tad vidyate bhūtaṃ mayi yan na pratiṣṭhitamd yāvanmātraṃ bhaved bhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmam idaṃ jagatd jīvabhūto hy ahaṃ tasmiṃs tāvanmātraṃ pratiṣṭhitamd kiṃ cātra bahunoktena satyam eva bravīmi ted yad bhūtaṃ yad bhaviṣyac ca tat sarvam aham eva tud mayā sṛṣṭāni bhūtāni manmayāni ca bhāratad mām eva na vijānanti māyayā mohitāni med evaṃ sarvaṃ jagad idaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣamd mattaḥ prabhavate rājan mayy eva pravilīyated vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad evam ātmodbhavaṃ sarvaṃ jagad uddiśya keśavaḥd bhagavān uvācad dharmān dharmātmajasyātha puṇyān akathayat prabhuḥd śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena pavitraṃ pāpanāśanamd kathyamānaṃ mayā puṇyaṃ dharmaśāstraphalaṃ mahatd yaḥ śṛṇoti śucir bhūtvā ekacittas tapoyutaḥd svargyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ dharmyaṃ jñeyaṃ yudhiṣṭhirad śraddadhānasya tasyeha yat pāpaṃ pūrvasaṃcitamd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad vinaśyaty āśu tat sarvaṃ madbhaktasya viśeṣataḥd evaṃ śrutvā vacaḥ puṇyaṃ satyaṃ keśavabhāṣitamd prahṛṣṭamanaso bhūtvā cintayanto dbhutaṃ paramd devā brahmarṣayaḥ sarve gandharvāpsarasas tathād bhūtā yakṣagrahāś caiva guhyakā bhujagās tathād vālakhilyā mahātmāno yoginas tattvadarśinaḥd tathā bhāgavatāś cāpi pañcakālam upāsakāḥd kautūhalasamāyuktāḥ prahṛṣṭendriyamānasāḥd śrotukāmāḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaśāsanātd hṛdi kartuṃ ca tad vākyaṃ praṇemuḥ śirasā natāḥd tatas te vāsudevena dṛṣṭāḥ saumyena cakṣuṣād vimuktapāpān ālokya praṇamya śirasā harimd papraccha keśavaṃ dharmaṃ dharmaputraḥ pratāpavānd kīdṛśī brāhmaṇasyātha kṣatriyasyāpi kīdṛśīd vaiśyasya kīdṛśī deva gatiḥ śūdrasya kīdṛśīd kathaṃ badhyeta pāśena brāhmaṇas tu yamālayed kṣatriyo vātha vaiśyo vā śūdro vā badhyate kathamd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad etat karmaphalaṃ brūhi lokanātha namo stu ted pṛṣṭo tha keśavo hy evaṃ dharmaputreṇa dhīmatād uvāca saṃsāragatiṃ cāturvarṇyasya karmajāmd bhagavān uvācad śṛṇu varṇakrameṇaiva dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varad nāsti kiṃ cin naraśreṣṭha duṣkṛtaṃ brāhmaṇasya tud ye sthitāḥ syuḥ sadādhyātme saṃdhyāṃ ye cāpy upāsated yaiś ca pūrṇāhutiḥ prāptā vidhivaj juhvate ca yed vaiśvadevaṃ ca ye kuryuḥ pūjayanty atithīṃś ca yed nityaṃ svādhyāyaśīlāś ca japayajñaparāś ca yed sāyaṃprātar hutāśāś ca śūdrabhojanavarjitāḥd ḍambhānṛtavimuktāś ca svadāraniratāś ca yed pañcayajñaratā ye ca ye gnihotram upāsated dahanti duṣkṛtaṃ yeṣāṃ hūyamānāgnayas trayaḥd naṣṭaduṣkṛtakarmāṇo brahmalokaṃ vrajanti ted brahmaloke punaḥ kāmaṃ gandharvair brahmagāyakaiḥd udgīyamānāḥ prayataiḥ pūjyamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvād brahmaloke pramodante yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavamd kṣatriyo pi sthito rājye svadharmaparipālakaḥd samyak prajāḥ pālayitā ṣaḍbhāganirataḥ sadād yajñadānarato dhīraḥ svadāranirataḥ sadād śāstrānusārī tattvajñaḥ prajākāryaparāyaṇaḥd viprebhyaḥ kāmado nityaṃ bhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇe rataḥd satyasaṃdhaḥ śucir nityaṃ lobhaḍambhavivarjitaḥd kṣatriyo py uttamāṃ yāti gatiṃ devaniṣevitāmd tatra divyāpsarobhis tu gandharvaiś ca viśeṣataḥd sevyamāno mahātejāḥ krīḍate śakrapūjitaḥd caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā tatra devavatd iha mānuṣaloke tu caturvedī dvijo bhavetd kṛṣigopālanirato dharmānveṣaṇatatparaḥd dānadharme pi nirato vipraśuśrūṣakas tathād satyasaṃdhaḥ śucir nityaṃ lobhaḍambhavivarjitaḥd ṛjuḥ svadāranirato hiṃsādrohavivarjitaḥd vaṇigdharmān namuñcan vai devabrāhmaṇapūjakaḥd vaiśyaḥ svargatim āpnoti pūjyamāno psarogaṇaiḥd caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā daśa pañca cad iha mānuṣyaloke ca rājā bhavati vīryavānd suvarṇakoṭyaḥ pañcāśad ratnānāṃ ca śataṃ tathād hastyaśvarathasaṃyuktān mahābhogāṃś ca sevated trayāṇām api varṇānāṃ śuśrūṣānirataḥ sadād viśeṣatas tu viprāṇāṃ dāsavad yas tu tiṣṭhatid ayācitapradātā ca satyaśaucasamanvitaḥd gurudevārcanarataḥ paradāravivarjitaḥd parapīḍām akṛtvaiva bhṛtyavargaṃ bibharti yaḥd śūdro pi svargam āpnoti jīvānām abhayapradaḥd sa svargaloke krīḍitvā varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥd iha mānuṣaloke tu vaiśyo dhanapatir bhavetd evaṃ dharmāt paraṃ nāsti mahat saṃsāramokṣaṇamd na ca dharmāt paraṃ kiṃ cit pāpakarmavyapohanamd tasmād dharmaḥ sadā kāryo mānuṣyaṃ prāpya durlabhamd na hi dharmānuraktānāṃ loke kiṃ cin na durlabhamd svayaṃbhuvihito dharmo yo yasyeha nareśvarad sa tena kṣapayet pāpaṃ samyag ācaritena cad sahajaṃ yad bhavet karma na tat tyājyaṃ hi kena citd sa eva tasya dharmo hi tena siddhiṃ sa gacchatid viguṇo pi svadharmas tu pāpakarma vyapohatid yudhiṣṭhira uvācad evam eva tu dharmo pi kṣīyate pāpavardhanātd bhagavan devadeveśa śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi med bhagavān uvācad śubhasyāpy aśubhasyāpi kṣayavṛddhī yathākramamd śṛṇu pārthiva tat sarvaṃ dharmaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sanātanamd durvijñeyatamaṃ nityam atra bhagnā mahājanāḥd yathaiva śītam udakam uṣṇena bahunāvṛtamd bhavet tu tatkṣaṇād uṣṇaṃ śītatvaṃ ca vinaśyatid yathoṣṇaṃ vā bhaved alpaṃ śītena bahunāvṛtamd śītalaṃ tad bhavet sarvam uṣṇatvaṃ ca vinaśyatid evaṃ tu yad bhaved bhūri sukṛtaṃ vātha duṣkṛtamd tad alpaṃ kṣapayec chīghraṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇād samatve sati rājendra tayoḥ sukṛtapāpayoḥd gūhitasya bhaved vṛddhiḥ kīrtitasya bhavet kṣayaḥd khyāpanenānutāpena prāyaḥ pāpaṃ vinaśyatid tathā kṛtas tu rājendra dharmo naśyati mānadad tāv ubhau gūhitau samyag vṛddhiṃ yātau na saṃśayaḥd tasmāt sarvaprayatnena na pāpaṃ gūhayed budhaḥd tasmād etat prayatnena kīrtayet kṣayakāraṇātd tasmāt saṃkīrtayet pāpaṃ satyaṃ dharmaṃ ca gūhayetd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad evaṃ śrutvā vacas tasya dharmaputro cyutasya tud yudhiṣṭhira uvācad papraccha punar apy anyān dharmān dharmātmajo harimd vṛthā ca kati janmāni vṛthā dānāni yāni cad vṛthā ca jīvitaṃ keṣāṃ narāṇāṃ puruṣottamad kīdṛśāsu vyavasthāsu dānaṃ dattaṃ janārdanad iha loke nubhavati puruṣaḥ puruṣottamad garbhasthe kiṃ samaśnāti kiṃ bālye vāpi keśavad yauvanasthe pi kiṃ kṛṣṇa vārdhake vāpi kiṃ bhavetd sāttvikaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ rājasaṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhavetd tāmasaṃ kīdṛśaṃ deva tarpayiṣyati kiṃ prabhod uttamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ madhyamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhavetd adhamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ teṣāṃ vā vada kiṃ phalamd kiṃ dānaṃ nayati hy ūrdhvaṃ kiṃ gatiṃ madhyamāṃ bhavetd gatiṃ jaghanyām atha vā devadeva bravīhi med etad icchāmi vijñātuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi med tvadīyaṃ vacanaṃ satyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca madhusūdanad vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad evaṃ dharmaṃ prayatnena pṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍusutena vaid uvāca vāsudevo tha dharmān dharmātmajasya cad śṛṇu rājan yathānyāyaṃ vacanaṃ tathyam uttamamd kathyamānaṃ mayā puṇyaṃ sarvapāpavyapohanamd vṛthā ca daśa janmāni catvāri ca narādhipad vṛthā dānāni pañcāśat pañcaiva ca yathākramamd vṛthā ca jīvitaṃ yeṣāṃ te ca ṣaṭ parikīrtitāḥd anukrameṇa sarvāṇi tāni vakṣyāmi pārthivad dharmaghnānāṃ vṛthā janma lubdhānāṃ pāpināṃ tathād vṛthā pākaṃ ca ye śnanti paradāraratāś ca yed pākabhedakarā ye ca ye ca syuḥ satyavarjitāḥd mṛṣṭam aśnāti yaś caiko dṛśyamānas tu bāndhavaiḥd pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva upādhyāyaṃ guruṃ tathād mātulaṃ mātulānīṃ ca yo nihanyāc chapeta vād brāhmaṇaś caiva yo bhūtvā saṃdhyopāsanavarjitaḥd nirbrahmo niḥsvadhaś caiva śūdrāṇām annabhug dvijaḥd mama vā śaṃkarasyāpi brahmaṇo vā yudhiṣṭhirad atha vā brāhmaṇānāṃ tu ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥd vṛthā janmāny athaiteṣāṃ pāpināṃ viddhi pāṇḍavad aśraddhayā ca yad dattam avamānena vāpi yatd ḍambhārtham api yad dattaṃ yat pāṣaṇḍihṛtaṃ nṛpad śūdrācārāya yad dattaṃ yad dattvā cānukīrtitamd roṣayuktaṃ tu yad dattaṃ yad dattam anuśocitamd ḍambhārjitaṃ ca yad dattaṃ yac ca vāpy anṛtārjitamd brāhmaṇasvaṃ ca yad dattaṃ cauryeṇāpy ārjitaṃ ca yatd abhiśastāhṛtaṃ yat tu yad dattaṃ patite dvijed nirbrahmābhihṛtaṃ yat tu yad dhṛtaṃ sarvayācakaiḥd vrātyais tu yad dhṛtaṃ dānam ārūḍhapatitaiś ca yatd yad dattaṃ svairiṇībhartuḥ śvaśurān anuvartined yad grāmayācakahṛtaṃ yat kṛtaghnahṛtaṃ tathād upapātakine dattaṃ vedavikrayiṇe ca yatd strījitāya ca yad dattaṃ vyālagrāhihṛtaṃ ca yatd purohitāya yad dattaṃ cikitsakahṛtaṃ ca yatd yad vaṇikkarmiṇe dattaṃ kṣudramantropajīvined yac chūdrajīvine dattaṃ yac ca devalakāya cad devadravyāśine yac ca yad dattaṃ citrakarmiṇed raṅgopajīvine dattaṃ yac ca māṃsopajīvined sevakāya ca yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ brāhmaṇabruved agnihīne ca yad dattaṃ dattaṃ vārdhuṣikāya cad yad anācāriṇe dattaṃ yat tu dattam anagnayed asaṃdhyopāsine dattaṃ yac chūdragrāmavāsined yan mithyāliṅgine dattaṃ dattaṃ sarvāśine ca yatd nāstikāya ca yad dattaṃ dharmavikrayiṇe ca yatd cārakāya ca yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ kūṭasākṣiṇed grāmakūṭāya yad dattaṃ dānaṃ pārthivapuṃgavad vṛthā bhavati tat sarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇād vipranāmadharā hy ete lolupā brāhmaṇādhamāḥd nātmānaṃ tārayanty ete na dātāraṃ yudhiṣṭhirad etebhyo dattamātrāṇi dānāni ca bahūny apid vṛthā bhavanti rājendra bhasmany ājyāhutir yathād eteṣu yat phalaṃ kiṃ cid bhaviṣyati kathaṃ canad rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca tad vilumpanti harṣitāḥd vṛthā hy etāni dattāni kathitāni samāsataḥd jīvitaṃ tu vṛthā yeṣāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhirad ye māṃ na pratipadyante śaṃkaraṃ vā narādhamāḥd brāhmaṇān vā mahīdevān vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥd hetuśāstreṣu ye saktāḥ kudṛṣṭipatham āśritāḥd vedān nindanty anācārā vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥd kuśalaiḥ kṛtaśāstrāṇi paṭhitvā ye narādhamāḥd viprān nindanti yajñāṃś ca vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥd ye ca durgāṃ kumāraṃ vā vāyum agniṃ jalaṃ ravimd pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva gurum indraṃ niśākaramd mūḍhā nindanty anācārā vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥd vidyamāne dhane yas tu dānadharmavivarjitaḥd mṛṣṭam aśnāti yaś caiko vṛthā jīvati so pi cad vṛthā jīvitam ākhyātaṃ dānakālaṃ bravīmi ted tamoniviṣṭacittena dattaṃ dānaṃ tu yad bhavetd sa tasya phalam aśnāti naro garbhagato nṛpad īrṣyāmātsaryasaṃyukto ḍambhārthaṃ cārthakāraṇātd dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo bālabhāve tad aśnuted bhoktuṃ bhogaṃ na śaktas tu vyādhibhiḥ pīḍito bhṛśamd dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo vṛddhabhāve tad aśnuted śraddhāyuktaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ prasannendriyamānasaḥd dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo yauvane sa tad aśnuted svayaṃ nītvā tu yad dānaṃ bhaktyā pātre pradīyated tat sārvakālikaṃ viddhi dānam āmaraṇāntikamd sāttvikaṃ rājasaṃ caiva tāmasaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhirad dānaṃ dānaphalaṃ caiva gatiṃ ca trividhāṃ śṛṇud dānaṃ dātavyam ity eva matiṃ kṛtvā dvijāya vaid upakāraviyuktāya yad dattaṃ tad dhi sāttvikamd śrotriyāya daridrāya bahubhṛtyāya pāṇḍavad dīyate yat prahṛṣṭena tat sāttvikam udāhṛtamd vedākṣaravihīnāya yat tu pūrvopakāriṇed samṛddhāya ca yad dattaṃ tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtamd saṃbandhine ca yad dattaṃ pramattāya ca pāṇḍavad phalārthibhir apātrāya tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtamd vaiśvadevavihīnāya dānam aśrotriyāya cad dīyate taskarāyāpi tad dānaṃ tāmasaṃ smṛtamd saroṣam avadhūtaṃ ca kleśayuktam avajñayād sevakāya ca yad dattaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtamd devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś caiva munayaś cāgnayas tathād sāttvikaṃ dānam aśnanti tuṣyanti ca nareśvarad dānavā daityasaṃghāś ca grahā yakṣāḥ sarākṣasāḥd rājasaṃ dānam aśnanti varjitaṃ pitṛdaivataiḥd piśācāḥ pretasaṃghāś ca kaśmalā ye malīmasāḥd tāmasaṃ dānam aśnanti gatiṃ ca trividhāṃ śṛṇud sāttvikānāṃ tu dānānām uttamaṃ phalam ucyated madhyamaṃ rājasānāṃ tu tāmasānāṃ tu paścimamd abhigamyopanītānāṃ dānānām uttamaṃ phalamd madhyamaṃ tu samāhūya jaghanyaṃ yācate phalamd ayācitapradātā yaḥ sa yāti gatim uttamāmd samāhūya tu yo dadyān madhyamāṃ sa gatiṃ vrajetd yācito yaś ca vai dadyāj jaghanyāṃ sa gatiṃ vrajetd uttamā daivikā jñeyā madhyamā mānuṣī gatiḥd gatiṃ jaghanyāṃ tiryakṣu gatir eṣā tridhā smṛtād pātrabhūteṣu vipreṣu susthiteṣv āhitāgniṣud yat tu nikṣipyate dānam akṣayyaṃ saṃprakīrtitamd śrotriyāṇāṃ daridrāṇāṃ bharaṇaṃ kuru pārthivad samṛddhānāṃ dvijātīnāṃ kuryāt teṣāṃ ca rakṣaṇamd daridrān vṛttihīnāṃś ca pradānaiḥ suṣṭhu pūjayad āturasyauṣadhaiḥ kāryaṃ nīrujasya kim auṣadhaiḥd pāpaṃ pratigrahītāraṃ pradātur upagacchatid pratigrahītur yat puṇyaṃ pradātāram upaiti tatd tasmād dānaṃ sadā kāryaṃ paratra hitam icchatād vedavidyāvadāteṣu sadā śūdrānnavarjiṣud prayatnena vidhātavyo mahādānamayo nidhiḥd yeṣāṃ dārāḥ pratīkṣante sahasrasyeva lambhanamd bhuktaśeṣasya bhaktasya tān nimantraya pāṇḍavad āmantrya tu nirāśāni na kartavyāni bhāratad kulāni sudaridrāṇāṃ teṣām āśā hatā bhavetd madbhaktā ye naraśreṣṭha madgatā matparāyaṇāḥd madyājino manniyamās tān prayatnena pūjayetd teṣāṃ tu pāvanāyāhaṃ nityam eva yudhiṣṭhirad ubhe saṃdhye pi tiṣṭhāmi hy askannaṃ tad vrataṃ mamad tasmād aṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ madbhaktair vītakalmaṣaiḥd saṃdhyākāleṣu japtavyaṃ satataṃ cātmaśuddhayed anyeṣām api viprāṇāṃ kilbiṣaṃ hi praṇaśyatid ubhe saṃdhye py upāsīta tasmād vipro viśuddhayed daive śrāddhe ca vipraḥ sa niyoktavyo jugupsayād jugupsitas tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ dahaty agnir ivendhanamd bhārataṃ mānavo dharmo vedāḥ sāṅgāś cikitsitamd ājñāsiddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥd na brāhmaṇān parīkṣeta daive karmaṇi dharmavitd mahān bhavet parīvādo brāhmaṇānāṃ parīkṣaṇed brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādaṃ yaḥ kuryāt puruṣādhamaḥd rāsabhānāṃ śunāṃ yoniṃ gacchet puruṣadūṣakaḥd śvatvaṃ prāpnoti ninditvā parīvādāt kharo bhavetd kṛmir bhavaty abhibhavāt kīṭo bhavati matsarīd durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā prākṛtā vā susaṃskṛtāḥd brāhmaṇā nāvamantavyā bhasmacchannā ivāgnayaḥd kṣatriyaṃ caiva sarpaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ ca bahuśrutamd nāvamanyeta medhāvī kṛśān api kadā canad etat trayaṃ hi puruṣaṃ nirdahed avamānitamd tasmād etat prayatnena nāvamanyeta buddhimānd yathā sarvāsv avasthāsu pāvako daivataṃ mahatd tathā sarvāsv avasthāsu brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahatd vyaṅgāḥ kāṇāś ca kubjāś ca vāmanāṅgās tathaiva cad sarve daive niyoktavyā vyāmiśrā vedapāragaiḥd manyuṃ notpādayet teṣāṃ na cāriṣṭān samācaretd manyupraharaṇā viprā na viprāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥd manyunā ghnanti te śatrūn vajreṇendra ivāsurānd brāhmaṇo hi mahad daivaṃ jātimātreṇa jāyated īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmakośasya guptayed kiṃ punar ye ca kaunteya saṃdhyāṃ nityam upāsated yasyāsyena samaśnanti havyāni tridivaukasaḥd kavyāni caiva pitaraḥ kiṃ bhūtam adhikaṃ tathād utpattir eva viprasya mūrtir dharmasya śāśvatīd sa hi dharmārtham utpanno brahmabhūyāya kalpated svam eva brāhmaṇo bhuṅkte svaṃ vaste svaṃ dadāti cad ānṛśaṃsyād brāhmaṇasya bhuñjate hītare janāḥd tasmāt te nāvamantavyā madbhaktā hi dvijāḥ sadād āraṇyakopaniṣadi ye tu paśyanti māṃ dvijāḥd nigūḍhaṃ niṣkalāvasthaṃ tān prayatnena pūjayad svagṛhe vā pravāse vā divārātram athāpi vād śraddhayā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyā madbhaktā ye ca pāṇḍavad nāsti viprasamaṃ daivaṃ nāsti viprasamo guruḥd nāsti viprāt paro bandhur nāsti viprāt paro nidhiḥd nāsti viprāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ na puṇyaṃ brāhmaṇāt paramd na pavitraṃ paraṃ viprān na dvijāt pāvanaṃ paramd nāsti viprāt paro dharmo nāsti viprāt parā gatiḥd pāpakarmasamākṣiptaṃ patantaṃ narake naramd trāyate dānam apy ekaṃ pātrabhūte kṛtaṃ dvijed bālāhitāgnayo ye ca śāntāḥ śūdrānnavarjitāḥd mām arcayanti madbhaktās tebhyo dattam ihākṣayamd pradānaiḥ pūjito vipro vandito vāpi saṃstutaḥd saṃbhāṣito vā dṛṣṭo vā madbhakto divam unnayetd ye paṭhanti namasyanti dhyāyanti puruṣottamamd tān spṛṣṭvā vātha vā dṛṣṭvā naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyated madbhaktā madgataprāṇā madgatā matparāyaṇāḥd bījayoniviśuddhā ye śrotriyāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥd śūdrānnaviratā nityaṃ te punantīha darśanātd svayaṃ nītvā viśeṣeṇa dānaṃ teṣāṃ gṛheṣv athad nivāpayet tu yad bhaktyā tad dānaṃ koṭisaṃmitamd jāgrataḥ svapato vāpi pravāseṣu gṛheṣv athad hṛdaye na praṇaśyāmi yasya viprasya bhāvataḥd saṃpūjito vā dṛṣṭo vā spṛṣṭo vāpi dvijottamaḥd saṃbhāṣito vā rājendra punāty eva naraṃ sadād evaṃ sarvāsv avasthāsu sarvadānāni pāṇḍavad vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad madbhaktebhyaḥ pradattāni svargamārgapradāni vaid śrutvaiva sāttvikaṃ dānaṃ rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ tathād pṛthak pṛthak tv eva gatiṃ phalaṃ cāpi pṛthak pṛthakd avitṛptaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā puṇyaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ punaḥd yudhiṣṭhiro dharmarataḥ keśavaṃ punar abravītd bījayoniviśuddhānāṃ lakṣaṇāni vadasva med bījadoṣeṇa lokeśa jāyante ca kathaṃ narāḥd ācāradoṣaṃ deveśa vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥd brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣaṃ ca guṇadoṣau ca keśavad cāturvarṇasya kṛtsnasya vartamānāḥ pratigrahed kena viprā viśeṣeṇa tarante tārayanti cad bhagavān uvācad etān kathaya deveśa tvadbhaktasya namo stu ted śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttaṃ bījayoniśubhāśubhamd yena tiṣṭhati loko yaṃ vinaśyati ca pāṇḍavad aviplutabrahmacaryo yas tu vipro yathāvidhid subījaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ tasya bījaṃ śubhaṃ bhavetd kanyā cākṣatayoniḥ syāt kulīnā pitṛmātṛtaḥd brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu pariṇītā yathāvidhid sā praśastā varārohā tasyā yoniḥ praśasyated manasā karmaṇā vācā yā bhavet svairacāriṇīd sā kulaghnīti vijñeyā tasyāṃ jātaḥ śvapācakaḥd daive pitrye tathā dāne bhojane sahabhāṣaṇed śayane sahasaṃbandhe na yogyā duṣṭayonijāḥd na tasmād duṣṭayonyāṃ tu garbham utpādayed budhaḥd mohena kurute yas tu kulaṃ hanti tripūruṣamd kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca tathobhau kuṇḍagolakaud ārūḍhapatitāj jātaḥ patitasyāpi yaḥ sutaḥd ṣaḍ ete viśvacaṇḍālā nikṛṣṭāḥ śvapacād apid yo yatra tatra vā retaḥ siktvā śūdrāsu vā caretd kāmacārī sa pāpātmā bījaṃ tasyāśubhaṃ bhavetd aśubhaṃ tad bhaved bījaṃ śuddhāṃ yoniṃ na cārhatid dūṣayaty api tāṃ yoniṃ śunā līḍhaṃ havir yathād śūdrayonau pated bījaṃ hāhāśabdaṃ dvijanmanaḥd kuryāt purīṣagarteṣu patito smīti duḥkhitaḥd mām adhaḥ pātayaty eṣa pāpātmā kāmamohitaḥd adhogatiṃ vrajet kṣipram iti śaptvā patet tu tatd ātmā hi śuklam uddiṣṭaṃ daivataṃ paramaṃ mahatd tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nirundhyāc chuklam ātmanaḥd āyus tejo balaṃ vīryaṃ prajñā śrīś ca mahad yaśaḥd puṇyaṃ ca matpriyatvaṃ ca labhate brahmacaryayād aviplutabrahmacaryair gṛhasthāśramam āśritaiḥd pañcayajñaparair dharmaḥ sthāpyate pṛthivītaled sāyaṃ prātas tu ye saṃdhyāṃ samyaṅ nityam upāsated nāvaṃ vedamayīṃ kṛtvā tarante tārayanti cad yo japet pāvanīṃ devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaramd na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthivīṃ ca sasāgarāmd ye cāsya duḥsthitāḥ ke cid grahāḥ sūryādayo divid te cāsya saumyā jāyante śivāḥ śubhakarās tathād yatra yatra sthitāś caiva dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥd ghorarūpā mahākāyā dharṣayanti na taṃ dvijamd punantīha pṛthivyāṃ ca cīrṇavedavratā narāḥd caturṇām api vedānāṃ sā ca rājan garīyasīd acīrṇavratavedā ye vikarmapatham āśritāḥd brāhmaṇā nāmamātreṇa te pi pūjyā yudhiṣṭhirad kiṃ punar yas tu saṃdhye dve nityam evopatiṣṭhatid śīlam adhyayanaṃ dānaṃ śaucaṃ mārdavam ārjavamd tasmād vedād viśiṣṭāni manur āha prajāpatiḥd bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti brahma yo vedaparamaṃ dvijaḥd svadāranirato dāntaḥ sa vidvān sa ca bhūsuraḥd saṃdhyām upāsate viprā nityam eva dvijottamāḥd te yānti naraśārdūla brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥd sāvitrīmātrasāro pi varo vipraḥ suyantritaḥd nāyantritaś caturvedī sarvāśī sarvavikrayīd sāvitrīṃ caiva vedāṃś ca tulayātolayan purād sadevarṣigaṇāś caiva sarve brahmapuraḥsarāḥd caturṇām api vedānāṃ sā hi rājan garīyasīd yathā vikasite puṣpe madhu gṛhṇati ṣaṭpadāḥd samutsṛjya rasaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam asāravatd evaṃ gṛhītā sāvitrī sarvavede ca pāṇḍavad tasmāt tu sarvavedānāṃ sāvitrī prāṇa ucyated nirjīvā hītare vedā vinā sāvitriyā nṛpad nāyantritaś caturvedī śīlabhraṣṭaḥ sa kutsitaḥd śīlavṛttasamāyuktaḥ sāvitrīpāṭhako varaḥd sahasraparamāṃ devīṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarāmd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad sāvitrīṃ japa kaunteya sarvapāpapraṇāśinīmd trailokyanātha he kṛṣṇa sarvabhūtātmako hy asid nānāyogapara śreṣṭha tuṣyase kena karmaṇād bhagavān uvācad yadi bhārasahasraṃ tu guggulvādi pradhūpayetd karoti cen namaskāram upahāraṃ ca kārayetd stauti yaḥ stutibhir māṃ ca ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ sadād na toṣayati ced viprān nāhaṃ tuṣyāmi bhāratad brāhmaṇe pūjite nityaṃ pūjito smi na saṃśayaḥd ākruṣṭe cāham ākruṣṭo bhavāmi bharatarṣabhad parā mayi gatis teṣāṃ pūjayanti ca māṃ hi ted yad ahaṃ dvijarūpeṇa vasāmi vasudhātaled yas tān pūjayati prājño madgatenāntarātmanād tam ahaṃ svena rūpeṇa paśyāmi narapuṃgavad kubjāḥ kāṇā vāmanāś ca daridrā vyādhitās tathād nāvamānyā dvijāḥ prājñair mama rūpā hi te dvijāḥd ye ke cit sāgarāntāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ dvijasattamāḥd mama rūpaṃ hi teṣv evam arciteṣv arcito smy ahamd bahavas tu na jānanti narā jñānabahiṣkṛtāḥd yathāhaṃ dvijarūpeṇa vasāmi vasudhātaled avamanyanti ye viprān svadharmāt pātayanti ted preṣaṇaiḥ preṣayante ca śuśrūṣāṃ kārayanti cad mṛtāś cātra paratremān yamadūtā mahābalāḥd nikṛntanti yathākāmaṃ sūtramārgeṇa śilpinaḥd ākrośaparivādābhyāṃ ye ramante dvijātiṣud tān mṛtān yamalokasthān nipātya pṛthivītaled ākramyorasi pādena krūraḥ saṃraktalocanaḥd agnivarṇais tu saṃdaṃśair yamo jihvāṃ samuddharetd ye ca viprān nirīkṣante pāpāḥ pāpena cakṣuṣād abrahmaṇyāḥ śruter bāhyā nityaṃ brahmadviṣo narāḥd teṣāṃ ghorā mahākāyā vakratuṇḍā mahābalāḥd uddharanti muhūrtena khagāś cakṣur yamājñayād yaḥ prahāraṃ dvijendrāya dadyāt kuryāc ca śoṇitamd asthibhaṅgaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt prāṇair vā viprayojayetd so nupūrvyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatimd śūlam āropito gatvā jvalane paripacyated bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi pacyamānas tv avākśirāḥd nāvamucyeta durmedhā na tasya kṣīyate gatiḥd brāhmaṇāyāvicāryaivaṃ vrajan vai vadhakāṅkṣayād śatavarṣasahasrāṇi tāmisre paripacyated utpādya śoṇitaṃ gātrāt saṃrambhān matipūrvakamd sa paryāyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatimd tasmān nākuśalaṃ brūyān na śuṣkāṃ giram īrayetd na brūyāt paruṣāṃ vāṇīṃ na caivaitān atikrametd ye viprāñ śraddhayā vācā pūjayanti narottamāḥd arcitaś ca tataś caiva tair bhavāmi na saṃśayaḥd tarjayanti ca ye viprān krośayanti ca bhāratad ākruṣṭas tarjitaś cāhaṃ tair bhavāmi na saṃśayaḥd yaś candanaiś cāgarudhūpadīpaird abhyarcayet kāṣṭhamayīṃ mamārcāmd tenārcito naiva bhavāmi samyagd viprārcanād asmi samarcito hamd vipraprasādād dharaṇīdharo haṃd vipraprasādād asurāñ jayāmid vipraprasādāc ca sadakṣiṇo haṃd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad vipraprasādād ajito ham asmid devadeveśa daityaghna paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi med etat kathaya sarvajña tvadbhaktasya ca keśavad mānuṣasya ca lokasya dharmalokasya cāntaramd kīdṛśaṃ kiṃpramāṇaṃ vā kim adhiṣṭhānam eva cad taranti mānuṣā deva kenopāyena mādhavad tvagasthimāṃsanirmukte pañcabhūtavivarjited kathayasva mahādeva sukhaduḥkham aśeṣataḥd jīvasya karmalokeṣu karmabhis tu śubhāśubhaiḥd anubaddhasya taiḥ pāśair nīyamānasya dāruṇaiḥd mṛtyudūtair durādharṣair ghorair ghoraparākramaiḥd vadhyasyākṣipyamāṇasya vidrutasya yamājñayād puṇyapāpakṛtaṃ tiṣṭhet sukhaduḥkham aśeṣataḥd yamadūtair durādharṣair nīyate vā kathaṃ punaḥd kiṃ vā tatra gatā deva karma kurvanti mānavāḥd kathaṃ dharmaparā yānti devatādvijapūjakāḥd kathaṃ vā pāpakarmāṇo yānti pretapuraṃ narāḥd kiṃ rūpaṃ kiṃ pramāṇaṃ vā varṇaḥ ko vāsya keśavad bhagavān uvācad jīvasya gacchato nityaṃ yamalokaṃ bravīhi med śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasid tat te haṃ kathayiṣyāmi madbhaktasya nareśvarad ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ yudhiṣṭhirad mānuṣyasya ca lokasya yamalokasya cāntaramd na tatra vṛkṣacchāyā vā na taṭākaṃ saro pi vād na vāpyo dīrghikā vāpi na kūpo vā yudhiṣṭhirad na maṇṭapaṃ sabhā vāpi na prapā na niketanamd na parvato nadī vāpi na bhūmer vivaraṃ kva citd na grāmo vāśramo vāpi nodyānaṃ vā vanāni cad na kiṃ cid āśrayasthānaṃ pathi tasmin yudhiṣṭhirad jantor hi prāptakālasya vedanārtasya vai bhṛśamd karaṇais tyaktadehasya prāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagataiḥ punaḥd śarīrāc cālyate jīvo hy avaśo mātariśvanād nirgato vāyubhūtas tu ṣaṭkośāt tu kalevarātd śarīram anyat tadrūpaṃ tadvarṇaṃ tatpramāṇakamd adṛśyaṃ tat praviṣṭas tu so py adṛṣṭena kena citd so ntarātmā dehavatām aṣṭāṅgo yas tu saṃcaretd chedanād bhedanād dāhāt tāḍanād vā na naśyatid nānārūpadharair ghoraiḥ pracaṇḍaiś caṇḍasādhanaiḥd nīyamāno durādharṣair yamadūtair yamājñayād putradāramayaiḥ pāśaiḥ saṃniruddho vaśo balātd svakarmabhiś cānugataḥ kṛtaiḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtaiḥd ākrandamānaḥ karuṇaṃ bandhubhir duḥkhapīḍitaiḥd tyaktvā bandhujanaṃ sarvaṃ nirapekṣas tu gacchatid mātṛbhiḥ pitṛbhiś cāpi bhrātṛbhir mātulais tathād dāraiḥ putrair vayasyaiś ca rudadbhis tyajyate punaḥd adṛśyamānas tair dīnair aśrupūrṇamukhekṣaṇaiḥd svaśarīraṃ parityajya vāyubhūtas tu gacchatid andhakāram apāraṃ taṃ mahāghoraṃ tamovṛtamd duḥkhāntaṃ duṣpratāraṃ ca durgamaṃ pāpakarmaṇāmd duḥsahāyaṃ durantaṃ ca durnirīkṣaṃ durāsadamd durāpam atiduḥkhaṃ ca pāpiṣṭhānāṃ narottamad ṛṣibhiḥ kathyamānaṃ tat pāraṃparyeṇa pārthivad trāsaṃ janayati prāyaḥ śrūyamāṇaṃ kathāsv apid avaśyaṃ caiva gantavyaṃ tadadhvānaṃ yudhiṣṭhirad prāptakālena saṃtyajya bandhūn bhogān dhanāni cad jarāyujair aṇḍajaiś ca svedajair udbhijjais tathād jaṅgamaiḥ sthirajaiś caiva gantavyaṃ yamasādanamd devāsurair manuṣyādyair vaivasvatavaśānugaiḥd strīpuṃnapuṃsakaiś cāpi pṛthivyāṃ jīvasaṃjñitaiḥd madhyamair yuvabhir vāpi bālair vṛddhais
