tathaiva cad jātamātraiś ca garbhasthair gantavyaḥ sa mahāpathaḥd pūrvāhṇe vāparāhṇe vā saṃdhyākāle tha vā punaḥd pradoṣe vārdharātre vā pratyūṣe vāpy upasthited pravāsasthair vanasthair vā parvatasthair jalasthitaiḥd kṣetrasthair vā nabhaḥsthair vā gṛhamadhyagatair apid bhuñjadbhir vā pibadbhir vā khādadbhir vā narottamad āsīnair vā sthitair vāpi śayanīyagatair apid jāgradbhir vā prasuptair vā gantavyas tu mahāpathaḥd mṛtyudūtair durādharṣaiḥ pracaṇḍaiś caṇḍaśāsanaiḥd ākṣipyamāṇā hy avaśāḥ prayānti yamasādanamd kva cid bhītaiḥ kva cit trastaiḥ praskhaladbhiḥ kva cit kva citd krandadbhir vedanārtais tu gantavyaṃ yamasādanamd nirbhartsyamānair udvignair vidhūtair bhayavihvalaiḥd tudyamānaśarīraiś ca gantavyaṃ tarjanaiḥ sadād kaṇṭakākīrṇamārgeṇa taptavālukapāṃsunād dahyamānais tu gantavyaṃ narair dānavivarjitaiḥd kāṣṭhopalaśilāghātair daṇḍolmukakaśāṅkuśaiḥd hanyamānair yamapuraṃ gantavyaṃ dharmavarjitaiḥd medaḥśoṇitapūyārdrair vaktragātraiś ca savraṇaiḥd dagdhakṣatajakīrṇaiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥd krandadbhiś ca rudadbhiś ca krośadbhiś cāpi visvanamd vedanārtaiś ca kūjadbhir vikrośadbhiś ca visvaramd vedanārtaiḥ patadbhiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥd bhagnapādoruhastāṅgair bhagnadantaśirodharaiḥd chinnakaṇṭhoṣṭhanāsaiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥd śaktibhir bhiṇḍipālaiś ca śaṅkutomarasāyakaiḥd tudyamānais tu śūlāgrair gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥd śvabhir vyāghrair vṛkaiḥ kākair bhakṣyamāṇāḥ samantataḥd tudyamānāś ca gacchanti rākṣasair māṃsakhādibhiḥd mahiṣaiś ca mṛgaiś cāpi sūkaraiḥ pṛṣatais tathād bhakṣyamāṇais tadadhvānaṃ gantavyaṃ māṃsakhādibhiḥd sūcīsutīkṣṇatuṇḍābhir makṣikābhiḥ samantataḥd tudyamānais tu gantavyaṃ pāpiṣṭhair bālaghātakaiḥd visrabdhaṃ svāminaṃ mitraṃ striyaṃ vā ghnanti ye narāḥd śastrair nirbhidyamānais tair gantavyaṃ yamasādanamd ghātayanti ca ye jīvān duḥkham āpādayanti cad rākṣasaiś ca śvabhiś caiva bhakṣyamāṇā vrajanti ted ye haranti ca vastrāṇi śayyāḥ prāvaraṇāni cad te yānti vidrutā nagnāḥ piśācā iva tatpathamd gāś ca dhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca balāt kṣetragṛhaṃ tathād ye haranti durātmānaḥ parasvaṃ pāpakāriṇaḥd pāṣāṇair ulmukair daṇḍaiḥ kāṣṭhaghātaiś ca jharjharaiḥd hanyamānaiḥ kṣatākīrṇair gantavyaṃ tair yamālayamd brahmasvaṃ ye harantīha narā narakanirbhayāḥd ākrośantīha vā nityaṃ praharanti ca ye dvijānd śuṣkakaṇṭhā nibaddhās te chinnajihvākṣināsikāḥd pūyaśoṇitadurgandhā bhakṣyante kākajambukaiḥd caṇḍālair bhīṣaṇaiś caṇḍais tudyamānāḥ samantataḥd krośantaḥ karuṇaṃ ghoraṃ gacchanti yamasādanamd tatra cāpi gatāḥ pāpā viṣṭhākūpeṣv anekaśaḥd jīvanto varṣakoṭīs tu kliśyante vedanārditāḥd tataś ca muktāḥ kālena loke cāsmin narādhamāḥd viṣṭhākrimitvaṃ gacchanti janmakoṭiśataṃ nṛpad vidyamānadhanair yas tu lobhaḍambhānṛtānvitaiḥd śrotriyebhyo na dattāni dānāni kurupuṃgavad grīvāpāśanibaddhās te hanyamānāś ca rākṣasaiḥd kṣutpipāsāśramārtās tu yānti pretapuraṃ narāḥd adattadānā gacchanti śuṣkakaṇṭhāsyatālukāḥd annaṃ pānīyasahitaṃ prārthayantaḥ punaḥ punaḥd svāmin bubhukṣātṛṣṇārtā gantuṃ naivādya śaknumaḥd mamānnaṃ dīyatāṃ svāmin pānīyaṃ dīyatāṃ mamad vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad iti bruvantas tair dūtair yāpayanti yamālayamd tac chrutvā vacanaṃ viṣṇoḥ papāta bhuvi pāṇḍavaḥd niḥsaṃjño pi bhayatrasto mūrchayā samabhiplutaḥd tato labdhvā śanaiḥ saṃjñāṃ samāśvasto cyutena saḥd netre prakṣālya toyena bhūyaḥ keśavam abravītd bhīto smy ahaṃ mahādeva śrutvā mārgasya vistaramd bhagavān uvācad kenopāyena tanmārgaṃ taranti puruṣāḥ sukhamd iha ye dhārmikā loke jīvaghātavivarjitāḥd guruśuśrūṣaṇe yuktā devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥd asmān mānuṣyakāl lokāt sabhāryāḥ sahabāndhavāḥd yam adhvānaṃ tu gacchanti yathāvat taṃ nibodha med brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradānāni nānārūpāṇi pārthivad ye prayacchanti vidvadbhyas te sukhaṃ yānti tatpathamd annaṃ ye ca prayacchanti brāhmaṇebhyaḥ susaṃskṛtamd śrotriyebhyo viśeṣeṇa prītyā paramayā yutāḥd te vimānair mahātmāno yānti citrair yamālayamd sevyamānā varastrībhir apsarobhir mahāpathamd ye ca nityaṃ prabhāṣante satyaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ vacaḥd te pi yānty amalābhrābhair vimānais taṃ yamālayamd kapilādyāni puṇyāni gopradānāni ye narāḥd brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchanti śrotriyebhyo viśeṣataḥd te yānty amalavarṇābhair vimānair vṛṣayojitaiḥd vaivasvatapuraṃ prāpya apsarobhir niṣevitāḥd upānahau ca chattraṃ ca śayanāny āsanāni cad viprebhyo ye prayacchanti vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni cad te yānty aśvair vṛṣair vāpi kuñjarair apy alaṃkṛtāḥd dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ sauvarṇacchattraśobhitāḥd ye ca bhakṣyāṇi dāsyanti bhojyaṃ peyaṃ tathaiva cad snigdhānnāny api viprebhyaḥ śraddhayā parayā yutāḥd te yānti kāñcanair yānaiḥ sukhaṃ vaivasvatālayamd varastrībhir yathākāmaṃ sevyamānāḥ sahasraśaḥd ye ca kṣīraṃ prayacchanti ghṛtaṃ dadhi guḍaṃ madhud brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayatnena śraddadhānāḥ susaṃskṛtāḥd cakravākaprayuktais tu yānai rukmamayaiḥ śubhaiḥd yānti gandharvavāditraiḥ sevyamānā yamālayamd ye phalāni prayacchanti puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi cad haṃsayuktair vimānais tu yānti dharmapuraṃ narāḥd ye prayacchanti viprebhyo vicitrānnaṃ ghṛtāplutamd te vrajanty amalābhrābhair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥd puraṃ tat pretanāthasya nānājanasamākulamd pānīyaṃ ye prayacchanti sarvabhūtaprajīvanamd te sutṛptāḥ sukhaṃ yānti vimānair haṃsacoditaiḥd ye tilāṃs tiladhenuṃ vā ghṛtadhenum athāpi vād śrotriyebhyaḥ prayacchanti saumyabhāvasamanvitāḥd somamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair yānais te yānti nirmalaiḥd gīyamānais tu gandharvair vaivasvatapuraṃ nṛpad yeṣāṃ vāpyaś ca kūpāś ca taṭākāni sarāṃsi cad dīrghikāḥ puṣkariṇyaś ca sajalāś ca jalāśayāḥd yānais te yānti candrābhair divyaghaṇṭānināditaiḥd cāmarais tālavṛntaiś ca vījyamānā mahāprabhāḥd nityatṛptā mahātmāno gacchanti yamasādanamd yeṣāṃ devagṛhāṇīha citrāṇy āyatanāni cad manoharāṇi kāntāni darśanīyāni bhānti cad te vrajanty amalābhrābhair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥd puraṃ tat pretanāthasya nānājanasamākulamd vaivasvataṃ ca paśyanti sukhacittaṃ sukhasthitamd yamena pūjitā yānti devasālokyatāṃ tataḥd devān uddiśya lokeṣu prapāsu karakoddhṛtamd śītalaṃ salilaṃ ramyaṃ tṛṣitebhyo diśanti yed te tu tṛptiṃ parāṃ prāpya sukhaṃ yānti mahāpathamd kāṣṭhapādukadā yānti tadadhvānaṃ sukhaṃ narāḥd sauvarṇamaṇipīṭheṣu pādau kṛtvā rathottamed ārāmān vṛkṣaṣaṇḍāṃś ca ropayanti ca ye narāḥd saṃvardhayanti cāvyagrāḥ phalapuṣpopaśobhitānd vṛkṣacchāyāsu ramyāsu śītalāsu svalaṃkṛtāḥd yānti te vāhanair divyaiḥ pūjyamānā muhur muhuḥd sevyamānāḥ surūpābhir uttamābhiḥ prayatnataḥd strībhiḥ kanakavarṇābhir yathākāmaṃ yathāsukhamd aśvayānaṃ tu goyānaṃ hastiyānam athāpi vād ye prayacchanti viprebhyo vimānaiḥ kanakopamaiḥd suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi vidrumaṃ mauktikaṃ tathād ye prayacchanti te yānti vimānaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥd te vrajanti varastrībhiḥ sevyamānā yathāsukhamd bhūmidā yānti taṃ lokaṃ sarvakāmaiḥ sutarpitāḥd uditādityasaṃkāśair vimānair vṛṣayojitaiḥd kanyāṃ ye ca prayacchanti viprāya śrotriyāya cad divyakanyāvṛtā yānti vimānais te yamālayamd sugandhān gandhasaṃyogān puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi cad prayacchanti dvijāgrebhyo bhaktyā paramayā yutāḥd sugandhāḥ suṣṭhuveṣāś ca suprabhāḥ sragvibhūṣaṇāḥd yānti dharmapuraṃ yānair vicitrair apy alaṃkṛtāḥd dīpadā yānti yānaiś ca dyotayanto diśo daśad ādityasadṛśākārair dīpyamānā ivāgnayaḥd gṛhāvasathadātāro grahaiḥ kāñcanavedikaiḥd vrajanti bālasūryābhair dharmarājapuraṃ narāḥd jalabhājanadātāraḥ kuṇḍikākarakapradāḥd pūjyamānā varastrībhir yānti tṛptā mahāgajaiḥd pādābhyaṅgaṃ śirobhyaṅgaṃ pānaṃ pādodakaṃ tathād ye prayacchanti viprebhyas te yānty aśvair yamālayamd viśrāmayanti ye viprāñ śrāntān adhvani karśitānd cakravākaprayuktena yānti yānena te pi cad svāgatena ca yo viprān pūjayed āsanena cad sa gacchati tadadhvānaṃ sukhaṃ paramanirvṛtaḥd namo brahmaṇyadeveti yo māṃ dṛṣṭvābhivādayetd vratavat prayato nityaṃ sa sukhaṃ yāti tatpathamd namaḥ sarvasabhābhyaś cety abhikhyāya dine dined namaskaroti gobhyo yaḥ sa sukhaṃ yāti tatpathamd namo stu priyadattāyety evaṃvādī dine dined bhūmim ākramate prātaḥ śayanād utthitaś ca yaḥd sarvakāmaiḥ sa tṛptātmā sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥd yāti yānena divyena sukhaṃ vaivasvatālayamd anantarāśino ye tu ḍambhāhaṃkāravarjitāḥd te pi sārasayuktena yānti yānena vai sukhamd ye cāpy ekena bhuktena vartante ḍambhavarjitāḥd haṃsayuktair vimānais tu sukhaṃ yānti yamālayamd caturthena ca bhuktena vartante ye jitendriyāḥd yānti te dharmanagaraṃ yānair barhiṇayojitaiḥd tṛtīyadivaseneha bhuñjate ye jitendriyāḥd te pi hastirathaṃ yānti tatpathaṃ kanakojjvalaiḥd ṣaṣṭhāhnakāliko yas tu varṣam ekaṃ tu vartated kāmakrodhavinirmuktaḥ śucir nityaṃ jitendriyaḥd sa yāti kuñjarasthas tu jayaśabdaravair yutaḥd pakṣopavāsino yānti yānaiḥ śārdūlayojitaiḥd dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ divyastrīgaṇasevitamd ye ca māsopavāsaṃ vai kurvate saṃyatendriyāḥd te pi sūryodayaprakhyair yānti yānair yamālayamd agnipraveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanād sa yāty agniprakāśena vimānena yamālayamd prāṇāṃs tyajati yo vipro māṃ prapanno hy anāśakaḥd sa bālārkaprakāśena vrajed yānena tatpathamd praviṣṭo ntarjale yas tu prāṇāṃs tyajati mānavaḥd somamaṇḍalakalpena yāti yānena tatpathamd svaśarīraṃ hi gṛdhrāṇāṃ manmanā yaḥ prayacchatid sa yāti rathamukhyena kāñcanena yamālayamd gokṛte strīkṛte caiva hatā viprakṛte pi cad te yānty amarakanyābhiḥ sevyamānā raviprabhāḥd ye ca kurvanti madbhaktās tīrthayātrāṃ jitendriyāḥd te panthānaṃ mahātmāno yānair yānti sunirvṛtāḥd ye yajanti dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥd haṃsasārasasaṃyuktair yānais te yānti tatpathamd parapīḍām akṛtvaiva bhṛtyān bibhrati ye narāḥd tatpathaṃ te sukhaṃ yānti vimānaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥd ye samāḥ sarvabhūteṣu jīvānām abhayapradāḥd krodhalobhavinirmuktā nigṛhītendriyās tathād pūrṇacandrapratīkāśair vimānais te mahāprabhāḥd yānti vaivasvatapuraṃ devagandharvasevitāḥd ye mām ekāntabhāvena devaṃ tryambakam eva cad pūjayanti namasyanti stuvanti ca dine dined dharmarājapuraṃ yānti yānais te rkasamaprabhaiḥd pūjitās tatra dharmeṇa svayaṃ mālyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥd yānty eva mama lokaṃ vā rudralokam athāpi vād vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad śrutvā yamapurādhvānaṃ jīvānāṃ gamanaṃ tathād dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravītd devadeveśa daityaghna ṛṣisaṃghair abhiṣṭutad bhavān bhavakaraḥ śrīmān sahasrādityasaprabhad sarvasaṃbhava sarvajña sarvadharmapravartakad sarvadānaphalaṃ saumya kathayasva mamācyutad dānaṃ deyaṃ kathaṃ kṛṣṇa kīdṛśāya dvijāya vaid kīdṛśaṃ vā tapaḥ kṛtvā tatphalaṃ kutra bhujyated evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo dharmaputreṇa dhīmatād uvāca dharmaputrāya puṇyān dharmān koṭīdhanapatir bhavetd yaś ca rūpyaṃ prayacched vai daridrāya dvijāya vaid kṛśavṛtte kṛśagave sa muktaḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥd pūrṇacandraprakāśena vimānena virājatād kāmarūpī yathā kāmaṃ svargaloke mahīyated tato vatīrṇaḥ kālena loke cāsmin mahāyaśāḥd sarvalokārcitaḥ śrīmān rājā bhavati vīryavānd tilaparvatakaṃ yas tu śrotriyāya prayacchatid viśeṣeṇa daridrāya tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalamd puṇyaṃ vṛṣāyutotsarge yat proktaṃ pāṇḍunandanad tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpya tatkṣaṇād virajo bhavetd yathā tvaco bhujaṅgo vai tyaktvā śuddhatanur bhavetd tathā tilapradānād vai pāpaṃ tyaktvā viśudhyatid tilaṣaṇḍaṃ prayuñjāno jāmbūnadavibhūṣitamd vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍhaḥ pitṛloke mahīyated ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi kāmarūpī mahāyaśāḥd tilapradātā ramate pitṛloke yathāsukhamd yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tiladhenuṃ narādhipad śrotriyāya daridrāya śṛṇu tasyāpi yat phalamd gosahasrapradānena yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtamd tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti tiladhenuprado naraḥd tilānāṃ kuḍavair yas tu tiladhenuṃ prayacchatid tāvat koṭisamā rājan svargaloke mahīyated aṣṭāḍhakatilaiḥ kṛtvā tiladhenuṃ narādhipad dvātriṃśan niṣkasaṃyuktaṃ viṣuve yaḥ prayacchatid madbhaktyā madgatātmā vai tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud kanyādānasahasrasya vidhidattasya yat phalamd tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpto mama loke mahīyated mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so smiṃl loke bhijāyated ṛgyajuḥsāmavedānāṃ pārago brāhmaṇarṣabhaḥd gāṃ tu yas tu daridrāya śrotriyāya prayacchatid prasannāṃ kṣīriṇīṃ puṇyāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīmd yat kiṃ cid duṣkṛtaṃ karma tasya pūrvakṛtaṃ nṛpad tat sarvaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva vinaśyati na saṃśayaḥd yānaṃ ca vṛṣasaṃyuktaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svalaṃkṛtamd ārūḍhaḥ kāmagaṃ divyaṃ golokam adhigacchatid yāvanti caiva romāṇi tasyā gos tu narādhipad tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi gavāṃ loke mahīyated golokād avatīrṇas tu loke smin brāhmaṇo bhavetd satrayājī vadānyaś ca sarvarājabhir arcitaḥd tilaṃ gāvaḥ suvarṇaṃ cāpy annaṃ kanyā vasuṃdharād tārayantīha dattāni brāhmaṇebhyo mahābhujad brāhmaṇaṃ vṛttasaṃpannam āhitāgnim alolupamd tarpayed vidhivad rājan sa nidhiḥ pāralaukikaḥd āhitāgniṃ daridraṃ ca śrotriyaṃ ca jitendriyamd śūdrānnavarjitaṃ caiva dvijaṃ yatnena pūjayetd āhitāgniḥ sadā pātram agnihotraś ca vedavitd pātrāṇām api tat pātraṃ śūdrānnaṃ yasya nodared yac ca vedamayaṃ pātraṃ yac ca pātraṃ tapomayamd asaṃkīrṇaṃ ca yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyatid nityaṃ svādhyāyaniratās tv aprakīrṇendriyāś ca yed pañcayajñaratā nityaṃ pūjitās tārayanti ted ye kṣāntidāntāḥ śrutipūrṇakarṇād jitendriyā prāṇivadhe nivṛttāḥd pratigrahe saṃkucitā gṛhasthāsd te brāhmaṇās tārayituṃ samarthāḥd nityodakī nityayajñopavītīd nityasvādhyāyī vṛṣalānnavarjīd ṛtau gacchan vidhivac cāpi juhvand sa brāhmaṇas tārayituṃ samarthaḥd brāhmaṇo yas tu madbhakto madyājī matparāyaṇaḥd mayi saṃnyastakarmā ca sa vipras tārayed dhruvamd dvādaśākṣaratattvajñaś caturvyūhavibhāgavitd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad acchidrapañcakālajñaḥ sa vipras tārayiṣyatid vāsudevena dāneṣu kathiteṣu yathākramamd avitṛptas tu dharmeṣu keśavaṃ punar abravītd deva dharmāmṛtam idaṃ śṛṇvato pi paraṃtapad na vidyate suraśreṣṭha mama tṛptir hi mādhavad anaḍutsaṃpradānasya yat phalaṃ tu vidhīyated tat phalaṃ kathayasveha tava bhaktasya me cyutad yāni cānyāni dānāni tvayā noktāni kāni citd tāny ācakṣva suraśreṣṭha teṣāṃ cānukramāt phalamd bhagavān uvācad pavitratvāt supuṇyatvāt pāvanatvāt tathaiva cad śṛṇu dharmāmṛtaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dattasyānaḍuhaḥ phalamd daśadhenusamo naḍvān eko pi kurupuṃgavad medomāṃsavipuṣṭāṅgo nīrogaḥ kopavarjitaḥd yuvā bhadraḥ suśīlaś ca sarvadoṣavivarjitaḥd dhuraṃ dhārayate kṣipraṃ datto viprāya pāṇḍavad sa tena puṇyadānena varṣakoṭiṃ yudhiṣṭhirad yathākāmaṃ mahātejā gavāṃ loke mahīyated yaś ca dadyād anaḍuhau dvau yuktau ca dhuraṃdharaud suvṛttāya daridrāya śrotriyāya viśeṣataḥd tasya yat puṇyam ākhyātaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhirad sahasragopradānena yat proktaṃ phalam uttamamd tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yāti lokān sa māmakānd yāvanti caiva romāṇi tayor anaḍuhor nṛpad tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi mama loke mahīyated daridrāyaiva dātavyaṃ na samṛddhāya pāṇḍavad varṣāṇāṃ hi taṭākeṣu phalaṃ naiva payodhiṣud yas tu dadyād anaḍuhaṃ daridrāya dvijātayed sa tena puṇyadānena pūtātmā kurupuṃgavad vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍho divyarūpī yathāsukhamd mama lokeṣu ramate yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavamd gṛhaṃ dīpaprabhāyuktaṃ śayyāsanavibhūṣitamd bhājanopaskarair yuktaṃ dhānyapūrṇam alaṃkṛtamd dāsīgobhūmisaṃyuktaṃ saphalaṃ sarvasādhanaiḥd brāhmaṇāya daridrāya śrotriyāya yudhiṣṭhirad dadyāt sadakṣiṇaṃ yas tu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś caiva agnayo ṛṣayas tathād prayacchanti prahṛṣṭā vai yānam ādityasaṃnibhamd tena gacchec chriyā yukto brahmalokam anuttamamd strīsahasrāvṛte divye bhavane tatra kāñcaned modate brahmalokastho yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavamd śayyāṃ prastaraṇopetāṃ yaḥ prayacchati pāṇḍavad arcayitvā dvijaṃ bhaktyā vastramālyānulepanaiḥd bhojayitvā vicitrānnaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud dhenudānasya yat puṇyaṃ vidhidattasya pāṇḍavad tat puṇyaṃ tam anuprāpya pitṛloke mahīyated śilpam adhyayanaṃ vāpi vidyāmantrauṣadhāni cad yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud āhitāgnisahasrasya pūjitasyaiva yat phalamd tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yas tu vidyāṃ prayacchatid chandobhiḥ saṃprayuktena vimānena virājatād saptarṣilokān vrajati pūjyate brahmavādibhiḥd caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā tatra devavatd iha mānuṣyake loke vipro bhavati vedavitd viśrāmayati yo vipraṃ śrāntam adhvani karśitamd vinaśyati tadā pāpaṃ tasya varṣakṛtaṃ nṛpad atha prakṣālayet pādau tasya toyena bhaktimānd daśavarṣakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohati na saṃśayaḥd ghṛtena vātha tailena pādau tasya tu pūjayetd tad dvādaśasamārūḍhaṃ pāpam āśu vyapohatid dhenukāñcanadattasya yac ca puṇyam udāhṛtamd tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yas tv evaṃ vipram arcayetd svāgatena ca yo vipraṃ pūjayed āsanena cad pratyutthānena vā rājan sa devānāṃ priyo bhavetd svāgatenāgnayo rājann āsanena śatakratuḥd pratyutthānena pitaraḥ prītiṃ yānty atithipriyāḥd agniśakrapitṝṇāṃ ca teṣāṃ prītyā narādhipad saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya sadyo vinaśyatid yaḥ prayacchati viprāya āsanaṃ mālyabhūṣitamd sa yāti maṇicitreṇa rathenendraniketanamd puraṃdarapure tatra divyanārīvibhūṣitaḥd ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥd vāhanaṃ yaḥ prayaccheta brāhmaṇāya yudhiṣṭhirad sa yāti ratnacitreṇa vāhanena surālayamd sa tatra kāmaṃ krīḍitvā sevyamāno psarogaṇaiḥd iha rājā bhaved rājan nātra kāryā vicāraṇād pādapaṃ pallavākīrṇaṃ puṣpitaṃ phalitaṃ tathād gandhamālyair athābhyarcya vastrābharaṇabhūṣitamd yaḥ prayacchati viprāya śrotriyāya sadakṣiṇamd bhojayitvā yathākāmaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud jāmbūnadavicitreṇa vimānena virājatād puraṃdarapuraṃ yāti jayaśabdaravair yutaḥd tataḥ śakrapure ramye tasya kalpakapādapaḥd dadāti cepsitaṃ sarvaṃ manasā yad yad icchatid yāvanti tasya patrāṇi puṣpāṇi ca phalāni cad tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyated śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca mānuṣyaṃ lokam āgataḥd rathāśvagajasaṃpūrṇaṃ puraṃ rājyaṃ ca rakṣatid sthāpayitvā tu madbhaktyā yo matpratikṛtiṃ naraḥd ālayaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā pūjākarma ca kārayetd svayaṃ vā pūjayed bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud aśvamedhasahasrasya yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtamd tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti matsālokyaṃ prapadyated na jāne nirgamaṃ tasya mama lokād yudhiṣṭhirad devālaye vipragṛhe govāṭe catvare pi vād prajvālayati yo dīpaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud āruhya kāñcanaṃ yānaṃ dyotayan sarvatodiśamd gacched ādityalokaṃ sa sevyamānaḥ surottamaiḥd tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥd iha loke bhaved vipro vedavedāṅgapāragaḥd devālayeṣu vā rājan brāhmaṇāvasatheṣu vād catvare vā catuṣke vā rātrau vā yadi vā divād nānāgandharvavādyāni dharmaśrāvaṇikāni cad yas tu kārayate bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanād tasya devā naraśreṣṭha pitaraś cāpi harṣitāḥd suprītāḥ saṃprayacchanti vimānaṃ kāmagaṃ śubhamd sa ca tena vimānena yāti devapuraṃ naraḥd tatra divyāpsarobhis tu sevyamānaḥ pramodated devalokāvatīrṇas tu so smiṃl loke narādhipad vedavedāṅgatattvajño bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavetd catvare vā sabhāyāṃ vā vistīrṇe vā sabhāṅgaṇed kṛtvāgnikuṇḍaṃ vipulaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā yudhiṣṭhirad tatrāgniṃ caturo māsāñ jvalayed yas tu bhaktimānd samāpteṣu ca māseṣu pauṣyādiṣu tato dvijānd bhojayet pāyasaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ madgatenāntarātmanād dakṣiṇāṃ ca yathāśakti brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayetd evam agniṃ tu yaḥ kuryān nityam evārcayaṃs tu māmd tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan nibodha yudhiṣṭhirad tenāhaṃ śaṃkaraś caiva pitaro hy agnayas tathād yāsyāmaḥ paramāṃ prītiṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇād ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣaśatāni cad so smat prītikaraḥ śrīmān mama loke mahīyated mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so smiṃl loke mahāyaśāḥd vedavedāṅgavid vipro jāyate rājapūjitaḥd yaḥ karoti naraśreṣṭha bharaṇaṃ brāhmaṇasya tud śrotriyasyābhijātasya daridrasya viśeṣataḥd tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan nibodha yudhiṣṭhirad gavāṃ koṭipradānena yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtamd tatpuṇyaphalam āpnoti varṣeṇaikena pāṇḍavad kāñcanena vicitreṇa yānenāmbaraśobhinād sa yāti māmakaṃ lokaṃ divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥd gīyamāno varastrībhir varṣāṇāṃ koṭiviṃśatimd krīḍitvā māmake loke tatra devair abhiṣṭutaḥd mānuṣyam avatīrṇas tu vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavetd karakaṃ kuṇḍikāṃ vāpi mahad vā jalabhājanamd yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud brahmakūrcena yat pīte phalaṃ proktaṃ yathāvidhid tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti jalabhājanado naraḥd sutṛptaḥ suprabhaḥ saumyaḥ prahṛṣṭendriyamānasaḥd haṃsasārasayuktena vimānena virājatād sa yāti vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ divyagandharvasevitaḥd pānīyaṃ yaḥ prayacched vai jīvānāṃ jīvanaṃ paramd grīṣmakeṣu ca māseṣu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud kapilākoṭidānasya yat puṇyaṃ tu vidhīyated tatpuṇyaphalam āpnoti pānīyaṃ yaḥ prayacchatid pūrṇacandraprakāśena vimānena virājatād sa gacchec cendrasadanaṃ sevyamāno psarogaṇaiḥd triṃśatkoṭiyugaṃ tatra divyagandharvasevitaḥd krīḍitvā mānuṣe loke caturvedī dvijo bhavetd śiro bhyaṅgapradānena tejasvī priyadarśanaḥd subhago rūpavāñ śūraḥ paṇḍitaś ca bhaved dvijaḥd vastradāyī tu tejasvī sarvatra priyadarśanaḥd sukhabhogapatiḥ śrīmān strīṇāṃ nityaṃ manoramaḥd upānahau ca chattraṃ ca yo dadāti narottamaḥd sa yāti naramukhyena kāñcanena virājatād śakralokaṃ mahātejāḥ sevyamāno psarogaṇaiḥd kāṣṭhapādukado yāti vimānair vṛṣanirmitaiḥd dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ sevyamāno psarottamaiḥd dantakāṣṭhapradānena priyavākyo bhaven naraḥd sugandhavadanaḥ śrīmān medhāsaubhāgyasaṃyutaḥd kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ vāpi guḍaṃ madhurasaṃ tathād ye prayacchanti viprebhyaḥ parāṃ bhaktiṃ gatā narāḥd te vṛṣair aśvayānaiś ca śvetasragdāmabhūṣitāḥd upagīyamānā gandharvair yāntīśvarapuraṃ narāḥd tatra divyāpsarobhis tu sevyamānā yathāsukhamd ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi modante devasaṃnibhāḥd tataḥ kālāvatīrṇāś ca jāyante tv iha mānavāḥd prabhūtadhanadhānyāś ca bhogavanto narottamāḥd vaiśākhe māsi vaiśākhe divase pāṇḍunandanad vaivasvataṃ samuddiśya parāṃ bhaktim upāgatāḥd abhyarcya vidhivad viprāṃs tilān guḍasamāyutānd ye prayacchanti viprebhyas teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud gopradānena yat puṇyaṃ vidhivat pāṇḍunandanad tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpto yamaloke mahīyated tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha rājā bhaviṣyatid tasminn eva dine viprān bhojayitvā sadakṣiṇamd toyapūrṇāni divyāni bhājanāni diśanti yed te yānty ādityavarṇābhair vimānair varuṇālayamd tatra divyāṅganābhis tu ramante kāmakāminaḥd tato vatīrṇāḥ kālena te cāsmin mānuṣe punaḥd bhogavanto dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥd anantarāśī yaś cāpi vartate vratavat sadād satyavāk krodharahitaḥ śuciḥ snānarataḥ sadād sa vimānena divyena yāti śakrapuraṃ naraḥd tatra divyāpsarobhis tu varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥd krīḍitvā mānuṣe loke jāyate vedavid dvijaḥd ekabhuktena yaś cāpi varṣam ekaṃ tu vartated brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ satyaśaucasamanvitaḥd sa vimānena divyena yāti śakrapuraṃ naraḥd daśakoṭisahasrāṇi krīḍitvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥd iha mānuṣyake loke brāhmaṇo vedavid bhavetd caturthakālaṃ yo bhuṅkte brahmacārī jitendriyaḥd vartate caikavarṣaṃ tu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud citrabarhiṇayuktena vicitradhvajaśobhinād yāti yānena divyena sa mahendrapuraṃ naraḥd akṛśābhir varastrībhiḥ sevyamāno yathāsukhamd tato dvādaśakoṭiṃ sa samāḥ samyak pramodated śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca loke cāsmin narādhipad bhaved vai brāhmaṇo vidvān kṣamāvān vedapāragaḥd ṣaṣṭhakāle tu yo śnāti varṣam ekam akalmaṣaḥd brahmacaryavratair yuktaḥ śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥd tapoyuktasya tasyātha śṛṇuṣva phalam uttamamd atyādityaprakāśena vimānenārkasaṃnibhaḥd sa yāti mama lokān vai divyanārīniṣevitaḥd tatra sādhyair marudbhiś ca pūjyamāno yathāsukhamd paśyann eva sadā māṃ tu krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥd pakṣopavāsaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanād samāpte tu vrate tasmiṃs tarpayec chrotriyān dvijānd so pi gacchati divyena vimānena mahātapāḥd dyotayan prabhayā vyoma mama lokaṃ prapadyated sa tatra modate kāmaṃ kāmarūpī yathāsukhamd triṃśatkoṭisamā rājan krīḍitvā tatra devavatd iha mānuṣyake loke pūjanīyo dvijo bhavetd trayāṇām api vedānāṃ sāṅgānāṃ pārago bhavetd yaś ca māsopavāsaṃ vai kurute madgatātmanād jitendriyo jitakrodho jitadhīḥ snānatatparaḥd samāpte niyame tatra bhojayitvā dvijottamānd dakṣiṇāṃ ca tato dadyāt prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanād sa gacchati mahātejā brahmalokam anuttamamd siṃhayuktena yānena divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥd sa tatra brahmaṇo loke divyarṣigaṇasevitaḥd śatakoṭisamā rājan yathākāmaṃ pramodated tataḥ kālāvatīrṇaś ca so smiṃl loke dvijo bhavetd ṣaḍaṅgavic caturvedī triṃśaj janmāny arogavānd yas tyaktvā sarvakarmāṇi śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥd mahāprasthānam ekāgro yāti madgatamānasaḥd sa gacched indrasadanaṃ vimānena mahātapāḥd mahāmaṇivicitreṇa sauvarṇena virājatād śatakoṭisamās tatra surādhipatipūjitaḥd nākapṛṣṭhe nivasati divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥd śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca mānuṣeṣūpajāyated rājñāṃ rājā mahātejāḥ sarvalokārcitaḥ prabhuḥd prāyopaveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanād namo brahmaṇyadevāyety uktvā mantraṃ samāhitaḥd antaḥsvastho jitakrodhas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud kāmagaḥ kāmarūpī ca bālasūryasamaprabhaḥd sa vimānena divyena yāti lokān anāmayānd svargāt svargaṃ mahātejā gatvā caiva yathāsukhamd mama lokeṣu ramate yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavamd agnipraveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanād so pi yānena divyena mama lokaṃ prapadyated tataḥ sarvaguṇopetaḥ paśyann api sa māṃ sadād triṃśatkoṭisamā rājan modate mama saṃnidhaud tato vatīrṇaḥ kālena vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavetd karṣaṇaṃ sādhayan yas tu māṃ prasannaḥ śucivrataḥd namo brahmaṇyadevāyety etaṃ mantram udāharand bālasūryaprakāśena vimānena virājatād mama lokaṃ samāsādya ṣaṭkoṭiṃ tu pramodated mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so smiṃl loke nṛpo bhavetd niveśayati manmūrtyā ātmānaṃ madgataḥ śuciḥd rudradakṣiṇamūrtyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥd siddhair brahmarṣibhiś caiva devalokaiś ca pūjitaḥd gandharvair bhūtasaṃghaiś ca gīyamāno mahātapāḥd praviśet sa mahātejā māṃ vā śaṃkaram eva vād tasyāpunarbhavaṃ sicrājan nātra kāryā vicāraṇād gokṛte strīkṛte caiva guruviprakṛte pi vād hanyante ye tu rājendra śakralokaṃ vrajanti ted tatra jāmbūnadamaye vimāne kāmagāminid manvantaraṃ pramodante divyanārīniṣevitāḥd āśrutasyāpradānena dattasya haraṇena cad janmaprabhṛti yad dattaṃ sarvaṃ naśyati bhāratad nāgopradās tatra payaḥ pibantid nābhūmidā bhūmim athāśnuvantid yān yān kāmān brāhmaṇebhyo dadātid tāṃs tān kāmān svargaloke ca bhuṅkted yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenopārjitaṃ ca yatd tat tad guṇavate deyaṃ tad evākṣayam icchatād anupoṣya trirātrāṇi tīrthāny anabhigamya cad adattvā kāñcanaṃ gāṃ ca daridro nāma jāyated dānaṃ yat tat phalaṃ naiti śrotriyāya na dīyated śrotriyā yatra nāśnanti na devās tatra bhuñjated śrotriyebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti paramaṃ daivataṃ mahatd nidhānaṃ cāpi rājendra tasmāc chrotriyabhojanātd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad viprayoge śarīrasya sendriyasya viśeṣataḥd bhagavān uvācad antarā vartamānasya gatiḥ prāṇasya kīdṛśīd śubhāśubhakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ prāpnotīha phalaṃ naraḥd na tu sarvasya bhūtasya pañcatvaṃ vāpi vidyated pañcatvaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha bhūribhūtikaraṃ nṛṇāmd teṣāṃ pañca mahāyajñān ye kurvanti dvijottamāḥd pañcatvaṃ pañcabhir bhūtair viyogaṃ saṃpracakṣated na jāyate na mriyate puruṣaḥ śāśvataḥ sadād prāyeṇa maraṇaṃ nāma pāpinām eva pāṇḍavad yeṣāṃ tu na gatiḥ puṇyā teṣāṃ maraṇam ucyated prāyeṇākṛtakṛtyās tu mṛtyor udvijate janaḥd kṛtakṛtyāḥ pratīkṣante mṛtyuṃ priyam ivātithimd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad pañca yajñāḥ kathaṃ deva kriyante tra dvijātibhiḥd bhagavān uvācad teṣāṃ nāma ca deveśa vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥd śṛṇu pañca mahāyajñān kīrtyamānān yudhiṣṭhirad yair eva brahmasālokyaṃ labhyate gṛhamedhinād ṛṣiyajñaṃ brahmayajñaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ ca pārthivad nṛyajñaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ ca pañca yajñān pracakṣated tarpaṇaṃ ṛṣiyajñaṃ syāt svādhyāyo brahmayajñakaḥd bhūtayajño balir yajño nṛyajño tithipūjanamd pitṝn uddiśya yat karma pitṛyajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥd hutaṃ cāpy ahutaṃ caiva tathā prahutam eva cad prāśitaṃ balidānaṃ ca pākayajñān pracakṣated vaiśvadevādayo homā hutam ity ucyate budhaiḥd ahutaṃ ca bhaved dattaṃ prahutaṃ brāhmaṇāśitamd prāṇāgnihotrahomaṃ ca prāśitaṃ vidhivad viduḥd balikarma ca rājendra pākayajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥd ke cit pañca mahāyajñān pākayajñān pracakṣated apare brahmayajñādīn mahāyajñavido viduḥd sarva ete mahāyajñāḥ sarvathā parikīrtitāḥd bubhukṣitān brāhmaṇāṃs tu yathāśakti na hāpayetd ahany ahani ye tv etān akṛtvā bhuñjate svayamd kevalaṃ malam aśnanti te narā na ca saṃśayaḥd tasmāt snātvā dvijo vidvān kuryād etān dine dined yudhiṣṭhira uvācad ato nyathā tu bhuñjan vai prāyaścittīyate dvijaḥd devadeva namas te stu tvadbhaktasya janārdanad bhagavān uvācad vaktum arhasi deveśa snānasya ca vidhiṃ mamad śṛṇu pāṇḍava tat sarvaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanamd snātvā yena vidhānena mucyante kilbiṣād dvijāḥd mṛdaṃ ca gomayaṃ caiva tilān darbhāṃs tathaiva cad puṣpāṇy api yathānyāyam ādāya tu jalaṃ vrajetd nadyāṃ satyāṃ na ca snāyād anyatra dvijasattamad sati prabhūte payasi nālpe snāyāt kadā canad gatvodakasamīpaṃ tu śucau deśe manohared tato mṛdgomayādīni tatra prokṣya vinikṣipetd bahiḥ prakṣālya pādau ca dvir ācamya prayatnataḥd pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskuryāt tu taj jalamd na ca prakṣālayet tīrtham adbhir vidvān kadā canad na ca pādena vā hanyād dhastenānyena taj jalamd sarvadevamayā hy āpo manmayāḥ pāṇḍunandanad tasmāt tās tu na hantavyās tv adbhiḥ prakṣālayet sthalamd kevalaṃ prathamaṃ majjen nāṅgāni vimṛjed budhaḥd tat tu tīrthaṃ samāsādya kuryād ācamanaṃ punaḥd gokarṇākṛtivat kṛtvā karaṃ triḥ prapibej jalamd dvis tat parimṛjed vaktraṃ pādāv abhyukṣya cātmanaḥd śīrṣaṇyāṃs tu tataḥ prāṇān sakṛd eva tu saṃspṛśetd bāhū dvau ca tataḥ spṛṣṭvā hṛdayaṃ nābhim eva cad pratyaṅgam udakaṃ spṛṣṭvā mūrdhānaṃ tu punaḥ spṛśetd āpaḥ punāntv ity uktvā ca punar ācamanaṃ caretd soṃkārā vyāhṛtīr vāpi sadasaspatim ity ṛcamd ācamya mṛttikāḥ paścāt tridhā kṛtvā samālabhetd ṛcedaṃ viṣṇur ity aṅgam uttamādhamamadhyamamd ālabhya vāruṇaiḥ sūktair namaskṛtya jalaṃ tataḥd sravantī cet pratisrotaḥ pratyarkaṃ cānyavāriṣud majjed om ity udāhṛtya na ca prakṣobhayej jalamd gomayaṃ ca tridhā kṛtvā jale pūrvaṃ samālabhetd savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ ca japet punaḥd punar ācamanaṃ kṛtvā madgatenāntarātmanād āpo hi ṣṭheti tisṛbhir darbhapūtena vāriṇād tathā tarat samandībhiḥ siñcec catasṛbhiḥ kramātd gosūktenāśvasūktena śuddhavargeṇa cāpy athad vaiṣṇavair vāruṇaiḥ sūktaiḥ sāvitrair indradevataiḥd vāmadevena cātmānam anyair manmayasāmabhiḥd sthitvāntaḥsalile sūktaṃ japed vācāghamarṣaṇamd savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ vā tato japetd ā śvāsamokṣāt praṇavaṃ japed vā mām anusmarand utplutya tīrtham āsādya dhaute śukle ca vāsasīd śuddhe cācchādayet kakṣe na kuryāt paripāśaked pāśe nibaddhakakṣyo yat kurute karma vaidikamd rākṣasā dānavā daityās tad vilumpanti harṣitāḥd tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kakṣyāṃ pāśe na dhārayetd tataḥ prakṣālya pādau ca hastau caiva mṛdā śanaiḥd ācamya punar ācāmet tataḥ sāvitriyā dvijaḥd jale jalagataḥ śuddhaḥ sthala eva sthale sthitaḥd ubhayatra sthitas tasmād ācāmed ātmaśuddhayed darbheṣu darbhapāṇiḥ san prāṅmukhaḥ susamāhitaḥd prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān madgatenāntarātmanād sahasrakṛtvaḥ sāvitrīṃ śatakṛtvas tu vā japetd samāpte tu jape tasmin sāvitryā cābhimantrya cad mandehānāṃ vināśāya rakṣasāṃ vikṣipej jalamd udvargo sīty athācāntaḥ prāyaścittajalaṃ kṣipetd athādāya sapuṣpāṇi toyāny añjalinā dvijaḥd prakṣipya pratisūryaṃ ca vyomamudrāṃ prakalpayetd tato dvādaśakṛtvas tu sūryasyaikākṣaraṃ japetd tataḥ ṣaḍakṣarādīni ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ parivartayetd pradakṣiṇaṃ parāmṛśya mudrayā svamukhaṃ tayād ūrdhvabāhus tato bhūtvā sūryam īkṣet samāhitaḥd tanmaṇḍalasthaṃ māṃ dhyāyet tejomūrtiṃ caturbhujamd ud u tyaṃ ca japen mantraṃ citraṃ taccakṣur ity apid sāvitrīṃ ca yathāśakti japtvā sūktaṃ ca māmakamd manmayāni ca sāmāni puruṣavratam eva cad tataś cālokayed arkaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity ṛcād pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskṛtya divākaramd tatas tu tarpayed adbhiḥ brahmāṇaṃ māṃ ca śaṃkaramd prajāpatiṃ ca devāṃś ca tathā devamunīn apid sāṅgān api tathā vedān itihāsān kratūṃs tathād purāṇāni ca divyāni kulāny apsarasāṃ tathād ṛtūn saṃvatsarāṃś caiva kalākāṣṭhāntakaṃ tathād bhūtagrāmāṃś ca bhūtāni saritaḥ sāgarāṃs tathād śailāñ śailasthitān devān oṣadhīḥ savanaspatīḥd tarpayed upavītī tu pratyekaṃ tṛpyatām itid anvārabhya ca savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tud nivītī tarpayet paścād ṛṣīn mantrakṛtas tathād marīcyādīn ṛṣīṃś caiva nāradāntān samāhitaḥd prācīnāvīty athaitāṃs tu tarpayed devatāḥ pitṝnd tatas tu kavyavāḍ agniṃ somaṃ vaivasvataṃ tathād tataś cāryamaṇaṃ cāpi agniṣv āttāṃs tathaiva cad somapāṃś caiva darbhais tu satilair eva vāribhiḥd tṛpyadhvam iti paścāt tu svapitṝṃs tarpayet tataḥd pitṝn pitāmahāṃś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahānd pitāmahīṃ tathā cāpi tathaiva prapitāmahīmd tathā pitṛṣvasṝś caiva mātṛṣvasṝs tathaiva cad mātaraṃ cātmanaś caiva tathā mātāmahīm apid mātur mātāmahīṃ caiva gurum ācāryam eva cad upādhyāyān sakhīn bandhūñ śiṣyartvigjñātiputrakānd pramītān ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ tarpayet tān amatsaraḥd tarpayitvā tathācamya snānavastraṃ prapīḍayetd vṛddhiṃ bhṛtyajanasyāhuḥ snātakānāṃ ca tadvidaḥd atarpayitvā tān pūrvaṃ snānavastraṃ na pīḍayetd pīḍayec cet purā mohād devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tathād pitaras tu nirāśāś ca śaptvā yānti yathāgatamd prakṣālya tu mṛdā pādāv ācamya prayataḥ punaḥd darbheṣu darbhapāṇiḥ san svādhyāyaṃ tu samārabhetd vedam ādau samārabhya tatopari padakramānd yad adhīte svayaṃ śaktyā tat svādhyāyaṃ pracakṣated ṛcaṃ vātha yajur vāpi sāmagāthām athāpi vād itihāsapurāṇāni yathāśakti na hāpayetd utthāya ca namaskṛtvā diśo digdevatā apid brahmāṇaṃ ca tataś cāgniṃ pṛthivīm oṣadhīs tathād vācaṃ vācaspatiṃ caiva māṃ caiva saritas tathād namaskṛtvā tathādbhis tu praṇavādi ca pūjayetd tato namo dbhya ity uktvā namaskuryāt tu taj jalamd ghṛṇiḥ sūryas tathādityas tān praṇamya svamūrdhanid tatas tv ālokayann arkaṃ praṇavena samāhitaḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad tato mām arcayet puṣpair matpriyair eva nityaśaḥd tvatpriyāṇi prasūnāni tvadadhiṣṭhāni mādhavad bhagavān uvācad sarvāṇy ācakṣva deveśa tvadbhaktasya mamācyutad śṛṇuṣvāvahito rājan puṣpāṇi prītikṛnti med kumudaṃ karavīraṃ ca caṇakaṃ campakaṃ tathād mallikājātipuṣpaṃ ca nandyāvartaṃ ca nandikamd palāśapuṣpapatrāṇi dūrvā bhṛṅgakam eva cad vanamālā ca rājendra matpriyāṇi viśeṣataḥd sarveṣām api puṣpāṇāṃ sahasraguṇam utpalamd tasmāt padmaṃ tathā rājan padmāt tu śatapatrakamd tasmāt sahasrapatraṃ tu puṇḍarīkaṃ tataḥ paramd puṇḍarīkasahasrāt tu tulasī guṇato dhikād bakapuṣpaṃ tatas tasmāt sauvarṇaṃ tu tato dhikamd sauvarṇāt tu prasūnāc ca matpriyaṃ nāsti pāṇḍavad puṣpālābhe tulasyāstu patrair mām arcayed budhaḥd patrālābhe tu śākhābhiḥ śākhālābhe śiphāphalaiḥd śiphālābhe mṛdā tatra bhaktimān arcayed budhaḥd varjanīyāni puṣpāṇi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥd kiṅkiṇī munipuṣpaṃ ca duttūraṃ pāṭalaṃ tathād tathātimuktakaṃ caiva puṃnāgaṃ naktamālikād yaudhikaṃ kṣīrikāpuṣpaṃ nirguṇḍī lāṅgalī japād karṇikāraṃ tathāśokaṃ śalmalīpuṣpam eva cad kakubhāḥ kovidārāś ca vaibhītakam athāpi vād kuraṇṭakaprasūnāṃ ca tilvakaṃ lāṅgalī tathād aṅkolaṃ girikarṇī ca nīlāny eva ca sarvaśaḥd ekavarṇāni cānyāni sarvāṇy eva vivarjayetd arkapuṣpāṇi varjyāni cārkapatrasthitāni cad vyāghātapicumandāni sarvāṇy eva vivarjayetd anyais tu śuklapatrais tu gandhavadbhir narādhipad yudhiṣṭhira uvācad avarjyais tair yathālābhaṃ madbhakto māṃ samarcayetd kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo si mūrtayaḥ kīdṛśās tu ted vaikhānasāḥ kathaṃ brūyuḥ kathaṃ vā pāñcarātrikāḥd bhagavān uvācad śṛṇu pāṇḍava tat sarvam arcanākramam ātmanaḥd sthaṇḍile padmakaṃ kṛtvā cāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikamd aṣṭākṣaravidhānena hy atha vā dvādaśākṣaraiḥd vaidikair atha vā mantrair mama sūktena vā punaḥd sthāpitaṃ māṃ tatas tasminn arcayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥd puruṣaṃ ca tataḥ satyam acyutaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhirad aniruddhaṃ ca māṃ prāhur vaikhānasavido janāḥd anye tv evaṃ vijānanti māṃ rājan pāñcarātrikāḥd vāsudevaṃ ca rājendra saṃkarṣaṇam athāpi vād pradyumnaṃ cāniruddhaṃ ca caturmūrtiṃ pracakṣated etāś cānyāś ca rājendra saṃjñābhedena mūrtayaḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad viddhy anarthāntarā eva mām evaṃ cārcayed budhaḥd tvadbhaktāḥ kīdṛśā deva kāni teṣāṃ vratāni cad bhagavān uvācad etat kathaya deveśa tvadbhaktasya mamācyutad ananyadevatābhaktā ye madbhaktajanapriyāḥd mām eva śaraṇaṃ prāptās te madbhaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥd svargāṇy api yaśasyāni matpriyāṇi viśeṣataḥd madbhaktaḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha vratānīmāni dhārayetd nānyad ācchādayed vastraṃ madbhakto jalatāraṇed svasthas tu na divā svapyān madhumāṃsāni varjayetd pradakṣiṇaṃ vrajed viprān gām aśvatthaṃ hutāśanamd na dhāvet patite varṣe nāgrabhikṣāṃ ca lopayetd pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ nādyāt saubhañjanakagṛñjanaud grāsamuṣṭiṃ gave dadyād dhānyāmlaṃ caiva varjayetd tathā paryuṣitaṃ cāpi pakvaṃ parigṛhāgatamd aniveditaṃ ca yad dravyaṃ tat prayatnena varjayetd vibhītakakarañjānāṃ chāyāṃ dūraṃ vivarjayetd vipradevaparīvādaṃ na vadet pīḍito pi sand sāttvikā rājasāś cāpi tāmasāś cāpi pāṇḍavad mām arcayanti madbhaktās teṣām īdṛgvidhā gatiḥd tāmasās timiraṃ yānti rājasā raja eva tatd sāttvikāḥ sattvasaṃpannāḥ sattvam eva prayānti ted ye siddhāḥ santi sāṃkhyena yogasattvabalena cad nabhasādityacandrābhyāṃ paśyanti padavistaramd ekastambhe navadvāre tristhūṇe pañcadhātuked etasmin dehanagare rājasas tu sadā bhavetd udite savitary asya kriyāyuktasya dhīmataḥd caturvedavidaś cāpi dehe ṣaḍ vṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥd kṣatriyāḥ sapta vijñeyā vaiśyās tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥd niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdrāṇām ekaviṃśatiḥd kāmaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca mohaś ca mada eva cad mahāmohaś ca ity ete dehe ṣaḍ vṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥd garvaḥ stambho hy ahaṃkāra īrṣyā ca droha eva cad pāruṣyaṃ krūratā ceti saptaite kṣatriyāḥ smṛtāḥd tīkṣṇatā nikṛtir māyā śāṭhyaṃ ḍambho hy anārjavamd paiśunyam anṛtaṃ caiva vaiśyās tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥd tṛṣṇā bubhukṣā nidrā ca ālasyaṃ cāghṛṇādayād ādhiś cāpi vivādaś ca pramādo hīnasattvatād bhayaṃ viklabatā jāḍyaṃ pāpakaṃ manyur eva cad āśā cāśraddadhānatvam anavasthāpy ayantraṇamd āśaucaṃ malinatvaṃ ca śūdrā hy ete prakīrtitāḥd yasminn ete na dṛśyante sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyated yeṣu yeṣu hi bhāveṣu yatkālaṃ vartate dvijaḥd tattatkālaṃ sa vijñeyaḥ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥd prāṇān āyamya yatkālaṃ yena māṃ cāpi cintayetd tatkāle vai dvijo jñeyaḥ śeṣakālo hy athetaraḥd tasmāt tu sāttviko bhūtvā śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥd mām arcayet tu satataṃ matpriyatvaṃ yad icchatid alolajihvaḥ samupasthito dhṛtird nidhāya cakṣur yugamātram eva cad manaś ca vācaṃ ca nigṛhya cañcalaṃd bhayān nivṛtto mama bhakta ucyated īdṛśādhyātmino ye tu brāhmaṇā niyatendriyāḥd teṣāṃ śrāddheṣu tṛpyanti tena tṛptāḥ pitāmahāḥd dharmo jayati nādharmaḥ satyaṃ jayati nānṛtamd kṣamā jayati na krodhaḥ kṣamāvān brāhmaṇo bhavetd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad dānapuṇyaphalaṃ śrutvā tapaḥ puṇyaphalāni cad dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravītd yā caiṣā kapilā deva pūrvam utpāditā vibhod homadhenuḥ sadā puṇyā caturvaktreṇa mādhavad sā kathaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo hi deyā kasmin dine pi vād kīdṛśāya ca viprāya dātavyā puṇyalakṣaṇād kati vā kapilāḥ proktāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvād kair vā deyāś ca tā deva śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥd evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo dharmaputreṇa saṃsadid abravīt kapilāsaṃkhyāṃ tāsāṃ māhātmyam eva cad śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ paramd yac chrutvā pāpakarmāpi naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyated agnimadhyodbhavāṃ divyām agnijvālāsamaprabhāmd agnijvālojjvalacchṛṅgīṃ pradīptāṅgāralocanāmd agnipucchām agnikhurām agniromaprabhānvitāmd tām āgneyīm agnijihvām agnigrīvāṃ jvalatprabhāmd bhuñjate kapilāṃ ye tu śūdrā lobhena mohitāḥd patitāṃs tān vijānīyāc caṇḍālasadṛśā hi ted na teṣāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ kaś cid gṛhe kuryāt pratigrahamd dūrāc ca parihartavyā mahāpātakino pi ted sarvakālaṃ hi te sarvair varjitāḥ pitṛdaivataiḥd te sadā hy apratigrāhyā hy asaṃbhāṣyāś ca pāpinaḥd pibanti kapilāṃ yāvat tāvat teṣāṃ pitāmahāḥd amedhyam upabhuñjanti bhūmyāṃ vai śvasṛgālavatd kapilāyā ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi takram athāpi vād ye śūdrā upabhuñjanti teṣāṃ gatim imāṃ śṛṇud kapilopajīvī śūdras tu mṛto gacchati rauravamd kliśyate raurave ghore varṣakoṭiśataṃ vasand rauravāc ca paribhraṣṭo viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate krimiḥd viṣṭhāgarteṣu saṃviṣṭo durgandheṣu sahasraśaḥd tatraiva jāyamāno sau nottāraṃ tatra vindatid brāhmaṇaś caiva yas teṣāṃ gṛhe kuryāt pratigrahamd tataḥ prabhṛti tasyāpi pitaraḥ syur amedhyapāḥd na tena sārdhaṃ saṃbhāṣen na cāpy ekāsanaṃ vrajetd sa nityaṃ varjanīyo hi dūrāt tu brāhmaṇādhamaḥd yas tena saha saṃbhāṣed ekaśayyāṃ vrajeta vād prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ sa ca tenaiva śudhyatid kapilopajīvinaḥ śūdrād yaḥ karoti pratigrahamd prāyaścittaṃ bhavet tasya viprasyaitan na saṃśayaḥd brahmakūrcaṃ tu kurvīta cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vād mucyate kilbiṣāt tasmād etena brāhmaṇo hi saḥd kapilā hy agnihotrārthe yajñārthe ca svayaṃbhuvād sarvatas teja uddhṛtya brahmaṇā nirmitā purād pavitraṃ ca pavitrāṇāṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalamd puṇyānāṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ kapilā pāṇḍunandanad tapasāṃ tapa evāgryaṃ vratānāṃ vratam uttamamd dānānāṃ paramaṃ dānaṃ nidānaṃ hy etad akṣayamd pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni puṇyāny āyatanāni cad pavitrāṇi ca ramyāṇi sarvalokeṣu pāṇḍavad tebhyas tejaḥ samuddhṛtya brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇād lokanistāraṇāyaiva nirmitāḥ kapilāḥ svayamd sarvatejomayī hy eṣā kapilā pāṇḍunandanad sadāmṛtamayī medhyā śuciḥ pāvanam uttamamd kṣīreṇa kapilāyās tu dadhnā vai saghṛtena vād hotavyāny agnihotrāṇi sāyaṃ prātar dvijātibhiḥd kapilāyā ghṛtenāpi dadhnā kṣīreṇa vā punaḥd juhvate ye gnihotrāṇi brāhmaṇā vidhivat prabhod pūjayanty atithīṃś caiva parāṃ bhaktim upāgatāḥd śūdrānnād viratā nityaṃ ḍambhānṛtavivarjitāḥd te yānty ādityasaṃkāśair vimānair dvijasattamāḥd sūryamaṇḍalamadhyena brahmalokam anuttamamd brahmaṇo bhavane divye kāmagāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥd brahmaṇā pūjyamānās tu modante kalpam akṣayamd evaṃ hi kapilā rājan puṇyā mantrāmṛtāraṇiḥd ādāv evāgnimadhyāt tu maitreyī brahmanirmitād śṛṅgāgre kapilāyās tu sarvatīrthāni pāṇḍavad brahmaṇo hi niyogena nivasanti dine dined prātar utthāya yo martyaḥ kapilāśṛṅgamastakātd cyutā āpas tu śīrṣeṇa prayato dhārayec chuciḥd sa tena puṇyatīrthena sahasā dagdhakilbiṣaḥd varṣatrayakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ pradahaty agnivat tṛṇamd mūtreṇa kapilāyās tu yas tu prātar upaspṛśetd snānena tena puṇyena naṣṭapāpaḥ sa mānavaḥd triṃśadvarṣakṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥd prātar utthāya yo bhaktyā prayacchet tṛṇamuṣṭikamd tasya naśyati tat pāpaṃ triṃśadrātrikṛtaṃ nṛpad prātar utthāya madbhaktyā kuryād yas tāṃ pradakṣiṇamd pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tena pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥd pradakṣiṇena caikena śraddhāyuktasya pāṇḍavad daśarātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya tan naśyati dhruvamd kapilāpañcagavyena yaḥ snāyāt tu śucir naraḥd sa gaṅgādyeṣu tīrtheṣu snāto bhavati pāṇḍavad tena snānena tasyāpi śraddhāyuktasya pāṇḍavad daśarātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyatid dṛṣṭvā tu kapilāṃ bhaktyā śrutvā humbhāravaṃ tathād vyapohati naraḥ pāpam ahorātrakṛtaṃ nṛpad yatra vā tatra vā cāṅge kapilāṃ yaḥ spṛśec chuciḥd saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vināśayati pāṇḍavad gosahasraṃ ca yo dadyād ekāṃ ca kapilāṃ naraḥd samaṃ tasya phalaṃ prāha brahmaloke pitāmahaḥd yas tv ekāṃ kapilāṃ hanyān naraḥ kiṃ cit pramādataḥd gosahasraṃ hataṃ tena bhaven nātra vicāraṇād yaś caikāṃ kapilāṃ dadyāc chrotriyāyāhitāgnayed gavāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu dattaṃ bhavati pāṇḍavad daśaiva kapilāḥ proktāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvād yo dadyāc chrotriyebhyo vai svargaṃ gacchati tac chṛṇud prathamā svarṇakapilā dvitīyā gaurapiṅgalād tṛtīyā raktapiṅgākṣī caturthī galapiṅgalād pañcamī babhruvarṇābhā ṣaṣṭhī ca śvetapiṅgalād saptamī raktapiṅgākṣī aṣṭamī khurapiṅgalād navamī pāṭalā jñeyā daśamī pucchapiṅgalād daśaitāḥ kapilāḥ proktās tārayanti narān sadād maṅgalyāś ca pavitrāś ca sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥd evam eva hy anaḍvāho daśa proktā nareśvarad brāhmaṇo vāhayet tāṃs tu nānyo varṇaḥ kathaṃ canad na ghātayet tu daṇḍena kṣetre vādhvani vā dvijaḥd vāhayed dhuṃkṛtenaiva śākhayā vā sapatrayād na daṇḍena na yaṣṭyā vā na pāśena ca vā punaḥd na kṣuttṛṣṇāśramaśrāntān vāhayed vikalendriyānd atṛpteṣu na bhuñjīyāt pibet pīteṣu codakamd śuśrūṣor mātaraś caitāḥ pitaras te prakīrtitāḥd ahnāṃ pūrve tribhāge tu dhuryāṇāṃ vāhanaṃ smṛtamd viśrāmen madhyame bhāge bhāge cānte yathāsukhamd yatra vā tvarayā kṛtyaṃ saṃśayo yatra vādhvanid vāhayet tatra dhuryāṃs tu na sa pāpena lipyated anyathā vāhayan rājan nirayaṃ yāti rauravamd rudhiraṃ pātayet teṣāṃ yas tu mohān narādhipad brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpaṃ tasya syāt pāṇḍunandanad tena pāpena pāpātmā nirayaṃ yāty asaṃśayamd narakeṣu ca sarveṣu samāsthitvā śataṃ śatamd iha mānuṣyake loke balīvardo bhaviṣyatid tasmāt tu muktim anvicchan dadyāt tu kapilāṃ naraḥd kapilāṃ vāhayed yas tu vṛṣalo lobhamohitaḥd tena devās trayastriṃśat pitaraś cāpi vāhitāḥd sa devaiḥ pitṛbhir nityaṃ vadhyamānaḥ sudurmatiḥd narakān narakaṃ ghoraṃ gacched āpralayaṃ nṛpad brahmā rudras tathāgniś ca kapilānāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥd tasmāt te tu na hantavyāḥ pūjyās te tu viśeṣataḥd niḥśvasanti yadā śrāntās tadā hanyuś ca tat kulamd yāvanti teṣāṃ romāṇi tāvad varṣaśataṃ nṛpad narake paripacyante tatra tadvāhakā narāḥd kapilā sarvayajñeṣu dakṣiṇārthaṃ vidhīyated tasmāt tā dakṣiṇā deyā yajñeṣv eva dvijātibhiḥd homārthaṃ cāgnihotrasya yāṃ prayacchet prayatnataḥd śrotriyāya daridrāya śrāntāyāmitatejased tena dānena pūtātmā so gniloke mahīyated yāvanti caiva romāṇi kapilāṅge yudhiṣṭhirad tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi naraḥ svarge ca vartated suvarṇakhuraśṛṅgīṃ ca kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchatid viṣuve cāyane vāpi so śvamedhaphalaṃ labhetd tenāśvamedhatulyena mama lokaṃ sa gacchatid svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ rūpyakhurāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīmd vastrair alaṃkṛtāṃ puṣṭāṃ gandhair mālyaiś ca śobhitāmd pavitraṃ hi pavitrāṇāṃ suvarṇam iti me matiḥd tasmāt suvarṇābharaṇā dātavyā cāgnihotriṇed evaṃ dattvā tu rājendra saptapūrvān parān apid tārayiṣyati rājendra nātra kāryā vicāraṇād agniṣṭomasahasrasya vājapeyasamaṃ bhavetd vājapeyasahasrasya aśvamedhaṃ ca tatsamamd aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca rājasūyaṃ ca tatsamamd kapilānāṃ sahasreṇa vidhidattena pāṇḍavad rājasūyaphalaṃ prāpya mama loke mahīyated na tasya punarāvṛttir vidyate kurupuṃgavad prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīmd tais tair guṇaiḥ kāmadughā ca bhūtvād naraṃ pradātāram upaiti sā gauḥd svakarmabhiś cāpy anubadhyamānaṃd tīvrāndhakāre narake patantamd mahārṇave naur iva vāyunītād dattā hi gaus tārayate manuṣyamd putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś ca kulaṃ ca sarvamd āsaptamaṃ tārayate paratrad yāvan manuṣyān pṛthivīṃ bibhartid tāvat pradātāram ito paratrad yathauṣadhaṃ mantrakṛtaṃ narasyad prayuktamātraṃ vinihanti rogānd tathaiva dattā kapilā supātred pāpaṃ narasyāśu nihanti sarvamd yathaiva dṛṣṭvā bhujagāḥ suparṇaṃd naśyanti dūrād vivaśā bhayārtāḥd tathaiva dṛṣṭvā kapilāpradānaṃd naśyanti pāpāni narasya śīghramd yathā tvacaṃ svāṃ bhujago vihāyad punar navaṃ rūpam upaiti puṇyamd tathaiva muktaḥ puruṣaḥ svapāpaird virājate vai kapilāpradānātd yathāndhakāraṃ bhavane vilagnaṃd dīpto hi niryātayati pradīpaḥd tathā naraḥ pāpam api pralīnaṃd niṣkrāmayed vai kapilāpradānamd yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti tasyād vatsānvitāyāś ca śarīrajānid tāvat pradātā yugavarṣakoṭiṃd sa brahmaloke uttamamd dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravītd devadeveśa kapilā yadā viprāya dīyated kathaṃ sarveṣu cāṅgeṣu tasyās tiṣṭhanti devatāḥd yāś caitāḥ kapilāḥ proktā daśa caiva tvayā mamad tāsāṃ kati suraśreṣṭha kapilāḥ puṇyalakṣaṇāḥd kathaṃ vānugṛhītās tāḥ suraiḥ pitṛgaṇair apid kena yuktāś ca varṇena śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi med yudhiṣṭhireṇaivam uktaḥ keśavaḥ satyavāk tadād guhyānāṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ vaktum evopacakramed śṛṇu rājan pavitraṃ vai rahasyaṃ dharmam uttamamd grahaṇīyaṃ satyam idaṃ na śrāvyaṃ hetuvādināmd yadā vatsasya pādau dvau prasave śirasā sahad dṛśyete dānakālaṃ tam āhuḥ kālavido janāḥd antarikṣagato vatso yāvad bhūmiṃ na yāsyatid gaus tāvat pṛthivī jñeyā tasmād deyā tu tādṛśīd yāvanti dhenvā romāṇi savatsāyā yudhiṣṭhirad yāvantyaḥ sikatāś cāpi garbhodakapariplutāḥd tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi dātā svarge mahīyated suvarṇābharaṇāṃ kṛtvā savatsāṃ kapilāṃ tilaiḥd pracchādya tāṃ tu dadyād vai sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtāmd sasamudrā mahī tena saśailavanakānanād caturantā bhaved dattā nātra kāryā vicāraṇād pṛthivīdānatulyena tena dānena mānavaḥd saṃsārasāgarāt tīrṇo yāti lokaṃ prajāpateḥd brahmahā yadi vā goghno bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥd mahāpātakayukto pi dānenānena śudhyatid idaṃ paṭhati yaḥ puṇyaṃ kapilādānam uttamamd prātar utthāya madbhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud manasā karmaṇā vācā matipūrvaṃ yudhiṣṭhirad pāpaṃ rātrikṛtaṃ hanyād asyādhyāyasya pāṭhakaḥd idam āvartamānas tu śrāddhe yas tarpayed dvijānd tasyāpy amṛtam aśnanti pitaro tyantaharṣitāḥd yaś cedaṃ śṛṇuyād bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanād tasya rātrikṛtaṃ sarvaṃ pāpam āśu praṇaśyatid ataḥ paraṃ viśeṣaṃ tu kapilānāṃ bravīmi ted yāś caitāḥ kapilāḥ proktā daśa rājan mayā tavad tāsāṃ catasraḥ pravarāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpanāśanāḥd suvarṇakapilā puṇyā tathā raktākṣipiṅgalād piṅgalākṣī ca yā gauś ca yad vā piṅgalapiṅgalād etāś catasraḥ pravarāḥ puṇyāḥ pāpapraṇāśanāḥd namaskṛtā vā spṛṣṭā vā ghnanti pāpaṃ narasya tud yasyaitāḥ kapilāḥ santi gṛhe pāpapraṇāśanāḥd tatra śrīr vijayaḥ kīrtiḥ sthitā nityaṃ yudhiṣṭhirad etāsāṃ prītim āyāti kṣīreṇa tu vṛṣadhvajaḥd dadhnā tu tridaśāḥ sarve ghṛtena tu hutāśanaḥd pitaraḥ pitāmahāś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥd sakṛd dattena tuṣyanti varṣakoṭiṃ yudhiṣṭhirad kapilāyā ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi pāyasam eva vād śrotriyebhyaḥ sakṛd dattvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyated upavāsaṃ tu yat kṛtvā ahorātraṃ jitendriyaḥd kapilāpañcagavyaṃ tu pītvā cāndrāyaṇāt paramd saumye muhūrte tat prāśya śuddhātmā śuddhamānasaḥd krodhānṛtavinirmukto madgatenāntarātmanād kapilāpañcagavyena samantreṇa pṛthak pṛthakd yo matpratikṛtiṃ vāpi śaṃkarākṛtim eva vād snāpayed viṣuve yas tu so śvamedhaphalaṃ labhetd sa muktapāpaḥ śuddhātmā yānenāmbaraśobhinād mama lokaṃ vrajen martyo rudralokam athāpi vād brahmaṇā tu purā sṛṣṭā kapilā kāñcanaprabhād agnikuṇḍāt parair mantrair homadhenur mahāprabhād sṛṣṭamātrāṃ tu tāṃ dṛṣṭvā devā rudrādayo divid siddhā brahmarṣayaś caiva vedāḥ sāṅgāḥ sahādhvarāḥd sāgarāḥ saritaś cāpi parvatāḥ sabalāhakāḥd gandharvāpsaraso yakṣāḥ pannagāś cāpy upasthitāḥd sarve vismayam āpannāḥ śikhimadhye mahāprabhāmd mantraiś ca vividhaiḥ sarvais tuṣṭuvus tām anekaśaḥd kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve tāmraśṛṅgīṃ trilocanāmd śirobhiḥ patitā bhūmau savatsām amṛtāraṇimd ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve caturvaktraṃ pitāmahamd ājñāpaya mahādeva kiṃ te karma priyaṃ vibhod evam uktaḥ suraiḥ sarvair brahmā vacanam abravītd bhavanto py anugṛhṇantu dogdhrīm enāṃ payasvinīmd homadhenur iyaṃ jñeyā hy agniṃ saṃtarpayiṣyatid tato gnis tarpitaḥ sarvān bhavatas tarpayiṣyatid prītāḥ kṣīrāmṛtenāsyā jātavīryaparākramāḥd jayiṣyatha yathākāmaṃ dānavān sarva eva tud jātavīryabalaiśvaryāḥ sattvavanto jitārayaḥd asaṃkhyeyabalāḥ sarve pālayiṣyatha vai prajāḥd pālitāś ca prajāḥ sarvā bhavadbhir iha dharmataḥd pūjayiṣyanti vo nityaṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥd evam uktāḥ surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinād tataḥ saṃhṛṣṭamanasaḥ kapilāyai varaṃ daduḥd yasmāl lokahitāyādya brahmaṇā tvaṃ vinirmitād tasmāt pūtā pavitrā ca bhava pāpavyapohinīd ye tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā namasyanti spṛṣṭvā cāpi karair narāḥd teṣāṃ varṣakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tvadbhaktānāṃ praṇaśyatid akāmakṛtam ajñātam adṛṣṭaṃ yac ca pātakamd tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā ye namasyanti narāḥ sarvaṃsaheti cad teṣāṃ tad vilayaṃ yāti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathād ity uktvāsyai varaṃ dattvā prayayus te yathāgatamd lokanistāraṇārthāya sā ca lokāṃś cacāra had tasyām eva samudbhūtā hy etāś ca kapilānaghad vicaranti mahīm enāṃ lokānugrahakāraṇātd tasmāt tu kapilā deyā paratra hitam icchatād yathā ca dīyate rājan kapilā hy agnihotriṇed tathāgraśṛṅgayos tasyā viṣṇur indraś ca tiṣṭhataḥd candravajradharau cāpi tiṣṭhataḥ śṛṅgamūlayoḥd śṛṅgamadhye tathā brahmā lalāṭe govṛṣadhvajaḥd karṇayor aśvinau devau cakṣuṣoḥ śaśibhāskaraud danteṣu maruto devā jihvāyāṃ vāk sarasvatīd romānte munayaḥ sarve carmaṇy eva prajāpatiḥd niśvāseṣu sthitā vedāḥ saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥd nāsāpuṭe sthitā gandhāḥ puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi cad adhare vasavaḥ sarve mukhe cāgniḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥd sādhyā devāḥ sthitāḥ kakṣe grīvāyāṃ pārvatī sthitād pṛṣṭhe ca nakṣatragaṇāḥ kakuddeśe nabhaḥsthalamd apāne sarvatīrthāni gomūtre jāhnavī svayamd iṣṭatuṣṭamayī lakṣmīr gomaye vasate sadād nāsikāyāṃ tadā devī jyeṣṭhā vasati bhāminīd śroṇītaṭasthāḥ pitaro ramā lāṅgūlam āśritāḥd pārśvayor ubhayoḥ sarve viśve devāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥd tiṣṭhaty urasi tāsāṃ tu prītaḥ śaktidharo guhaḥd jānujaṅghorudeśeṣu pañca tiṣṭhanti vāyavaḥd khuramadhyeṣu gandharvāḥ khurāgreṣu ca pannagāḥd catvāraḥ sāgarāḥ pūrṇās tasyā eva payodharāḥd ratir medhā kṣamā svāhā śraddhā śāntir dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥd kīrtir dīptiḥ kriyā kāntis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiś ca saṃtatiḥd diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva sevante kapilāṃ sadād devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś cāpi gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd lokā dvīpārṇavāś caiva gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathād grahāḥ pitṛgaṇāś cāpi vedāḥ sāṅgāḥ sahādhvaraiḥd vedoktair vividhair mantraiḥ stuvanti hṛṣitās tathād vidyādharāś ca ye siddhā bhūtās tārāgaṇās tathād puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca varṣanti pranṛtyanti ca harṣitāḥd brahmaṇotpāditā devī vahnikuṇḍān mahāprabhād namas te kapile puṇye sarvadevair namaskṛted kapile tha mahāsattve sarvatīrthamaye śubhed dātāraṃ svajanopetaṃ brahmalokaṃ naya svayamd aho ratnam idaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnam uttamamd aho dharmārjitaṃ śuddham idam agryaṃ mahādhanamd ity ākāśe sthitā devā jalpanti ca namanti cad tasyāḥ pratigṛhītā ca bhuṅkte yāvad dvijottamaḥd tāvad devagaṇāḥ sarve kapilām arcayanti cad svarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurā gandhaiḥ puṣpaiś ca pūjitād vastrābhyām ahatābhyāṃ tu yāvat tiṣṭhaty alaṃkṛtād tāvad yad icchet kapilā mantrapūtā susaṃskṛtād bhūlokavāsinaḥ sarvān brahmalokaṃ nayet svayamd bhūr aśvaḥ kanakaṃ gāvo raupyam annaṃ tilā yavāḥd dīyamānāni viprāya prahṛṣyanti dine dined atha tv aśrotriyebhyo vai tāni dattāni pāṇḍavad tathā nindanty athātmānam aśubhaṃ kiṃ nu naḥ kṛtamd aho rakṣaḥpiśācaiś ca lupyamānāḥ samantataḥd yāsyāmo nirayaṃ śīghram iti śocanti tāni vaid etāny api dvijebhyo vai śrotriyebhyo viśeṣataḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad dīyamānāni vardhante dātāraṃ tārayanti cad devadeveśa daityaghna kālaḥ ko havyakavyayoḥd bhagavān uvācad ke tatra pūjām arhanti varjanīyāś ca ke dvijāḥd daivaṃ pūrvāhṇikaṃ jñeyaṃ paitṛkaṃ cāparāhṇikamd kālahīnaṃ ca yad dānaṃ tad dānaṃ rākṣasaṃ viduḥd avaghuṣṭaṃ ca yad bhuktam anṛtena ca bhāratad parāmṛṣṭaṃ śunā vāpi tadbhāgaṃ rākṣasaṃ viduḥd yāvantaḥ patitā viprā jaḍonmattādayo pi cad daive ca pitrye ye cāpi rājan nārhanti satkriyāmd klībaḥ plīhī ca kuṣṭhī ca rājayakṣmānvitaś ca yaḥd apasmārī ca yaś cāpi pitrye nārhati satkriyāmd cikitsakā devalakā vṛthā niyamadhāriṇaḥd somavikrayiṇaś cāpi śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtimd ekoddiṣṭasya ye cānnaṃ bhuñjate vidhivad dvijāḥd cāndrāyaṇam akṛtvā te punar nārhanti satkṛtimd gāyakā nartakāś caiva plavakā vādakās tathād kathakā yaudhikāś caiva śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtimd anagnayaś ca ye viprāḥ pretaniryātakāś ca yed stenāś cāpi vikarmasthā rājan nārhanti satkṛtimd aparijñātapūrvāś ca gaṇaputrāś ca ye dvijāḥd putrikāputrakāś cāpi śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtimd ṛṇakartā ca yo vipro yaś ca vāṇijyako dvijaḥd prāṇivikrayavṛttiś ca śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtimd cīrṇavratā guṇair yuktā nityaṃ svādhyāyatatparāḥd sāvitrījñāḥ kriyāvantas te śrāddhe satkṛtikṣamāḥd śrāddhasya brāhmaṇaḥ kālaḥ prāpto dadhi ghṛtaṃ tadād darbhāḥ sumanasaḥ kṣetraṃ tatkāle śrāddhado bhavetd cāritraniyatā rājan kṛśā ye kṛśavṛttayaḥd arthinaś copagacchanti tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalamd tapasvinaś ca ye viprās tathā bhaikṣacarāś ca yed arthinaḥ ke cid icchanti teṣāṃ dattaṃ mahat phalamd evaṃ dharmavidāṃ śreṣṭha jñātvā sarvātmanā tadād śrotriyāya daridrāya prayacchānupakāriṇed dānaṃ yat te priyaṃ kiṃ cic chrotriyāṇāṃ ca yat priyamd tat prayacchasva dharmajña yad icchasi tad akṣayamd nirayaṃ ye ca gacchanti tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhirad gurvarthaṃ vā bhayārthaṃ vā no ced anyatra pāṇḍavad vadanti ye nṛtaṃ viprās te vai nirayagāminaḥd paradārābhihartāraḥ paradārābhimarśakāḥd paradāraprayoktāras te vai nirayagāminaḥd sūcakāḥ saṃdhibhettāraḥ paradravyopajīvinaḥd akṛtajñāś ca mitrāṇāṃ te vai nirayagāminaḥd varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye bāhyāḥ pāṣaṇḍasthāś ca pāṇḍavad upāsate ca tān ye tu te sarve narakālayāḥd vedavikrayiṇaś caiva vedānāṃ caiva dūṣakāḥd vedānāṃ lekhakāś caiva te vai nirayagāminaḥd rasavikrayiṇo rājan viṣavikrayiṇaś ca yed kṣīravikrayiṇaś cāpi te vai nirayagāminaḥd caṇḍālebhyas tu ye kṣīraṃ prayacchanti narādhamāḥd arthārtham atha vā snehāt te vai nirayagāminaḥd paśūnāṃ damakāś caiva tathā nāsānuvedhakāḥd puṃstvasya hiṃsakāś caiva te vai nirayagāminaḥd adātāraḥ samarthā ye dravyāṇāṃ lobhakāraṇātd dīnānāthān na paśyanti te vai nirayagāminaḥd kṣāntān dāntān kṛśān prājñān dīrghakālaṃ sadoṣitānd tyajanti kṛtakṛtyā ye te vai nirayagāminaḥd bālānām atha vṛddhānāṃ śrāntānāṃ cāpi ye narāḥd adattvāśnanti ye mṛṣṭaṃ te vai nirayagāminaḥd ete pūrvarṣibhiḥ proktā narā nirayagāminaḥd ye svargaṃ samanuprāptās tāñ śṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhirad dānena tapasā caiva satyena ca damena cad ye dharmam anuvartante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd śuśrūṣayāpy upādhyāyāc chrutam ādāya pāṇḍavad ye pratigrahaniḥsnehās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd madhumāṃsāsavebhyas tu nivṛttā vṛttavat tu yed paradāranivṛttāś ca te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva śuśrūṣanti ca ye narāḥd bhrātṝṇām api sasnehās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd ye tu bhojanakāle tu niyatāś cātithipriyāḥd dvārarodhaṃ na kurvanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd vaivāhikaṃ tu kanyānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ ca ye narāḥd kārayanti ca kurvanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd rasānām atha bījānām oṣadhīnāṃ tathaiva cad dātāraḥ śraddhayopetās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd kṣemākṣemaṃ ca mārgeṣu samāni viṣamāṇi cad arthināṃ ye ca vakṣyanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd parvadvaye caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ saṃdhyayor dvayoḥd ārdrāyāṃ janmanakṣatre viṣuve śravaṇe tathād ye grāmyadharmaviratās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥd havyakavyavidhānaṃ ca narakasvargagāminaud yudhiṣṭhira uvācad dharmādharmau ca kathitau bhūyaḥ kiṃ śrotum icchasid idaṃ me tattvato deva vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥd hiṃsām akṛtvā yo martyo brahmahatyām avāpnuyātd bhagavān uvācad brāhmaṇaṃ svayam āhūya bhikṣārthaṃ kṛśavṛttinamd brūyān nāstīti yaḥ paścāt tam āhur brahmaghātakamd madhyasthasyeha viprasya yo nūcānasya bhāratad vṛttiṃ harati durbuddhis tam āhur brahmaghātakamd gokulasya tṛṣārtasya jalānte vasudhādhipad utpādayati yo vighnaṃ tam āhur brahmaghātakamd yaḥ pravṛttāṃ śrutiṃ satyāṃ śāstraṃ vā munibhiḥ kṛtamd dūṣayaty anabhijño yas taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakamd āśrame vā vane vāpi grāme vā nagare pi vād agniṃ yaḥ prakṣipet kruddhas tam āhur brahmaghātakamd cakṣuṣā vāpi hīnasya paṅgor vāpi jaḍasya cad hared vai yas tu sarvasvaṃ taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakamd krodhād vā yadi vā dveṣād ākruṣṭas tarjito pi vād ṛtau striyaṃ vā nopeyāt tam āhur brahmaghātakamd yāvat sāro bhaved dhīras tannāśe yasya duḥsthitiḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad tat sarvasvaṃ hared yo vai tam āhur brahmaghātakamd sarveṣām api dānānāṃ yat tu dānaṃ viśiṣyated bhagavān uvācad abhojyānnāś ca ye viprās tān bravīhi surottamad annam eva praśaṃsanti devā brahmapuraḥsarāḥd annena sadṛśaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyatid annam ūrjaskaraṃ loke annāt prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥd abhojyānnān imān rājan vakṣyamāṇān nibodha med dīkṣitasya kadaryasya baddhasya nikṛtasya cad abhiśastasya ṣaṇḍasya pākabhedakarasya cad cikitsakasya sarvasya tathā cocchiṣṭabhojinaḥd ugrānnaṃ sūtakānnaṃ ca śūdroccheṣaṇam eva cad dviṣadannaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ patitānnaṃ ca yac chrutamd tathā ca piśunasyānnaṃ yajñavikrayiṇas tathād śailūṣatantuvāyānnaṃ kṛtaghnasyānnam eva cad ambaṣṭhasya niṣādasya raṅgāvatarakasya cad suvarṇakartur vaiṇasya śastravikrayiṇas tathād sūtānāṃ śauṇḍikānāṃ ca vaidyasya rajakasya cad strījitasya nṛśaṃsasya tathā māhiṣikasya cad anirdaśānāṃ pretānāṃ gaṇikānāṃ tathaiva cad vandino dyūtakartuś ca tathā dyūtavidām apid parivittasya yac cānnaṃ parivettus tathaiva cad yaś cāgradidhiṣur vipro didhiṣūpapatis tathād tayor apy ubhayor annaṃ rājñaś cāpi vivarjayetd rājānnaṃ teja ādatte śūdrānnaṃ brahmavarcasamd āyuḥ suvarṇakārānnaṃ yaśaś carmāvakṛntinaḥd gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca lokebhyaḥ parikṛntatid āyuś cikitsakasyānnaṃ śuklaṃ tu vṛṣalīpateḥd viṣṭhā vārdhuṣikasyānnaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayetd teṣāṃ tvagasthiromāṇi bhuṅkte yo nnaṃ tu bhakṣayetd amātyānnam athaiteṣāṃ bhuktvā tu triyahaṃ kṣipetd matyā bhuktvā sakṛd vāpi prājāpatyaṃ cared dvijaḥd dānānāṃ ca phalaṃ yad vai śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvataḥd jaladas tṛptim āpnoti sukham akṣayam annadaḥd tiladas tu prajām iṣṭāṃ dīpadaś cakṣur uttamamd bhūmido bhūmim āpnoti dīrgham āyur hiraṇyadaḥd gṛhado gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpam uttamamd vāsodaś candrasālokyam aśvisālokyam aśvadaḥd anaḍuddaḥ śriyaṃ juṣṭāṃ godaś ca bradhnaviṣṭapamd yānaśayyāprado bhāryām aiśvaryam abhayapradaḥd dhānyadaḥ śāśvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahmasāmyatāmd sarveṣām eva dānānāṃ brahmadānaṃ viśiṣyated hiraṇyabhūgavāśvājavastraśayyāsanādiṣud yo rcitaṃ pratigṛhṇāti dadāty arcitam eva cad tāv ubhau gacchataḥ svargaṃ narakaṃ ca viparyayed anṛtaṃ na vaded iṣṭvā tapas taptvā na vismayetd nārto py apavaded viprān na dattvā parikīrtayetd yajño nṛtena kṣarati tapaḥ kṣarati vismayātd āyurviprāpavādena dānaṃ tu parikīrtanātd ekaḥ prajāyate jantur eka eva pramīyated eko nubhuṅkte sukṛtam ekaś cāpnoti duṣkṛtamd mṛtaṃ śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamaṃ kṣitaud vimukhā bāndhavā yānti dharmas tam anuvartated anāgatāni kāryāṇi kartuṃ gaṇayate manaḥd śarīrakaṃ samuddiśya smayate nūnam antakaḥd tasmād dharmasahāyo stu dharmaṃ saṃcinuyāt sadād dharmeṇa hi sahāyena tamas tarati dustaramd yeṣāṃ taṭākāni bahūdakānid sabhāś ca kūpāś ca pratiśrayāś cad annapradānaṃ madhurā ca vāṇīd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad yamasya te nirviṣayā bhavantid anekāntaṃ bahudvāraṃ dharmam āhur manīṣiṇaḥd bhagavān uvācad kiṃlakṣaṇo sau bhavati tan me brūhi janārdanad śṛṇu rājan samāsena dharmaśaucavidhikramamd ahiṃsā satyam asteyam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ damaḥ śamaḥd ārjavaṃ caiva rājendra niścitaṃ dharmalakṣaṇamd brahmacaryaṃ tapaḥ kṣāntir madhumāṃsasya varjanamd maryādāyāṃ sthitiś caiva śamaḥ śaucasya lakṣaṇamd bālye vidyāṃ niṣeveta yauvane dārasaṃgrahamd vārdhakye maunam ātiṣṭhet sarvadā dharmam ācaretd brāhmaṇān nāvamanyeta gurūn parivaden na cad yatīnām anukūlaḥ syād eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥd yatir gurur dvijātīnāṃ varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥd patir eva guruḥ strīṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ pārthivo guruḥd yad gṛhasthārjitaṃ pāpaṃ jñānato jñānato pi vād nirdahiṣyati tat sarvam ekarātroṣito yatiḥd durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā jñānino jñānino pi vād gṛhasthair yatayaḥ pūjyāḥ paratra hitakāṅkṣibhiḥd ekadaṇḍī tridaṇḍī vā śikhaṇḍī muṇḍito pi vād kāṣāyadaṇḍadhāro pi yatiḥ pūjyo yudhiṣṭhirad apūjito gṛhasthair vā tathā cāpy avamānitaḥd yatir vāpy atithir vāpi narake pātayiṣyataḥd tasmāt tu yatnataḥ pūjyā madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥd mayi saṃnyastakarmāṇaḥ paratra hitakāṅkṣibhiḥd praharen na dvijān prājño gāṃ na hanyāt kadā canad bhrūṇahatyāsamaṃ caitad ubhayaṃ yo niṣevated nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamen na ca pādau pratāpayetd nādhaḥ kuryāt kadā cit tu na pṛṣṭhaṃ paritāpayetd nāntarāgamanaṃ kuryān na cāmedhyaṃ vinikṣipetd ucchiṣṭo na spṛśed agnim āśaucastho na jātu citd śvacaṇḍālādibhiḥ spṛṣṭo nāṅgam agnau pratāpayetd sarvadevamayo vahnis tasmāc chuddhaḥ sadā spṛśetd prāptamūtrapurīṣas tu na spṛśed vahnim ātmavānd yāvat tu dhārayed vegaṃ tāvad aprayato bhavetd pacanāgniṃ na gṛhṇīyāt paraveśmani jātu citd tena pakvena cānnena yat karma kurute śubhamd tac chubhasya phalasyārdham agnidasya bhaven nṛpad tasmāc chubhataraṃ karma prakuryād avināśitamd pramādād yadi vājñānāt tasya nāśo bhaviṣyatid yudhiṣṭhira uvācad gṛhṇīyāt tu mathitvā vā śrotriyāgārato pi vād kīdṛśāḥ sādhavo viprāḥ kebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalamd bhagavān uvācad kīdṛśebhyo hi dātavyaṃ tan me brūhi janārdanad akrodhanāḥ satyaparā dharmanityā jitendriyāḥd tādṛśāḥ sādhavo viprās tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalamd amāninaḥ sarvasahā dṛṣṭārthā vijitendriyāḥd sarvabhūtahitā maitrās tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalamd alubdhāḥ śucayo vaidyā hrīmantaḥ satyavādinaḥd svadharmaniratā ye tu tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalamd sāṅgāṃś ca caturo vedān yo dhīyīta dine dined śūdrānnaṃ yasya dehe na tatpātram ṛṣayo viduḥd prajñāśrutābhyāṃ vṛttena śīlena ca samanvitaḥd tārayet tat kulaṃ sarvam eko pīha yudhiṣṭhirad gām aśvam annaṃ vittaṃ vā tadvidhe pratipādayetd niśamya ca guṇopetaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ sādhusaṃmatamd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad dūrād āhṛtya satkṛtya taṃ prayatnena pūjayetd dharmādharmavidhir deva mama bhīṣmeṇa bhāṣitaḥd bhīṣmavākyāt sārabhūtaṃ vada dharmaṃ sureśvarad bhagavān uvācad annena dhāryate sarvaṃ jagad etac carācaramd annāt prabhavati prāṇaḥ pratyakṣaṃ nāsti saṃśayaḥd kalatraṃ pīḍayitvāpi deśe kāle ca śaktitaḥd dātavyaṃ bhikṣave cānnam ātmano bhūtim icchatād vipram adhvapariśrāntaṃ bālaṃ vṛddham athāpi vād arcayed guruvat prīto gṛhastho gṛham āgatamd krodham utpatitaṃ hitvā suśīlo vītamatsaraḥd arcayed atithiṃ prītaḥ paratra hitabhūtayed atithiṃ nāvamanyeta nānṛtāṃ giram īrayetd na pṛcched gotracaraṇaṃ nādhītaṃ vā kadā canad caṇḍālo vā śvapāko vā kāle yaḥ kaś cid āgataḥd annena pūjanīyaḥ sa paratra hitam icchatād pidhāya tu gṛhadvāraṃ bhuṅkte hy ekaḥ prahṛṣṭavatd svargadvārapidhānaṃ vai kṛtaṃ tena yudhiṣṭhirad pitṝn devān ṛṣīn viprān atithīṃś ca nirāśrayānd yo naraḥ prīṇayaty annais tasya puṇyaphalaṃ mahatd kṛtvāpi pāpaṃ bahuśo yo dadyād annam arthined brāhmaṇāya viśeṣeṇa sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyated annadaḥ prāṇado loke prāṇadaḥ sarvado bhavetd tasmād annaṃ viśeṣeṇa dātavyaṃ bhūtim icchatād annaṃ hy amṛtam ity āhur annaṃ prajananaṃ smṛtamd annapraṇāśe sīdanti śarīre pañca dhātavaḥd balaṃ balavato naśyed annahīnasya dehinaḥd tasmād
