bhaved devī mahī prītā ca pāṇḍavad tasyāṃ sasyāni rohanti yair jīvanty akhilāḥ prajāḥd māṃsamedosthimajjānāṃ saṃbhavas tebhya eva hid evaṃ sūryaś ca pavano meghaḥ śakras tathaiva cad eka eva smṛto rāśir yato bhūtāni jajñired bhavanāni ca divyāni divi teṣāṃ mahātmanāmd nānāsaṃsthānarūpāṇi nānābhūtayutāni cad candramaṇḍalaśubhrāṇi kiṅkiṇījālavanti cad taruṇādityavarṇāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi cad anekaśatasaṃkhyāni sāntarjalavanāni cad tatra puṣpaphalopetāḥ kāmadāḥ surapādapāḥd vāpyo vīthyaḥ sabhāḥ kūpā dīrghikāś ca sahasraśaḥd ghoṣavanti ca yānāni yuktāny atha sahasraśaḥd bhakṣyabhojyamayāḥ śailā vāsāṃsy ābharaṇāni cad kṣīrasravantyaḥ saritas tathā caivānnaparvatāḥd prāsādāḥ pāṇḍarāḥ śubhrāḥ śayyāś ca kanakojjvalāḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad annadās tatra tiṣṭhanti tasmād annaprado bhavetd annadānaphalaṃ śrutvā prīto smi madhusūdanad bhagavān uvācad bhojanasya vidhiṃ vaktuṃ devadeva tvam arhasid bhojanasya dvijātīnāṃ vidhānaṃ śṛṇu pāṇḍavad snātaḥ śuciḥ śucau deśe nirjane hutapāvakaḥd maṇḍalaṃ kārayitvā tu caturaśraṃ dvijottamaḥd kṣatriyaś cet tato vṛttaṃ vaiśyo rdhendusamākṛtimd ārdrapādas tu bhuñjīyāt prāṅmukhaś cāsane śucaud pādābhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ spṛṣṭvā pādenaikena vā punaḥd naikavāsās tu bhuñjīyān na cāntardhāya vā dvijaḥd na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta parṇapṛṣṭhe tathaiva cad annaṃ pūrvaṃ namaskuryāt prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanād nānyad ālokayed annān na jugupseta tatparaḥd jugupsitaṃ ca yac cānnaṃ rākṣasā eva bhuñjated pāṇinā jalam uddhṛtya kuryād annaṃ pradakṣiṇamd apeyaṃ tad vijānīyāt pītvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd pariveṣajalād anyat peyam etat tu mantravatd pañca prāṇāhutīḥ kuryāt samaṃ tu pṛthak pṛthakd yathā rasaṃ na jānāti jihvā prāṇāhutau nṛpad tathā samāhitaḥ kuryāt prāṇāhutim atandritaḥd viditvānnam athānnādaṃ pañca prāṇāṃś ca pāṇḍavad yaḥ kuryād āhutīḥ pañca teneṣṭāḥ pañca vāyavaḥd ato nyathā tu bhuñjāno brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥd tenānnenāsurān pretān rākṣasāṃs tarpayiṣyatid vaktrapramāṇān piṇḍāṃś ca grased ekaikaśaḥ punaḥd vaktrādhikaṃ tu yat piṇḍam ātmocchiṣṭaṃ tad ucyated piṇḍāvaśiṣṭam anyac ca vaktraniḥsṛtam eva cad abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd svam ucchiṣṭaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte yo bhuṅte muktabhojanamd cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyam athāpi vād pibataḥ patite toye bhojane mukhaniḥsṛted abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd pītaśeṣaṃ tu tan nāma na peyaṃ pāṇḍunandanad pibed yadi hi tan mohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd pānīyāni pibed yena tat pātraṃ dvijasattamaḥd anucchiṣṭaṃ bhavet tāvad yāvad bhūmau na nikṣipetd maunī vāpy atha vāmaunī prahṛṣṭaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥd bhuñjīta vidhivad vipro na cocchiṣṭaṃ pradāpayetd sadā cātyāśanaṃ nādyān nātihīnaṃ ca karhi citd yathānnena vyathā na syāt tathā bhuñjīta nityaśaḥd udakyām api caṇḍālaṃ śvānaṃ vā rurum eva vād bhuñjāno yadi vā paśyet tad annaṃ ca parityajetd bhuñjāno hy atyajan mohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca mukhamārutavījitamd abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd utthāya ca punaḥ spṛṣṭaṃ pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca laṅghitamd annaṃ tad rākṣasaṃ vidyāt tasmāt tat parivarjayetd rākṣasocchiṣṭabhug vipraḥ sapta pūrvān parān apid niraye raurave ghore svapitṝn pātayiṣyatid tasminn ācamanaṃ kuryād yasmin pātre sa bhuktavānd yady uttiṣṭhaty anācānto bhuktavān āsanāt tataḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad snānaṃ sadyaḥ prakurvīta so nyathāprayato bhavetd tṛṇamuṣṭividhānaṃ ca tṛṇamāhātmyam eva cad ikṣoḥ somasamudbhūtiṃ vaktum arhasi mānadad bhagavān uvācad pitaro vṛṣabhā jñeyā gāvo lokasya mātaraḥd tāsāṃ tu pūjayā rājan pūjitāḥ pitṛmātaraḥd sabhā prapā gṛhaṃ cāpi devatāyatanāni cad śudhyanti śakṛdā yāsāṃ kiṃ pūtam adhikaṃ tataḥd grāsamuṣṭiṃ paragave dadyāt saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥd akṛtvā svayam āhāraṃ vrataṃ tat sārvakālikamd gāvo me mātaraḥ sarvāḥ pitaraś caiva govṛṣāḥd grāsamuṣṭiṃ mayā dattāṃ pratigṛhṇantu mātaraḥd ity uktvānena mantreṇa sāvitryā vā samāhitaḥd abhimantrya grāsamuṣṭiṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇud yat kṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ tena jñānato jñānato pi vād tasya naśyati tat sarvaṃ duḥsvapnaṃ ca vinaśyatid tilāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpaghnā nārāyaṇasamudbhavāḥd tilāñ śrāddhe praśaṃsanti dānam etad anuttamamd tilān dadyāt tilān bhakṣyāt tilān prātar upaspṛśetd tilaṃ tilam iti brūyāt tilāḥ pāpaharā hi ted krītāḥ pratigṛhītā vā na vikreyā dvijātibhiḥd bhojanābhyañjanād dānād yo nyat tu kurute tilaiḥd kṛmir bhūtvā śvaviṣṭhāyāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha majjatid tilān na pīḍayed vipro yantracakre svayaṃ nṛpad pīḍayan hi dvijo mohān narakaṃ yāti rauravamd ikṣuvaṃśodbhavaḥ somaḥ somavaṃśodbhavā dvijāḥd ikṣūn na pīḍayet tasmād ikṣughātyātmaghātakaḥd ikṣudaṇḍasahasrāṇām ekaikena yudhiṣṭhirad brahmahatyām avāpnoti brāhmaṇo yantrapīḍakaḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad tasmān na pīḍayed ikṣūn yantracakre dvijottamaḥd samuccayaṃ tu dharmāṇāṃ bhojyābhojyaṃ tathaiva cad bhagavān uvācad śrutaṃ mayā tvatprasādād āpaddharmaṃ bravīhi med durbhikṣe rāṣṭrasaṃbādhe tvāśauce mṛtasūtaked dharmakāle dhvani tathā niyamo naiva lupyated dūrādhvagamanāt khinno dvijālābhe tha śūdrataḥd akṛtānnaṃ ca yat kiṃ cid gṛhṇīyād ātmavṛttayed āturo duḥkhito vāpi bhayārto vā bubhukṣitaḥd bhuñjann avidhinā vipraḥ prāyaścittīyate na cad nimantritas tu yo vipro vidhivad dhavyakavyayoḥd māṃsāny api ca bhuñjānaḥ prāyaścittīyate na cad aṣṭau tāny avrataghnāni āpo mūlaṃ ghṛtaṃ payaḥd havir brāhmaṇakāmāya guror vacanam auṣadhamd aśakto vidhivat kartuṃ prāyaścittāni yo naraḥd viduṣāṃ vacanenāpi dānenāpi viśudhyatid anṛtāv ṛtukāle vā divā rātrau tathāpi vād yudhiṣṭhira uvācad proṣitas tu striyaṃ gacchet prāyaścittīyate na cad praśasyāḥ kīdṛśā viprā nindyāś cāpi sureśvarad bhagavān uvācad aṣṭakāyāś ca kaḥ kālas tan me kathaya suvratad satyasandhaṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā sthānād vepati bhāskaraḥd eṣa me maṇḍalaṃ bhittvā yāti brahma sanātanamd kulīnaḥ karmakṛd vaidyas tathā cāpy ānṛśaṃsyavānd hrīmān ṛjuḥ satyavādī pātraṃ sarva ime dvijāḥd ete cāgrāsanasthās tu bhuñjānāḥ prathamaṃ dvijāḥd tasyāṃ paṅktyāṃ ca ye cānye tān punanty eva darśanātd madbhaktā ye dvijaśreṣṭhā madgatā matparāyaṇāḥd tān paṅktipāvanān viddhi pūjyāṃś caiva viśeṣataḥd nindyāñ śṛṇu dvijān rājann api vā vedapāragānd brāhmaṇacchadmanā loke carataḥ pāpakāriṇaḥd anagnir anadhīyānaḥ pratigraharucis tu yaḥd yatra kutra tu bhuñjānas taṃ vidyāt paṅktidūṣakamd mṛtasūtakapuṣṭāṅgo yaś ca śūdrānnabhug dvijaḥd ahaṃ cāpi na jānāmi gatiṃ tasya narādhipad śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgo hy adhīyāno pi nityaśaḥd japato juhvato vāpi gatir ūrdhvā na vidyated āhitāgniś ca yo vipraḥ śūdrānnān na nivartated pañca tasya praṇaśyanti ātmā brahma trayo gnayaḥd śūdrapreṣaṇakartuś ca brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥd bhūmāv annaṃ pradātavyaṃ śvasṛgālasamo hi saḥd pretabhūtaṃ tu yaḥ śūdraṃ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥd anugacchen nīyamānaṃ trirātram aśucir bhavetd trirātre tu tataḥ pūrṇe nadīṃ gatvā samudragāmd prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kṛtvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyatid anāthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ pretaṃ ye vahanti dvijottamāḥd pade pade śvamedhasya phalaṃ te prāpnuvanti hid na teṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃ cit pāpaṃ vāśubhakarmaṇāmd jalāvagāhanād eva sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyated śūdraveśmani vipreṇa kṣīraṃ vā yadi vā dadhid nirvṛtena na bhoktavyaṃ viddhi śūdrānnam eva tatd viprāṇāṃ bhoktukāmānām atyantaṃ cānnakāṅkṣayād yo vighnaṃ kurute martyas tato nānyo sti pāpakṛtd sarve ca vedāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥd sāṃkhyaṃ purāṇaṃ ca kule ca janmad naitāni sarvāṇi gatir bhavantid śīlavyapetasya nṛpa dvijasyad grahoparāge viṣuve yanānted pitrye maghāsu svasute ca jāted gayeṣu piṇḍeṣu ca pāṇḍuputrad dattaṃ bhaven niṣkasahasratulyamd vaiśākhamāsasya ca yā tṛtīyād navamy asau kārtikaśuklapakṣed nabhasyamāsasya ca kṛṣṇapakṣed trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghed upaplave candramaso raveś cad śrāddhasya kālo hy ayanadvaye cad yas tv ekapaṅktyāṃ viṣayaṃ dadātid snehād bhayād vā yadi vārthahetoḥd krūraṃ durācāram anātmavantaṃd brahmaghnam enaṃ munayo vadantid ihaivaikasya nāmutra amutraikasya no ihad iha cāmutra caikasya nāmutraikasya no ihad dhanāni yeṣāṃ vipulāni santid nityaṃ ramante paralokamūḍhāḥd teṣām ayaṃ śatruvaraghnalokod nānyaḥ sadā dehasukhe ratānāmd ye yogayuktās tapasi prasaktāḥd svādhyāyaśīlā jarayanti dehamd jitendriyā bhūtahite niviṣṭāsd teṣām asau nāyam arighnalokaḥd ye dharmam eva prathamaṃ carantid dharmeṇa labdhvāpi dhanāni kāled dārān avāpya kratubhir jayanted teṣām ayaṃ caiva paraś ca lokaḥd ye naiva vidyāṃ na tapo na dānaṃd na cāpi mūḍhāḥ prajane yatanted na cāpi gacchanti sukhāni bhogāṃsd teṣām ayaṃ caiva paraś ca nāstid yudhiṣṭhira uvācad nārāyaṇa purāṇeśa yogāvāsa namo stu ted śrotum icchāmi kārtsnyena dharmasārasamuccayamd bhagavān uvācad dharmasāraṃ mahārāja manunā proktam āditaḥd pravakṣyāmi manuproktaṃ paurāṇaṃ śrutisaṃhitamd agnicit kapilā satrī rājā bhikṣur mahodadhiḥd dṛṣṭamātrāḥ punanty ete tasmāt paśyeta tān sadād gaur ekasyaiva dātavyā na bahūnāṃ yudhiṣṭhirad sā gaur vikrayam āpannā dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulamd bahūnāṃ na pradātavyā gaur vastraṃ śayanaṃ striyaḥd tādṛgbhūtaṃ tu tad dānaṃ dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhatid ākramya brāhmaṇair bhuktam anāryāṇāṃ tu veśmanid gobhiś ca puṇyaṃ tat teṣāṃ rājasūyād viśiṣyated mā dadātv iti yo brūyād gavyagnau brāhmaṇeṣu cad tiryagyoniśataṃ gatvā caṇḍāleṣūpajāyated brāhmaṇasvaṃ tu devasvaṃ daridrasya ca yad dhanamd guroś cāpi hṛtaṃ rājan svargastham api pātayetd dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ śrutiḥd dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstrāṇi tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṃgrahaḥd ā samudrāc ca yat pūrvād ā samudrāc ca paścimātd himavadvindhyayor madhyam āryāvartaṃ pracakṣated sarasvatīdṛṣadvatyor devanadyor yad antaramd tad devanirmitaṃ deśaṃ brahmāvartaṃ pracakṣated yasmin deśe ya ācāraḥ pāraṃparyakramāgataḥd varṇānāṃ sāntarālānāṃ sa sadācāra ucyated kurukṣetraṃ ca matsyāś ca pāñcālāḥ śūrasenayaḥd ete brahmarṣideśās tu brahmāvartād anantarāḥd etaddeśaprasūtasya sakāśād agrajanmanaḥd svaṃ cāritraṃ tu gṛhṇīyuḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvamānavāḥd himavadvindhyayor madhyaṃ yat prāg viśasanād apid pratyag eva prayāgāt tu madhyadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥd kṛṣṇasāras tu carati mṛgo yatra svabhāvataḥd sa jñeyo yajñiyo deśo mlecchadeśas tataḥ paramd etān vijñāya deśāṃs tu saṃśrayeyur dvijātayaḥd śūdras tu yasmin kasmin vā nivased vṛttikarśitaḥd ācāraprabhavo dharmo hy ahiṃsā satyam eva cad dānaṃ caiva yathāśakti niyamāś ca yamaiḥ sahad vaidikaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyair niṣekādir dvijanmanāmd kāryaḥ śarīrasaṃskāraḥ pāvanaḥ pretya ceha cad garbhahomair jātakarmanāmacaulopanāyanaiḥd svādhyāyais tadvrataiś caiva vivāhasnātakavrataiḥd mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥd dharmārthau yatra na syātāṃ śuśrūṣā vāpi tadvidhād vidyā tasmin na vaptavyā śubhaṃ bījam ivoṣared laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi tathādhyātmikam eva vād yasmāj jñānam idaṃ prāptaṃ taṃ pūrvam abhivādayetd savyena savyaṃ saṃgṛhya dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇamd na kuryād ekahastena guroḥ pādābhivādanamd niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhid adhyāpayati caivainaṃ sa vipro gurur ucyated kṛtvopanayanaṃ vedān yo dhyāpayati nityaśaḥd sakalpān sarahasyāṃś ca sa copādhyāya ucyated sāṅgāṃś ca vedān adhyāpya śikṣayitvā vratāni cad vivṛṇoti ca mantrārthān ācāryaḥ so bhidhīyated upādhyāyād daśācārya ācāryāṇāṃ śataṃ pitād pituḥ śataguṇaṃ mātā gauraveṇātiricyated tasmāt teṣāṃ vaśe tiṣṭhet tacchuśrūṣāparo bhavetd avamānād dhi teṣāṃ tu narakaṃ syād asaṃśayaḥd hīnāṅgān atiriktāṅgān vidyāhīnān vayodhikānd rūpadraviṇahīnāṃś ca jātihīnāṃś ca nākṣipetd śapatā yat kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ śapyamānaṃ tu gacchatid śapyamānasya yat pāpaṃ śapantam anugacchatid nāstikyaṃ vedanindāṃ ca devatānāṃ ca kutsanamd dveṣaṃ ḍambhaṃ ca mānaṃ ca krodhaṃ taikṣṇyaṃ ca varjayetd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad bhagavaṃs tava bhaktasya mama dharmajanapriyad bhagavān uvācad dharmaṃ puṇyatamaṃ deva pṛcchataḥ kathayasva med yad etad agnihotraṃ vai sṛṣṭaṃ varṇatrayasya tud mantravad yad dhutaṃ samyag vidhinā cāpy upāsitamd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad āhitāgniṃ nayaty ūrdhvaṃ sapatnīkaṃ sabāndhavamd kathaṃ tad brāhmaṇair deva hotavyaṃ kṣatriyaiḥ kathamd vaiśyair vā devadeveśa kathaṃ vā suhutaṃ bhavetd kasmin kāle tha vā kasya ādheyo gniḥ surottamad āhitasya kathaṃ vāpi samyag ācaraṇaṃ bhavetd katy agnayaḥ kim ātmānaḥ sthānaṃ kiṃ kasya vā vibhod katarasmin hute sthāne kiṃ vrajed āgnihotrikaḥd agnihotranimittaṃ ca kim utpannaṃ purānaghad katham evātha hūyante prīyante ca surāḥ kathamd vidhivan mantravad bhaktyā pūjitās tv agnayaḥ kathamd kāṃ gatiṃ vadatāṃ śreṣṭha nayanti hy agnihotriṇaḥd durhutāś cāpi bhagavann avijñātās trayo gnayaḥd kim āhitāgneḥ kurvanti duścīrṇā vāpi keśavad utsannāgnis tu pāpātmā kāṃ yoniṃ deva gacchatid etat sarvaṃ samāsena bhaktyā hy upagatasya med bhagavān uvācad vaktum arhasi sarvajña sarvāvāsa namo stu ted śṛṇu rājan mahāpuṇyam idaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ paramd yat tu tārayate yuktān brāhmaṇān agnihotriṇaḥd brahmatvenāsṛjaṃ lokān aham ādau mahādyuted sṛṣṭo gnir mukhataḥ pūrvaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayād yasmād agre sa bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ nirmito mayād tasmād agnīty abhihitaḥ purāṇajñair manīṣiṇaḥd yasmāt tu sarvakṛtyeṣu pūrvam asmai pradīyated āhutir dīpyamānāya tasmād agnīti kīrtyated yasmāc ca nayati hy agryāṃ gatiṃ viprān supūjitaḥd tasmāc ca nayanād rājan vedeṣv agnīti kīrtyated yasmāc ca durhutaḥ so yam alaṃ bhakṣayituṃ kṣaṇātd yajamānaṃ naraśreṣṭha kravyādo gnis tataḥ smṛtaḥd sarvabhūtātmako rājan devānām eṣa vai mukhamd prathamaṃ manmukhāt sṛṣṭo lokārthe pacanaḥ prabhuḥd sṛṣṭamātro jagat sarvam attum aicchat purā khalud tataḥ praśamitaḥ so gnir upāsyaiva mayā purād satatopāsanāt so yam aupāsana iti smṛtaḥd āhutiḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ tasmin vasati so nalaḥd āvasathya iti khyātas tenāsau brahmavādibhiḥd tasmin pañca mahāyajñā vartante yasya dharmataḥd somamaṇḍalamadhyena gatis tasya dvijanmanaḥd te ca saptarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ saṃyatendriyabuddhayaḥd gatā hy amarasāyujyam ekāgnyarcanatatparāḥd apare cāvasathyaṃ ca pacanāgniṃ pracakṣated tasmin pañca mahāyajñā vaiśvadevaś ca vartated sthālīpāka ca gārhaṃ ca sarve hy asmin pratiṣṭhitāḥd gṛhyakarmavaho yasmāt tasmād gṛhapatis tu saḥd aupāsanaṃ cāvasathyaṃ sabhyaṃ pacanapāvakamd āhur brahmavidaḥ ke cin matam etan mamāpi cad agnihotraprakāraṃ tu śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥd trayāṇāṃ guṇanāmāni vahnīnām ucyate mayād gṛhāṇāṃ hi patitvaṃ hi gṛhapatyam iti smṛtamd gṛhapatyaṃ tu yasyāsīt tasyāsīd gārhapatyatād yajamānaṃ tu yasmāt tu dakṣiṇāṃ tu gatiṃ nayetd dakṣiṇāgniṃ tam āhus taṃ dakṣiṇāyatanaṃ dvijāḥd āhutiḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ havanaṃ havyavāhanamd sarvahavyavaho vahnir gataś cāhavanīyatāmd yas tv āvasathyaṃ juhuyān mūlāgniṃ vidhivad dvijaḥd āvasathyaṃ tu ye cāgniṃ pacanāgniṃ pracakṣated teṣāṃ sa bhāgato vahniḥ sabhya ity abhidhīyated āvasathyas tu yo vahniḥ prathamaḥ sa prajāpatiḥd brahmā ca gārhapatyo gnis tasmād eva tu so bhavetd dakṣiṇāgnis tv ayaṃ rudraḥ krodhātmā caṇḍa eva saḥd aham āhavanīyo gnir ā homād yasya vai mukhed sabhyo gniḥ pañcamo yas tu skanda eva narādhipad pṛthivī gārhapatyo gnir antarikṣaṃ ca dakṣiṇaḥd svarga āhavanīyo gnir evam agnitrayaṃ smṛtamd vṛtto hi gārhapatyo gnir yasmād vṛttā ca medinīd ardhacandrākṛtiḥ khaṃ vai dakṣiṇāgnis tathā bhavetd caturaśraṃ tataḥ svargaṃ nirmalaṃ yan nirāmayamd tasmād āhavanīyo gniś caturaśro bhaven nṛpad juhuyād gārhapatyaṃ yo bhuvaṃ jayati sa dvijaḥd juhoti dakṣiṇāgniṃ yaḥ sa jayaty antarikṣakamd pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ carṣigaṇaiḥ sahad jayaty āhavanīyaṃ yo juhuyād bhaktimān dvijaḥd ābhimukhyena homas tu yasya yajñeṣu vartated tenāpy āhavanīyatvaṃ gato vahnir mahādyutiḥd ā homād yo gnihotreṣu yajñe vā yatra sarvaśaḥd yasmād asmin pravartante tato hy āhavanīyatād yas tv āvasathyaṃ juhuyān mūlāgniṃ vidhivad dvijaḥd sa tu saptarṣilokeṣu sapatnīkaḥ pramodated yaś cāpy upāsate sabhyaṃ vidhivat prayatātmavānd jayet sa vāṅmayaṃ sarvaṃ tathā tv ṛṣisabhām apid agnīnām atha vāgnes tu yasya homaḥ pradīyated iṣṭo bhavati sarvāgner agnihotraṃ ca tad bhavetd trayāṇāṃ yajamānasya cāturhotram iti smṛtamd ho ity eva viṣādo vai viṣādo duḥkham ucyated duḥkhaṃ tāpatrayaṃ proktaṃ tāpaṃ hi narakaṃ viduḥd tasmād vai trāyate duḥkhād yajamānaṃ huto nalaḥd tasmāt tu vidhivat proktam agnihotram iti śrutaud tad agnihotraṃ sṛṣṭaṃ vai brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇād vedāś cāpy agnihotrārthaṃ jajñire svayam eva tud agnihotraphalā vedā śīlavṛttaphalaṃ śrutamd ratiputraphalā dārā dānabhogaphalaṃ dhanamd trivedamantrasaṃyogād agnihotraṃ pravartated ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ sthāpyate sūtrasaṃyutaiḥd vasante brāhmaṇasya syād ādheyo gnir narādhipad vasanto brāhmaṇaḥ prokto vedayoniḥ sa ucyated agnyādheyaṃ tu yenātha vasante kriyate nṛpad tasya śrīr brahmavṛddhiś ca brāhmaṇasya vivardhated kṣatriyasyāgnir ādheyo grīṣme śreṣṭhaḥ sa vai nṛpad yenādhānaṃ tu vai grīṣme kriyate tasya vardhated śrīḥ prajāḥ paśavaś caiva vittaṃ tejo balaṃ yaśaḥd śaradrātre tha vaiśyasya hy ādhānīyo hutāśanaḥd śaradrātraṃ svayaṃ vaiśyo vaiśyayoniḥ sa ucyated śarady ādhānam evaṃ vai kriyate yena pāṇḍavad tasyāpi śrīḥ prajāyuś ca paśavo rthaś ca vardhated paśavaḥ sarva evaite tribhir vedair alaṃkṛtāḥd agnihotrāt pravartante yair idaṃ dhriyate jagatd grāmyāraṇyāś ca paśavas tathā vṛkṣās tṛṇāni cad phalāny oṣadhayaś cāpi hy agnihotrakṛte hi tāḥd rasāḥ snehās tathā gandhā ratnāni maṇayas tathād kāñcanāni ca lohāni hy agnihotrakṛte bhavand āyurvedo dhanurvedo mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥd dharmaśāstraṃ ca tat sarvam agnihotrakṛte kṛtamd chandaḥ śikṣāś ca kalpāś ca tathā vyākaraṇaṃ nṛpad śāstraṃ jyotir niruktaṃ cāpy agnihotrakṛte kṛtamd itihāsapurāṇaṃ ca gāthāś copaniṣat tathād ātharvaṇāni karmāṇi cāgnihotrakṛte kṛtamd yac caitasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ hi kiṃ cid asti carācaramd tat sarvam agnihotrasya kṛte sṛṣṭaṃ svayaṃbhuvād agnihotrasya darśasya paurṇamāsasya cāpy athad yūpeṣṭipaśubandhānāṃ somapānakriyāvatāmd tithinakṣatrayogānāṃ muhūrtakaraṇātmanāmd kālasya vedanārthaṃ tu jyotirjñānaṃ kṛtaṃ purād ṛgyajuḥsāmamantrāṇāṃ ślokatattvārthacintanātd pratyāpattivikalpānāṃ chando jñānaṃ prakalpitamd varṇākṣarapadārthānāṃ saṃdhiliṅgaṃ vivakṣitamd nāmadhātuvivekārthaṃ purā vyākaraṇaṃ kṛtamd yūpavedy adhvarārthaṃ tu prokṣaṇaśravaṇāya tud yajñadaivatayogārthaṃ śikṣājñānaṃ prakalpitamd yajñapātrapavitrārthaṃ dravyasaṃbhāraṇāya cad sarvayajñavikalpāya purākalpaṃ prakalpitamd nāmadhātuvibhaktīnāṃ tattvārthaniyamāya cad sarvavedaniruktānāṃ niruktam ṛṣibhiḥ kṛtamd vedyarthaṃ pṛthivī sṛṣṭā saṃbhārārthaṃ tathaiva cad idhmārtham atha yūpārthaṃ brahmā cakre vanaspatimd grāmyāraṇyāś ca paśavo jāyante yajñakāraṇātd mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaṃ ca proṣitā śrāvaṇaṃ tathād anūyājaprayājāṃś ca marutāṃ śaṃsinas tathād udgātṝṃś caiva sāmnāṃ vai baliprasthānam eva cad viṣṇukramāṇāṃ kramaṇaṃ dakṣiṇāvabhṛthaṃ tathād trikālam arcanaṃ caiva sthāneṣūpahṛtaṃ tathād devatāgrahaṇaṃ mokṣaṃ haviṣāṃ śravaṇaṃ tathād nāvabudhyanti ye viprā nindanti ca paśor vadhamd te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ rauravaṃ tamasāvṛtamd śatavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra sthitvā narādhamāḥd krimibhir bhakṣyamāṇāś ca tiṣṭheyuḥ pūyaśoṇited yūpās tu mantrasaṃskārair eṣāṃ vai paśavas tathād yajamānena sahitāḥ svargaṃ yānti nareśvarad yāvat kālaṃ hi yajvā vai svargaloke mahīyated tāvat kālaṃ pramodante paśavo hy adhvare hatāḥd vṛkṣā yūpatvam icchanti paśutvaṃ paśavas tathād tṛṇānīcchanti darbhatvam oṣadhyaś ca haviṣyatāmd somatvaṃ ca latāḥ sarvā veditvaṃ vai vasuṃdharād yasmāt paśutvam icchanti paśavaḥ svargalipsayād tasmāt paśuvadhe hiṃsā nāsti yajñeṣu pāṇḍavad ahiṃsā vaidikaṃ karma brahmakarmeti tat smṛtamd vedoktaṃ ye na kurvanti hiṃsābuddhyā kratuṃ dvijāḥd sadyaḥ śūdratvam āyānti pretya caṇḍālatām apid gāvo yajñārtham utpannā dakṣiṇārthaṃ tathaiva cad suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ caiva pātrī kumbhārtham eva cad darbhāḥ saṃstaraṇārthaṃ tu rakṣasāṃ rakṣaṇāya cad yajanārthaṃ dvijāḥ sṛṣṭās tārakā divi devatāḥd kṣatriyā rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu vaiśyā vārtānimittataḥd śuśrūṣārthaṃ trayāṇāṃ tu śūdrāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvād evam etaj jagat sarvam agnihotrakṛte kṛtamd nāvabudhyanti ye caitan narās tu tamasā vṛtāḥd te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ rauravaṃ nāma viśrutamd rauravād vipramuktās tu krimiyoniṃ vrajanti ted yathoktam agnihotrāṇāṃ śuśrūṣanti ca ye dvijāḥd tair dattaṃ suhutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ dattam adhyāpitaṃ bhavetd evam iṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca yad vipraiḥ kriyate nṛpad tat sarvaṃ samyag āhṛtya cāditye sthāpayāmy ahamd mayā sthāpitam āditye lokasya sukṛtaṃ hi tatd dhārayet tat sahasrāṃśuḥ sukṛtaṃ hy agnihotriṇāmd yāvat kālaṃ tu tiṣṭhanti loke cāpy agnihotriṇaḥd tāvat teṣāṃ hi puṇyena dīpyante raviṇāmbared svarge svargaṃ gatānāṃ tu vīryād bhavati vīryavānd tatra te hy upayuñjanti hy agnihotrasya yat phalamd samānarūpā devānāṃ tiṣṭhanty ābhūtasaṃplavamd vṛthāgninā ca ye ke cid dahyante hy agnihotriṇaḥd na te gnihotriṇāṃ lokaṃ manasāpi vrajanti vaid vīraghnās te durācārāḥ sudaridrā narādhamāḥd vikalā vyādhitāś cāpi jāyante śūdrayoniṣud tasmād aproṣitair nityam agnihotraṃ dvijātibhiḥd hotavyaṃ vidhivad rājann ūrdhvam icchanti ye gatimd ātmavat tatra mantavyam agnihotraṃ yudhiṣṭhirad na tyājyaṃ kṣaṇam apy etad gṛhītavyaṃ dvijātibhiḥd vṛddhatve py agnihotraṃ vai gṛhṇanti vidhivad dvijāḥd śūdrānnād viratā dāntāḥ saṃyatendriyabuddhayaḥd pañcayajñaparā nityaṃ krodhalobhavivarjitāḥd dvikālam atithīṃś caiva pūjayanti ca bhaktitaḥd te pi sūryodayaprakhyair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥd mama loke pramodante dṛṣṭvā māṃ ca yudhiṣṭhirad manvantaraṃ ca tatraikaṃ moditvā dvijasattamāḥd iha mānuṣyake loke jāyante dvijasattamāḥd bālāhitāgnayo ye ca śūdrānnād viratāḥ sadād krodhalobhavinirmuktāḥ prātaḥsnānaparāyaṇāḥd yathoktam agnihotraṃ vai juhvate vijitendriyāḥd ātitheyāḥ sadā saumyā dvikālaṃ matparāyaṇāḥd te yānty apunarāvṛttiṃ bhittvā cādityamaṇḍalamd mama lokaṃ sapatnīkā yānaiḥ sūryodayaprabhaiḥd tatra bālārkasaṃkāśāḥ kāmagāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥd aiśvaryaguṇasaṃpannāḥ krīḍanti ca yathāsukhamd ity eṣā hy āhitāgnīnāṃ vibhūtiḥ pāṇḍunandanad ye ca devaśrutiṃ ke cin nindamānā hy abuddhayaḥd pramāṇaṃ na ca kurvanti te yānti hy akṣayaṃ tamaḥd pramāṇam itihāsaṃ ca vedān kurvanti ye dvijāḥd yudhiṣṭhira uvācad te yānty amarasāyujyaṃ nityam āstikyabuddhayaḥd cakrāyudha namas te stu deveśa garuḍadhvajad cāndrāyaṇavidhiṃ puṇyam ākhyāhi bhagavan mamad bhagavān uvācad śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena sarvapāpapraṇāśanamd pāpino yena śudhyanti tat te vakṣyāmi sarvaśaḥd brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyo vā caritavrataḥd yathāvat kartukāmo yas tasyeyaṃ prathamā kriyād śodhayet tu śarīraṃ svaṃ pañcagavyena yantritaḥd śarīraṃ kakṣapakṣāntaṃ tataḥ kurvīta pāvanamd śuddhavāsāḥ śucir bhūtvā mauñjīṃ badhnīta mekhalāmd pālāśadaṇḍam ādāya brahmacārivrate sthitaḥd kṛtopavāsaḥ pūrvaṃ tu śuklapratipadi dvijaḥd nadīsaṃgamatīrtheṣu śucau deśe gṛhe pi vād gomayenopalipte tha sthaṇḍile gniṃ nidhāpayetd āghārāv ājyabhāgau ca praṇavaṃ vyāhṛtīs tathād vāruṇaiś cāpi pañcaiva hutvā sarvān yathākramamd satyāya viṣṇave ceti brahmarṣibhyo tha brahmaṇed viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyaḥ prajāpataya eva cad ṣaṭkṛtvo juhuyāt paścāt prāyaścittāhutiṃ dvijaḥd tataḥ samāpayed agniṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvātha pauṣṭikamd praṇamyāgniṃ ca somaṃ ca bhasma dhṛtvā tathātmanid nadīṃ gatvā viviktātmā somāya varuṇāya cad ādityāya namaskṛtvā tataḥ snāyāt samāhitaḥd uttīryodakam ācamya tv āsīnaḥ pūrvatomukhaḥd prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pavitrair abhiṣecanamd ācāntas tv abhivīkṣeta cordhvabāhur divākaramd kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ paścāt kuryāc caiva pradakṣiṇamd nārāyaṇaṃ vā rudraṃ vā brahmāṇam atha vāpi vād vāruṇaṃ mantrasūktaṃ vā prāgbhojanam athāpi vād vīraghnam ṛṣabhaṃ vāpi tathā cāpy aghamarṣaṇamd gāyatrīṃ mama vā devīṃ sāvitrīṃ vā japet tataḥd tataś cāṣṭādaśaṃ vāpi sahasram atha vāparamd tato madhyāhnakāle vai pāyasaṃ yāvakaṃ hi vād pācayitvā prayatnena prayataḥ susamāhitaḥd pātraṃ tu susamādāya sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tu vād tāmraṃ vā mṛnmayaṃ vāpi audumbaram athāpi vād vṛkṣāṇāṃ yājñiyānāṃ tu parṇair ārdrair akutsitaiḥd puṭakena tu guptena cared bhaikṣaṃ samāhitaḥd brāhmaṇānāṃ gṛhāṇāṃ tu saptānāṃ nāparaṃ vrajetd godohamātraṃ tiṣṭhet tu vāgyataḥ saṃyatendriyaḥd na hasec ca na vīkṣec ca nābhibhāṣeta vā striyamd dṛṣṭvā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca caṇḍālaṃ vā rajasvalāmd patitaṃ ca tathā śvānam ādityam avalokayetd yo hi pādukam āruhya sarvadā pracared dvijaḥd taṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpakarmāṇam ādityam avalokayetd tatas tv āvasathaṃ prāpto bhikṣāṃ nikṣipya bhūtaled prakṣālya pādāv ā jānvor hastāv ākūrparaṃ punaḥd ācamya vāriṇā tena vahniṃ viprāṃś ca pūjayetd pañca saptātha vā kuryād bhāgān bhaikṣasya tasya vaid teṣām anyatamaṃ piṇḍam ādityāya nivedayetd brahmaṇe cāgnaye caiva somāya varuṇāya cad viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyo dadyād annaṃ yathākramamd avaśiṣṭam athaikaṃ tu vaktramātraṃ prakalpayetd aṅgulyagre sthitaṃ piṇḍaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantrayetd aṅgulībhis tribhiḥ piṇḍaṃ prāśnīyāt prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥd yathā ca vardhate somo hrasate ca yathā punaḥd tathā piṇḍāś ca vardhante hasante ca dine dined trikālaṃ snānam asyoktaṃ dvikālam atha vā sakṛtd brahmacārī sadā vāpi na ca vastraṃ prapīḍayetd sthāne na divasaṃ tiṣṭhed rātrau vīrāsanaṃ vrajetd bhavet sthaṇḍilaśāyī vāpy atha vā vṛkṣamūlikaḥd valkalaṃ yadi vā kṣaumaṃ śāṇaṃ kārpāsakaṃ tu vād ācchādanaṃ bhavet tasya vastrārthaṃ pāṇḍunandanad evaṃ cāndrāyaṇe pūrṇe māsasyānte prayatnavānd brāhmaṇān bhojayed bhaktyā dadyāc caiva ca dakṣiṇāmd cāndrāyaṇena cīrṇena yat kṛtaṃ tena duṣkṛtamd tat sarvaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavatd brahmahatyātha gohatyā suvarṇastainyam eva cad bhrūṇahatyā surāpānaṃ guror dāravyatikramaḥd evam anyāni pāpāni pātakīyāni yāni cad cāndrāyaṇena naśyanti vāyunā pāṃsavo yathād anirdaśāyā goḥ kṣīram auṣṭram āvikam eva cad mṛtasūtakayoś cānnaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd upapātakinaś cānnaṃ patitānnaṃ tathaiva cad śūdrasyoccheṣaṇaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd ākāśasthaṃ tu hastastham āsanasthaṃ tathaiva cad parahastasthitaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd athāgredidhiṣor annaṃ didhiṣūpapates tathād parivettus tathā cānnaṃ parivittānnam eva cad kuṇḍānnaṃ golakānnaṃ ca devalānnaṃ tathaiva cad tathā purohitasyānnaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd surāsavaṃ viṣaṃ sarpir lākṣā lavaṇam eva cad tailaṃ cāpi ca vikrīṇan dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte dinamadhyagato pi yaḥd bhinnabhāṇḍe tu yo bhuṅkte dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd yo bhuṅkte nupanītena yo bhuṅkte ca striyā sahad yo bhuṅkte kanyayā sārdhaṃ dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd ucchiṣṭaṃ sthāpayed vipro yo mohād bhojanāntared dadyād vā yadi saṃmohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd tumbakośātakaṃ caiva palaṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ tathād chattrākaṃ laghunaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd tathā paryuṣitaṃ cānnaṃ pakvaṃ paragṛhāgatamd vipakvaṃ ca tathā māṃsaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd udakyayā śunā vāpi caṇḍālair vā dvijottamaḥd dṛṣṭam annaṃ tu bhuñjāno dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caretd etat purā viśuddhyartham ṛṣibhiś caritaṃ vratamd pāvanaṃ sarvapāpānāṃ puṇyaṃ pāṇḍava coditamd etena vasavo rudrāś cādityāś ca divaṃ gatāḥd etad ādyaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ smṛtamd yathoktam etad yaḥ kuryād dvijaḥ pāpapraṇāśanamd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad sa divaṃ yāti pūtātmā nirmalādityasaṃnibhaḥd keśavenaivam ukte tu cāndrāyaṇavidhikramed yudhiṣṭhira uvācad ekabhuktena madbhakto māsam ekaṃ tu vartated jalaṃ vā na piben māse nāntaraṃ bhojanāt paramd ādityarūpaṃ māṃ nityam arcayan susamāhitaḥd vratānte bhojayed viprān dakṣiṇāṃ saṃpradāya cad pūrṇam ekabhuktena yaḥ kṣipetd bhagavān uvācad tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan mamācakṣva keśavad śṛṇu pāṇḍava satyaṃ me vacanaṃ puṇyam uttamamd yad akṛtvātha vā kṛtvā naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyated ekabhuktena varteta naraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥd brahmacārī hy adhaḥśāyī jitakrodho jitendriyaḥd śuciḥ snānarato vyagraḥ satyavāg anasūyakaḥd arcayann eva māṃ nityaṃ madgatenāntarātmanād saṃdhyayos tu guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathād guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthajñānasya dhāraṇamd narāṇāṃ poṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ gārhasthyaṃ tīrtham ucyated ātitheyaṃ paraṃ tīrtham atithis tīrtham ucyated brahmacaryaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ brahmatīrthaṃ sanātanamd kṣamā tu paramaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu pāṇḍavad kṣamāvatām ayaṃ lokaḥ paraś caiva kṣamāvatāmd mānito mānito vāpi pūjito pūjito pi vād ākṛṣṭas tarjito vāpi kṣamāvāṃs tīrtham ucyated kṣamā damaḥ kṣamā dānaṃ kṣamā yajñaḥ kṣamā tapaḥd kṣamāhiṃsā kṣamā dharmaḥ kṣamā cendriyanigrahaḥd kṣamā dayā kṣamā yajñaḥ kṣamayaitad dhṛtaṃ jagatd kṣamāvān prāpnuyāt svargaṃ kṣamāvān prāpnuyād yaśaḥd kṣamāvān prāpnuyān mokṣaṃ tasmāt sā tīrtham ucyated ātmā nadī bhāratapuṇyatīrthamd ātmā tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthapradhānamd ātmā tu yajñaḥ satataṃ manyate vaid svargo mokṣaḥ sarvam ātmany samantraṃ tu pṛthak pṛthakd māsi māsi pibed yas tu tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyatid pāpaṃ ca brahmakūrcaṃ ca śṛṇu mantraṃ ca bhāratad pālāśaṃ padmapatraṃ vā tāmraṃ vātha hiraṇmayamd sādayitvā tu gṛhṇīyāt tat tu pātram udāhṛtamd gāyatryā gṛhya gomūtraṃ gandhadvāreti gomayamd āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇeti vai dadhid tejo si śukram ity ājyaṃ devasyeti kuśodakamd āpo hi ṣṭheti saṃgṛhya yavacūrṇaṃ yathāvidhid brahmaṇe ca yathā hutvā samiddhe ca hutāśaned āloḍya praṇavenaiva nirmathya praṇavena tud uddhṛtya praṇavenaiva pibet tu praṇavena tud mahatāpi sa pāpena tvacevāhir vimucyated bhadraṃ na agnihotraṃ vṛthā rājan vṛthā vedās tathaiva cad śīlena devās tuṣyanti śrutayas tatra kāraṇamd kṣāntaṃ dāntaṃ jitakrodhaṃ jitātmānaṃ jitendriyamd tam agryaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ manye śeṣāḥ śūdrā iti smṛtāḥd agnihotravrataparān svādhyāyaniratāñ śucīnd upavāsaratān dāntāṃs tān devā brāhmaṇān viduḥd na jātiḥ pūjyate rājan guṇāḥ kalyāṇakāraṇāḥd caṇḍālam api vṛttasthaṃ taṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ viduḥd manaḥśaucaṃ karmaśaucaṃ kulaśaucaṃ ca bhāratad śarīraśaucaṃ vākśaucaṃ śaucaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtamd pañcasv eteṣu śauceṣu hṛdi śaucaṃ viśiṣyated hṛdayasya tu śaucena svargaṃ gacchanti mānavāḥd agnihotraparibhraṣṭaḥ prasaktaḥ krayavikrayed varṇasaṃkarakartā ca brāhmaṇo vṛṣalaiḥ samaḥd yasya vedaśrutir naṣṭā karṣakaś cāpi yo dvijaḥd vikarmasevī kaunteya sa vai vṛṣala ucyated vṛṣo hi dharmo vijñeyas tasya yaḥ kurute layamd vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād apid stutibhir brahmapūtābhir yaḥ śūdraṃ stauti mānavaḥd na ca māṃ stauti pāpātmā sa mām ākrośayed bhṛśamd śvadṛtau tu yathā kṣīraṃ brahma vai bhagavān devaḥ pṛthām āmantrya cārtavatd dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca gāndhārīṃ viduraṃ draupadīṃ tathād kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsam ṛṣīn anyāṃś ca mantriṇaḥd subhadrām ātmajayutām uttarāṃ spṛśya pāṇinād nirgatya veśmanas tasmād āruroha mahārathamd vājibhiḥ sainyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥd yuktaṃ ca dhvajabhūtena patagendreṇa dhīmatād anvāruroha cāpy enaṃ premṇā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥd apāsya cāśu yantāraṃ dārukaṃ sūtasattamamd abhīśūn pratijagrāha svayaṃ kurupatis tadād upāruhyārjunaś cāpi cāmaravyajanaṃ śubhamd rukmadaṇḍaṃ bṛhan mūrdhni dudhāvābhipradakṣiṇamd chattraṃ śataśalākaṃ ca divyamālyopaśobhitamd vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍaṃ ca cāmīkaravibhūṣitamd dadhāra tarasā bhīmaḥ chattraṃ tac chārṅgadhanvinaḥd bhīmasenārjunau cāpi yamau cāpy arisūdanaud pṛṣṭhato nuyayuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ mā śabda iti harṣitāḥd triyojane vyatīte tu pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavānd visṛjya kṛṣṇas tān sarvān praṇatān dvārakāṃ yayaud tathā praṇamya govindaṃ tadā prabhṛti pāṇḍavāḥd kapilādyāni dānāni dadur dharmaparāyaṇāḥd madhusūdanavākyāni smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ punaḥd manasā pūjayām āsur hṛdayasthāni pāṇḍavāḥd yudhiṣṭhiras tu dharmātmā hṛdi kṛtvā janārdanamd tadbhaktas tanmanā yuktas tadyājī tatparo bhavatd evam etat purāvṛttaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaśāsanamd mayā te kathitaṃ rājan pavitraṃ pāpanāśanamd tac chṛṇuṣva mahārāja viṣṇuproktaṃ kurūdvahad tena gacchasi nānyena tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
